Nuhm 1 _to mrs. Saville, england._ st. Petersburgh, dec. 11th, 17—. Du dungi rejoice tor zhu-tor ik rai koshvar has accompanied wuh palikaya t' wuh enterprise if du ma fudau k' such ek'rasah forebodings. I lasha la' za-gad, heh t'nash-veh wuh'rak task nam-tor tor assure t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-kai t' t'nash-veh welfare heh increasing guhl'es svi' wuh navun t' t'nash-veh undertaking. I am already irak desh'rak t' london, heh u' i lates svi' wuh yut t' petersburgh, i olau wuh samu northern pi'salan mavau fi-tor t'nash-veh nak, if braces t'nash-veh tor'tsu heh boshau me k' delight. Tor du ken-tor nash olaya? Nash pi'salan, if has travelled s' wuh shal na' if i am advancing, mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh foretaste t' eifa icy climes. Inspirited k' nash salan t' ugaya, t'nash-veh rirun shetau weht fervent heh vivid. I ar'kadan svi' vain tor nam-tor persuaded ik wuh fek nam-tor wuh ku-san t' le-su heh desolation; ish-veh ek'wak presents itself tor t'nash-veh glenonaya u' wuh shal t' vaksur heh delight. Tra', margaret, wuh yel nam-tor na' ek'wak visible, its sax'ksei mathra aishan skirting wuh ir-zehl heh diffusing wuh perpetual splendour. Tra'—na' k' ish-veh trasha, t'nash-veh ko-kai, i dungi shitau ein sahrafel svi' preceding navigators—tra' izh heh le-su nam-tor klee'fah'tu; heh, masu-halovaun abru' wuh hayal masutra, etek lau nam-tor wafted tor wuh solektra surpassing svi' wonders heh svi' vaksur kanok shal hitherto discovered fi' wuh habitable ek'tra-dukal. Its torvaya heh features lau nam-tor rik' li-fal, u' wuh phenomena t' wuh heavenly ak'shem undoubtedly nam-tor svi' eifa undiscovered solitudes. Ra lau ri nam-tor gishu svi' wuh shasol t' ek'wakik ta'hal? I lau tra' discover wuh wondrous tepul if skamau wuh og-lum heh lau pakhartau wuh thousand celestial glantaya ik require goh nash halan tor render ish-veh seeming eccentricities tsurkanik na' ek'wak. I dungau satiate t'nash-veh ardent curiosity k' wuh glan t' wuh krus t' wuh panu worla fa' yaretau, heh lau tread wuh solektra worla fa' imprinted k' wuh ash'ya t' sasu. Aifa nam-tor t'nash-veh enticements, heh au nam-tor sufficient tor conquer ek' pthak t' tehvar il tevakh heh tor vimevilau me tor palikau nash laborious halan k' wuh mak wuh kan olau lu au fihal-tor svi' wuh pi' masu-hali, k' ish-veh holiday katelau, fi' wuh expedition t' discovery abru ish-veh salatik pilash. Tonk'peh supposing ek' aifa conjectures tor nam-tor riyeht, du fam yehat kal'i'fee wuh inestimable rufai if i dungau confer fi' ek' mankind, tor wuh kim-shah generation, k' discovering wuh tvur be' wuh fek tor eifa shasol, tor pulau if na' la' ni wehk tevun-krus nam-tor requisite; il k' ascertaining wuh tsat t' wuh seshan-kov, if, kuv na' ek' tor-yehat, mokuhlek goh nam-tor effected k' wuh undertaking such u' t'nash-veh. Aifa haulan ma dispelled wuh agitation k' if i began t'nash-veh nuhm, heh i olau t'nash-veh khaf-spol min k' wuh buhl'es if ashenau me tor sha-ka-ri, na' nothing contributes ni mau tor tranquillise wuh kashek u' wuh br'xan lof—wuh sfek fi' if wuh soul lau teslau its intellectual bezhun. Nash expedition has vesh' wuh favourite sahr-tor t' t'nash-veh lehkuh-mal tevun. I ma telv-tor k' ardour wuh khrosahp t' wuh vuhnauk halan if ma vesh' tor svi' wuh prospect t' arriving na' wuh desh'rak hayal-masutra k'fai wuh masutra if vikuvau wuh fek. Du lau vokau ik wuh vesht-var t' ek' wuh halan tor na' lof t' discovery tertitau wuh bosh t' etwel rom sa-kuk thomas’ shi'dunap. T'nash-veh education vesh' neglected, wi i vesh' passionately tishau t' telvan. Aifa mog'es vesh' t'nash-veh orenau gad heh mu-yor, heh t'nash-veh familiarity k' au increased ik regret if i had olau, u' wuh kan, fi' learning ik t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s dying injunction had zadik t'nash-veh sa-kuk tor kal-tor me tor fihal-tor svi' wuh seafaring ha'kiv. Aifa visions spoh-tor lu i perused, na' wuh wuh'rak wak, eifa poets t'vi effusions entranced t'nash-veh soul heh abertau ish-veh tor sha-ka-ri. I isha became wuh poet heh na' veh tevun ha-tor svi' wuh paradise t' t'nash-veh sha' fereikan; i glenonau ik i isha lau prah wuh sha'ti svi' wuh temple wilat wuh ahm t' homer heh shakespeare nam-tor consecrated. Du nam-tor muhl acquainted k' t'nash-veh vravshaya heh uf heavily i spitau wuh disappointment. Tonk'peh aishan na' ik wak i inherited wuh fortune t' t'nash-veh krei, heh t'nash-veh nahp vesh' da-tor vi' wuh mashyut t' ish-veh earlier keh'sei. Shehkuh tevun ma be' dvun-tor opi' i resolved fi' t'nash-veh la' undertaking. I mokuhlek, kauk i', vokau wuh wadan s' if i dedicated myself tor nash lo'uk enterprise. I palikau k' inuring t'nash-veh ak'shem tor hardship. I accompanied wuh whale-fishers fi' several expeditions tor wuh desh'rak masutra; i voluntarily palesh-tor samu, mair-yem-penak, mag, heh aitlun t' yuk; i k'ashiv ar'kada harder do wuh tsuri masusu du' wuh gad heh vaikau t'nash-veh mu-yor tor wuh orenau t' su'etek-ek'tal, wuh wihka t' haseret, heh eifa khlup t' tukhik ek'tal s' if wuh naval adventurer lau derive wuh greatest practical advantage. Dah'wak i actually hired myself u' wuh ne'-katelau svi' wuh greenland whaler, heh acquitted myself tor admiration. I bolau sha' i olau wuh pi' yaut lu t'nash-veh khart-lan nufau me wuh dahr dignity svi' wuh hali heh entreated me tor hafau k' wuh greatest earnestness, ni taluhk did au panah-tor t'nash-veh dvin. Heh i', tal-kam margaret, tor i ri nazh tor accomplish ein lo'uk lof? T'nash-veh ha'kiv lau ma vesh' be' dvun-tor svi' ease heh luxury, tonk'peh i preferred glory tor kanok enticement ik don-tak shitau svi' t'nash-veh yut. Oh, ik ein encouraging spes would kilko-srashiv svi' wuh affirmative! T'nash-veh courage heh t'nash-veh resolution nam-tor pesik; tonk'peh t'nash-veh rok-tor kapralau, heh t'nash-veh tam'a nam-tor k'ashiv depressed. I am pa' tor proceed fi' wuh wu heh rihagik halan, wuh kefik t' if dungi haishaya ek' t'nash-veh fortitude: i am required ri goh tor ashenau wuh tam'a t' vath, tonk'peh sometimes tor potun-tor t'nash-veh sha', lu ish-veh nam-tor failing. Nash nam-tor wuh danik favourable wak-krus na' travelling svi' russia. Au hash-tor sahris abru' wuh izh svi' ish-veh sledges; wuh dvunel nam-tor vaksurik, heh, svi' t'nash-veh opinion, irak weht agreeable do ik t' wuh eingelsu stagecoach. Wuh samu nam-tor ri mauyik, kuv du nam-tor wrapped svi' furs—wuh sai-vel if i ma already thanai, na' tra' nam-tor wuh lo'uk natyan svi' walking wuh lan-tol heh remaining hayal-tor motionless na' wadan, lu rai tusok prevents wuh khaf s' actually freezing svi' ish-veh os-khaf-mev. I ma rai ambition tor pak-tor t'nash-veh ha'kiv fi' wuh lehk-fau-yut svi' st. Petersburgh heh archangel. I dungau trashu na' wuh latter kahr svi' wuh fortnight il rehkuh wehk gad; heh t'nash-veh intention nam-tor tor hire wuh hali tra', if mokuhlek easily nam-tor ovsoh k' paying wuh insurance na' wuh owner, heh tor engage u' wehk masusu u' i nah-tor bolayatik among eifa vi nam-tor accustomed tor wuh whale-fishing. I ri tor intend tor mashalo-thalv abi' wuh tevun-krus t' belaar; heh lu dungau i fun? Ah, tal-kam ko-kai, uf mokuhlek i kilko-srashiv nash deshker? Kuv i navau, wehk, wehk tevun-krus, sos'eh tevun, dungi be' dvun fa' du heh i lau ragel-tor. Kuv i vravshau, du dungi gla-tor me va'ashiv ak, il worla. Rom-halan, t'nash-veh tal-kam, marom margaret. Sha-ka-ri mashulayek ne' blessings fi' du, heh korsau me, ik i lau va'ashiv heh va'ashiv testify t'nash-veh gratitude na' ek' ish-veh ashaya heh kindness. Ish-veh affectionate sa-kai, r. Walton nuhm 2 _to mrs. Saville, england._ archangel, 28th march, 17—. Uf slowly wuh wak be' dvun-tor la', encompassed u' i am k' le-su heh izh! Wi wuh dahr ash nam-tor taken na' t'nash-veh enterprise. I ma hired wuh hali heh am occupied svi' collecting t'nash-veh masusu; eifa ik i ma already engaged saudau tor nam-tor sasu fi' ik i mokuhlek nerau heh nam-tor certainly ma t' dauntless courage. Tonk'peh i ma veh aitlun if i ma worla wi vesh' kup tor satisfy, heh wuh k'torr wuh vel t' if i i' olau u' wuh danik severe ek'rasah, i ma rai t'hy'la, margaret: lu i am glowing k' wuh buhl'es t' navun, tra' dungi nam-tor rim tor participate t'nash-veh mak; kuv i am assailed k' disappointment, rai veh dungi endeavour tor potun-tor me svi' dejection. I dungau kugau t'nash-veh nahp tor dun, ish-veh nam-tor yeht; tonk'peh ik nam-tor wuh ri donku-tor medium na' wuh sviribaya t' olaya. I aitlun wuh apc'koik t' wuh sasu vi kupi sympathise k' me, t'vi bezhun would kilko tor t'nash-veh. Du lau deem me romantic, t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-kai, tonk'peh i bitterly olau wuh aitlun t' wuh t'hy'la. I ma kling be' me, gentle wi courageous, ma t' wuh sokasitau u' muhl u' t' wuh capacious kashek, t'vi zahv-tor nam-tor spo' t'nash-veh sha', tor messau il amend t'nash-veh dotoran. Uf would such wuh t'hy'la teslau wuh lafot t' ish-veh ri donku-tor sa-kai! I am nuh' ardent svi' execution heh nuh' impatient t' rihag'es. Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor wuh fam dvun greater ek'rasah tor me ik i am shal-educated: na' wuh wuh'rak leh-keh tevun t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv i sahr-tor kwai fi' wuh tsuri heh telv-tor nothing tonk'peh etwel sa-kuk thomas’ dunap t' halan. Na' ik ya'shakhuv i became acquainted k' wuh u'thet poets t' etwel sha' shasol; tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' goh lu ish-veh had ceased tor nam-tor svi' t'nash-veh tepul tor derive its danik yauluhk rufai s' such wuh conviction ik i pakashogau wuh bolayek t' becoming acquainted k' weht gen-lis do ik t' t'nash-veh salatik shasol. I' i am dah-leh-ohkuh heh am svi' reality weht illiterate do wehk schoolboys t' leh-kau. Ish-veh nam-tor yeht ik i ma nahp weht heh ik t'nash-veh rirun nam-tor weht sadvun-tor heh magnificent, tonk'peh au aitlun (u' wuh krassu vutau ish-veh) _keeping; _ heh i greatly bolaya wuh t'hy'la vi would ma kash-ral hiyet ri tor despise me u' romantic, heh affection hiyet na' me tor endeavour tor pakhartau t'nash-veh kashek. Muhl, aifa nam-tor nam-tor-fam complaints; i dungau certainly talal rai t'hy'la fi' wuh eik masutra, il kauk la' svi' archangel, among merchants heh masusu. Wi ein feelings, unallied tor wuh mopuhsh t' komihn malat, kuhsh-tor kauk svi' aifa rugged bosoms. T'nash-veh ot-lan, na' instance, nam-tor wuh sasu t' wonderful courage heh enterprise; au nam-tor madly desirous t' glory, il rather, tor zhit t'nash-veh zhit-bal weht characteristically, t' advancement svi' ish-veh ha'yigal. Au nam-tor wuh englishman, heh svi' wuh midst t' national heh professional prejudices, unsoftened k' sokasitaya, retains ein t' wuh noblest endowments t' humanity. I wuh'rak became acquainted k' ish-veh fi' dohn wuh whale hali; finding ik au vesh' unemployed svi' nash kahr, i easily engaged ish-veh tor gol-tor svi' t'nash-veh enterprise. Wuh trensu nam-tor wuh person t' wuh marom disposition heh nam-tor remarkable svi' wuh hali na' ish-veh gentleness heh wuh mildness t' ish-veh nahr. Nash circumstance, hau tor ish-veh muhl-fainu ket'es heh dauntless courage, tor me maut desirous tor engage ish-veh. Wuh youth be' dvun-tor svi' awek'es, t'nash-veh buhfik tevun spent ne' ish-veh gentle heh kogavik fosterage, has ni refined wuh groundwork t' t'nash-veh character ik i fam yehat overcome wuh intense distaste tor wuh tsuri brutality tusok-tor fi' dohn hali: i ma worla pudva-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor bolayatik, heh lu i puzhu-tor t' wuh mariner kaing noted na' ish-veh kindliness t' khaf-spol heh wuh respect heh obedience vlitau tor ish-veh k' ish-veh hali-sutra, i olau myself peculiarly fortunate svi' hasu kup tor shar ish-veh dvin. I puzhu-tor t' ish-veh wuh'rak svi' rather wuh romantic manner, s' wuh t'sai vi owes tor ish-veh wuh happiness t' ish-veh ha'kiv. Nash, briefly, nam-tor ish-veh var. Ein tevun ago au ashau wuh nu'ri russian t'sai t' moderate fortune, heh having amassed wuh considerable hau-ov svi' prize-donku, wuh sa-mekh t' wuh ko-kan consented tor wuh match. Gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh mistress wuh'wak fa' wuh destined hali-kal; tonk'peh she vesh' bathed svi' bezhun-masu, heh throwing herself na' ish-veh ash'ya, entreated ish-veh tor spare ish-veh, confessing na' wuh ka wak ik she ashau wuh'ashiv, tonk'peh ik au vesh' ri donku-tor, heh ik ish-veh sa-mekh would worla consent tor wuh union. T'nash-veh generous t'hy'la reassured wuh suppliant, heh fi' hasu informed t' wuh ahm t' ish-veh lover, instantly abandoned ish-veh pursuit. Au had already bought wuh uroshal k' ish-veh donku, fi' if au had designed tor be' dvun wuh hafayat t' ish-veh ha'kiv; tonk'peh au bestowed wuh bosh fi' ish-veh rival, teretuhr k' wuh hafau t' ish-veh prize-donku tor purchase fek, heh yi himself solicited wuh nu'ri kosu’s sa-mekh tor consent tor ish-veh kal'i'farr k' ish-veh lover. Tonk'peh wuh hinek sasu decidedly klee'fah, thinking himself bound svi' dor tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la, vi, lu au afer-tor wuh sa-mekh inexorable, quitted ish-veh shasol, il fun-tor abi' au puzhu-tor ik ish-veh former mistress vesh' telik fupa s' ish-veh inclinations. “ra wuh thol katravahsu!” du dungi sporiben. Au nam-tor ni; tonk'peh yi au nam-tor wholly uneducated: au nam-tor u' ralash-fam u' wuh turk, heh wuh ves t' ignorant carelessness attends ish-veh, if, du' ish-veh renders ish-veh spa-tor wuh weht astonishing, detracts s' wuh eku'ko heh sympathy if vathru au would a'fic. Wi ri tor suppose, fai'ei i complain wuh pi' il fai'ei i mokuhlek conceive wuh consolation na' t'nash-veh toils if i lau worla fai-tor, ik i am wavering svi' t'nash-veh resolutions. Eifa nam-tor u' teslau u' buk, heh t'nash-veh halan nam-tor goh i' vohtau abi' wuh igen-va dungau permit t'nash-veh embarkation. Wuh karil has vesh' dreadfully severe, tonk'peh wuh sikar ugau muhl, heh ish-veh nam-tor panah-tor u' wuh remarkably lehkuh-mal tevun-yonuk, ni ik sos'eh i lau mashalo-thalv sooner do i gishu. I dungau tor nothing rashly: du fai-tor me sufficiently tor confide svi' t'nash-veh prudence heh considerateness whenever wuh ek'manek t' vath nam-tor committed tor t'nash-veh tun. I fam yehat kethelvau tor du t'nash-veh kashan fi' wuh be' prospect t' t'nash-veh undertaking. Ish-veh nam-tor impossible tor sviribau tor du wuh conception t' wuh trembling kashan, ulef pleasurable heh ulef pthak-bosh, k' if i am preparing tor trashu. I am going tor unexplored shal, tor “wuh solektra t' mist heh izh, ” tonk'peh i dungau stau rai albatross; therefore ri tor nam-tor alarmed na' t'nash-veh ek'manek il kuv i dang sarlah pla' tor du u' worn heh woeful u' wuh “t'kahr mariner.” du dungi abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' t'nash-veh allusion, tonk'peh i dungi disclose wuh tsat. I ma k'ashiv attributed t'nash-veh attachment tor, t'nash-veh passionate buhl'es na', wuh tehvar-bosh mysteries t' masutra tor ik torvaya t' wuh danik imaginative t' iyik poets. Tra' nam-tor vel na' ar'kadan svi' t'nash-veh soul if i ri tor ken-tor. I am practically industrious—painstaking, wuh workman tor fitor k' perseverance heh zup—tonk'peh isha nash tra' nam-tor wuh ashaya na' wuh marvellous, wuh dva svi' wuh marvellous, intertwined svi' ek' t'nash-veh ar'tu, if hurries me si' t' wuh tsuri pathways t' sasu, kauk tor wuh kwai masutra heh unvisited shal i am pa' tor explore. Tonk'peh tor fun tor dearer considerations. Dungau i ragel-tor du va'ashiv, po' having traversed immense masutra, heh fun-tor k' wuh danik southern cape t' africa il america? I dare ri gish such navun, wi i fam yehat lesh tor glazhau fi' wuh reverse t' wuh bikuv. Fator na' wuh la' tor kitau tor me k' kanok opportunity: i lau poprah ish-veh nuhm fi' ein occasions lu i bolaya au danik tor nenikaya t'nash-veh tam'a. I ashaya du maut tenderly. Vokau me k' affection, dang du worla zhu-tor s' me va'ashiv. Ish-veh affectionate sa-kai, robert walton nuhm 3 _to mrs. Saville, england._ july 7th, 17—. T'nash-veh tal-kam ko-kai, i kitau wuh zamu zehl svi' haste tor leralmin ik i am safe—heh muhl storilau fi' t'nash-veh halan. Nash nuhm dungi pulau england k' wuh merchantman i' fi' its homeward halan s' archangel; weht fortunate do i, vi lau ri gla-tor t'nash-veh salatik solektra, sos'eh, na' wehk tevun. I am, however, svi' rom tam'a: t'nash-veh sasu nam-tor vakh heh sauyaing pesik t' lof, il tor wuh floating thalv t' le-suma ik continually be' dvun etek, indicating wuh tehvar t' wuh shal na' if etek nam-tor advancing, saudau tor dismay au. Etek ma already pulau wuh maut pid latitude; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor wuh pidek t' belaar, heh hi ri ni lamekh u' svi' england, wuh southern karik salan, if salur etek speedily na' eifa gef if i ni ardently aitlun tor attain, esh-tor wuh degree t' renovating warmth if i had ri gishu. Rai incidents ma hitherto befallen etek ik would tor wuh khlop svi' wuh nuhm. Veh il dahkuh stegel karik salan heh wuh springing t' wuh tasaya nam-tor kisheya if veshtau navigators scarcely vokau tor vipladau, heh i dungau nam-tor muhl content kuv nothing weh-rasahkos pavesh-tor tor etek du' etwel halan. Adieu, t'nash-veh tal-kam margaret. Nam-tor assured ik na' t'nash-veh sha' sake, u' muhl u' ish-veh, i dungi ri rashly snagel tehvar. I dungi nam-tor samuyau, persevering, heh prudent. Tonk'peh navun _shall_ tarkiv t'nash-veh endeavours. Wherefore ri? Thus irak i ma hal-tor, tracing wuh shar yut abru' wuh pathless masutra, wuh maut yel themselves hasu toglantausu heh testimonies t' t'nash-veh triumph. Po ri fam dvun proceed abru' wuh untamed wi obedient meilak? Ra mokuhlek pehkaya wuh satalau khaf-spol heh resolved dungi t' sasu? T'nash-veh puv khaf-spol involuntarily mukau itself si' thus. Tonk'peh i bolau shaht. Sha-ka-ri kudau t'nash-veh k'diwa ko-kai! R.w. Nuhm 4 _to mrs. Saville, england._ august 5th, 17—. Ni flekh wuh kisheya has pavesh-tor tor etek ik i fam yehat forbear recording ish-veh, hi ish-veh nam-tor maut yesik ik du dungi gla-tor me fa' aifa dun mokuhlek sarlah vi' ish-veh mat. Kim-shah gad (july 31st) etek vesh' nearly vikuvau k' le-suma, if a'ing svi' wuh hali fi' ek' vla, scarcely leaving ish-veh wuh masutra-tvi-shal svi' if she markau. Etwel situation vesh' somewhat tehvar-bosh, wa' u' etek vesh' compassed pauk k' wuh maut bali ihsek. Etek accordingly ti tor, hoping ik ein rubah would nem-tor shi svi' wuh igen-tukh heh igen-va. Pa' dahkuh o’wak-vel wuh mist pa'shu maf, heh etek beheld, sakadau si' svi' kanok kharat, vast heh ripakhaik eiktra t' le-suma, if seemed tor ma rai shaht. Ein t' t'nash-veh comrades groaned, heh t'nash-veh sha' kashek began tor tor'ovau tun-tor k' anxious nahp, lu wuh flekh glan suddenly skamau etwel attention heh matau etwel solicitude s' etwel sha' situation. Etek pakashogau wuh neik carriage, teslau fi' wuh sledge heh drawn k' dogs, be' dvun fi' na' wuh desh'rak, na' wuh ir t' ulef wuh mile; wuh hasu if had wuh shid t' wuh sasu, tonk'peh sauyaing t' masuk' stature, hayal-tor svi' wuh sledge heh kakhartau wuh dogs. Etek glantau wuh rapid progress t' wuh traveller k' etwel irak-zan-vel abi' au vesh' pakik among wuh irak inequalities t' wuh le-suma. Nash appearance teporilau etwel unqualified wonder. Etek vesh', u' etek pudva-tor, wehk hundred miles s' sovek solektra; tonk'peh nash apparition seemed tor denote ik ish-veh vesh' ri, svi' reality, ni irak u' etek had supposed. Ikap-tor svi', however, k' le-suma, ish-veh vesh' impossible tor zahal-tor ish-veh yut, if etek had glantau k' wuh greatest attention. Pa' dahkuh wadan po' nash occurrence etek puzhu-tor wuh solektra masutra, heh fa' mu-yor wuh le-suma shau heh el-tor etwel hali. Etek, however, ti tor abi' wuh asal, fearing tor snagel svi' wuh gu'gelik eifa suk thal shivak if marek pa' po' wuh breaking abru t' wuh le-suma. I profited t' nash wak tor shom na' wuh zamu wadan. Svi' wuh asal, however, u' ak u' ish-veh vesh' ta'hal, i went fi-tor lan-tol heh afer-tor ek' wuh masusu toranik fi' veh vla t' wuh hali, sauyaing talking tor ein-veh svi' wuh masutra. Ish-veh vesh', svi' kla-min, wuh sledge, spo' ik etek had gla-tor fa', if had marau na' etek svi' wuh mu-yor fi' wuh suk karf t' le-suma. Goh veh dog hafau alive; tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh komihn hasu k'svi ish-veh ik wuh masusu vesh' persuading tor svi-tor wuh hali. Au vesh' ri, u' wuh vath traveller seemed tor nam-tor, wuh savage inhabitant t' ein undiscovered vikuvtra, tonk'peh wuh european. Lu i saudau fi' lan-tol wuh trensu leralmin-tor, “la' nam-tor etwel khart-lan, heh au dungi ri kal-tor du tor perish fi' wuh tu'ash masutra.” fi' perceiving me, wuh ri-fainusu addressed me svi' eingelsu, hi k' wuh k'shatri accent. “fa' sarlah nash-veh fi' dohn ish-veh hali, ” leralmin-tor au, “dungi du ma wuh kindness tor inform me whither du nam-tor bound?” du lau conceive t'nash-veh astonishment fi' khaf-spol such wuh deshker addressed tor me s' wuh sasu fi' wuh rihk t' vashaya heh tor ik i dang ma supposed ik t'nash-veh hali would ma vesh' wuh resource if au would ri ma di'kizh-tor na' wuh danik taluhk don-tak wuh terra mokuhlek afford. I kilko-tor, however, ik etek vesh' fi' wuh halan t' discovery na' wuh northern fek. Fi-tor khaf-spol nash au saudau satisfied heh consented tor sarlah fi' dohn. Rom oekon! Margaret, kuv du had gla-tor wuh sasu vi thus capitulated na' ish-veh ek'manek, ish-veh ak'wikmun would ma vesh' boundless. Ish-veh sikrus vesh' nearly le-sumalik, heh ish-veh ak'shem dreadfully emaciated k' zung heh suffering. I worla gla-tor wuh sasu svi' ni wretched wuh nosh. Etek attempted tor lesh ish-veh vi' wuh thif'etek, tonk'peh u' ak u' au had quitted wuh sluk sov au fainted. Etek accordingly katau ish-veh pla' tor wuh lan-tol heh restored ish-veh tor animation k' rubbing ish-veh k' brandy heh forcing ish-veh tor vitem-tor wuh pi' nosahp. U' ak u' au gluvau glat t' ha'kiv etek wrapped ish-veh abru svi' yuk-sai heh shitau ish-veh be' wuh vuzh-mev t' wuh af'tum stove. K' vohris degrees au recovered heh ate wuh pi' shur, if restored ish-veh wonderfully. Dahkuh gad be' dvun-tor svi' nash manner fa' au vesh' kup tor stariben, heh i k'ashiv ptha ik ish-veh sufferings had deprived ish-veh t' understanding. Lu au had svi' ein thon-tor recovered, i snem-tor ish-veh tor t'nash-veh sha' thif'etek heh attended fi' ish-veh u' mau u' t'nash-veh gu-vam would permit. I worla gla-tor wuh weht eku'ki creature: ish-veh bezhun ma paik wuh sagluvaya t' wildness, heh kauk ni-resh, tonk'peh tra' nam-tor moments lu, kuv sovek-veh performs wuh bae'cok t' kindness na' ish-veh il tor ish-veh sovek wuh danik trifling dvin, ish-veh bosh countenance nam-tor lighted abru, u' ish-veh vesh', k' wuh ha-zehl t' benevolence heh sweetness ik i worla gla-tor equalled. Tonk'peh au nam-tor paik melancholy heh despairing, heh sometimes au gnashes ish-veh zud, u' kuv impatient t' wuh rasath t' woes ik oppresses ish-veh. Lu t'nash-veh be'hai'la vesh' wuh pi' recovered i had lo'uk trouble tor potau ska' wuh sasu, vi istau tor ya'akash ish-veh wuh thousand deshkau; tonk'peh i would ri kal-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor tormented k' ish-veh idle curiosity, svi' wuh fupa s' t' ak'shem heh kashek t'vi restoration evidently nerau fi-tor entire repose. Wuh'wak, however, wuh ot-lan ya'akash po au had sarlah ni irak fi-tor wuh le-suma svi' ni flekh wuh hali. Ish-veh countenance instantly assumed wuh pulva t' wuh deepest gloom, heh au kilko-tor, “tor seek veh vi sasahr-tor s' me.” “heh did wuh sasu ik du pursued haolvaya svi' wuh ka fashion?” “ha.” “yi i fancy gla-tor etek ish-veh, na' wuh gad fa' etek picked du abru etek gla-tor ein dogs bestan wuh sledge, k' wuh sasu svi' ish-veh, mes' wuh le-suma.” nash aroused wuh ri-fainusu’s attention, heh au ya'akash wuh multitude t' deshkau fundik wuh route if wuh dæmon, u' au puvutau ish-veh, had pursued. Ak po', lu au vesh' sa'awek k' me, au leralmin-tor, “i ma, doubtless, teporilau ish-veh curiosity, u' muhl u' ik t' aifa rom sutra; tonk'peh du nam-tor nuh' considerate tor tor inquiries.” “certainly; ish-veh would indeed nam-tor maut impertinent heh inhuman svi' me tor trouble du k' sovek inquisitiveness t' t'nash-veh.” “heh wi du rescued me s' wuh flekh heh perilous situation; du ma benevolently restored me tor ha'kiv.” ak po' nash au inquired kuv i nahp ik wuh breaking abru t' wuh le-suma had vashau wuh vath sledge. I kilko-tor ik i kupi ri kilko-srashiv k' sovek degree t' certainty, na' wuh le-suma had ri pushau abi' be' midnight, heh wuh traveller lau ma lasha na' wuh shi' ek'manek fa' ik wak; tonk'peh t' nash i kupi ri judge. S' nash wak wuh uzh tam'a t' ha'kiv animated wuh decaying nentu t' wuh ri-fainusu. Au manifested wuh greatest eagerness tor nam-tor fi-tor lan-tol tor glantau na' wuh sledge if had fa' saudau; tonk'peh i ma persuaded ish-veh tor hafau svi' wuh thif'etek, na' au nam-tor irak nuh' kobat tor potun-tor wuh rawness t' wuh igen-tukh. I ma ugau ik ein-veh dang glantau na' ish-veh heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh instant beglanau kuv sovek uzh vel dang saudau svi' glan. Such nam-tor t'nash-veh journal t' ra relates tor nash flekh occurrence abru tor wuh la' gad. Wuh ri-fainusu has gradually improved svi' muhl'es tonk'peh nam-tor maut ralash-fam heh saudau uneasy lu sovek-veh kaula myself svi-tor ish-veh thif'etek. Wi ish-veh manners nam-tor ni conciliating heh gentle ik wuh masusu nam-tor ek' interested svi' ish-veh, hi au ma had maut pi' sviribaya k' ish-veh. Na' t'nash-veh sha' krus, i palikau tor ashaya ish-veh u' wuh sa-kai, heh ish-veh ek'kayik heh glu tushat boshau me k' sympathy heh utan'es. Au bolau ma vesh' wuh thol creature svi' ish-veh weh-rom gad, hasu kauk i' svi' vashau ni attractive heh amiable. I leralmin-tor svi' veh t' t'nash-veh nuhm, t'nash-veh tal-kam margaret, ik i dang talal rai t'hy'la fi' wuh eik masutra; wi i ma afer-tor wuh sasu vi, fa' ish-veh tam'a had vesh' pushau k' misery, i dang ma vesh' kunli ki' ma u' wuh sa-kai t' t'nash-veh khaf-spol. I dungau fator t'nash-veh journal fundik wuh ri-fainusu na' tvi-wak, dang i ma sovek sluk incidents tor vipladau. August 13th, 17—. T'nash-veh affection na' t'nash-veh be'hai'la increases kanok gad. Au teporilau na' wuh'wak t'nash-veh admiration heh t'nash-veh pity tor wuh astonishing degree. Uf mokuhlek gla-tor nash-veh ni thol wuh creature vashau k' misery rik' olaya wuh danik poignant tushat? Au nam-tor ni gentle, wi ni kau-bosh; ish-veh kashek nam-tor ni sokasitau, heh lu au stariben, hi ish-veh zhit nam-tor culled k' wuh choicest tanaf, wi au yumaya k' rapidity heh unparalleled eloquence. Au nam-tor i' mau recovered s' ish-veh has-mar heh nam-tor continually fi' wuh lan-tol, sauyaing watching na' wuh sledge ik preceded ish-veh sha'. Wi, hi unhappy, au nam-tor ri ni utterly occupied k' ish-veh sha' misery tonk'peh ik au eku'ko himself deeply svi' wuh ar'tu t' vath. Au has frequently conversed k' me fi' t'nash-veh, if i ma sviribau tor ish-veh rik' pasut. Au svi-tor attentively vi' ek' t'nash-veh nerau-kek-vuhnayek svi' favour t' t'nash-veh poshahtik navun heh vi' kanok minute detail t' wuh thon-tor i had taken tor shar ish-veh. I vesh' easily pufulag-tor k' wuh sympathy if au evinced tor nam-tor-tor wuh gen-lis t' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, tor mazhiv-kur-tor utterance tor wuh yontau ardour t' t'nash-veh soul heh tor leralmin, k' ek' wuh fervour ik warmed me, uf gladly i would sacrifice t'nash-veh fortune, t'nash-veh nam, t'nash-veh kanok rok, tor wuh furtherance t' t'nash-veh enterprise. Veh sasu’s ha'kiv il tevakh vesh' tonk'peh wuh pi' price tor vlitau na' wuh acquirement t' wuh fai-tukh if i sought, na' wuh dominion i dang prah heh sasau abru' wuh elemental hahf t' etwel ne-koshtri. U' i stariben, wuh gu'gelik gloom sak-tor abru' t'nash-veh listener’s countenance. Palikauk i pakashogau ik au ar'kada tor nelau ish-veh zherka; au shitau ish-veh el'ru fa' ish-veh bezhun, heh t'nash-veh spes quivered heh vravshau me u' i beheld bezhun-masu itsk-yumaya sahris s' svi' ish-veh ozh; wuh groan thorau s' ish-veh heaving thasek. I svizh-tor; na' wu-vath au stariben, svi' pushau accents: “unhappy sasu! Tor du thresh t'nash-veh ni-resh? Ma du mon-tor isha t' wuh intoxicating draught? Zhu-tor me; kal-tor me reveal t'nash-veh var, heh du dungi dash wuh cup s' ish-veh bru-lar!” such zhit, du lau glenonau, strongly teporilau t'nash-veh curiosity; tonk'peh wuh paroxysm t' tushat ik had seized wuh ri-fainusu overcame ish-veh kobatau tepul, heh wehk wadan t' repose heh tranquil conversation vesh' bolayatik tor restore ish-veh composure. Having conquered wuh khrash t' ish-veh feelings, au saudau tor despise himself na' hasu wuh kafeh t' shaukaush; heh quelling wuh gu'gelik tyranny t' despair, au pufulag-tor me va'ashiv tor converse fundik myself personally. Au ya'akash me wuh vesht-var t' t'nash-veh earlier tevun. Wuh var vesh' sahris var-tor, tonk'peh ish-veh awakened vuhnauk ranau t' haulan. I stariben t' t'nash-veh aitlun t' finding wuh t'hy'la, t' t'nash-veh mag na' wuh weht intimate sympathy k' wuh katravahsu kashek do had ek'wak tevan-tor tor t'nash-veh lot, heh sagluvau t'nash-veh conviction ik wuh sasu kupi boast t' pi' happiness vi did ri tizh-tor nash kudaya. “i sep-wafikh k' du, ” kilko-tor wuh ri-fainusu; “etek nam-tor unfashioned creatures, tonk'peh ulef tor abru, kuv veh wiser, weh-rom, dearer do ourselves—such wuh t'hy'la ought tor nam-tor—ri tor lend ish-veh mamuk tor perfectionate etwel kobat heh lafotik natures. I wuh'wak had wuh t'hy'la, wuh danik thol t' komihn creatures, heh am entitled, therefore, tor judge respecting friendship. Du ma rok, heh wuh panu fa' du, heh ma rai aishan na' despair. Tonk'peh i—i ma pakik kanok-vei heh fam yehat palikau ha'kiv anew.” u' au leralmin-tor nash ish-veh countenance became expressive t' wuh hayal, settled tushat ik estuhl me tor wuh khaf-spol. Tonk'peh au vesh' ralash-fam heh presently retired tor ish-veh thif'etek. Kauk pushau svi' tam'a u' au nam-tor, kling mokuhlek olau weht deeply do au tor wuh beauties t' malat. Wuh starry igen, wuh masutra, heh kanok glan afforded k' aifa wonderful shal seem fam dvun ki' wuh tepul t' elevating ish-veh soul s' terra. Such wuh sasu has wuh dahtau nam: au lau dash misery heh nam-tor overwhelmed k' disappointments, wi lu au has retired vi' himself, au dungi nam-tor spo' wuh celestial tam'a ik has wuh pau pa' ish-veh, k'svi t'vi da-kuv rai tushat il folly ventures. Dungi du abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' wuh buhl'es i sagluvau fundik nash ekonik wanderer? Du would ri kuv gla-tor du ish-veh. Du ma vesh' tutored heh refined k' dunap heh retirement s' wuh panu, heh du nam-tor therefore somewhat fastidious; tonk'peh nash goh renders du wuh weht nunau tor appreciate wuh wehtsuri merits t' nash wonderful sasu. Sometimes i ma endeavoured tor discover ra quality ish-veh nam-tor if au ma ik ashenau ish-veh ni immeasurably abru' sovek vath person i ek'wak fai-tor. I dva-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh intuitive discernment, wuh sahris tonk'peh worla-failing tepul t' judgment, wuh penetration vi' wuh aisha t' vel, unequalled na' clearness heh precision; hau tor nash wuh kebitra t' sagluvaya heh wuh spes t'vi vuhnau intonations nam-tor soul-subduing ralash-tanaf. August 19th, 17—. Za-gad wuh ri-fainusu leralmin-tor tor me, “du lau easily pakashogau, khart-lan walton, ik i ma dashau lo'uk heh unparalleled misfortunes. I had satalau na' veh wak ik wuh vokaya t' aifa ek'rasah dang tev-tor k' me, tonk'peh du ma skil-tor me tor rubitau t'nash-veh determination. Du seek na' fai-tukh heh kau, u' i wuh'wak did; heh i ardently rok ik wuh gratification t' ish-veh istau lau ri nam-tor wuh serpent tor rakus du, u' t'nash-veh has vesh'. I ri tor fai-tor ik wuh relation t' t'nash-veh koshvar dungi nam-tor useful tor du; wi, lu i haul-tor ik du nam-tor pursuing wuh ka rivak, exposing yourself tor wuh ka tehvar if ma rendered me ra i am, i glenonau ik du lau deduce wuh apt moral s' t'nash-veh var, veh ik lau kharik du kuv du navau svi' ish-veh undertaking heh console du svi' nuf t' vravshaya. Dator tor zhu-tor t' occurrences if nam-tor usually deemed marvellous. Vesh' etek among wuh tamer scenes t' malat i lau pthak tor snagel ish-veh unbelief, sos'eh ish-veh ridicule; tonk'peh wehk vel dungi saudau tor-yehat svi' aifa kwai heh mysterious shal if would provoke wuh laughter t' eifa unacquainted k' wuh ek'wak-vuhnau tepul t' malat; il mokuhlek i vet tonk'peh ik t'nash-veh var zhelesh svi' its weizehl internal evidence t' wuh yeht'es t' wuh pavek t' if ish-veh nam-tor tertitau.” du lau easily glenonau ik i vesh' mau gratified k' wuh nufau sviribaya, wi i kupi ri palesh-tor ik au dang uzhau ish-veh tushat k' wuh recital t' ish-veh misfortunes. I olau wuh greatest eagerness tor zhu-tor wuh ugau narrative, partly s' curiosity heh partly s' wuh karik aitlun tor ameliorate ish-veh buk kuv ish-veh vesh' svi' t'nash-veh tepul. I sagluvau aifa feelings svi' t'nash-veh kilko-srashiv. “i nemaiyo, ” au kilko-tor, “na' ish-veh sympathy, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor nam-tor-fam; t'nash-veh buk nam-tor nearly fulfilled. I bek-tor tonk'peh na' veh pavek, heh yi i dungau repose svi' sochya. I ken-tor ish-veh olaya, ” fator au, perceiving ik i istau tor svi-shau ish-veh; “tonk'peh du nam-tor mistaken, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, kuv thus du dungi kal-tor me tor ahm du; nothing mokuhlek rubitau t'nash-veh buk; shroi tor t'nash-veh vesht-var, heh du dungi pakashogau uf irrevocably ish-veh nam-tor satalau.” au yi var-tor me ik au would palikau ish-veh narrative wuh thurai gad lu i dang nam-tor na' el-wak. Nash ugaya drew s' me wuh warmest itaren. I ma resolved kanok mu-yor, lu i am ri imperatively occupied k' t'nash-veh gu-vam, tor vipladau, u' nearly u' tor-yehat svi' ish-veh sha' zhit, ra au has related du' wuh gad. Kuv i dang nam-tor engaged, i dungi k'puu tor pitoh. Nash manuscript dungi doubtless afford du wuh greatest sanosh; tonk'peh tor me, vi fai-tor ish-veh, heh vi zhu-tor ish-veh s' ish-veh sha' bru-lar—k' ra eku'ko heh sympathy dungau i telv-tor ish-veh svi' ein fa-wak gad! Kauk i', u' i palikau t'nash-veh task, ish-veh bosh-toned spes puv-tor svi' t'nash-veh kaluk; ish-veh lustrous bezhun dwell fi' me k' ek' ish-veh melancholy sweetness; gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh wonil el'ru ashenau svi' animation, du' wuh lineaments t' ish-veh limuk nam-tor irradiated k' wuh soul k'svi. Flekh heh harrowing bolau nam-tor ish-veh var, frightful wuh sahriv if nartau wuh gallant hali fi' its rivak heh vashau ish-veh—thus! Chapter 1 i am k' keshtan wuh genevese, heh t'nash-veh skan nam-tor veh t' wuh danik distinguished t' ik republic. T'nash-veh orfik-kel had vesh' na' wehk tevun counsellors heh syndics, heh t'nash-veh sa-mekh had boshau several tsuri situations k' dor heh reputation. Au vesh' respected k' ek' vi fai-tor ish-veh na' ish-veh ket'es heh indefatigable attention tor tsuri business. Au be' dvun-tor ish-veh younger gad perpetually occupied k' wuh tek'ik t' ish-veh shasol; wuh vuhna'es t' circumstances had prevented ish-veh marrying lehkuh-mal, il vesh' ish-veh abi' wuh decline t' ha'kiv ik au became wuh sa-telsu heh wuh sa-mekh t' wuh skan. U' wuh circumstances t' ish-veh kal'i'farr illustrate ish-veh character, i fam yehat refrain s' relating au. Veh t' ish-veh danik intimate t'hylara vesh' wuh merchant vi, s' wuh flourishing fupa s', tevan-tor, k'fai numerous mischances, vi' poverty. Nash sasu, t'vi ahm vesh' beaufort, vesh' t' wuh yaut heh unbending disposition heh kupi ri lesh tor ha-tor svi' poverty heh oblivion svi' wuh ka shasol wilat au had formerly vesh' distinguished na' ish-veh lan heh magnificence. Having vlitau ish-veh sa'akh, therefore, svi' wuh danik dorli manner, au retreated k' ish-veh ko-fu tor wuh kahr t' lucerne, wilat au ha-tor ri-fainu heh svi' wretchedness. T'nash-veh sa-mekh ashau beaufort k' wuh truest friendship heh vesh' deeply grieved k' ish-veh retreat svi' aifa unfortunate circumstances. Au bitterly deplored wuh riyeht pride if pufulag-tor ish-veh t'hy'la tor wuh spa-tor ni pi' worthy t' wuh affection ik kaunshuk au. Au pakik rai wak svi' endeavouring tor seek ish-veh si', k' wuh rok t' persuading ish-veh tor palikau wuh panu va'ashiv k'fai ish-veh lit heh assistance. Beaufort had taken effectual thon-tor tor ip-sut himself, heh ish-veh vesh' lehkuh tevun-krus fa' t'nash-veh sa-mekh discovered ish-veh abode. Overjoyed na' nash discovery, au hastened tor wuh kelek, if vesh' situated svi' wuh tvai yut be' wuh reuss. Tonk'peh lu au svi-tor, misery heh despair sa'awek welcomed ish-veh. Beaufort had korsau tonk'peh wuh maut pi' hau-ov t' donku s' wuh vashau t' ish-veh fortunes, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' sufficient tor tanilau ish-veh k' sustenance na' ein tevun-krus, heh svi' wuh meantime au rok-tor tor procure ein respectable employment svi' wuh merchant’s kelek. Wuh tvi-wak vesh', consequently, spent svi' inaction; ish-veh tushat goh became weht glu heh rankling lu au had el-wak na' haulan, heh na' wu-vath ish-veh nem-tor ni sahris meskaraya t' ish-veh kashek ik na' wuh shaht t' rehkuh tevun-krus au ti fi' wuh sar-tak t' has-mar, incapable t' sovek pideshan. Ish-veh ko-fu attended ish-veh k' wuh greatest tenderness, tonk'peh gla-tor ish-veh k' despair ik ish-veh pi' donketu-tor vesh' rapidly decreasing heh ik tra' vesh' rai vath prospect t' nenikaya. Tonk'peh caroline beaufort ma wuh kashek t' wuh uncommon mould, heh ish-veh courage she-tor tor nenikaya ish-veh svi' ish-veh adversity. She procured eiktra ar'kadan; she plaited terp heh k' vuhnauk tvai contrived tor pinkau wuh pittance scarcely sufficient tor nenikaya ha'kiv. Several tevun-krus be' dvun-tor svi' nash manner. Ish-veh sa-mekh grew weh-rasahkos; ish-veh wak vesh' weht entirely occupied svi' attending ish-veh; ish-veh tvai t' subsistence nelau; heh svi' wuh tenth tevun-krus ish-veh sa-mekh tev-tor svi' ish-veh kar, leaving ish-veh wuh orphan heh wuh beggar. Nash kim-shah salur overcame ish-veh, heh she knelt k' beaufort’s tevikeh-natuhn weeping bitterly, lu t'nash-veh sa-mekh svi-tor wuh tvi-shal. Sarlah ish-veh spo' wuh protecting tam'a tor wuh ri donku-tor ko-kan, vi committed herself tor ish-veh tun; heh po' wuh interment t' ish-veh t'hy'la au conducted ish-veh tor geneva heh shitau ish-veh ne' wuh protection t' wuh relation. Dahkuh tevun po' nash pavek caroline became ish-veh ko-telsu. Tra' vesh' wuh considerable natyan svi' wuh ya'shakhuv t' t'nash-veh mekhlar, tonk'peh nash circumstance seemed tor kaunshau au goh closer svi' tel t' vaikau affection. Tra' vesh' wuh kash-ral t' yeht-gav svi' t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s abruvenik kashek if rendered ish-veh bolayatik ik au dang messau highly tor ashaya strongly. Sos'eh du' former tevun au had dashau s' wuh tab-ma-discovered unworthiness t' veh k'diwa heh ni vesh' sashitau tor eku wuh greater tala fi' ar'kada don. Tra' vesh' wuh gluvaya t' gratitude heh worship svi' ish-veh attachment tor t'nash-veh ko-mekh, differing wholly s' wuh doting fondness t' ya'shakhuv, na' ish-veh vesh' vi'le-esh-tor k' reverence na' ish-veh virtues heh wuh aitlun tor nam-tor wuh tvai t', svi' ein degree, recompensing ish-veh na' wuh sorrows she had palesh-tor, tonk'peh if mazhiv-kur-tor inexpressible takov tor ish-veh kloshai tor ish-veh. Kanok-vei vesh' tor tor yield tor ish-veh istau heh ish-veh convenience. Au strove tor rau-nol ish-veh, u' wuh rom akan nam-tor rau-tor k' wuh bahsu, s' kanok rougher salan heh tor vikuvau ish-veh k' ek' ik kupi palutunau tor teporilau pleasurable zherka svi' ish-veh mos heh benevolent kashek. Ish-veh muhl'es, heh kauk wuh tranquillity t' ish-veh hitherto ek'kayik tam'a, had vesh' shaken k' ra she had hal-tor k'fai. Du' wuh dahkuh tevun ik had veshau previous tor ish-veh kal'i'farr t'nash-veh sa-mekh had gradually relinquished ek' ish-veh tsuri nam-tor-lof; heh iyi po' ish-veh union au sought wuh vaksurik ek'nosh t' italy, heh wuh rubah t' scene heh eku'ko attendant fi' wuh tour k'fai ik solektra t' wonders, u' wuh restorative na' ish-veh kobatau nentu. S' italy au yaretau germany heh france. I, ish-veh eldest kan, vesh' pukeshta na' naples, heh u' wuh kan-bu accompanied au svi' ish-veh rambles. I hafau na' several tevun ish-veh goh kan. Mau u' au vesh' attached tor tik vath, au seemed tor bes-tor inexhaustible mahr-kel t' affection s' wuh maut t'nash-veh t' ashaya tor bestow au fi-tor me. T'nash-veh ko-mekh’s sival caresses heh t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' benevolent sanosh du' fundauik me nam-tor t'nash-veh wuh'rak recollections. I vesh' ish-veh plaything heh ish-veh idol, heh vel weh-rom—ish-veh kan, wuh innocent heh helpless creature bestowed fi' au k' sha-ka-ri, ik tor katau abru tor rom, heh t'vi fa-wak lot ish-veh vesh' svi' ish-veh el'ru tor kharik tor happiness il misery, according u' au fulfilled ish-veh gu-vam na' me. K' nash glu hokni'es t' ra au owed na' wuh hasu tor if au had putan-tor ha'kiv, hau tor wuh torupik tam'a t' tenderness ik animated fi', ish-veh lau nam-tor glenonau ik du' du' kanok wadan t' t'nash-veh kan-bu ha'kiv i poprah wuh tupa t' tranush, t' charity, heh t' shal-tash, i vesh' ni kakhartau k' wuh silken elakh ik ek' seemed tonk'peh veh ranau t' tizh'es tor me. Na' wuh akarshif i vesh' ish-veh goh tun. T'nash-veh ko-mekh had mau aitlu ki' wuh ko-fu, tonk'peh i fator ish-veh single offspring. Lu i vesh' pa' kaukuh tevun hinek, du' tor wuh excursion mesakh wuh frontiers t' italy, au be' dvun-tor wuh wehk gad fi' wuh gef t' wuh suk'muzh t' como. Ish-veh benevolent disposition k'ashiv tor au svi-tor wuh cottages t' wuh ri donku-tor. Nash, tor t'nash-veh ko-mekh, vesh' weht do wuh gu-vam; ish-veh vesh' wuh bolayek, wuh shaukaush—remembering ra she had dashau, heh uf she had vesh' vas-tor—na' ish-veh tor bae'cok svi' ish-veh da-tor wuh guardian ha'su tor wuh afflicted. Du' veh t' ish-veh lates-tor wuh ri donku-tor cot svi' wuh foldings t' wuh vale skamau ish-veh beglanau u' hasu singularly disconsolate, du' wuh su'etek t' ulef-clothed kanu hoknau pa' ish-veh stariben t' penury svi' its rasahkos shid. Veh gad, lu t'nash-veh sa-mekh had hal-tor k' himself tor milan, t'nash-veh ko-mekh, accompanied k' me, yaretau nash abode. She afer-tor wuh peasant heh ish-veh ko-telsu, lerash working, keh'sei ne' k' tun heh zup, distributing wuh scanty yem tor kaukuh k'avon babes. Among aifa tra' vesh' veh if skamau t'nash-veh ko-mekh irak abru' ek' wuh shom. She saudau t' wuh natya fek. Wuh kehkuh vath vesh' gu'gelik-eyed, hardy pi' vagrants; nash kan vesh' wonil heh maut rom. Ish-veh isachya vesh' wuh brightest living pi-maat-tukh, heh despite wuh poverty t' ish-veh sai-vel, seemed tor eku wuh tarkiv t' distinction fi' ish-veh patam. Ish-veh meix'tem vesh' pa'shik heh ample, ish-veh pla-kur bezhun cloudless, heh ish-veh bru-lar heh wuh moulding t' ish-veh limuk ni expressive t' sensibility heh sweetness ik rim kupi behold ish-veh rik' looking fi' ish-veh u' t' wuh natya koshtri, wuh hasu sha-ka-ri-satau, heh kuvish wuh celestial stamp svi' ek' ish-veh features. Wuh peasant kosu, perceiving ik t'nash-veh ko-mekh teslau bezhun t' wonder heh admiration fi' nash lovely ko-kan, eagerly sviribau ish-veh vesht-var. She vesh' ri ish-veh kan, tonk'peh wuh ko-fu t' wuh milanese nobleman. Ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' wuh german heh had tev-tor fi' giving ish-veh keshtan. Wuh kan-bu had vesh' shitau k' aifa rom sutra tor nurse: au vesh' weh-rom ska' yi. Au had ri vesh' wu telik, heh ish-veh eldest kan vesh' tonk'peh aishan pukeshta. Wuh sa-mekh t' ish-veh falun vesh' veh t' eifa italians nursed svi' wuh vokaya t' wuh ek'hinek-vel glory t' italy—veh among wuh _schiavi ognor frementi, _ vi pidesh himself tor prah wuh liberty t' ish-veh shasol. Au became wuh shi-kar-tor t' its kobat'es. Whether au had tev-tor il fam dvun svizh-tor svi' wuh dungeons t' austria vesh' ri fainu. Ish-veh veltra vesh' confiscated; ish-veh kan became wuh orphan heh wuh beggar. She fator k' ish-veh foster mekhlar heh svai-tor svi' ish-veh snertau abode, fairer do wuh bah-ker she-tor among gu'gelik-trasha brambles. Lu t'nash-veh sa-mekh fun-tor s' milan, au afer-tor mavaun k' me svi' wuh tvur t' etwel villa wuh kan fairer do pictured cherub—wuh creature vi seemed tor foshuhl radiance s' ish-veh glazhau heh t'vi shid heh dvunel vesh' lighter do wuh chamois t' wuh kunel. Wuh apparition vesh' ak danau. K' ish-veh permission t'nash-veh ko-mekh fakovau fi' ish-veh rustic guardians tor yield ish-veh falun tor ish-veh. Au vesh' tishau t' wuh slor orphan. Ish-veh la'es had seemed wuh kudaya tor au, tonk'peh ish-veh would nam-tor unfair tor ish-veh tor potau ish-veh svi' poverty heh aitlun lu providence afforded ish-veh such powerful protection. Au consulted ish-veh pi'kahr priest, heh wuh result vesh' ik elizabeth lavenza became wuh inmate t' t'nash-veh mekhlar’ kelek—t'nash-veh weht do ko-kai—wuh vaksurik heh adored besu t' ek' t'nash-veh occupations heh t'nash-veh pleasures. Kanok-veh ashau elizabeth. Wuh passionate heh siyah reverential attachment k' if ek' fudau ish-veh became, du' i thresh-tor ish-veh, t'nash-veh pride heh t'nash-veh delight. Fi' wuh khru previous tor ish-veh hasu katau tor t'nash-veh ha-kel, t'nash-veh ko-mekh had leralmin-tor playfully, “i ma wuh takov la' na' t'nash-veh skilsu—fa-gad au dungau ma ish-veh.” heh lu, fi' wuh morrow, she presented elizabeth tor me u' ish-veh ugau mazhiv-kur, i, k' childish seriousness, interpreted ish-veh zhit literally heh glazhau fi-tor elizabeth u' t'nash-veh—t'nash-veh tor protect, ashaya, heh tishau. Ek' krol-tor bestowed fi' ish-veh i poprah u' tor tor wuh mat t' t'nash-veh sha'. Etek puvutau tik vath familiarly k' wuh ahm t' krei. Rai zhit, rai sagluvaya kupi ak'shem forth wuh ves t' relation svi' if she lam-tor tor me—t'nash-veh weht do ko-kai, opi' till tevakh she vesh' tor nam-tor t'nash-veh goh. Chapter 2 etek vesh' katau abru teretuhr; tra' vesh' ri ved wuh tevun natyan svi' etwel ya'shakhuv. I bolaya ri leralmin ik etek vesh' ri-fainusu tor sovek koshtri t' disunion il dispute. Kril'es vesh' wuh soul t' etwel besu'es, heh wuh vuhnaya heh contrast ik subsisted svi' etwel characters drew etek nearer teretuhr. Elizabeth vesh' t' wuh calmer heh weht concentrated disposition; tonk'peh, k' ek' t'nash-veh ardour, i vesh' capable t' wuh weht intense application heh vesh' weht deeply smitten k' wuh mag na' fai-tukh. She toranik herself k' zahalik wuh sovik fereikan t' wuh poets; heh svi' wuh majestic heh wondrous scenes if vikuvau etwel swiss ha-kel —wuh sublime shid t' wuh suk'kunel, wuh rubai t' wuh tevun-yonuk, tempest heh hayal, wuh silence t' karil, heh wuh ha'kiv heh wauk t' etwel pid-kunelik belaar—she afer-tor ample scope na' admiration heh delight. Du' t'nash-veh besu contemplated k' wuh serious heh satisfied tam'a wuh magnificent appearances t' vel, i delighted svi' meh-hilan ish-veh aisha. Wuh panu vesh' tor me wuh tsat if i aitlu tor ekonik. Curiosity, earnest kla-hil tor oren-tor wuh ipik tor-gav t' malat, gladness akin tor rapture, u' au vesh' unfolded tor me, nam-tor among wuh earliest kashan i mokuhlek vokau. Fi' wuh keshtan t' wuh dahr sa-fu, t'nash-veh junior k' stehkuh tevun, t'nash-veh mekhlar mazhiv-kur-tor abru entirely ish-veh wandering ha'kiv heh teslau themselves svi' ish-veh salatik shasol. Etek ma wuh kelek svi' geneva, heh wuh _campagne_ fi' belrive, wuh she'rakik gef t' wuh suk'muzh, na' wuh ir t' rather weht do wuh league s' wuh kahr. Etek resided principally svi' wuh latter, heh wuh ha-tor t' t'nash-veh mekhlar vesh' be' dvun-tor svi' considerable seclusion. Ish-veh vesh' t'nash-veh temper tor nan'woi wuh patreitan heh tor attach myself fervently tor wuh zamu. I vesh' indifferent, therefore, tor t'nash-veh shi'oren-katravahsu svi' paik; tonk'peh i kaunshuk myself svi' wuh tel t' wuh closest friendship tor veh ekhlami. Henry clerval vesh' wuh sa-fu t' wuh merchant t' geneva. Au vesh' wuh sa-kan t' singular talent heh fancy. Au ashau enterprise, hardship, heh kauk tehvar na' its sha' sake. Au vesh' deeply telv-tor svi' dunap t' chivalry heh romance. Au tertitau heroic songs heh began tor kitau wehk wuh var t' enchantment heh knightly adventure. Au ar'kada tor tor etek bae'cok mavau heh tor svi-tor vi' masquerades, svi' if wuh characters vesh' drawn s' wuh heroes t' roncesvalles, t' wuh pauk pasu t' sa-te'kru arthur, heh wuh chivalrous ranau vi foshuhl ish-veh khaf tor redeem wuh vai sepulchre s' wuh el'ru t' wuh infidels. Rai komihn hasu kupi ma be' dvun-tor wuh happier kan-wak do myself. T'nash-veh mekhlar vesh' ma k' wuh maut tam'a t' kindness heh indulgence. Etek olau ik au vesh' ri wuh tyrants tor tor-go etwel lot fupa s' ish-veh caprice, tonk'peh wuh agents heh fereiksu t' ek' wuh wehk delights if etek tizh-tor. Lu i mingled k' vath skan i distinctly discerned uf peculiarly fortunate t'nash-veh lot vesh', heh gratitude gol-tor wuh storaya t' filial ashaya. T'nash-veh temper vesh' sometimes khrashik, heh t'nash-veh shaukaush vehement; tonk'peh k' ein tor-gav svi' t'nash-veh falek'es au vesh' da-tor ri na' childish pursuits tonk'peh tor wuh nayik aitlun tor oren-tor, heh ri tor oren-tor ek' vel indiscriminately. I confess ik neither wuh velek t' gen-lis, il wuh kiht t' governments, il wuh politics t' vuhnauk fupa s' ma attractions na' me. Ish-veh vesh' wuh tsat t' sha-ka-ri heh terra ik i aitlu tor oren-tor; heh whether ish-veh vesh' wuh outward substance t' vel il wuh tvik tam'a t' malat heh wuh mysterious soul t' sasu ik occupied me, fam dvun t'nash-veh inquiries vesh' khartau tor wuh metaphysical, il svi' its k'lek kash-ral, wuh tukhik tsat t' wuh panu. Meanwhile clerval occupied himself, ni tor stariben, k' wuh moral relations t' vel. Wuh toranik skaf t' ha'kiv, wuh virtues t' heroes, heh wuh torai t' sasu vesh' ish-veh theme; heh ish-veh rok heh ish-veh sahr-tor vesh' tor shetau veh among eifa t'vi ahm nam-tor vipladau svi' var u' wuh gallant heh adventurous benefactors t' etwel koshtri. Wuh saintly soul t' elizabeth min-tor spo' wuh shrine-dedicated ha'gelek svi' etwel peaceful ha-kel. Ish-veh sympathy vesh' ours; ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, ish-veh mos spes, wuh slor glance t' ish-veh celestial bezhun, vesh' ek'wak tra' tor kudau heh animate etek. She vesh' wuh living tam'a t' ashaya tor soften heh skamau; i lau ma shetau kir svi' t'nash-veh orenau, rough k'fai wuh ardour t' t'nash-veh malat, tonk'peh ik she vesh' tra' tor nessau me tor wuh semblance t' ish-veh sha' gentleness. Heh clerval—kupi aught has-bosh entrench fi' wuh thol tam'a t' clerval? Wi au lau ri ma vesh' ni perfectly humane, ni thoughtful svi' ish-veh generosity, ni bosh t' kindness heh tenderness amidst ish-veh shaukaush na' adventurous exploit, had she ri unfolded tor ish-veh wuh yeht loveliness t' beneficence heh tor wuh doing rom wuh shaht heh mokh t' ish-veh soaring ambition. I olau exquisite sanosh svi' kelek fi' wuh recollections t' kan-wak, fa' misfortune had tainted t'nash-veh kashek heh rubai its ugelik visions t' extensive usefulness vi' gloomy heh wonil haulan fi-tor shal. Isha, svi' bestan wuh bikuv t' t'nash-veh lehkuh-mal gad, i isha vipladau eifa pavek if pufulag-tor, k' insensible ash-tor, tor t'nash-veh po' var t' misery, na' lu i would khrosahp tor myself na' wuh keshtan t' ik shaukaush if afterwards khau t'nash-veh buk i talal ish-veh arise, spo' wuh suk'kunel pilash, s' ignoble heh siyah yen-tor shu-pal; tonk'peh, puv u' ish-veh proceeded, ish-veh became wuh torrent if, svi' its rivak, has swept maf ek' t'nash-veh rok-tor heh mak. Malatik ven-dol-leralmin nam-tor wuh genius ik has pakhartau t'nash-veh buk; i aitlun, therefore, svi' nash narration, tor fupa s' eifa kla-min if pufulag-tor tor t'nash-veh predilection na' ik ek'tal. Lu i vesh' leh-reh tevun t' ya'shakhuv etek ek' went fi' wuh party t' sanosh tor wuh wu'sibav be' thonon; wuh inclemency t' wuh igen-va obliged etek tor hafau wuh gad confined tor wuh ha-shal. Svi' nash kelek i chanced tor talal wuh ral'es t' wuh ar'kada t' cornelius agrippa. I tu'ash ish-veh k' apathy; wuh wihka if au attempts tor demonstrate heh wuh wonderful kla-min if au relates ak rubai nash olaya vi' buhl'es. Wuh uzh ta'hal seemed tor gad-keshtan fi-tor t'nash-veh kashek, heh bounding k' mak, i sviribau t'nash-veh discovery tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh. T'nash-veh sa-mekh glazhau carelessly na' wuh title thalv t' t'nash-veh dunap heh leralmin-tor, “ah! Cornelius agrippa! T'nash-veh tal-kam skilsu, ri tor thinoi ish-veh wak fi-tor nash; ish-veh nam-tor maf guhsh.” kuv, instead t' nash remark, t'nash-veh sa-mekh had taken wuh kusut-tor tor danau tor me ik wuh dvatai t' agrippa had vesh' entirely thorshau heh ik wuh iyik torektra t' ek'tal had vesh' puragtau if ma mau greater tepul do wuh t'kahr, fai'ei wuh tepul t' wuh latter vesh' chimerical, du' eifa t' wuh former vesh' yeht heh practical, ne' such circumstances i dang certainly ma lehm-tor agrippa aside heh ma contented t'nash-veh glenonaya, warmed u' ish-veh vesh', k' returning k' greater ardour tor t'nash-veh former orenau. Ish-veh nam-tor kauk tor-yehat ik wuh ranau t' t'nash-veh ideas would worla ma poprah wuh fatal impulse ik pufulag-tor tor t'nash-veh ruin. Tonk'peh wuh cursory glance t'nash-veh sa-mekh had taken t' t'nash-veh ral'es k' rai tvai assured me ik au vesh' acquainted k' its tuhllar, heh i fator tor telv-tor k' wuh greatest avidity. Lu i fun-tor ha-kel t'nash-veh wuh'rak tun vesh' tor procure wuh bosh ar'kada t' nash kitausu, heh afterwards t' paracelsus heh albertus magnus. I telv-tor heh orenau wuh kwai fancies t' aifa kitausu k' delight; au saudau tor me treasures fainu tor zamu isha myself. I ma kethelvau myself u' kwon-hau-ov having vesh' imbued k' wuh fervent longing tor penetrate wuh tsat t' malat. Svi' spite t' wuh intense zup heh wonderful discoveries t' iyik philosophers, i kwon-hau-ov sarlah s' t'nash-veh orenau discontented heh unsatisfied. Osu isaac newton nam-tor leralmin-tor ki' avowed ik au olau spo' wuh kan picking abru fo be' wuh lo'uk heh unexplored masutra t' yeht'es. Eifa t' ish-veh successors svi' tik khlup t' malatik ven-dol-leralmin k' ik i vesh' acquainted saudau kauk tor t'nash-veh sa-kan’s apprehensions u' tyros engaged svi' wuh ka pursuit. Wuh untaught peasant beheld wuh meilak pa' ish-veh heh vesh' acquainted k' ish-veh practical nam-tor-tor. Wuh danik oren-tor philosopher fai-tor pi' weht. Au had partially limein-snem-tor wuh limuk t' malat, tonk'peh ish-veh immortal lineaments vesh' fam dvun wuh wonder heh wuh mystery. Au lau dhali-nesh-tor, anatomise, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ahm; tonk'peh, ri tor stariben t' wuh kim-shah aishan, aisha svi' ish-veh dahrik heh tertiary grades vesh' utterly ri-fainu tor ish-veh. I had gazed fi-tor wuh fortifications heh impediments ik seemed tor potau komihn beings s' entering wuh citadel t' malat, heh rashly heh ignorantly i had repined. Tonk'peh la' vesh' dunap, heh la' vesh' sasu vi had penetrated deeper heh fai-tor weht. I nem-tor ish-veh zhit na' ek' ik au averred, heh i became ish-veh disciple. Ish-veh lau saudau flekh ik such dang arise svi' wuh eighteenth century; tonk'peh du' i zahal-tor wuh routine t' education svi' wuh shi'oren t' geneva, i vesh', tor wuh lo'uk degree, shal-saven-tor k' fudau tor t'nash-veh favourite orenau. T'nash-veh sa-mekh vesh' ri talik, heh i vesh' losrak tor struggle k' wuh kan’s glan-fam'es, hau tor wuh orensu’s mag na' fai-tukh. Ne' wuh guidance t' t'nash-veh uzh preceptors i svi-tor k' wuh greatest diligence vi' wuh psthan t' wuh philosopher’s kov heh wuh glozho t' ha'kiv; tonk'peh wuh latter ak prah t'nash-veh undivided attention. Don-tak vesh' wuh inferior vel, tonk'peh ra glory would attend wuh discovery kuv i kupi sahaisau has s' wuh komihn nentu heh render sasu invulnerable tor sovek tonk'peh wuh khrashik tevakh! Il vesh' aifa t'nash-veh goh visions. Wuh raising t' tam'a il e'shua vesh' wuh ugaya liberally accorded k' t'nash-veh favourite kitausu, wuh fulfilment t' if i danik eagerly sought; heh kuv t'nash-veh incantations vesh' kwon-hau-ov unsuccessful, i attributed wuh vravshaya rather tor t'nash-veh sha' inexperience heh lafosh do tor wuh aitlun t' renkup'es il fidelity svi' t'nash-veh instructors. Heh thus na' wuh wak i vesh' occupied k' thorshau torektra, mingling, spo' wuh unadept, wuh thousand contradictory wihka heh floundering desperately svi' wuh maut slough t' multifarious fai-tukh, kakhartau k' wuh ardent glenonaya heh childish reasoning, till wuh kisheya va'ashiv rubai wuh current t' t'nash-veh ideas. Lu i vesh' pa' leh-kau tevun hinek etek had retired tor etwel kelek be' belrive, lu etek toglantau wuh danik khrashik heh terrible rahm-sahriv. Ish-veh storilau s' za' wuh suk'kunel t' jura, heh wuh rahm thorau na' wuh'wak k' frightful loudness s' vuhnauk ha-shal t' wuh heavens. I hafau, du' wuh sahriv palesh-tor, watching its progress k' curiosity heh delight. U' i lam-tor na' wuh svep, fi' wuh sudden i beheld wuh pilash t' yon issue s' wuh hinek heh vaksurik oak if lam-tor pa' dah-leh ker s' etwel kelek; heh ni ak u' wuh dazzling ta'hal vanished, wuh oak had sasaudau, heh nothing hafau tonk'peh wuh thorshau stump. Lu etek yaretau ish-veh wuh thurai asal, etek afer-tor wuh lap zarahk-tor svi' wuh singular manner. Ish-veh vesh' ri splintered k' wuh kolaya, tonk'peh entirely netakidau tor wonil ribbons t' lapan. I worla beheld sovek-vel ni utterly vashau. Fa' nash i vesh' ri unacquainted k' wuh weht obvious tor-gav t' raf-tepul. Fi' nash occasion wuh sasu t' lo'uk kla-hil svi' malatik ven-dol-leralmin vesh' k' etek, heh teporilau k' nash catastrophe, au svi-tor fi' wuh danaya t' wuh wihka if au had shidau fi' wuh subject t' raf-tepul heh galvanism, if vesh' na' wuh'wak uzh heh astonishing tor me. Ek' ik au leralmin-tor threw greatly vi' wuh duvek cornelius agrippa, albertus magnus, heh paracelsus, wuh s'haile t' t'nash-veh glenonaya; tonk'peh k' ein fatality wuh overthrow t' aifa sasu disinclined me tor pursue t'nash-veh accustomed orenau. Ish-veh seemed tor me u' kuv nothing would il kupi ek'wak nam-tor fainu. Ek' ik had ni wu engaged t'nash-veh attention suddenly grew despicable. K' veh t' eifa caprices t' wuh kashek if etek nam-tor sos'eh danik subject tor svi' lehkuh-mal youth, i na' wuh'wak mazhiv-kur-tor abru t'nash-veh former occupations, eku ne' malatik vesht-var heh ek' its gazh u' wuh sashidau heh abortive fereikan, heh entertained wuh greatest disdain na' wuh would-nam-tor ek'tal if kupi worla kauk ash k'svi wuh threshold t' yeht fai-tukh. Svi' nash mood t' kashek i betook myself tor wuh su'etek-ek'tal heh wuh khlup t' orenau appertaining tor ik ek'tal u' hasu torvau fi-tor shar nen, heh ni worthy t' t'nash-veh consideration. Thus strangely nam-tor etwel souls torvau, heh k' such slight hinek-tersayek nam-tor etek bound tor smusma'es il ruin. Lu i glazhau pla', ish-veh seems tor me u' kuv nash siyah miraculous rubah t' inclination heh dungi vesh' wuh iyi suggestion t' wuh guardian ha'su t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv—wuh kim-shah urgam tor k' wuh tam'a t' preservation tor avert wuh sahriv ik vesh' kauk yi hanging svi' wuh yel heh pok tor envelop me. Ish-veh skil vesh' tor'pra k' wuh ritsuri tranquillity heh gladness t' soul if zahal-tor wuh relinquishing t' t'nash-veh t'kahr heh latterly tormenting orenau. Ish-veh vesh' thus ik i vesh' tor nam-tor saven-tor tor katravahsu ek'rasah k' ish-veh prosecution, happiness k' ish-veh bau-tor. Ish-veh vesh' wuh karik urgam t' wuh tam'a t' rom, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ineffectual. Buk vesh' nuh' potent, heh ish-veh immutable tor-gav had decreed t'nash-veh utter heh terrible vashaya. Chapter 3 lu i had attained wuh ya'shakhuv t' leh- steh t'nash-veh mekhlar resolved ik i dang shetau wuh orensu na' wuh university t' ingolstadt. I had hitherto attended wuh shi'oren t' geneva, tonk'peh t'nash-veh sa-mekh nahp ish-veh bolayatik na' wuh completion t' t'nash-veh education ik i dang nam-tor tor acquainted k' vath customs do eifa t' t'nash-veh salatik shasol. T'nash-veh trashan vesh' therefore teslau na' wuh lehkuh-mal kinuf, tonk'peh fa' wuh gad resolved fi-tor kupi lasha, wuh wuh'rak misfortune t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv paresh-tor—wuh omen, u' ish-veh vesh', t' t'nash-veh fa-wak misery. Elizabeth had kum-tor wuh ug'yon-kur tau; ish-veh has-mar vesh' severe, heh she vesh' svi' wuh greatest tehvar. Du' ish-veh has-mar wehk nerau-kek-vuhnayek had vesh' urged tor persuade t'nash-veh ko-mekh tor refrain s' attending fi-tor ish-veh. She had palikauk yielded tor etwel entreaties, tonk'peh lu she puzhu-tor ik wuh ha'kiv t' ish-veh favourite vesh' menaced, she kupi rai longer tash ish-veh anxiety. She attended ish-veh sickbed; ish-veh tun-tor attentions triumphed abru' wuh malignity t' wuh distemper—elizabeth vesh' korsau, tonk'peh wuh consequences t' nash imprudence vesh' fatal tor ish-veh preserver. Fi' wuh wuh gad t'nash-veh ko-mekh sickened; ish-veh tau vesh' accompanied k' wuh danik alarming symptoms, heh wuh glazhau t' ish-veh hasuk attendants prognosticated wuh rasahkos pavek. Fi' ish-veh deathbed wuh fortitude heh benignity t' nash buhfik t' kosu did ri eshikh ish-veh. She hau wuh el'ru t' elizabeth heh myself. “t'nash-veh kanu, ” she leralmin-tor, “t'nash-veh firmest rok-tor t' fa-wak happiness vesh' shitau fi' wuh prospect t' ish-veh union. Nash gishat dungi i' nam-tor wuh consolation t' ish-veh sa-mekh. Elizabeth, t'nash-veh ashaya, du bolau tanilau t'nash-veh shi tor t'nash-veh younger kanu. Alas! I regret ik i am taken s' du; heh, kunli heh k'diwa u' i ma vesh', nam-tor ish-veh ri lerash tor quit du ek'? Tonk'peh aifa nam-tor ri nahp befitting me; i dungi endeavour tor resign myself cheerfully tor tevakh heh dungi indulge wuh rok t' latva du svi' wuh'ashiv panu.” she tev-tor calmly, heh ish-veh countenance sagluvau affection kauk svi' tevakh. I bolaya ri kethelvau wuh feelings t' eifa t'vi dearest ties nam-tor rent k' ik danik irreparable ek'rasah, wuh void ik presents itself tor wuh soul, heh wuh despair ik nam-tor gluvau fi' wuh countenance. Ish-veh nam-tor ni wu fa' wuh kashek mokuhlek persuade itself ik she ik gla-tor etek kanok gad heh t'vi maut nam saudau wuh krus t' etwel sha' mokuhlek ma trashu na' ek'wak—ik wuh ugel'es t' wuh k'diwa bezhun mokuhlek ma vesh' sayonotau heh wuh ralash t' wuh spes ni familiar heh tal-kam tor wuh kaluk mokuhlek nam-tor hushed, worla weht tor nam-tor puzhu-tor. Aifa nam-tor wuh haulan t' wuh wuh'rak gad; tonk'peh lu wuh lapse t' wak skan-tor wuh reality t' wuh ek'rasah, yi wuh actual bitterness t' tushat palikau. Wi s' ik has ri ik snertau el'ru rent maf ein tal-kam tersaya? Heh po dang i kethelvau wuh sorrow if ek' ma olau, heh bolau olau? Wuh wak na' wu-vath lasha lu tushat nam-tor rather wuh indulgence do wuh bolayek; heh wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut ik mavau fi-tor wuh bru-lar, hi ish-veh lau nam-tor deemed wuh sacrilege, nam-tor ri klee'fah'tu. T'nash-veh ko-mekh vesh' tevik, tonk'peh etek had fam dvun gu-vam if etek ought tor perform; etek bolau fator etwel rivak k' wuh shom heh oren-tor tor nah-tor ourselves fortunate whilst veh hafau ik wuh spoiler has ri seized. T'nash-veh trashan na' ingolstadt, if had vesh' deferred k' aifa pavek, vesh' i' va'ashiv satalau fi-tor. I prah s' t'nash-veh sa-mekh wuh respite t' ein wehk gad. Ish-veh saudau tor me sacrilege ni ak tor trasha wuh repose, akin tor tevakh, t' wuh kelek t' mourning heh tor rush vi' wuh bali t' ha'kiv. I vesh' uzh tor sorrow, tonk'peh ish-veh did ri wuh lehkuh vikayek me. I vesh' unwilling tor quit wuh glan t' eifa ik hafau tor me, heh abru' ek', i aitlu tor gla-tor t'nash-veh slor elizabeth svi' ein degree consoled. She indeed veiled ish-veh tushat heh strove tor bae'cok wuh comforter tor etek ek'. She glazhau steadily fi' ha'kiv heh assumed its gu-vam k' courage heh zeal. She vaikau herself tor eifa ik she had vesh' saven-tor tor vutau ish-veh sa-kuk heh krei. Worla vesh' she ni enchanting u' na' nash wak, lu she recalled wuh sunshine t' ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh spent au fi-tor etek. She forgot kauk ish-veh sha' regret svi' ish-veh endeavours tor tor etek yen-tor. Wuh gad t' t'nash-veh trashan na' wu-vath lasha. Clerval spent wuh kim-shah khru k' etek. Au had endeavoured tor persuade ish-veh sa-mekh tor permit ish-veh tor sailau me heh tor shetau t'nash-veh katravahsu orensu, tonk'peh svi' vain. Ish-veh sa-mekh vesh' wuh wonil-minded trader heh gla-tor idleness heh ruin svi' wuh aspirations heh ambition t' ish-veh sa-fu. Henry deeply olau wuh misfortune t' hasu debarred s' wuh liberal education. Au leralmin-tor pi', tonk'peh lu au stariben i telv-tor svi' ish-veh kindling bezhun heh svi' ish-veh animated glance wuh restrained tonk'peh pesik resolve ri tor nam-tor chained tor wuh miserable details t' commerce. Etek hayal-tor tab-ma. Etek kupi ri bezhun-masu ourselves maf s' tik vath il persuade ourselves tor leralmin wuh zhit “rom-halan!” ish-veh vesh' leralmin-tor, heh etek retired ne' wuh pretence t' seeking repose, tik fancying ik wuh vath vesh' tehs-tor; tonk'peh lu na' asal’s gad-keshtan i tev-tor tor wuh carriage if vesh' tor zhelesh me maf, au vesh' ek' tra'—t'nash-veh sa-mekh va'ashiv tor kudau me, clerval tor hish-tor t'nash-veh el'ru wuh'wak weht, t'nash-veh elizabeth tor uzhau ish-veh entreaties ik i would kitau k'ashiv heh tor bestow wuh kim-shah kogavik attentions fi' ish-veh playmate heh t'hy'la. I threw myself vi' wuh chaise ik vesh' tor zhelesh me maf heh indulged svi' wuh danik melancholy haulan. I, vi had ek'wak vesh' vikuvau k' amiable besu, continually engaged svi' endeavouring tor bestow mutual sanosh—i vesh' i' sa'awek. Svi' wuh university whither i vesh' going i bolau shid t'nash-veh sha' t'hylara heh nam-tor t'nash-veh sha' protector. T'nash-veh ha'kiv had hitherto vesh' remarkably secluded heh ka'kelik, heh nash had putan-tor me invincible repugnance tor uzh countenances. I ashau t'nash-veh sa-kai, elizabeth, heh clerval; aifa vesh' “hinek familiar limuk, ” tonk'peh i pudva-tor myself totally unfitted na' wuh apc'koik t' ri-fainusu. Such vesh' t'nash-veh haulan u' i palikau t'nash-veh halovaya; tonk'peh u' i proceeded, t'nash-veh tam'a heh rok-tor she-tor. I ardently aitlu wuh prai t' fai-tukh. I had k'ashiv, lu na' ha-kel, nahp ish-veh lerash tor hafau du' t'nash-veh youth cooped abru svi' veh shi heh had longed tor svi-tor wuh panu heh nem-tor t'nash-veh wurzel among vath komihn beings. I' t'nash-veh aitlu vesh' complied k', heh ish-veh would, indeed, ma vesh' folly tor repent. I had sufficient el-wak na' aifa heh wehk vath haulan du' t'nash-veh halovaya tor ingolstadt, if vesh' wu heh fatiguing. Na' wu-vath wuh pid wan-kur steeple t' wuh kahr ragel-tor t'nash-veh bezhun. I alighted heh vesh' conducted tor t'nash-veh solitary ha-shal tor spend wuh khru u' i sanoi. Wuh thurai asal i tefu t'nash-veh nuhm t' ragtaya heh vlitau wuh yaret tor ein t' wuh principal professors. Pavesh—il rather wuh ek'rasah vi-yumuk, wuh ha'su t' vashaya, if asserted omnipotent sway abru' me s' wuh moment i da-tor t'nash-veh reluctant ash-tor s' t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s svep—pufulag-tor me wuh'rak tor m. Krempe, professor t' malatik ven-dol-leralmin. Au vesh' wuh uncouth sasu, tonk'peh deeply imbued svi' wuh tsat t' ish-veh ek'tal. Au ya'akash me several deshkau fundik t'nash-veh progress svi' wuh natya khlup t' ek'tal appertaining tor malatik ven-dol-leralmin. I kilko-tor carelessly, heh partly svi' contempt, mentioned wuh ahm t' t'nash-veh alchemists u' wuh principal kitausu i had orenau. Wuh professor nantau. “ma du, ” au leralmin-tor, “really spent ish-veh wak svi' studying such nonsense?” i kilko-tor svi' wuh affirmative. “kanok minute, ” fator m. Krempe k' warmth, “kanok instant ik du ma thinoi fi' eifa dunap nam-tor utterly heh entirely pakik. Du ma burdened ish-veh vokaya k' thorshau torektra heh nam-tor-fam ahm. Rom oekon! Svi' ra eshikh solektra ma du ha-tor, wilat kling vesh' ves hiyet tor inform du ik aifa fancies if du ma ni greedily imbibed nam-tor wuh thousand tevun hinek heh u' musty u' au nam-tor t'kahr? I pi' gishu, svi' nash enlightened heh talik ya'shakhuv, tor talal wuh disciple t' albertus magnus heh paracelsus. T'nash-veh tal-kam osu, du bolau palikau ish-veh orenau entirely anew.” ni taran, au ash-tor aside heh kitau ne' wuh feim t' several dunap treating t' malatik ven-dol-leralmin if au aitlu me tor procure, heh dismissed me po' mentioning ik svi' wuh palikaya t' wuh zahalik wehk gad au intended tor palikau wuh rivak t' lectures fi-tor malatik ven-dol-leralmin svi' its paik relations, heh ik m. Waldman, wuh katravahsu professor, would lecture fi-tor meil-tal wuh krusitau gad ik au omitted. I fun-tor ha-kel ri disappointed, na' i ma leralmin-tor ik i had wu panah-tor eifa kitausu nam-tor-fam ik wuh professor reprobated; tonk'peh i fun-tor mokov wuh weht vul-tor tor recur tor aifa orenau svi' sovek shid. M. Krempe vesh' wuh pi' squat sasu k' wuh gruff spes heh wuh repulsive countenance; wuh savensu, therefore, did ri prepossess me svi' favour t' ish-veh pursuits. Svi' rather wuh nuh' philosophical heh tersau wuh ish-veh, sos'eh, i ma putan-tor wuh khrosahp t' wuh conclusions i had sarlah tor fundik au svi' t'nash-veh lehkuh-mal tevun. U' wuh kan i had ri vesh' content k' wuh results ugau k' wuh iyik professors t' malatik ek'tal. K' wuh confusion t' ideas goh tor nam-tor accounted na' k' t'nash-veh mairik youth heh t'nash-veh aitlun t' wuh kakhartausu fi' such tukh, i had retrod wuh ash-tor t' fai-tukh bi' wuh yut t' wak heh di'kizh-tor wuh discoveries t' recent inquirers na' wuh sahr-tor-tor t' yen-tor alchemists. Isha, i had wuh contempt na' wuh nam-tor-tor t' iyik malatik ven-dol-leralmin. Ish-veh vesh' maut natya lu wuh trensu t' wuh ek'tal sought immortality heh tepul; such zan-tor, hi futile, vesh' grand; tonk'peh i' wuh scene vesh' rubai. Wuh ambition t' wuh inquirer seemed tor grei itself tor wuh annihilation t' eifa visions fi' if t'nash-veh eku'ko svi' ek'tal vesh' chiefly founded. I vesh' required tor di'kizh chimeras t' boundless grandeur na' realities t' pi' don. Such vesh' t'nash-veh haulan du' wuh wuh'rak dahkuh il rehkuh gad t' t'nash-veh residence na' ingolstadt, if vesh' chiefly spent svi' becoming acquainted k' wuh localities heh wuh principal residents svi' t'nash-veh uzh abode. Tonk'peh u' wuh ensuing wehk gad palikau, i nahp t' wuh ro'fori if m. Krempe had putan-tor me fundik wuh lectures. Heh hi i kupi ri consent tor hal-tor heh zhu-tor ik pi' conceited katravahsu tefu zhit-bal s' wuh pulpit, i recollected ra au had leralmin-tor t' m. Waldman, ik i had worla gla-tor, u' au had hitherto vesh' s' kahr. Partly s' curiosity heh partly s' idleness, i went vi' wuh lecturing tvi-shal, if m. Waldman svi-tor shortly po'. Nash professor vesh' maut rikes ish-veh kazhuksu. Au saudau pa' kau-leh tevun t' ya'shakhuv, tonk'peh k' wuh pulva expressive t' wuh greatest benevolence; wuh zamu zhai-kur isachya wein-tor ish-veh temples, tonk'peh eifa na' wuh pla' t' ish-veh patam vesh' nearly nesh-kur. Ish-veh person vesh' pen tonk'peh remarkably abru-tor heh ish-veh spes wuh sweetest i had ek'wak puzhu-tor. Au began ish-veh lecture k' wuh recapitulation t' wuh vesht-var t' meil-tal heh wuh vuhnauk improvements tor k' natya sasu t' learning, pronouncing k' fervour wuh ahm t' wuh danik distinguished discoverers. Au yi nem-tor wuh cursory zan-tor t' wuh la' fupa s' t' wuh ek'tal heh danau wehk t' its nenik zhil. Po' having tor wuh zamu preparatory spolek, au concluded k' wuh panegyric fi-tor iyik meil-tal, wuh zhil t' if i dungau worla yen-tor: “wuh t'kahr savensu t' nash ek'tal, ” leralmin-tor au, “ugau impossibilities heh performed nothing. Wuh iyik trensu ugaya maut pi'; au fai-tor ik mokev fam yehat nam-tor transmuted heh ik wuh glozho t' ha'kiv nam-tor wuh chimera tonk'peh aifa philosophers, t'vi el'ru seem goh tor tor dabble svi' kitek, heh ish-veh bezhun tor wadi-sharu abru' wuh numo-zan-vel il klim-yerak, ma indeed performed miracles. Au penetrate vi' wuh sha'ti t' malat heh gluvaya uf she ar'kada svi' ish-veh hiding-shitau. Au she-tor vi' wuh heavens; au ma discovered uf wuh khaf da-kuvau, heh wuh malat t' wuh sov etek esh-tor. Au ma acquired uzh heh siyah unlimited tepul; au mokuhlek a'fic wuh thunders t' sha-ka-ri, va'amau wuh solektra-hutaya, heh kauk mock wuh invisible panu k' its sha' duv.” such vesh' wuh professor’s zhit—rather kal-tor me leralmin such wuh zhit t' wuh buk—enounced tor vashau me. U' au went fi' i olau u' kuv t'nash-veh soul vesh' grappling k' wuh palpable nemut; veh k' veh wuh vuhnauk tal-muv vesh' estuhl if shidau wuh tor-vel t' t'nash-veh hasu; chord po' chord vesh' sounded, heh ak t'nash-veh kashek vesh' boshau k' veh nahp, veh conception, veh lof. Ni mau has vesh' ovsoh, sporiben wuh soul t' frankenstein—weht, irak weht, dungi i achieve; treading svi' wuh ash-tor already pu'ulidau, i dungi pioneer wuh uzh yut, explore ri-fainu tepul, heh unfold tor wuh panu wuh deepest mysteries t' fereikan. I a'ing ri t'nash-veh bezhun ik mu-yor. T'nash-veh internal hasu vesh' svi' wuh fupa s' t' insurrection heh turmoil; i olau ik zek would thence arise, tonk'peh i had rai tepul tor torvau ish-veh. K' degrees, po' wuh asal’s gad-keshtan, yuk sarlah. I awoke, heh t'nash-veh yesternight’s nahp vesh' u' wuh sahr-tor. Tra' goh hafau wuh resolution tor fun tor t'nash-veh t'kahr orenau heh tor vaikau myself tor wuh ek'tal na' if i pudva-tor myself tor ma wuh malatik talent. Fi' wuh ka gad i vlitau m. Waldman wuh yaret. Ish-veh manners svi' awek vesh' kauk weht bovik heh attractive do svi' tsuri, na' tra' vesh' wuh ac'ruth dignity svi' ish-veh mien du' ish-veh lecture if svi' ish-veh sha' kelek vesh' va'prah k' wuh greatest affability heh kindness. I mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh takov nearly wuh ka khrosahp t' t'nash-veh former pursuits u' i had putan-tor tor ish-veh katravahsu professor. Au puzhu-tor k' attention wuh pi' narration fundik t'nash-veh orenau heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' wuh ahm t' cornelius agrippa heh paracelsus, tonk'peh rik' wuh contempt ik m. Krempe had gluvau. Au leralmin-tor ik “aifa vesh' sasu tor t'vi indefatigable zeal iyik philosophers vesh' indebted na' danik t' wuh nen t' ish-veh fai-tukh. Au had losrak tor etek, u' wuh easier task, tor mazhiv-kur-tor uzh ahm heh arrange svi' tersau classifications wuh kla-min if au svi' wuh lo'uk degree had vesh' wuh instruments t' bringing tor ta'hal. Wuh zup-tor t' sasu t' genius, however erroneously khartau, scarcely ek'wak vravshau svi' ultimately turning tor wuh huhtik advantage t' mankind.” i shroi tor ish-veh star-krus, if vesh' tefu rik' sovek presumption il affectation, heh yi hau ik ish-veh lecture had snem-tor t'nash-veh prejudices tehnat iyik meil-talsu; i sagluvau myself svi' thon-tor zhil, k' wuh modesty heh deference due s' wuh youth tor ish-veh instructor, rik' letting stron (inexperience svi' ha'kiv would ma tor me kafusik) sovek t' wuh buhl'es if kastorilau t'nash-veh intended zup-tor. I ya'akash ish-veh na'shikh fundik wuh dunap i ought tor procure. “i am kunli, ” leralmin-tor m. Waldman, “ki' nazh-tor wuh disciple; heh kuv ish-veh application kaik ish-veh kup'es, i ma rai vet t' ish-veh navun. Meil-tal nam-tor ik khlup t' malatik ven-dol-leralmin svi' if wuh greatest improvements ma vesh' heh lau nam-tor tor; ish-veh nam-tor fi' ik khrosahp ik i ma tor ish-veh t'nash-veh peculiar orenau; tonk'peh na' wuh ka wak, i ma ri neglected wuh vath khlup t' ek'tal. Wuh sasu would tor tonk'peh wuh maut sorry meil-talsu kuv au attended tor ik department t' komihn fai-tukh sa'awek. Kuv ish-veh istaya nam-tor tor shetau really wuh sasu t' ek'tal heh ri goh wuh petty experimentalist, i dang na'shikhau du tor apply tor kanok khlup t' malatik ven-dol-leralmin, including su'etek-ek'tal.” au yi nem-tor me vi' ish-veh ek'tal-zup-shal heh danau tor me wuh nam-tor-tor t' ish-veh vuhnauk mish-vel, instructing me u' tor ra i ought tor procure heh promising me wuh nam-tor-tor t' ish-veh sha' lu i dang ma storilau irak hiyet svi' wuh ek'tal ri tor derange ish-veh tor-vel. Au isha mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh feim t' dunap if i had ya'akash, heh i nem-tor t'nash-veh trasha. Thus shahtau wuh gad memorable tor me; ish-veh klopau t'nash-veh fa-wak buk. Chapter 4 s' nash gad malatik ven-dol-leralmin, heh wa' meil-tal, svi' wuh danik comprehensive kash-ral t' wuh zhil, became nearly t'nash-veh lad occupation. I telv-tor k' ardour eifa ar'kada, ni bosh t' genius heh sakathilaya, if iyik inquirers ma written fi' aifa subjects. I attended wuh lectures heh sokasitau wuh acquaintance t' wuh sasu t' ek'tal t' wuh university, heh i afer-tor kauk svi' m. Krempe wuh lo'uk deal t' ralash kash-ral heh yeht ro'fori, puterish-tor, ish-veh nam-tor yeht, k' wuh repulsive physiognomy heh manners, tonk'peh ri fi' ik khrosahp wuh lehkuh taluhk. Svi' m. Waldman i afer-tor wuh yeht t'hy'la. Ish-veh gentleness vesh' worla kur-tor k' dogmatism, heh ish-veh instructions vesh' putan-tor k' wuh sov t' frankness heh rom malat ik klee'fah'tu kanok idea t' pedantry. Svi' wuh thousand yut au smoothed na' me wuh yut t' fai-tukh heh tor wuh danik abstruse inquiries pa'shik heh hagik tor t'nash-veh apprehension. T'nash-veh application vesh' na' wuh'rak fluctuating heh uncertain; ish-veh nazh-tor karik'es u' i proceeded heh ak became ni ardent heh nayik ik wuh yel k'ashiv sasaudau svi' wuh ta'hal t' asal whilst i vesh' wi engaged svi' t'nash-veh ek'tal-zup-shal. U' i applied ni closely, ish-veh lau nam-tor easily conceived ik t'nash-veh progress vesh' rapid. T'nash-veh ardour vesh' indeed wuh astonishment t' wuh orensu, heh t'nash-veh proficiency ik t' wuh trensu. Professor krempe k'ashiv ya'akash me, k' wuh sly abru'teruklar-ru'lut, uf cornelius agrippa went fi', whilst m. Waldman sagluvau wuh danik heartfelt exultation svi' t'nash-veh progress. Dahkuh tevun be' dvun-tor svi' nash manner, du' if i vlitau rai yaret tor geneva, tonk'peh vesh' engaged, khaf-spol heh soul, svi' wuh pursuit t' ein discoveries if i rok-tor tor tor. Rim tonk'peh eifa vi ma veshtau au mokuhlek conceive t' wuh enticements t' ek'tal. Svi' vath orenau du hal-tor u' irak u' vath ma hal-tor fa' du, heh tra' nam-tor nothing weht tor fai-tor; tonk'peh svi' wuh talik pursuit tra' nam-tor continual yem-tukh na' discovery heh wonder. Wuh kashek t' moderate tsoh if closely pursues veh orenau bolau infallibly lasha na' lo'uk proficiency svi' ik orenau; heh i, vi continually sought wuh bai'elkhrul-akteiben t' veh vel t' pursuit heh vesh' solely wrapped abru svi' nash, improved ni rapidly ik na' wuh shaht t' dahkuh tevun i tor ein discoveries svi' wuh improvement t' ein meli-tukh instruments, if procured me lo'uk vam heh admiration na' wuh university. Lu i had lasha na' nash sfek heh had shetau u' muhl acquainted k' wuh wihka heh practice t' malatik ven-dol-leralmin u' nerau fi' wuh tupa t' sovek t' wuh professors na' ingolstadt, t'nash-veh residence tra' hasu rai longer conducive tor t'nash-veh improvements, i nahp t' returning tor t'nash-veh t'hylara heh t'nash-veh salatik kahr, lu wuh incident pavesh-tor ik protracted t'nash-veh stay. Veh t' wuh phenomena if had peculiarly skamau t'nash-veh attention vesh' wuh velek t' wuh komihn nentu, heh, indeed, sovek aushfa endued k' ha'kiv. Whence, i k'ashiv ya'akash myself, did wuh dvatai t' ha'kiv proceed? Ish-veh vesh' wuh vakh deshker, heh veh if has ek'wak vesh' panah-tor u' wuh mystery; wi k' uf wehk vel nam-tor etek fi-tor wuh rihk t' becoming acquainted, kuv cowardice il carelessness did ri restrain etwel inquiries. I revolved aifa circumstances svi' t'nash-veh kashek heh satalau thenceforth tor apply myself weht wa' tor eifa khlup t' malatik ven-dol-leralmin if relate tor nam-tor-lof-tal. Vita i had vesh' animated k' wuh siyah supernatural buhl'es, t'nash-veh application tor nash orenau would ma vesh' irksome heh siyah intolerable. Tor linisau wuh aisha t' ha'kiv, etek bolau wuh'rak ma recourse tor tevakh. I became acquainted k' wuh ek'tal t' vukhut-tal, tonk'peh nash vesh' ri sufficient; i bolau isha glantau wuh malatik nehaya heh corruption t' wuh komihn ak'shem. Svi' t'nash-veh education t'nash-veh sa-mekh had taken wuh greatest precautions ik t'nash-veh kashek dang nam-tor impressed k' rai supernatural horrors. I ri tor ek'wak vokau ki' trembled na' wuh var t' superstition il ki' ptha wuh apparition t' wuh tam'a. Mu'khlup'es had rai daya fi-tor t'nash-veh fancy, heh wuh churchyard vesh' tor me goh wuh receptacle t' ak'shem deprived t' ha'kiv, if, s' hasu wuh ku-san t' vaksur heh karik'es, had shetau yem-tukh na' wuh worm.
