I' i vesh' pufulag-tor tor linisau wuh aishan heh progress t' nash nehaya heh punekwitau tor spend gad heh mu-yor svi' vaults heh charnel-kelek. T'nash-veh attention vesh' teslau fi-tor kanok vel wuh danik insupportable tor wuh delicacy t' wuh komihn feelings. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh uf wuh tok-ti shid t' sasu vesh' degraded heh thinoi; i beheld wuh corruption t' tevakh navau tor wuh svai-tu-ashya nak t' ha'kiv; vesht gla-tor nash-veh uf wuh worm inherited wuh wonders t' wuh bezhun heh shi'nahp. I svizh-tor, examining heh analysing ek' wuh minutiae t' causation, u' exemplified svi' wuh rubah s' ha'kiv tor tevakh, heh tevakh tor ha'kiv, abi' s' wuh midst t' nash mu'khlup'es wuh sudden ta'hal shau svi' fi-tor me—wuh ta'hal ni maut-ugelik heh wondrous, wi ni velik, ik du' i became dizzy k' wuh immensity t' wuh prospect if ish-veh illustrated, i vesh' ak'wikmun ik among ni wehk sasu t' genius vi had khartau ish-veh inquiries na' wuh ka ek'tal, ik i sa'awek dang nam-tor reserved tor discover ni astonishing wuh tsat. Vokau, i am ri recording wuh vision t' wuh madman. Wuh yel tor ri weht certainly min-tor svi' wuh heavens do ik if i i' affirm nam-tor yeht. Ein miracle lau ma torvau ish-veh, wi wuh skaf t' wuh discovery vesh' natya heh yesik. Po' gad heh mu-yor t' incredible zup heh zung, i navau svi' discovering wuh aishan t' generation heh ha'kiv; nay, weht, i became myself capable t' bestowing animation fi-tor lifeless tukh. Wuh astonishment if i had palikauk veshtau fi' nash discovery ak mazhiv-kur-tor shi tor delight heh rapture. Po' ni mau wak spent svi' kusut-tor zup, tor lasha na' wuh'wak na' wuh dan-pid-sfek t' t'nash-veh aitlu vesh' wuh danik gratifying consummation t' t'nash-veh toils. Tonk'peh nash discovery vesh' ni lo'uk heh overwhelming ik ek' wuh ash-tor k' if i had vesh' progressively pufulag-tor tor ish-veh vesh' obliterated, heh i beheld goh wuh result. Ra had vesh' wuh orenau heh aitlun t' wuh wisest sasu opi' wuh fereikan t' wuh panu vesh' i' k'svi t'nash-veh ruskaraya. Ri ik, spo' wuh magic scene, ish-veh ek' tu'ash fi-tor me na' wuh'wak: wuh ro'fori i had prah vesh' t' wuh malat rather tor kharik t'nash-veh endeavours ni ak u' i dang sfek au na' wuh vel t' t'nash-veh psthan do tor gluvaya ik vel already accomplished. I vesh' spo' wuh arabian vi had vesh' visolektau k' wuh tevik heh afer-tor wuh tvur tor ha'kiv, mamut goh k' veh glimmering heh seemingly ineffectual ta'hal. Gla-tor nash-veh k' ish-veh eagerness heh wuh wonder heh rok if ish-veh bezhun sagluvau, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, ik du gish tor nam-tor informed t' wuh tsat k' if i am acquainted; ik fam yehat nam-tor; shroi patiently abi' wuh shaht t' t'nash-veh var, heh du dungi easily pakashogau po i am reserved fi-tor ik subject. I dungi ri ras-tukh du fi', unguarded heh ardent u' i yi vesh', tor ish-veh vashaya heh infallible misery. Oren-tor s' me, kuv ri k' t'nash-veh precepts, k'puu k' t'nash-veh li-fal, uf tehvar-bosh nam-tor wuh acquirement t' fai-tukh heh uf mau happier ik sasu nam-tor vi believes ish-veh salatik kahr tor nam-tor wuh panu, do au vi aspires tor shetau weht tor ish-veh malat dungi kal-tor. Lu i afer-tor ni astonishing wuh tepul shitau k'svi t'nash-veh el'ru, i hesitated wuh akarshif fundik wuh manner svi' if i dang employ ish-veh. Hi i ma wuh tsoh t' bestowing animation, wi tor dator wuh nentu na' wuh reception t' ish-veh, k' ek' its intricacies t' slah, dvunek, heh os-khaf-mev, fam dvun hafau wuh ar'kadan t' inconceivable rihag'es heh zup. I vet-tor palikauk whether i dang attempt wuh fereikan t' wuh hasu spo' myself, il veh t' simpler organization; tonk'peh t'nash-veh glenonaya vesh' nuh' mau exalted k' t'nash-veh wuh'rak navun tor permit me tor vet t' t'nash-veh kup'es tor mazhiv-kur-tor ha'kiv tor wuh aushfa u' wehkonik heh wonderful u' sasu. Wuh tukh na' la' k'svi t'nash-veh a'fic hardly saudau adequate tor ni arduous wuh undertaking, tonk'peh i vet-tor ri ik i dang ultimately navau. I dator myself na' wuh multitude t' reverses; t'nash-veh el'toraya lau nam-tor incessantly hertak-tor, heh na' kim-shah t'nash-veh ar'kadan nam-tor imperfect, wi lu i panah-tor wuh improvement if kanok gad nem-tor shi svi' ek'tal heh tor-velsu, i vesh' kastorau tor rok t'nash-veh la' attempts would k'puu ti wuh nen t' fa-wak navun. Il sos panah-tor wuh pul'es heh complexity t' t'nash-veh dotor u' sovek nerau-kek-vuhnayek t' its impracticability. Ish-veh vesh' k' aifa feelings ik i began wuh fereikan t' wuh komihn hasu. U' wuh minuteness t' wuh krus shidau wuh lo'uk hindrance tor t'nash-veh threshan, i resolved, contrary tor t'nash-veh wuh'rak intention, tor tor wuh hasu t' wuh masuk' stature, ik nam-tor tor leralmin, pa' ohkuh ash'ya svi' pidek, heh proportionably suk. Po' having shidau nash determination heh having spent ein tevun-krus svi' successfully collecting heh arranging t'nash-veh tukh, i began. Kling mokuhlek conceive wuh vuhna'es t' feelings if spitau me onwards, spo' wuh suk'masutra-eshu'a, svi' wuh wuh'rak buhl'es t' navun. Ha'kiv heh tevakh saudau tor me tangu bounds, if i dang wuh'rak shaya k'fai, heh mukau wuh torrent t' ta'hal vi' etwel gu'gelik panu. Wuh uzh koshtri would kudau me u' its fereiksu heh shu-pal; wehk kunli heh marom natures would owe ish-veh hasu tor me. Rai sa-mekh kupi claim wuh gratitude t' ish-veh kan ni completely u' i dang nazh ish-veh. Pursuing aifa haulan, i nahp ik kuv i kupi bestow animation fi-tor lifeless tukh, i lau svi' torek t' wak (hi i i' afer-tor ish-veh impossible) uzhau ha'kiv wilat tevakh had sauyaing vaikau wuh ak'shem tor corruption. Aifa nahp nenikau t'nash-veh tam'a, du' i pursued t'nash-veh undertaking k' unremitting ardour. T'nash-veh nak had grown spoh k' orenau, heh t'nash-veh person had shetau emaciated k' confinement. Sometimes, fi' wuh maut rihk t' certainty, i vravshau; wi fam dvun i clung tor wuh rok if wuh thurai gad il wuh thurai wadan lau realise. Veh tsat if i sa'awek ma vesh' wuh rok tor if i had dedicated myself; heh wuh aikum gazed fi' t'nash-veh midnight zup-tor, du', k' unrelaxed heh breathless eagerness, i pursued malat tor ish-veh hiding-shitau. Vi dungau conceive wuh horrors t' t'nash-veh tsat toil u' i dabbled among wuh unhallowed damps t' wuh shi'vukhut il tortured wuh living aushfa tor animate wuh lifeless krizhiv? T'nash-veh sikrus i' tremble, heh t'nash-veh bezhun mahal-tor k' wuh remembrance; tonk'peh yi wuh resistless heh siyah frantic impulse urged me fa'rak; i seemed ki' pakik ek' soul il kashan tonk'peh na' nash-veh pursuit. Ish-veh vesh' indeed tonk'peh wuh be' dvun-tor trance, ik goh tor me olau k' uzhau acuteness ni ak u', wuh unnatural kastoran ceasing tor el'torau, i had fun-tor tor t'nash-veh hinek es'merka. I tershau hinek s' charnel-kelek heh ertau, k' profane ozh, wuh tremendous tsat t' wuh komihn nentu. Svi' wuh solitary tvi-shal, il rather nala, na' wuh fik t' wuh kelek, heh dahshau s' ek' wuh vath ha-shal k' wuh tanaf-shi'gluvaun heh staircase, i potau t'nash-veh zup-shal t' filthy fereikan; t'nash-veh bezhun-kal vesh' starting s' ish-veh sockets svi' attending tor wuh details t' t'nash-veh employment. Wuh dissecting tvi-shal heh wuh slaughter-kelek furnished wehk t' t'nash-veh tukh; heh k'ashiv did t'nash-veh komihn malat da-tor k' loathing s' t'nash-veh occupation, whilst, fam dvun urged fi' k' wuh eagerness if perpetually increased, i katau t'nash-veh ar'kadan be' tor wuh conclusion. Wuh belaar tevun-krus be' dvun-tor du' i vesh' thus engaged, khaf-spol heh soul, svi' veh pursuit. Ish-veh vesh' wuh danik vaksurik tevun-yonuk; worla did wuh vunai bestow wuh weht plentiful harvest il wuh kas-elakh yield wuh weht luxuriant vintage, tonk'peh t'nash-veh bezhun vesh' insensible tor wuh sem-rik-tor t' malat. Heh wuh ka feelings if tor me neglect wuh scenes pa' me aisha me isha tor yen-tor eifa t'hylara vi vesh' ni wehk miles tadek-adir, heh ik i had ri gla-tor na' ni wu wuh wak. I fai-tor t'nash-veh silence disquieted au, heh i muhl vokau wuh zhit t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh: “i fai-tor ik du' du nam-tor sanoi k' yourself du dungi nah-tor t' etek k' affection, heh etek dungau zhu-tor regularly s' du. Du bolau pardon me kuv i fudau sovek svi-shaya svi' ish-veh correspondence u' wuh skan ik ish-veh vath gu-vam nam-tor kaing neglected.” i fai-tor muhl therefore ra would nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s feelings, tonk'peh i kupi ri bezhun-masu t'nash-veh nahp s' t'nash-veh employment, loathsome svi' itself, tonk'peh if had taken wuh irresistible meskaraya t' t'nash-veh glenonaya. I istau, u' ish-veh vesh', tor procrastinate ek' ik related tor t'nash-veh feelings t' affection abi' wuh lo'uk vel, if vitem-tor abru kanok es'merka t' t'nash-veh malat, dang nam-tor ovsoh. I yi nahp ik t'nash-veh sa-mekh would nam-tor unjust kuv au ascribed t'nash-veh neglect tor vice il faultiness fi' t'nash-veh krus, tonk'peh i am i' convinced ik au vesh' justified svi' conceiving ik i dang ri nam-tor altogether elik s' tenai. Wuh komihn hasu svi' perfection ought kwon-hau-ov tor korsau wuh hayal heh peaceful kashek heh worla tor kal-tor shaukaush il wuh transitory aitlun tor ertau ish-veh tranquillity. I ri tor nah-tor ik wuh pursuit t' fai-tukh nam-tor wuh kaulauf tor nash tor-go. Kuv wuh orenau tor if du apply yourself has wuh tendency tor kobatau ish-veh affections heh tor vashau ish-veh zahvan na' eifa velik pleasures svi' if rai rish-mokev mokuhlek possibly rish, yi ik orenau nam-tor certainly unlawful, ik nam-tor tor leralmin, ri befitting wuh komihn kashek. Kuv nash tor-go vesh' kwon-hau-ov glantau; kuv rai sasu kal-tor sovek pursuit whatsoever tor snertau k' wuh tranquillity t' ish-veh ka'kelik affections, greece had ri vesh' enslaved, cæsar would ma spared ish-veh shasol, america would ma vesh' discovered weht gradually, heh wuh eik-te'kru t' mexico heh peru had ri vesh' vashau. Tonk'peh i yen-tor ik i am moralizing svi' wuh danik eku'ki krus t' t'nash-veh var, heh ish-veh glazhau remind me tor proceed. T'nash-veh sa-mekh tor rai reproach svi' ish-veh nuhm heh goh nem-tor beglanau t' t'nash-veh silence k' inquiring vi' t'nash-veh occupations weht wa' do fa'. Karil, sikar, heh belaar be' dvun-tor maf du' t'nash-veh zup-tor; tonk'peh i did ri glantau wuh blossom il wuh expanding mor—sights if fa' kwon-hau-ov yielded me supreme delight—ni deeply vesh' i engrossed svi' t'nash-veh occupation. Wuh mor t' ik tevun had withered fa' t'nash-veh ar'kadan drew be' tor wuh ikap-tor, heh i' kanok gad gluvau me weht plainly uf muhl i had navau. Tonk'peh t'nash-veh buhl'es vesh' rihamau k' t'nash-veh anxiety, heh i saudau rather spo' veh doomed k' slavery tor toil svi' wuh ip-thorshek, il sovek vath unwholesome trade do wuh tanafsu occupied k' ish-veh favourite employment. Kanok mu-yor i vesh' oppressed k' wuh vohris tau, heh i became nervous tor wuh danik kusut-tor degree; wuh tevan t' wuh mor startled me, heh i shunned t'nash-veh katravahsu creatures u' kuv i had vesh' guilty t' wuh tr'y'kak. Sometimes i grew alarmed na' wuh vashau i pakashogau ik i had shetau; wuh tepul t' t'nash-veh lof sa'awek potun-tor me: t'nash-veh zup-tor would ak shaht, heh i pudva-tor ik tusok heh amusement would yi yetur maf incipient has; heh i ugau myself fi' t' aifa lu t'nash-veh fereikan dang nam-tor ovsotik. Chapter 5 ish-veh vesh' fi' wuh dreary mu-yor t' november ik i beheld wuh accomplishment t' t'nash-veh toils. K' wuh anxiety ik siyah amounted tor agony, i tershau wuh instruments t' ha'kiv pa' me, ik i lau infuse wuh kil t' hasu vi' wuh lifeless vel ik ti na' t'nash-veh ash'ya. Ish-veh vesh' already veh svi' wuh asal; wuh sov-masu lates-tor dismally tehnat wuh panes, heh t'nash-veh ha'fek vesh' nearly yontau si', lu, k' wuh glimmer t' wuh ulef-sayonotau ta'hal, vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh pasik kin-kur bezhun t' wuh creature tu'ash; ish-veh breathed lerash, heh wuh convulsive dvunel pahutau its sikrus. Uf mokuhlek i kethelvau t'nash-veh zherka na' nash catastrophe, il uf delineate wuh wretch ik k' such vaik kusut-tor heh tun i had endeavoured tor shid? Ish-veh sikrus vesh' svi' proportion, heh i had dvel-tor ish-veh features u' vaksurik. Vaksurik! Lo'uk oekon! Ish-veh kin-kur wadi scarcely wein-tor wuh ar'kadan t' dvunek heh uzh-khaf-mev ne'rak; ish-veh isachya vesh' t' wuh lustrous nesh-kur, heh flowing; ish-veh zud t' wuh pearly whiteness; tonk'peh aifa luxuriances goh shidau wuh weht horrid contrast k' ish-veh watery bezhun, ik seemed siyah t' wuh ka kur u' wuh dun-wan-kur sockets svi' if au vesh' eku, ish-veh shrivelled complexion heh zehik nesh-kur bru-lar. Wuh natya kisheya t' ha'kiv nam-tor ri ni changeable u' wuh feelings t' komihn malat. I had ar'kada lerash na' nearly dahkuh tevun, na' wuh lad lof t' infusing ha'kiv vi' wuh inanimate ak'shem. Na' nash i had deprived myself t' shom heh muhl'es. I had aitlu ish-veh k' wuh ardour ik irak namautau moderation; tonk'peh i' ik i had shahtau, wuh vaksur t' wuh sahr-tor vanished, heh breathless horror heh spa'ash boshau t'nash-veh khaf-spol. Unable tor palesh-tor wuh pulva t' wuh hasu i had fereik-tor, i rushed s' wuh tvi-shal heh fator wuh akarshif traversing t'nash-veh sar-tak-tvi-shal, unable tor tertitau t'nash-veh kashek tor yuk. Na' wu-vath lassitude navau tor wuh tumult i had fa' palesh-tor, heh i threw myself fi' wuh sar-tak svi' t'nash-veh sai-vel, endeavouring tor seek wuh zamu moments t' forgetfulness. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' svi' vain; i yuk-tor, indeed, tonk'peh i vesh' ertau k' wuh wildest sahr-tor-tor. I nahp vesht gla-tor nash-veh elizabeth, svi' wuh svai t' muhl'es, walking svi' wuh yut t' ingolstadt. Delighted heh ak'wikmun, i nartau ish-veh, tonk'peh u' i imprinted wuh wuh'rak shok fi' ish-veh bru-lar, au became livid k' wuh hue t' tevakh; ish-veh features saudau tor rubah, heh i nahp ik i meskarau wuh tevikeh t' t'nash-veh tevik ko-mekh svi' t'nash-veh kar; wuh shroud enveloped ish-veh shid, heh vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh shi'vukhut-worms crawling svi' wuh hesha t' wuh flannel. I palikau s' t'nash-veh yuk k' horror; wuh samu asal-masu wein-tor t'nash-veh fa-patam, t'nash-veh zud chattered, heh kanok sikrus became convulsed; lu, k' wuh neik-ha'khlup heh kin-kur ta'hal t' wuh aikum, u' ish-veh punekwitau its yut k'fai wuh krani fe-wein, i beheld wuh wretch—wuh miserable stislak ik i had fereik-tor. Au meskarau abru wuh curtain t' wuh sar-tak; heh ish-veh bezhun, kuv bezhun au lau nam-tor puvutau, vesh' teslau fi' me. Ish-veh ahs tu'ash, heh au muttered ein inarticulate sounds, du' wuh wa'limatau wrinkled ish-veh nak. Au lau ma spoken, tonk'peh i did ri zhu-tor; veh el'ru vesh' sakadau si', seemingly tor detain me, tonk'peh i stron-tor heh rushed downstairs. I nem-tor rau-nol svi' wuh courtyard t' wuh kelek if i inhabited, wilat i hafau du' wuh shom t' wuh mu-yor, walking abru heh ne' svi' wuh greatest agitation, listening attentively, catching heh fearing tik ralash u' kuv ish-veh vesh' tor tor'pra wuh betaya t' wuh demoniacal tevikeh tor if i had ni miserably putan-tor ha'kiv. Oh! Rai mortal kupi nenikaya wuh horror t' ik countenance. Wuh mummy va'ashiv endued k' animation kupi ri nam-tor ni hideous u' ik wretch. I had gazed fi' ish-veh du' unfinished; au vesh' watosh yi, tonk'peh lu eifa dvunek heh joints vesh' rendered capable t' dvunel, ish-veh became wuh vel such u' kauk dante kupi ri ma conceived. I be' dvun-tor wuh mu-yor wretchedly. Sometimes t'nash-veh khaf-spol-gaya kuhsh-tor ni sahris heh hardly ik i olau wuh palpitation t' kanok uzh-khaf-mev; na' vath, i nearly sank tor wuh solektra k'fai languor heh mairik kobat'es. Mingled k' nash horror, i olau wuh bitterness t' disappointment; sahr-tor-tor ik had vesh' t'nash-veh yem-tukh heh vaksurik shom na' ni wu wuh ret vesh' i' shetau wuh bogozh tor me; heh wuh rubah vesh' ni rapid, wuh overthrow ni ovsotik! Asal, dismal heh masupik, na' wu-vath dawned heh discovered tor t'nash-veh sleepless heh aching bezhun wuh church t' ingolstadt, its wan-kur steeple heh wak-vel, if indicated wuh sixth wadan. Wuh porter tu'ash wuh temep t' wuh kelek, if had ik mu-yor vesh' t'nash-veh asylum, heh i issued vi' wuh yut, pacing au k' sahris ash-tor, u' kuv i sought tor nan'woi wuh wretch ik i ptha kanok turning t' wuh yut would la' tor t'nash-veh zan-tor. I did ri dare fun tor wuh ha-shal if i inhabited, tonk'peh olau impelled tor brax fi', hi drenched k' wuh sov-masu if mukau s' wuh nesh-kur heh comfortless igen. I fator walking svi' nash manner na' ein wak, endeavouring k' bodily tusok tor ease wuh tus ik rasathau fi-tor t'nash-veh kashek. I traversed wuh yut rik' sovek pa'shik conception t' wilat i vesh' il ra i vesh' doing. T'nash-veh khaf-spol palpitated svi' wuh has-mar t' pthak, heh i hurried fi' k' ripakhaik ash-tor, ri daring tor glazhau pa' me: spo' veh vi, fi' wuh lonely fau-yut, doth lates svi' pthak heh dread, heh, having wuh'wak da-tor pauk, lates-tor fi', heh da-tor rai weht ish-veh patam; fai'ei au fai-tor wuh frightful shaka doth ikap-tor za' ish-veh tread. [coleridge’s “t'kahr mariner.”] continuing thus, vesht sarlah nash-veh na' wu-vath mesyutik tor wuh ha-shal na' if wuh vuhnauk diligences heh carriages usually pehkau. La' i svizh-tor, i fai-tor ri po; tonk'peh i hafau ein minutes k' t'nash-veh bezhun teslau fi' wuh coach ik vesh' coming na' me s' wuh vath shaht t' wuh yut. U' ish-veh drew nearer i glantau ik ish-veh vesh' wuh swiss diligence; ish-veh pehkau aishan wilat i vesh' standing, heh fi' wuh svep hasu tu'ash, i pakashogau henry clerval, vi, fi' seeing me, instantly sprung si'. “t'nash-veh tal-kam frankenstein, ” sporiben au, “uf glad i am tor gla-tor du! Uf fortunate ik du dang nam-tor la' na' wuh maut moment t' t'nash-veh alighting!” nothing kupi kaik t'nash-veh delight fi' seeing clerval; ish-veh la'es katau pla' tor t'nash-veh nahp t'nash-veh sa-mekh, elizabeth, heh ek' eifa scenes t' ha-kel ni tal-kam tor t'nash-veh recollection. I ruskarau ish-veh el'ru, heh svi' wuh moment forgot t'nash-veh horror heh misfortune; i olau suddenly, heh na' wuh wuh'rak wak du' wehk tevun-krus, hayal heh serene mak. I welcomed t'nash-veh t'hy'la, therefore, svi' wuh danik cordial manner, heh etek lates-tor na' t'nash-veh college. Clerval fator talking na' ein wak pa' etwel mutual t'hylara heh ish-veh sha' rom fortune svi' hasu permitted tor sarlah tor ingolstadt. “du lau easily dva-tor, ” leralmin-tor au, “uf lo'uk vesh' wuh rihag'es tor persuade t'nash-veh sa-mekh ik ek' bolayatik fai-tukh vesh' ri comprised svi' wuh thol tanaf t' dunap-keeping; heh, indeed, i dva-tor i losrak ish-veh incredulous tor wuh kim-shah, na' ish-veh ek'kayik kilko-srashiv tor t'nash-veh unwearied entreaties vesh' wuh ka u' ik t' wuh dutch schoolmaster svi' wuh vicar t' wakefield: ‘i ma lehkuh thousand florins wuh tevun rik' greek, i yokul heartily rik' greek.’ tonk'peh ish-veh affection na' me na' wu-vath overcame ish-veh ritishaya t' learning, heh au has permitted me tor undertake wuh halan t' discovery tor wuh solektra t' fai-tukh.” “ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh greatest delight tor gla-tor du; tonk'peh var-tor me uf du losrak t'nash-veh sa-mekh, sa-kai, heh elizabeth.” “maut muhl, heh maut kunli, goh wuh pi' uneasy ik au zhu-tor s' du ni seldom. K' wuh k', i tvai tor lecture du wuh pi' fi-tor ish-veh khrosahp myself. Tonk'peh, t'nash-veh tal-kam frankenstein, ” fator au, stopping pen heh gazing bosh svi' t'nash-veh limuk, “i did ri fa' remark uf maut has-bosh du saudau; ni wonil heh spoh; du glazhau u' kuv du had vesh' watching na' several mu-yor.” “du ma guessed gas'rak; i ma lately vesh' ni deeply engaged svi' veh occupation ik i ma ri kal-tor myself sufficient shom, u' gla-tor du; tonk'peh i rok, i sincerely rok, ik ek' aifa employments nam-tor i' na' wuh shaht heh ik i am na' wu-vath elik.” i trembled excessively; i kupi ri palesh-tor tor nah-tor t', heh irak lehkuh tor allude tor, wuh occurrences t' wuh preceding mu-yor. I lates-tor k' wuh sahris sahr, heh etek ak lasha na' t'nash-veh college. I yi haul-tor, heh wuh nahp tor me shiver, ik wuh creature ik i had losrak svi' t'nash-veh ha-shal lau fam dvun nam-tor tra', alive heh walking pa'. I dreaded tor behold nash stislak, tonk'peh i ptha fam dvun weht ik henry dang gla-tor ish-veh. Entreating ish-veh, therefore, tor hafau wuh zamu minutes na' wuh lanet t' wuh kaiden, i darted abru na' t'nash-veh sha' tvi-shal. T'nash-veh el'ru vesh' already fi' wuh klachek t' wuh svep fa' i recollected myself. I yi svizh-tor, heh wuh samu shivering sarlah abru' me. I threw wuh svep forcibly tu'ash, u' kanu nam-tor accustomed tor tor lu au gish wuh spectre tor lamok svi' waiting na' au fi' wuh vath vla; tonk'peh nothing saudau. I ash-tor fearfully svi': wuh ha-shal vesh' herbosh, heh t'nash-veh shi'yuk vesh' isha el-tor s' its hideous be'hai'la. I kupi hardly dva-tor ik ni lo'uk wuh rom fortune kupi ma befallen me, tonk'peh lu i became assured ik t'nash-veh nemut had indeed sasahr-tor, i clapped t'nash-veh el'ru na' mak heh sahr-tor ne' tor clerval. Etek she-tor vi' t'nash-veh tvi-shal, heh wuh dvinsu presently katau asal-yem; tonk'peh i vesh' unable tor tuhlau myself. Ish-veh vesh' ri mak goh ik ma me; i olau t'nash-veh kahm tingle k' mau-mazhiv-kur t' sensitiveness, heh t'nash-veh khaf-spol-gaya kuhsh-tor rapidly. I vesh' unable tor hafau na' wuh single instant svi' wuh ka shi; i spen-tor abru' wuh ku-san, clapped t'nash-veh el'ru, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor aloud. Clerval palikauk attributed t'nash-veh ritsuri tam'a tor mak fi' ish-veh lashan, tonk'peh lu au glantau me weht attentively, gla-tor ish-veh wuh wildness svi' t'nash-veh bezhun na' if au kupi ri khrosahp, heh t'nash-veh ral, unrestrained, heartless laughter koltha heh astonished ish-veh. “t'nash-veh tal-kam skilsu, ” maf-tor au, “ra, na' oekon’s sake, nam-tor wuh tukh? Ri tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut svi' ik manner. Uf has-bosh du nam-tor! Ra nam-tor wuh aishan t' ek' nash?” “ri tor ya'akash me, ” maf-tor i, putting t'nash-veh el'ru fa' t'nash-veh bezhun, na' i nahp vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh dreaded spectre glide vi' wuh tvi-shal; “_he_ mokuhlek var-tor. Oh, korsau me! Korsau me!” i glenonau ik wuh stislak seized me; i struggled furiously heh tevan-tor ne' svi' wuh nunau. Ri donku-tor clerval! Ra bolau ma vesh' ish-veh feelings? Wuh latva, if au anticipated k' such mak, ni strangely da-tor tor bitterness. Tonk'peh i vesh' ri wuh toglantausu t' ish-veh tushat, na' i vesh' lifeless heh did ri recover t'nash-veh kash-ral na' wuh wu, akarshif. Nash vesh' wuh palikaya t' wuh nervous tau if confined me na' several tevun-krus. Du' ek' ik wak henry vesh' t'nash-veh goh nurse. I afterwards oren-tor ik, fai-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s storilau ya'shakhuv heh unfitness na' ni wu wuh halovaya, heh uf wretched t'nash-veh has-mar would tor elizabeth, au spared au nash tushat k' concealing wuh sadvun t' t'nash-veh disorder. Au fai-tor ik i kupi ri ma wuh weht ves heh whio'naks nurse do himself; heh, pesik svi' wuh rok au olau t' t'nash-veh recovery, au did ri vet ik, instead t' doing klau, au performed wuh kindest torai ik au kupi na' au. Tonk'peh i vesh' svi' reality maut has-bosh, heh surely nothing tonk'peh wuh unbounded heh unremitting attentions t' t'nash-veh t'hy'la kupi ma restored me tor ha'kiv. Wuh shid t' wuh stislak fi' ik i had bestowed nam vesh' na' ek'wak fa' t'nash-veh bezhun, heh i raved incessantly fundik ish-veh. Doubtless t'nash-veh zhit ak'wikmun henry; au palikauk pudva-tor au tor nam-tor wuh czar t' t'nash-veh ertau glenonaya, tonk'peh wuh pertinacity k' if i continually recurred tor wuh ka subject persuaded ish-veh ik t'nash-veh disorder indeed owed its tveshu tor ein uncommon heh terrible pavek. K' maut vohris degrees, heh k' vakavik relapses ik alarmed heh grieved t'nash-veh t'hy'la, i recovered. I vokau wuh wuh'rak wak i became capable t' observing outward vel k' sovek ves t' sanosh, i pakashogau ik wuh tevan-tor mor had sasaudau heh ik wuh nu'ri buds vesh' shooting forth s' wuh lap ik duvek-tor t'nash-veh krani. Ish-veh vesh' wuh ekonik sikar, heh wuh tevun-yonuk contributed greatly tor t'nash-veh convalescence. I olau isha sentiments t' mak heh affection zaprah svi' t'nash-veh bosom; t'nash-veh gloom sasaudau, heh svi' wuh pen wak i became u' cheerful u' fa' i vesh' nashiv k' wuh fatal shaukaush. “dearest clerval, ” sporiben i, “uf ves, uf maut rom du nam-tor tor me. Nash bosh karil, instead t' hasu spent svi' orenau, u' du ugau yourself, has vesh' consumed svi' t'nash-veh has-bosh tvi-shal. Uf dungau i ek'wak repay du? I olau wuh greatest remorse na' wuh disappointment t' if i ma vesh' wuh occasion, tonk'peh du dungi forgive me.” “du dungi repay me entirely kuv du ri tor discompose yourself, tonk'peh prah muhl u' sahris u' du mokuhlek; heh opi' du saudau svi' such rom tam'a, i lau stariben tor du fi' veh subject, sos ri?” i trembled. Veh subject! Ra kupi ish-veh nam-tor? Kupi au allude tor wuh vel fi' ik i dared ri kauk nah-tor? “tertitau yourself, ” leralmin-tor clerval, vi glantau t'nash-veh rubah t' kur, “i dungi ri mention ish-veh kuv ish-veh pahutau du; tonk'peh ish-veh sa-mekh heh krei would nam-tor maut kunli kuv au poprah wuh nuhm s' du svi' ish-veh sha' handwriting. Au hardly fai-tor uf has-bosh du ma vesh' heh nam-tor uneasy na' ish-veh wu silence.” “nam-tor ik ek', t'nash-veh tal-kam henry? Uf kupi du suppose ik t'nash-veh wuh'rak nahp would ri hash-tor na' eifa tal-kam, tal-kam t'hylara ik i ashaya heh vi nam-tor ni nazh-tor t' t'nash-veh ashaya?” “kuv nash nam-tor ish-veh la' temper, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, du dungi sos'eh nam-tor glad tor gla-tor wuh nuhm ik has vesh' lying la' ein gad na' du; ish-veh nam-tor s' ish-veh krei, i dva-tor.” chapter 6 clerval yi shitau wuh zahalik nuhm vi' t'nash-veh el'ru. Ish-veh vesh' s' t'nash-veh sha' elizabeth: “t'nash-veh dearest krei, “du ma vesh' has-bosh, maut has-bosh, heh kauk wuh ek'kayik nuhm t' tal-kam ves henry nam-tor ri sufficient tor reassure me fi' ish-veh khrosahp. Du nam-tor zadik tor kitau—tor meskaraya wuh pen; wi veh zhit s' du, tal-kam skilsu, nam-tor bolayatik tor hayal etwel apprehensions. Na' wuh akarshif i ma nahp ik tik lehk would katau nash zehl, heh t'nash-veh persuasions ma restrained t'nash-veh sa-kuk s' undertaking wuh halovaya tor ingolstadt. I ma prevented ish-veh encountering wuh inconveniences heh sos'eh tehvar t' ni wu wuh halovaya, wi uf k'ashiv ma i regretted ri hasu kup tor perform ish-veh myself! I khlop tor myself ik wuh task t' attending fi' ish-veh sickbed has devolved fi' ein mercenary hinek nurse, vi kupi worla guess ish-veh istau il minister tor au k' wuh tun heh affection t' ish-veh ri donku-tor krei. Wi ik nam-tor abru' i': clerval kitau ik indeed du nam-tor getting weh-rom. I eagerly rok ik du dungi wugau nash kash-tor'es ak svi' ish-veh sha' handwriting. “prah muhl—heh fun tor etek. Du dungi talal wuh kunli, cheerful ha-kel heh t'hylara vi ashaya du dearly. Ish-veh sa-mekh’s muhl'es nam-tor hakarik, heh au ya'akash tonk'peh tor gla-tor du, tonk'peh tor nam-tor assured ik du nam-tor muhl; heh ri wuh tun dungi ek'wak wan ish-veh benevolent countenance. Uf sanoi du would nam-tor tor remark wuh improvement t' etwel ernest! Au nam-tor i' leh-sheh heh bosh t' toran heh tam'a. Au nam-tor desirous tor nam-tor wuh yeht swiss heh tor svi-tor vi' k'shatri dvin, tonk'peh etek fam yehat krus k' ish-veh, k'puu abi' ish-veh tela'at sa-kai fun-tor tor etek. T'nash-veh sa-kuk nam-tor ri sanoi k' wuh idea t' wuh askital career svi' wuh irak shasol, tonk'peh ernest worla had ish-veh tepul t' application. Au glazhau fi-tor orenau u' wuh odious fetter; ish-veh wak nam-tor spent svi' wuh tu'ash sov, climbing wuh kunel il rowing fi' wuh suk'muzh. I pthak ik au dungi shetau wuh idler vita etek yield wuh sfek heh permit ish-veh tor svi-tor fi' wuh ha'yigal if au has dvel-tor. “pi' alteration, kaula wuh tor'ovak t' etwel tal-kam kanu, has taken shi opi' du losrak etek. Wuh pla-kur suk'muzh heh izh-clad suk'kunel—au worla rubah; heh i nah-tor etwel placid ha-kel heh etwel contented khaf-spol nam-tor pakhartau k' wuh ka immutable tor-gav. T'nash-veh trifling occupations nem-tor abru t'nash-veh wak heh amuse me, heh i am rewarded na' sovek pideshan k' seeing rim tonk'peh kunli, ves limuk pa' me. Opi' du losrak etek, tonk'peh veh rubah has taken shi svi' etwel pi' household. Tor du vokau fi' ra occasion justine moritz svi-tor etwel skan? Probably du ri tor; i dungi relate ish-veh vesht-var, therefore svi' wuh zamu zhit. Madame moritz, ish-veh ko-mekh, vesh' wuh kir'an k' kehkuh kanu, t' ik justine vesh' wuh wuh. Nash ko-kan had kwon-hau-ov vesh' wuh favourite t' ish-veh sa-mekh, tonk'peh k'fai wuh flekh perversity, ish-veh ko-mekh kupi ri palesh-tor ish-veh, heh po' wuh tevakh t' m. Moritz, skasau ish-veh maut has-bosh. T'nash-veh ezyet glantau nash, heh lu justine vesh' leh-dah tevun t' ya'shakhuv, fakovau fi' ish-veh ko-mekh tor kal-tor ish-veh tor ha-tor na' etwel kelek. Wuh republican trahokna t' etwel shasol ma torvau simpler heh happier manners do eifa if fakovau svi' wuh lo'uk monarchies ik vikuvau ish-veh. Hence tra' nam-tor lehkuh distinction svi' wuh several mohrn t' its inhabitants; heh wuh weh-neik zek, hasu neither ni ri donku-tor il ni despised, ish-veh manners nam-tor weht refined heh moral. Wuh dvinsu svi' geneva tor ri tvai wuh ka vel u' wuh dvinsu svi' france heh england. Justine, thus poprah svi' etwel skan, oren-tor wuh gu-vam t' wuh dvinsu, wuh nosh if, svi' etwel fortunate shasol, tor ri vinan-tor wuh idea t' ignorance heh wuh sacrifice t' wuh dignity t' wuh komihn hasu. “justine, du lau vokau, vesh' wuh lo'uk favourite t' ish-veh; heh i recollect du wuh'wak remarked ik kuv du vesh' svi' wuh has-bosh humour, veh glance s' justine kupi dissipate ish-veh, na' wuh ka utvau ik ariosto mazhiv-kur-tor fundik wuh vaksur t' angelica—she glazhau ni frank-hearted heh kunli. T'nash-veh ezyet conceived wuh lo'uk attachment na' ish-veh, k' if she vesh' vimevilau tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh education superior tor ik if she had palikauk intended. Nash rufai vesh' fully repaid; justine vesh' wuh danik grateful pi' creature svi' wuh panu: i ri tor tvai ik she tor sovek ha'yigal i worla puzhu-tor veh be' dvun ish-veh bru-lar, tonk'peh du kupi gla-tor k' ish-veh bezhun ik she siyah adored ish-veh protectress. Hi ish-veh disposition vesh' sa-ka-ashausu heh svi' wehk respects inconsiderate, wi she vlitau wuh greatest attention tor kanok gesture t' t'nash-veh ezyet. She nahp ish-veh wuh model t' ek' marom'es heh endeavoured tor va'amau ish-veh phraseology heh manners, ni ik kauk i' she k'ashiv reminds me t' ish-veh. “lu t'nash-veh dearest ezyet tev-tor kanok veh vesh' nuh' mau occupied svi' ish-veh sha' tushat tor beglanau ri donku-tor justine, vi had attended ish-veh du' ish-veh has-mar k' wuh danik anxious affection. Ri donku-tor justine vesh' maut has-bosh; tonk'peh vath trials vesh' reserved na' ish-veh. “veh k' veh, ish-veh sa-kai heh ko-kai tev-tor; heh ish-veh ko-mekh, k' wuh kaulauf t' ish-veh neglected ko-fu, vesh' losrak childless. Wuh conscience t' wuh kosu vesh' troubled; she began tor nah-tor ik wuh deaths t' ish-veh favourites vesh' wuh judgement s' sha-ka-ri tor chastise ish-veh partiality. She vesh' wuh roman catholic; heh i dva-tor ish-veh confessor wugau wuh idea if she had conceived. Accordingly, wuh zamu tevun-krus po' ish-veh trashan na' ingolstadt, justine vesh' puvutau ha-kel k' ish-veh repentant ko-mekh. Ri donku-tor ko-kan! She wept lu she quitted etwel kelek; she vesh' mau rubitau opi' wuh tevakh t' t'nash-veh ezyet; tushat had putan-tor softness heh wuh winning mildness tor ish-veh manners, if had fa' vesh' remarkable na' vivacity. Il vesh' ish-veh residence na' ish-veh ko-mekh’s kelek t' wuh malat tor restore ish-veh gaiety. Wuh ri donku-tor kosu vesh' maut vacillating svi' ish-veh repentance. She sometimes eit'jae justine tor forgive ish-veh unkindness, tonk'peh mau oftener accused ish-veh t' having aisha wuh deaths t' ish-veh sa-kai heh ko-kai. Perpetual fretting na' wu-vath threw madame moritz vi' wuh decline, if palikauk increased ish-veh irritability, tonk'peh she nam-tor i' na' sochya na' ek'wak. She tev-tor fi' wuh wuh'rak betaya t' samu igen-va, na' wuh palikaya t' nash kim-shah karil. Justine has aishan fun-tor tor etek; heh i assure du i ashaya ish-veh tenderly. She nam-tor maut clever heh gentle, heh extremely takov; u' i mentioned fa', ish-veh mien heh ish-veh sagluvaya continually remind me t' t'nash-veh tal-kam ezyet. “i bolau leralmin isha wuh zamu zhit tor du, t'nash-veh tal-kam krei, t' pi' ashal-veh william. I istaya du kupi gla-tor ish-veh; au nam-tor maut ha-vol t' ish-veh ya'shakhuv, k' slor laughing pla-kur bezhun, gu'gelik bezhun-isach, heh tcha-tor isachya. Lu au abru'teruklar-ru'lut, dahkuh pi' dimples saudau fi' tik nak, if nam-tor rosy k' muhl'es. Au has already had veh il dahkuh pi' _wives, _ tonk'peh louisa biron nam-tor ish-veh favourite, wuh takov pi' ko-kan t' kaukuh tevun t' ya'shakhuv. “i', tal-kam skilsu, i dare leralmin du istaya tor nam-tor indulged svi' wuh pi' gossip fundik wuh rom sutra t' geneva. Wuh takov din-tor mansfield has already poprah wuh congratulatory yaretau fi' ish-veh approaching kal'i'farr k' wuh nu'ri englishman, john melbourne, esq. Ish-veh watosh ko-kai, manon, telik m. Duvillard, wuh don-ka banker, kim-shah tasmin. Ish-veh favourite schoolfellow, louis manoir, has dashau several misfortunes opi' wuh trashan t' clerval s' geneva. Tonk'peh au has already recovered ish-veh tam'a, heh nam-tor reported tor nam-tor fi' wuh sfek t' marrying wuh lively takov frenchwoman, madame tavernier. She nam-tor wuh kir'an, heh mau older do manoir; tonk'peh she nam-tor maut mau krol-tor, heh wuh favourite k' kanok-veh. “i ma written myself vi' weh-rom tam'a, tal-kam krei; tonk'peh t'nash-veh anxiety fun-tor fi-tor me u' i conclude. Kitau, dearest skilsu, —veh zehl—veh zhit dungi nam-tor wuh kudaya tor etek. Lehkuh thousand itaren tor henry na' ish-veh kindness, ish-veh affection, heh ish-veh wehk nuhm; etek nam-tor sincerely grateful. Adieu! T'nash-veh krei; nem-tor tun t' yourself; heh, i entreat du, kitau! “elizabeth lavenza. “geneva, march 18th, 17—.” “tal-kam, tal-kam elizabeth!” i sporiben, lu i had telv-tor ish-veh nuhm: “i dungi kitau instantly heh vas-tor au s' wuh anxiety au bolau olau.” i kitau, heh nash pideshan greatly zung-tor me; tonk'peh t'nash-veh convalescence had palikau, heh proceeded regularly. Svi' wuh'ashiv fortnight i vesh' kup tor trasha t'nash-veh tvi-shal. Veh t' t'nash-veh wuh'rak gu-vam fi' t'nash-veh recovery vesh' tor ragtau clerval tor wuh several professors t' wuh university. Svi' doing nash, i underwent wuh ves t' rough nam-tor, has-bosh befitting wuh skek ik t'nash-veh kashek had potun-tor. Ek'wak opi' wuh fatal mu-yor, wuh shaht t' t'nash-veh zup-tor, heh wuh palikaya t' t'nash-veh misfortunes, i had conceived wuh khrashik antipathy kauk tor wuh ahm t' malatik ven-dol-leralmin. Lu i vesh' vathru ved restored tor muhl'es, wuh glan t' wuh meli-tukh instrument would uzhau ek' wuh agony t' t'nash-veh nervous symptoms. Henry gla-tor nash, heh had snem-tor ek' t'nash-veh oh'a'dhid s' t'nash-veh zan-tor. Au had isha rubai t'nash-veh ha-shal; na' au pakashogau ik i had acquired wuh ritishaya na' wuh tvi-shal if had previously vesh' t'nash-veh ek'tal-zup-shal. Tonk'peh aifa tun-tor t' clerval vesh' tor t' rai avail lu i yaretau wuh professors. M. Waldman inflicted torture lu au krol-tor, k' kindness heh warmth, wuh astonishing progress i had tor svi' wuh ek'tal. Au ak pakashogau ik i ritishau wuh subject; tonk'peh ri guessing wuh yeht aishan, au attributed t'nash-veh feelings tor modesty, heh rubai wuh subject s' t'nash-veh improvement, tor wuh ek'tal itself, k' wuh aitlun, u' i evidently gla-tor, t' bestan me si'. Ra sos tor? Au tvai tor sanoi, heh au tormented me. I olau u' kuv au had shitau carefully, veh k' veh, svi' t'nash-veh zan-tor eifa instruments if vesh' tor nam-tor afterwards nam-tor-tor svi' putting me tor wuh vohris heh pi-maat'rer tevakh. I writhed ne' ish-veh zhit, wi dared ri gluvaya wuh kusut i olau. Clerval, t'vi bezhun heh feelings vesh' kwon-hau-ov sahris svi' discerning wuh kashan t' vath, declined wuh subject, alleging, svi' tobeg, ish-veh ovus ignorance; heh wuh conversation nem-tor wuh weht paik da-tor. I itaren t'nash-veh t'hy'la s' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, tonk'peh i did ri stariben. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh plainly ik au vesh' ak'wikmun, tonk'peh au worla attempted tor bes-tor t'nash-veh tsat s' me; heh hi i ashau ish-veh k' wuh rish t' affection heh reverence ik fai-tor rai bounds, wi i kupi worla persuade myself tor confide svi' ish-veh ik pavek if vesh' ni k'ashiv la' tor t'nash-veh recollection, tonk'peh if i ptha wuh detail tor wuh'ashiv would goh impress weht deeply. M. Krempe vesh' ri kaing docile; heh svi' t'nash-veh nosh na' ik wak, t' siyah insupportable sensitiveness, ish-veh harsh pasik encomiums mazhiv-kur-tor me kauk weht kusut do wuh benevolent approbation t' m. Waldman. “d—n wuh katravahsu!” maf-tor au; “po, m. Clerval, i assure du au has outstript etek ek'. Ay, nantaya kuv du sanoi; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor nevertheless yeht. Wuh youngster vi, tonk'peh wuh zamu tevun ago, pudva-tor svi' cornelius agrippa u' firmly u' svi' wuh gospel, has i' eku himself na' wuh patam t' wuh university; heh kuv au nam-tor ri ak seshau ne', etek dungau ek' nam-tor s' countenance.—ay, ay, ” fator au, observing t'nash-veh limuk expressive t' suffering, “m. Frankenstein nam-tor modest; wuh marom quality svi' wuh nu'ri sasu. Nu'ri sasu dang nam-tor diffident t' themselves, du fai-tor, m. Clerval: i vesh' myself lu nu'ri; tonk'peh ik sai-vel-tor si' svi' wuh maut pen wak.” m. Krempe had i' palikau wuh krolun fi' himself, if kunling da-tor wuh conversation s' wuh subject ik vesh' ni annoying tor me. Clerval had worla sympathised svi' t'nash-veh zahv-tor na' malatik ek'tal; heh ish-veh literary pursuits differed wholly s' eifa if had occupied me. Au sarlah tor wuh university k' wuh design t' tor himself ovsotik trensu t' wuh oriental gen-lis, heh thus au dang tu'ash wuh vunai na' wuh dotor t' ha'kiv au had pu'ulidau si' na' himself. Resolved tor pursue rai inglorious career, au da-tor ish-veh bezhun na' wuh she'rak, u' affording scope na' ish-veh tam'a t' enterprise. Wuh persian, arabic, heh sanskrit gen-lis engaged ish-veh attention, heh i vesh' easily vimevilau tor svi-tor fi' wuh ka orenau. Idleness had ek'wak vesh' irksome tor me, heh i' ik i istau tor hash-tor s' haulan, heh fnu-ven t'nash-veh former orenau, i olau lo'uk vas svi' hasu wuh katravahsu-glan-sharu k' t'nash-veh t'hy'la, heh afer-tor ri goh instruction tonk'peh consolation svi' wuh ar'kada t' wuh orientalists. I did ri, spo' ish-veh, attempt wuh bolik fai-tukh t' ish-veh dialects, na' i did ri contemplate tor sovek vath nam-tor-tor t' au do rikwonik amusement. I telv-tor goh tor ken-tor ish-veh meaning, heh au muhl repaid t'nash-veh zup-tor. Ish-veh melancholy nam-tor soothing, heh ish-veh mak elevating, tor wuh degree i worla veshtau svi' studying wuh kitausu t' sovek vath shasol. Lu du telv-tor ish-veh kitaun, ha'kiv saudau tor consist svi' wuh lamekh yel heh wuh bah-ker t' roses, —svi' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh kwal-tor t' wuh rom nemut, heh wuh yon ik consumes ish-veh sha' khaf-spol. Uf natya s' wuh manly heh heroical poetry t' greece heh rome! Belaar be' dvun-tor maf svi' aifa occupations, heh t'nash-veh fun tor geneva vesh' teslau na' wuh latter shaht t' tasmin; tonk'peh hasu vohtau k' several kisheya, karil heh izh lasha, wuh fau-yut vesh' deemed impassable, heh t'nash-veh halovaya vesh' retarded abi' wuh ensuing sikar. I olau nash vohtaya maut bitterly; na' i longed tor gla-tor t'nash-veh salatik kahr heh t'nash-veh k'diwa t'hylara. T'nash-veh fun had goh vesh' vohtau ni wu, s' wuh unwillingness tor trasha clerval svi' wuh flekh shi, fa' au had shetau acquainted k' sovek t' its inhabitants. Wuh karil, however, vesh' spent cheerfully; heh hi wuh sikar vesh' uncommonly tab-ma, lu sarlah ish-veh its vaksur torabrau na' its dilatoriness. Wuh tevun-krus t' lau had already palikau, heh i gishu wuh nuhm kanok-gadik if vesh' tor teslau wuh kinuf t' t'nash-veh trashan, lu henry proposed wuh pedestrian tour svi' wuh environs t' ingolstadt, ik i lau nufai wuh personal rom-halan tor wuh shasol i had ni wu inhabited. I acceded k' sanosh tor nash proposition: i vesh' tishau t' tusok, heh clerval had kwon-hau-ov vesh' t'nash-veh favourite besu svi' wuh ramble t' nash malat ik i had taken among wuh scenes t' t'nash-veh salatik shasol. Etek be' dvun-tor wuh fortnight svi' aifa perambulations: t'nash-veh muhl'es heh tam'a had wu vesh' restored, heh au nazh-tor hayaik karik'es s' wuh salubrious sov i breathed, wuh malatik incidents t' etwel progress, heh wuh conversation t' t'nash-veh t'hy'la. Orenau had fa' secluded me s' wuh intercourse t' t'nash-veh katravahsu-creatures, heh rendered me unsocial; tonk'peh clerval puvutau forth wuh weh-rom feelings t' t'nash-veh khaf-spol; au va'ashiv saven-tor me tor ashaya wuh pulva t' malat, heh wuh cheerful limuk t' kanu. Marom t'hy'la! Uf sincerely du did ashaya me, heh endeavour tor ashenau t'nash-veh kashek abi' ish-veh vesh' fi' wuh volik k' ish-veh sha'. Wuh selfish pursuit had runelau heh wonilau me, abi' ish-veh gentleness heh affection warmed heh tu'ash t'nash-veh kash-ral; i became wuh ka kunli creature vi, wuh zamu tevun ago, ashau heh k'diwa k' ek', had rai sorrow il tun. Lu kunli, inanimate malat had wuh tepul t' bestowing fi' me wuh danik delightful kashan. Wuh serene igen heh verdant vunai boshau me k' prahk'es. Wuh la' tevun-yonuk vesh' indeed ekonik; wuh svai t' sikar svai-tor svi' wuh labah, du' eifa t' belaar vesh' already svi' bud. I vesh' undisturbed k' nahp if du' wuh preceding tevun had hish-tor fi-tor me, notwithstanding t'nash-veh endeavours tor lehm au ska', k' wuh invincible burden. Henry rejoiced svi' t'nash-veh gaiety, heh sincerely sympathised svi' t'nash-veh feelings: au pidesh himself tor amuse me, du' au sagluvau wuh kashan ik boshau ish-veh soul. Wuh resources t' ish-veh kashek fi' nash occasion vesh' truly astonishing: ish-veh conversation vesh' bosh t' glenonaya; heh maut k'ashiv, svi' imitation t' wuh persian heh arabic kitausu, au fereik-tor var t' wonderful fancy heh shaukaush. Na' vath wak au ashiv-tor t'nash-veh favourite poems, il drew me si' vi' nerau-kek-vuhnayek, if au nenikau k' lo'uk ingenuity. Etek fun-tor tor etwel college fi' wuh gad aru: wuh peasants vesh' taman, heh kanok veh etek ragel-tor saudau sa-ka-ashausu heh kunli. T'nash-veh sha' tam'a vesh' pid, heh i bounded bi' k' feelings t' unbridled mak heh hilarity. Chapter 7 fi' t'nash-veh fun, i afer-tor wuh zahalik nuhm s' t'nash-veh sa-mekh: — “t'nash-veh tal-kam skilsu, “du ma probably bek-tor impatiently na' wuh nuhm tor teslau wuh kinuf t' ish-veh fun tor etek; heh i vesh' palikauk tempted tor kitau goh wuh zamu zehl, goh mentioning wuh gad fi' if i dang gish du. Tonk'peh ik would nam-tor wuh pi-maat'rer kindness, heh i dare ri tor ish-veh. Ra would nam-tor ish-veh ak'wikmun, t'nash-veh sa-fu, lu du gishu wuh kunli heh glad welcome, tor behold, fi' wuh contrary, bezhun-masu heh wretchedness? Heh uf, skilsu, mokuhlek i relate etwel misfortune? Absence fam yehat ma rendered du callous tor etwel mak heh griefs; heh uf dungau i inflict kusut fi' t'nash-veh wu tadek-adir sa-fu? I istaya tor dator du na' wuh woeful ro'fori, tonk'peh i fai-tor ish-veh nam-tor impossible; kauk i' ish-veh bezhun skims abru' wuh thalv tor seek wuh zhit if nam-tor tor zhelesh tor du wuh horrible tidings. “william nam-tor tevik!—ik slor kan, t'vi abru'teruklar-ru'lut delighted heh warmed t'nash-veh khaf-spol, vi vesh' ni gentle, wi ni sa-ka-ashausu! Skilsu, au nam-tor riyeht-stau! “i dungi ri attempt tor console du; tonk'peh dungi veling relate wuh circumstances t' wuh transaction. “kim-shah gad (lau 7th), i, t'nash-veh ko-bath, heh ish-veh dahkuh sa-kai, went tor lates svi' plainpalais. Wuh khru vesh' lamekh heh serene, heh etek prolonged etwel lates weh-irak do tsuri. Ish-veh vesh' already dusk fa' etek nahp t' returning; heh yi etek discovered ik william heh ernest, vi had hal-tor fi' fa', vesh' ri tor nam-tor afer-tor. Etek accordingly shom-tor fi' wuh ku-san abi' au dang fun. Presently ernest sarlah, heh enquired kuv etek had gla-tor ish-veh sa-kai; au leralmin-tor, ik au had vesh' mavaun k' ish-veh, ik william had sahr-tor maf tor ip-sut himself, heh ik au vainly sought na' ish-veh, heh afterwards bek-tor na' wuh akarshif, tonk'peh ik au did ri fun. “nash khrosahp rather alarmed etek, heh etek fator tor psthan na' ish-veh abi' mu-yor tevan-tor, lu elizabeth conjectured ik au lau ma fun-tor tor wuh kelek. Au vesh' ri tra'. Etek fun-tor va'ashiv, k' torches; na' i kupi ri shom, lu i nahp ik t'nash-veh slor sa-kan had pakik himself, heh vesh' ko'nar tor ek' wuh damps heh dews t' mu-yor; elizabeth isha dashau mairik thonaya. Pa' kaukuh svi' wuh asal i discovered t'nash-veh lovely sa-kan, ik wuh mu-yor fa' i had gla-tor svai-tu-ashya heh torupik svi' muhl'es, sakadau fi' wuh yar livid heh motionless; wuh hish t' wuh riyeht-staya’s ozh vesh' fi' ish-veh talu. “au vesh' zhelesh ha-kel, heh wuh thonaya ik vesh' visible svi' t'nash-veh countenance pusvik-tor wuh tsat tor elizabeth. She vesh' maut earnest tor gla-tor wuh tevikeh. Palikauk i attempted tor prevent ish-veh tonk'peh she persisted, heh entering wuh tvi-shal wilat ish-veh ti, hastily linisau wuh talu t' wuh shi-kar-tor, heh clasping ish-veh el'ru sporiben, ‘o oekon! I ma riyeht-stau t'nash-veh ashal-veh kan!’ “she fainted, heh vesh' restored k' mairik rihag'es. Lu she va'ashiv ha-tor, ish-veh vesh' goh tor tusa heh spes-tevan. She var-tor me, ik ik ka khru william had teased ish-veh tor kal-tor ish-veh sai-vel-tor wuh maut taluhk miniature ik she ma t' ish-veh ko-mekh. Nash bikuv nam-tor hal-tor, heh vesh' doubtless wuh temptation if urged wuh murderer tor wuh deed. Etek ma rai zavikau t' ish-veh na' la', hi etwel pideshan tor discover ish-veh nam-tor unremitted; tonk'peh au dungi ri restore t'nash-veh k'diwa william! “sarlah, dearest skilsu; du sa'awek mokuhlek console elizabeth. She tusa-tor continually, heh accuses herself unjustly u' wuh aishan t' ish-veh tevakh; ish-veh zhit tilau t'nash-veh khaf-spol. Etek nam-tor ek' unhappy; tonk'peh dungi ri ik nam-tor wuh hayaik dvubolek na' du, t'nash-veh sa-fu, tor fun heh nam-tor etwel comforter? Ish-veh tal-kam ko-mekh! Alas, skilsu! I i' leralmin, itaren oekon she did ri ha-tor tor toglantausu wuh pi-maat'rer, miserable tevakh t' ish-veh youngest ashal-veh! “sarlah, skilsu; ri brooding nahp t' vengeance tehnat wuh assassin, tonk'peh k' feelings t' sochya heh gentleness, ik dungi hakau, instead t' festering, wuh skek t' etwel kashkau. Svi-tor wuh kelek t' mourning, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, tonk'peh k' kindness heh affection na' eifa vi ashaya du, heh ri k' hatred na' ish-veh nemut. “ish-veh affectionate heh afflicted sa-mekh, “alphonse frankenstein. “geneva, lau 12th, 17—.” clerval, vi had glantau t'nash-veh countenance u' i telv-tor nash nuhm, vesh' ak'wikmun tor glantau wuh despair ik navau wuh mak i palikauk sagluvau fi' receiving uzh s' t'nash-veh t'hylara. I threw wuh nuhm fi' wuh pasu, heh wein-tor t'nash-veh limuk k' t'nash-veh el'ru. “t'nash-veh tal-kam frankenstein, ” sporiben henry, lu au pakashogau me tusa k' bitterness, “nam-tor du kwon-hau-ov tor nam-tor unhappy? T'nash-veh tal-kam t'hy'la, ra has pavesh-tor?” i motioned ish-veh tor nem-tor abru wuh nuhm, du' i lates-tor abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal svi' wuh extremest agitation. Bezhun-masu isha gushed s' wuh bezhun t' clerval, u' au telv-tor wuh khrosahp t' t'nash-veh misfortune. “i mokuhlek nufai du rai consolation, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, ” leralmin-tor au; “ish-veh koshvar nam-tor irreparable. Ra tor du intend tor tor?” “tor hal-tor instantly tor geneva: sarlah k' me, henry, tor zek wuh jarel.” du' etwel lates, clerval endeavoured tor leralmin wuh zamu zhit t' consolation; au kupi goh sagluvau ish-veh heartfelt sympathy. “ri donku-tor william!” leralmin-tor au, “tal-kam lovely kan, au i' sleeps k' ish-veh ha'su ko-mekh! Vi ik had gla-tor ish-veh ugelik heh joyous svi' ish-veh nu'ri vaksur, tonk'peh bolau tusa abru' ish-veh untimely pak! Tor tev-tor ni miserably; tor olau wuh murderer’s ruskaraya! Uf mau weht wuh riyeht-stau ik kupi vashau radiant innocence! Ri donku-tor pi' katravahsu! Veh goh consolation ma etek; ish-veh t'hylara la'tusa heh tusa, tonk'peh au nam-tor na' shom. Wuh pang nam-tor abru', ish-veh sufferings nam-tor na' wuh shaht na' ek'wak. Wuh sod wein-tor ish-veh gentle shid, heh au fai-tor rai kusut. Au mokuhlek rai longer nam-tor wuh subject na' pity; etek bolau reserve ik na' ish-veh miserable survivors.” clerval stariben thus u' etek hurried k'fai wuh yut; wuh zhit impressed themselves fi' t'nash-veh kashek heh i vokau au afterwards svi' awek'es. Tonk'peh i', u' ak u' wuh jarel lasha, i hurried vi' wuh cabriolet, heh bade rom-halan tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la. T'nash-veh halovaya vesh' maut melancholy. Palikauk i istau tor brax fi', na' i longed tor console heh sympathise k' t'nash-veh ashau heh sorrowing t'hylara; tonk'peh lu i drew be' t'nash-veh salatik kahr, i slackened t'nash-veh progress. I kupi hardly potun-tor wuh multitude t' feelings ik crowded vi' t'nash-veh kashek. I be' dvun-tor k'fai scenes familiar tor t'nash-veh youth, tonk'peh if i had ri gla-tor na' nearly shehkuh tevun. Uf rubitau kanok vel lau nam-tor du' ik wak! Veh sudden heh desolating rubah had taken shi; tonk'peh wuh thousand pi' circumstances lau ma k' degrees ar'kada vath alterations, if, hi au vesh' ovsoh weht tranquilly, lau ri nam-tor wuh lehkuh decisive. Pthak overcame me; i dared rai storilaya, dreading wuh thousand nameless ek'rasah ik tor me tremble, hi i vesh' unable tor mesprah au. I hafau dahkuh gad na' lausanne, svi' nash kusut-tor fupa s' t' kashek. I contemplated wuh suk'muzh: wuh mashau vesh' placid; ek' pa' vesh' hayal; heh wuh snowy suk'kunel, “wuh palaces t' malat, ” vesh' ri rubai. K' degrees wuh hayal heh heavenly scene restored me, heh i fator t'nash-veh halovaya na' geneva. Wuh fau-yut sahr-tor k' wuh vla t' wuh suk'muzh, if became narrower u' i betau t'nash-veh salatik kahr. I discovered weht distinctly wuh nesh-kur vla t' jura, heh wuh ugelik dan-pid-sfek t' mont blanc. I wept spo' wuh kan. “tal-kam suk'kunel! T'nash-veh sha' vaksurik suk'muzh! Uf tor du welcome ish-veh wanderer? Ish-veh dan-pid-sfek nam-tor pa'shik; wuh igen heh suk'muzh nam-tor pla-kur heh placid. Nam-tor nash tor prognosticate sochya, il tor mock na' t'nash-veh unhappiness?” i pthak, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, ik i dungau render myself tedious k' kelek fi' aifa preliminary circumstances; tonk'peh au vesh' gad t' comparative happiness, heh i nah-tor t' au k' sanosh. T'nash-veh shasol, t'nash-veh k'diwa shasol! Vi tonk'peh wuh salatik mokuhlek var-tor wuh delight i nem-tor svi' va'ashiv beholding thy pilash, thy suk'kunel, heh, weht do ek', thy lovely suk'muzh! Wi, u' i drew nearer ha-kel, tushat heh pthak va'ashiv overcame me. Mu-yor isha a'ing pa'; heh lu i kupi hardly gla-tor wuh gu'gelik suk'kunel, i olau fam dvun weht gloomily. Wuh bikuv saudau wuh vast heh neik-ha'khlup scene t' ek'rasah, heh i foresaw obscurely ik i vesh' destined tor shetau wuh danik wretched t' komihn beings. Alas! I prophesied truly, heh vravshau goh svi' veh single circumstance, ik svi' ek' wuh misery i glenonau heh dreaded, i did ri conceive wuh hundredth krus t' wuh thonaya i vesh' destined tor palesh-tor. Ish-veh vesh' completely gu'gelik lu i lasha svi' wuh environs t' geneva; wuh temep t' wuh kahr vesh' already ikap-tor; heh i vesh' obliged tor be' dvun wuh mu-yor na' secheron, wuh pi'kahr na' wuh ir t' ulef wuh league s' wuh kahr. Wuh igen vesh' serene; heh, u' i vesh' unable tor shom, i resolved tor yaret wuh gla-tor wilat t'nash-veh ri donku-tor william had vesh' riyeht-stau. U' i kupi ri be' dvun k'fai wuh kahr, i vesh' obliged tor tuhs wuh suk'muzh svi' wuh masu-hali tor lasha na' plainpalais. Du' nash pen halan vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh igen-wesh mavaun fi' wuh dan-pid-sfek t' mont blanc svi' wuh danik vaksurik khlop. Wuh sahriv saudau tor betaya rapidly, heh, fi' landing, i she-tor wuh neik kunel, ik i lau glantau its progress. Ish-veh storilau; wuh heavens vesh' clouded, heh i ak olau wuh sov-masu coming slowly svi' suk eku-tor, tonk'peh its khrash sahris increased. I quitted t'nash-veh ku-san, heh lates-tor fi', hi wuh mu'khlup'es heh sahriv increased kanok minute, heh wuh rahm thorau k' wuh terrific tevul abru' t'nash-veh patam. Ish-veh vesh' echoed s' salêve, wuh juras, heh wuh alps t' savoy; vivid kahai t' igen-wesh dazzled t'nash-veh bezhun, illuminating wuh suk'muzh, tor ish-veh saudau spo' wuh vast thalv t' yon; yi na' wuh instant kanok vel seemed t' wuh pitchy mu'khlup'es, abi' wuh bezhun recovered itself s' wuh preceding kahai. Wuh sahriv, u' nam-tor k'ashiv wuh nuf svi' switzerland, saudau na' wuh'wak svi' vuhnauk krus t' wuh heavens. Wuh danik khrashik sahriv geldau exactly desh'rak t' wuh kahr, abru' wuh krus t' wuh suk'muzh if ti svi' wuh promontory t' belrive heh wuh pi'kahr t' copêt. Wuh'ashiv sahriv enlightened jura k' faint kahai; heh wuh'ashiv mu'glau heh sometimes disclosed wuh môle, wuh peaked suk'kunel tor wuh she'rak t' wuh suk'muzh. Du' i glantau wuh tempest, ni vaksurik wi terrific, i czar-tor fi' k' wuh hasty ash. Nash thol t'naehm svi' wuh igen ashenau t'nash-veh tam'a; i clasped t'nash-veh el'ru, heh sporiben aloud, “william, tal-kam ha'su! Nash nam-tor thy mem-lu til-kum, nash thy dirge!” u' i leralmin-tor aifa zhit, i pakashogau svi' wuh gloom wuh khlop if vazgau s' za' wuh clump t' lap be' me; i lam-tor teslau, gazing intently: i kupi ri nam-tor mistaken. Wuh kahai t' igen-wesh illuminated wuh vel, heh discovered its shid plainly tor me; its masuk' stature, heh wuh riyeht-shid'es t' its pulva weht hideous do belongs tor humanity, instantly informed me ik ish-veh vesh' wuh wretch, wuh filthy dæmon, tor ik i had putan-tor ha'kiv. Ra did au tra'? Kupi au nam-tor (i ak'shem-hutau na' wuh conception) wuh murderer t' t'nash-veh sa-kai? Rai sooner did ik idea tuhs t'nash-veh glenonaya, do i became convinced t' its yeht'es; t'nash-veh zud chattered, heh i vesh' punekwitau tor galat tehnat wuh lap na' nenikaya. Wuh khlop be' dvun-tor me sahris, heh i pakik ish-veh svi' wuh gloom. Nothing svi' komihn shid kupi ma vashau wuh rom kan. _he_ vesh' wuh murderer! I kupi ri vet ish-veh. Wuh mere la'es t' wuh idea vesh' wuh irresistible skan t' wuh kla-min. I nahp t' pursuing wuh e'shua; tonk'peh ish-veh would ma vesh' svi' vain, na' wuh'ashiv kahai discovered ish-veh tor me hanging among wuh kov t' wuh nearly sazehik shen t' mont salêve, wuh kunel ik bounds plainpalais fi' wuh khu'rak. Au ak pulau wuh dan-pid-sfek, heh sasaudau. I hafau motionless. Wuh rahm ceased; tonk'peh wuh sov-masu fam dvun fator, heh wuh scene vesh' enveloped svi' wuh impenetrable mu'khlup'es. I revolved svi' t'nash-veh kashek wuh pavek if i had abi' i' sought tor yen-tor: wuh bosh ranau t' t'nash-veh progress na' wuh fereikan; wuh appearance t' wuh ar'kada t' t'nash-veh sha' el'ru na' t'nash-veh bedside; its trashan. Dahkuh tevun had i' nearly veshau opi' wuh mu-yor fi' if au wuh'rak poprah ha'kiv; heh vesh' nash ish-veh wuh'rak tr'y'kak? Alas! I had da-tor thal vi' wuh panu wuh depraved wretch, t'vi delight vesh' svi' carnage heh misery; had au ri riyeht-stau t'nash-veh sa-kai? Kling mokuhlek conceive wuh thonaya i dashau du' wuh hafayat t' wuh mu-yor, if i spent, samu heh masupik, svi' wuh tu'ash sov. Tonk'peh i did ri olau wuh inconvenience t' wuh igen-va; t'nash-veh glenonaya vesh' toranik svi' scenes t' ek'rasah heh despair. I panah-tor wuh hasu ik i had vishizhau among mankind, heh endowed k' wuh dungi heh tepul tor daya lof t' horror, such u' wuh deed if au had i' ovsoh, nearly svi' wuh ta'hal t' t'nash-veh sha' vampire, t'nash-veh sha' tam'a kal-tor thal s' wuh shi'vukhut, heh punekwitau tor vashau ek' ik vesh' tal-kam tor me. Gad dawned; heh i khartau t'nash-veh ash-tor na' wuh kahr. Wuh temep vesh' tu'ash, heh i hastened tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s kelek. T'nash-veh wuh'rak nahp vesh' tor discover ra i fai-tor t' wuh murderer, heh aishan instant pursuit tor nam-tor tor. Tonk'peh i svizh-tor lu i haul-tor fi' wuh var ik i had tor var-tor. Wuh hasu ik i myself had shidau, heh endued k' ha'kiv, had ragel-tor me na' midnight among wuh precipices t' wuh inaccessible suk'kunel. I vokau isha wuh nervous tau k' if i had vesh' seized aishan na' wuh wak ik i dated t'nash-veh fereikan, heh if would mazhiv-kur-tor wuh sov t' delirium tor wuh var vathru ni utterly improbable. I muhl fai-tor ik kuv sovek vath had sviribau such wuh relation tor me, i dang ma glazhau fi-tor ish-veh u' wuh ravings t' riyeht-kashik. Isha, wuh flekh malat t' wuh aushfa would savlau ek' pursuit, kauk kuv i vesh' ni irak credited u' tor persuade t'nash-veh tomasu tor palikau ish-veh. Heh yi t' ra nam-tor-tor would nam-tor pursuit? Vi kupi pehkaya wuh creature capable t' scaling wuh overhanging vla t' mont salêve? Aifa haulan satalau me, heh i resolved tor hafau ralash-fam. Ish-veh vesh' pa' kaukuh svi' wuh asal lu i svi-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s kelek. I var-tor wuh dvinsu ri tor ertau wuh skan, heh went vi' wuh shi'dunap tor attend ish-veh tsuri wadan t' rising. Shehkuh tevun had veshau, be' dvun-tor svi' wuh sahr-tor tonk'peh na' veh indelible zavikau, heh i lam-tor svi' wuh ka shi wilat i had kim-shah nartau t'nash-veh sa-mekh fa' t'nash-veh trashan na' ingolstadt. K'diwa heh venerable parent! Au fam dvun hafau tor me. I gazed fi' wuh bikuv t' t'nash-veh ko-mekh, if lam-tor abru' wuh mantel-krus. Ish-veh vesh' wuh historical subject, kras-tor na' t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s aitlun, heh represented caroline beaufort svi' wuh agony t' despair, kneeling k' wuh tevikeh-natuhn t' ish-veh tevik sa-mekh. Ish-veh garb vesh' rustic, heh ish-veh nak spoh; tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh sov t' dignity heh vaksur, ik hardly permitted wuh sentiment t' pity. Ne' nash bikuv vesh' wuh miniature t' william; heh t'nash-veh bezhun-masu yumau lu i glazhau fi-tor ish-veh. Du' i vesh' thus engaged, ernest svi-tor: au had puzhu-tor me lasha, heh hastened tor welcome me: “welcome, t'nash-veh dearest skilsu, ” leralmin-tor au. “ah! I istaya du had sarlah rehkuh tevun-krus ago, heh yi du would ma afer-tor etek ek' joyous heh delighted. Sarlah du tor etek i' tor thresh wuh misery if nothing mokuhlek alleviate; wi ish-veh la'es dungi, i rok, zaprah etwel sa-mekh, vi seems sinking ne' ish-veh misfortune; heh ish-veh persuasions dungi vimevilau ri donku-tor elizabeth tor cease ish-veh vain heh tormenting shal-accusations.—ri donku-tor william! Au vesh' etwel ashal-veh heh etwel pride!” bezhun-masu, unrestrained, tevan-tor s' t'nash-veh sa-kai’s bezhun; wuh kash-ral t' mortal agony crept abru' t'nash-veh nentu. Fa', i had goh glenonau wuh wretchedness t' t'nash-veh desolated ha-kel; wuh reality sarlah fi' me u' wuh uzh, heh wuh ri lehkuh terrible, koshvar. I ar'kada tor hayal ernest; i enquired weht minutely fundik t'nash-veh sa-mekh, heh la' i ahmau t'nash-veh krei. “she danik t' ek', ” leralmin-tor ernest, “requires consolation; she accused herself t' having aisha wuh tevakh t' t'nash-veh sa-kai, heh ik tor ish-veh maut wretched. Tonk'peh opi' wuh murderer has vesh' discovered—” “wuh murderer discovered! Rom oekon! Uf mokuhlek ik nam-tor? Vi kupi attempt tor pursue ish-veh? Ish-veh nam-tor impossible; veh lau u' muhl ar'kadan tor overtake wuh salan, il confine wuh suk'kunel-pilash k' wuh terp. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh nuh'; au vesh' elik kim-shah mu-yor!” “i ri tor fai-tor ra du tvai, ” kilko-tor t'nash-veh sa-kai, svi' accents t' wonder, “tonk'peh tor etek wuh discovery etek ma tor ovsoh etwel misery. Rai veh would dva-tor ish-veh palikauk; heh kauk i' elizabeth dungi ri nam-tor convinced, notwithstanding ek' wuh evidence. Indeed, vi would lit ik justine moritz, vi vesh' ni amiable, heh tishau t' ek' wuh skan, kupi suddenly shetau ni capable t' ni frightful, ni appalling wuh tr'y'kak?” “justine moritz! Ri donku-tor, ri donku-tor ko-kan, nam-tor she wuh accused? Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor wrongfully; kanok veh fai-tor ik; kling believes ish-veh, surely, ernest?” “kling did palikauk; tonk'peh several circumstances sasarlah, ik ma siyah punekwitau conviction fi-tor etek; heh ish-veh sha' kloshai has vesh' ni confused, u' tor hau tor wuh evidence t' kla-min wuh rasath ik, i pthak, mor rai rok na' vet. Tonk'peh she dungi nam-tor ar'kada nash-gad, heh du dungi yi zhu-tor ek'.” au yi related ik, wuh asal fi' if wuh riyeht-staya t' ri donku-tor william had vesh' discovered, justine had vesh' taken has-bosh, heh confined tor ish-veh sar-tak na' several gad. Du' nash tvi-wak, veh t' wuh dvinsu, aisha tor linisau wuh apparel she had worn fi' wuh mu-yor t' wuh riyeht-staya, had discovered svi' ish-veh abru'lik wuh bikuv t' t'nash-veh ko-mekh, if had vesh' judged tor nam-tor wuh temptation t' wuh murderer. Wuh dvinsu instantly gluvau ish-veh tor veh t' wuh vath, vi, rik' taran wuh zhit tor sovek t' wuh skan, went tor wuh magistrate; heh, fi-tor ish-veh deposition, justine vesh' apprehended. Fi' hasu vifalunau k' wuh kla-min, wuh ri donku-tor ko-kan wugau wuh suspicion svi' wuh lo'uk thon-tor k' ish-veh mairik confusion t' manner. Nash vesh' wuh flekh var, tonk'peh ish-veh did ri hutau t'nash-veh odva; heh i kilko-tor earnestly, “du nam-tor ek' mistaken; i fai-tor wuh murderer. Justine, ri donku-tor, rom justine, nam-tor innocent.” na' ik instant t'nash-veh sa-mekh svi-tor. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh unhappiness deeply impressed fi' ish-veh countenance, tonk'peh au endeavoured tor welcome me cheerfully; heh, po' etek had di'kizh-tor etwel mournful na'shaya, would ma puragtau ein vath ong do ik t' etwel koshvar, had ri ernest sporiben, “rom oekon, papa! Skilsu leralmin-tor ik au fai-tor vi vesh' wuh murderer t' ri donku-tor william.” “etek tor isha, unfortunately, ” kilko-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh, “na' indeed i had rather ma vesh' na' ek'wak ignorant do ma discovered ni mau depravity heh ungratitude svi' veh i valued ni highly.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-mekh, du nam-tor mistaken; justine nam-tor innocent.” “kuv she nam-tor, oekon zadau ik she dang dash u' guilty. She nam-tor tor nam-tor ar'kada nash-gad, heh i rok, i sincerely rok, ik she dungi nam-tor acquitted.” nash starun hayal me. I vesh' firmly convinced svi' t'nash-veh sha' kashek ik justine, heh indeed kanok komihn hasu, vesh' guiltless t' nash riyeht-staya. I had rai pthak, therefore, ik sovek circumstantial evidence kupi nam-tor katau fa'rak karik hiyet tor convict ish-veh. T'nash-veh var vesh' ri veh tor tor'pra publicly; its astounding horror would nam-tor glazhau fi-tor u' ni-resh k' wuh vulgar. Did sovek veh indeed nam-tor, kaula i, wuh fereiksu, vi would dva-tor, vita ish-veh kash-ral convinced ish-veh, svi' wuh nam t' wuh living monument t' presumption heh kuriht ignorance if i had kal-tor thal fi-tor wuh panu? Etek vesh' ak hau k' elizabeth. Wak had rubitau ish-veh opi' i kim-shah beheld ish-veh; ish-veh had endowed ish-veh k' loveliness surpassing wuh vaksur t' ish-veh childish tevun. Tra' vesh' wuh ka candour, wuh ka vivacity, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' puk'ai'la tor wuh sagluvaya weht bosh t' sensibility heh kash-tor-vel. She welcomed me k' wuh greatest affection. “ish-veh lashan, t'nash-veh tal-kam krei, ” leralmin-tor she, “boshau me k' rok. Du sos'eh dungi talal ein tvai tor justify t'nash-veh ri donku-tor guiltless justine. Alas! Vi nam-tor safe, kuv she nam-tor convicted t' tr'y'kak? I rely fi' ish-veh innocence u' certainly u' i tor fi-tor t'nash-veh sha'. Etwel misfortune nam-tor doubly lerash tor etek; etek ma ri goh pakik ik lovely ashal-veh sa-kan, tonk'peh nash ri donku-tor ko-kan, ik i sincerely ashaya, nam-tor tor nam-tor torn maf k' kauk wuh weh-rasahkos buk. Kuv she nam-tor condemned, i worla dungau fai-tor mak weht. Tonk'peh she dungi ri, i am sure she dungi ri; heh yi i dungau nam-tor kunli va'ashiv, kauk po' wuh maf tevakh t' t'nash-veh pi' william.” “she nam-tor innocent, t'nash-veh elizabeth, ” leralmin-tor i, “heh ik dungau nam-tor skan-tor; pthak nothing, tonk'peh kal-tor ish-veh tam'a nam-tor cheered k' wuh assurance t' ish-veh acquittal.” “uf ves heh generous du nam-tor! Kanok veh else believes svi' ish-veh guilt, heh ik tor me wretched, na' i fai-tor ik ish-veh vesh' impossible: heh tor gla-tor kanok veh else prejudiced svi' ni tevalik wuh manner rendered me hopeless heh despairing.” she wept. “dearest ko-bath, ” leralmin-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh, “pseth ish-veh bezhun-masu. Kuv she nam-tor, u' du dva-tor, innocent, rely fi' wuh yeht-gav t' etwel tor-gav, heh wuh toran k' if i dungau prevent wuh slightest duv t' partiality.” chapter 8 etek be' dvun-tor wuh zamu maf wadan abi' leh-wun o’wak-vel, lu wuh trial vesh' tor palikau. T'nash-veh sa-mekh heh wuh shom t' wuh skan hasu obliged tor attend u' toglantausu, i accompanied au tor wuh kelek. Du' wuh bosh t' nash wretched mockery t' yeht-gav i dashau living torture. Ish-veh vesh' tor nam-tor klopau whether wuh result t' t'nash-veh curiosity heh lawless el'mish would aishan wuh tevakh t' dahkuh t' t'nash-veh katravahsu beings: veh wuh smiling babe bosh t' innocence heh mak, wuh vath irak weht dreadfully riyeht-stau, k' kanok aggravation t' infamy ik kupi tor wuh riyeht-staya memorable svi' horror. Justine isha vesh' wuh ko-kan t' merit heh ma qualities if ugau tor render ish-veh ha'kiv kunli; i' ek' vesh' tor nam-tor obliterated svi' wuh ignominious shi'vukhut, heh i wuh aishan! Wuh thousand wak rather would i ma confessed myself guilty t' wuh tr'y'kak ascribed tor justine, tonk'peh i vesh' tadek-adir lu ish-veh vesh' committed, heh such wuh afsakaya would ma vesh' panah-tor u' wuh ravings t' wuh madman heh would ri ma exculpated ish-veh vi dashau k'fai me. Wuh appearance t' justine vesh' hayal. She vesh' sai-vel-tor svi' mourning, heh ish-veh countenance, kwon-hau-ov engaging, vesh' rendered, k' wuh solemnity t' ish-veh feelings, exquisitely vaksurik. Wi she saudau confident svi' innocence heh did ri tremble, hi gazed fi' heh execrated k' thousands, na' ek' wuh kindness if ish-veh vaksur lau vathru ma teporilau vesh' obliterated svi' wuh kashkau t' wuh spectators k' wuh glenonaya t' wuh enormity she vesh' supposed ki' committed. She vesh' tranquil, wi ish-veh tranquillity vesh' evidently constrained; heh u' ish-veh confusion had fa' vesh' adduced u' wuh skan t' ish-veh guilt, she ar'kada abru ish-veh kashek tor wuh appearance t' courage. Lu she svi-tor wuh kelek she threw ish-veh bezhun pauk ish-veh heh sahris discovered wilat etek vesh' hayal-tor. Wuh bezhun-masu seemed tor neik-ha'khlup ish-veh bezhun lu gla-tor ish-veh etek, tonk'peh she sahris recovered herself, heh wuh glazhau t' sorrowful affection seemed tor attest ish-veh utter guiltlessness. Wuh trial began, heh po' wuh advocate tehnat ish-veh had fupa s' wuh falun, several toglantausu vesh' puvutau. Several flekh kla-min puterish-tor tehnat ish-veh, if lau ma staggered sovek-veh vi had ri such skan t' ish-veh innocence u' i had. She had vesh' si' wuh bosh t' wuh mu-yor fi' if wuh riyeht-staya had vesh' committed heh na' asal had vesh' pakashogau k' wuh mahr-kel-kosu ri irak s' wuh gla-tor wilat wuh ak'shem t' wuh riyeht-stau kan had vesh' afterwards afer-tor. Wuh kosu ya'akash ish-veh ra she did tra', tonk'peh she glazhau maut strangely heh goh fun-tor wuh confused heh unintelligible kilko-srashiv. She fun-tor tor wuh kelek pa' ohkuh o’wak-vel, heh lu veh inquired wilat she had be' dvun-tor wuh mu-yor, she kilko-tor ik she had vesh' looking na' wuh kan heh halishau earnestly kuv sovek-vel had vesh' puzhu-tor fundik ish-veh. Lu shown wuh ak'shem, she tevan-tor vi' khrashik hysterics heh potau ish-veh sar-tak na' several gad. Wuh bikuv vesh' yi torvau if wuh dvinsu had afer-tor svi' ish-veh abru'lik; heh lu elizabeth, svi' wuh faltering spes, skan-tor ik ish-veh vesh' wuh ka if, wuh wadan fa' wuh kan had vesh' din-tor, she had shitau pauk ish-veh talu, wuh murmur t' horror heh indignation boshau wuh kelek. Justine vesh' puvutau fi' na' ish-veh defence. U' wuh trial had proceeded, ish-veh countenance had rubitau. Ak'wikmun, horror, heh misery vesh' strongly sagluvau. Sometimes she struggled k' ish-veh bezhun-masu, tonk'peh lu she vesh' aitlu tor plead, she tershau ish-veh tepul heh stariben svi' wuh zhu-yehat hi vuhnayek spes. “oekon fai-tor, ” she leralmin-tor, “uf entirely i am innocent. Tonk'peh i ri tor pretend ik t'nash-veh protestations dang acquit me; i shom t'nash-veh innocence fi' wuh eiktra heh velik danaya t' wuh kla-min if ma vesh' adduced tehnat me, heh i rok wuh character i ma kwon-hau-ov borne dungi vul t'nash-veh judges tor wuh favourable interpretation wilat sovek circumstance saudau vet-bosh il suspicious.” she yi related ik, k' wuh permission t' elizabeth, she had be' dvun-tor wuh khru t' wuh mu-yor fi' if wuh riyeht-staya had vesh' committed na' wuh kelek t' wuh ezyet na' chêne, wuh pi'kahr situated na' pa' wuh league s' geneva. Fi' ish-veh fun, na' pa' naukuh o’wak-vel, she ragel-tor wuh sasu vi ya'akash ish-veh kuv she had gla-tor sovek-vel t' wuh kan vi vesh' pakik. She vesh' alarmed k' nash khrosahp heh be' dvun-tor several wadan svi' looking na' ish-veh, lu wuh temep t' geneva vesh' ikap-tor, heh she vesh' punekwitau tor hafau several wadan t' wuh mu-yor svi' wuh aushfa-kel t' wuh cottage, hasu unwilling tor vutau abru wuh inhabitants, tor ik she vesh' muhl fainu. Danik t' wuh mu-yor she spent la' watching; na' asal she pudva-tor ik she yuk-tor na' wuh zamu minutes; ein ash-tor ertau ish-veh, heh she awoke. Ish-veh vesh' gad-keshtan, heh she quitted ish-veh asylum, ik she lau va'ashiv endeavour tor talal t'nash-veh sa-kai. Kuv she had hal-tor be' wuh gla-tor wilat ish-veh ak'shem ti, ish-veh vesh' rik' ish-veh fai-tukh. Ik she had vesh' bewildered lu deshkau k' wuh mahr-kel-kosu vesh' ri surprising, opi' she had be' dvun-tor wuh sleepless mu-yor heh wuh buk t' ri donku-tor william vesh' wi uncertain. Fundik wuh bikuv she kupi mazhiv-kur-tor rai khrosahp. “i fai-tor, ” fator wuh unhappy shi-kar-tor, “uf heavily heh fatally nash-veh circumstance rasathau tehnat me, tonk'peh i ma rai tepul t' explaining ish-veh; heh lu i ma sagluvau t'nash-veh utter ignorance, i am goh losrak tor conjecture fundik wuh yesik'es k' if ish-veh lau ma vesh' shitau svi' t'nash-veh abru'lik. Tonk'peh la' isha i am rihamau. I dva-tor ik i ma rai nemut fi' terra, heh rim surely would ma vesh' ni wicked u' tor vashau me wantonly. Did wuh murderer shi ish-veh tra'? I fai-tor t' rai opportunity afforded ish-veh na' ni doing; il, kuv i had, po dang au ma stolen wuh ek'zer, tor krus k' ish-veh va'ashiv ni ak? “i kugau t'nash-veh aishan tor wuh yeht-gav t' t'nash-veh judges, wi gla-tor nash-veh rai tvi-shal na' rok. I eit'jae permission ki' wuh zamu toglantausu linisau fundik t'nash-veh character, heh kuv ish-veh testimony dungau ri overweigh t'nash-veh supposed guilt, i bolau nam-tor condemned, hi i would pledge t'nash-veh korsovaya fi' t'nash-veh innocence.” several toglantausu vesh' puvutau vi had fainu ish-veh na' wehk tevun, heh au stariben muhl t' ish-veh; tonk'peh pthak heh hatred t' wuh tr'y'kak t' if au supposed ish-veh guilty rendered au timorous heh unwilling tor sarlah fa'rak. Elizabeth gla-tor kauk nash kim-shah resource, ish-veh marom dispositions heh irreproachable spa-tor, pa' tor vravshau wuh accused, lu, hi violently pahutau, she aitlu permission tor shi'yavekh wuh kelek. “i am, ” leralmin-tor she, “wuh krei t' wuh unhappy kan vi vesh' riyeht-stau, il rather ish-veh ko-kai, na' i vesh' educated k' heh ma ha-tor k' ish-veh mekhlar ek'wak opi' heh kauk wu fa' ish-veh keshtan. Ish-veh lau therefore nam-tor judged indecent svi' me tor sarlah fa'rak fi' nash occasion, tonk'peh lu gla-tor nash-veh wuh katravahsu creature pa' tor perish k'fai wuh cowardice t' ish-veh pretended t'hylara, i istaya tor nam-tor kal-tor tor stariben, ik i lau leralmin ra i fai-tor t' ish-veh character. I am muhl acquainted k' wuh accused. I ma ha-tor svi' wuh ka kelek k' ish-veh, na' veh wak na' kaukuh heh na' wuh'ashiv na' nearly dahkuh tevun. Du' ek' ik wak-krus she saudau tor me wuh danik amiable heh benevolent t' komihn creatures. She nursed madame frankenstein, t'nash-veh ezyet, svi' ish-veh kim-shah has-mar, k' wuh greatest affection heh tun heh afterwards attended ish-veh sha' ko-mekh du' wuh tedious has-mar, svi' wuh manner ik teporilau wuh admiration t' ek' vi fai-tor ish-veh, po' if she va'ashiv ha-tor svi' t'nash-veh sa-kuk’s kelek, wilat she vesh' k'diwa k' ek' wuh skan. She vesh' warmly attached tor wuh kan vi nam-tor i' tevik heh bae'cok na' ish-veh spo' wuh danik affectionate ko-mekh. Na' t'nash-veh sha' krus, i ri tor hesitate tor leralmin ik, notwithstanding ek' wuh evidence torvau tehnat ish-veh, i dva-tor heh rely fi' ish-veh buhfik innocence. She had rai temptation na' such wuh torai; u' tor wuh bauble fi' if wuh chief skan shom-tor, kuv she had earnestly aitlu ish-veh, i dang ma willingly putan-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh, ni mau tor i vam heh tala ish-veh.” wuh murmur t' approbation zahal-tor elizabeth’s velik heh powerful appeal, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' teporilau k' ish-veh generous interference, heh ri svi' favour t' ri donku-tor justine, fi' ik wuh tsuri indignation vesh' da-tor k' uzhau khrash, charging ish-veh k' wuh blackest ingratitude. She herself wept u' elizabeth stariben, tonk'peh she did ri kilko-srashiv. T'nash-veh sha' agitation heh thonaya vesh' mairik du' wuh bosh trial. I pudva-tor svi' ish-veh innocence; i fai-tor ish-veh. Kupi wuh dæmon vi had (i did ri na' wuh minute vet) riyeht-stau t'nash-veh sa-kai isha svi' ish-veh hellish torvukh ma pusvik-tor wuh innocent tor tevakh heh ignominy? I kupi ri potun-tor wuh horror t' t'nash-veh situation, heh lu i pakashogau ik wuh popular spes heh wuh countenances t' wuh judges had already condemned t'nash-veh unhappy shi-kar-tor, i rushed s' wuh kelek svi' agony. Wuh tortures t' wuh accused did ri kaik t'nash-veh; she vesh' potun-tor k' innocence, tonk'peh wuh wu-zud t' remorse tore t'nash-veh bosom heh would ri forgo ish-veh meskaraya. I be' dvun-tor wuh mu-yor t' unmingled wretchedness. Svi' wuh asal i went tor wuh kelek; t'nash-veh bru-lar heh drahk vesh' parched. I dared ri ya'akash wuh fatal deshker, tonk'peh i vesh' fainu, heh wuh officer guessed wuh aishan t' t'nash-veh yaret. Wuh ballots had vesh' lehm-tor; au vesh' ek' nesh-kur, heh justine vesh' condemned. I fam yehat pretend tor kethelvau ra i yi olau. I had fa' veshtau kashan t' horror, heh i ma endeavoured tor bestow fi-tor au adequate sagluvaya, tonk'peh zhit fam yehat zhelesh wuh idea t' wuh khaf-spol-sickening despair ik i yi palesh-tor. Wuh person tor ik i addressed myself hau ik justine had already confessed ish-veh guilt. “ik evidence, ” au glantau, “vesh' hardly required svi' ni glaring wuh nuf, tonk'peh i am glad t' ish-veh, heh, indeed, rim t' etwel judges spo' tor condemn wuh criminal fi-tor circumstantial evidence, nam-tor ish-veh ek'wak ni decisive.” nash vesh' flekh heh ri-gishu kash-tor'es; ra kupi ish-veh tvai? Had t'nash-veh bezhun tehs-tor me? Heh vesh' i really u' mad u' wuh bosh panu would dva-tor me tor nam-tor kuv i disclosed wuh vel t' t'nash-veh suspicions? I hastened tor fun ha-kel, heh elizabeth eagerly halishau wuh result. “t'nash-veh krei, ” kilko-tor i, “ish-veh nam-tor klopau u' du lau ma gishu; ek' judges had rather ik lehkuh innocent dang dash do ish-veh guilty dang stron. Tonk'peh she has confessed.” nash vesh' wuh dire salur tor ri donku-tor elizabeth, vi had relied k' firmness fi-tor justine’s innocence. “alas!” leralmin-tor she. “uf dungau i ek'wak va'ashiv dva-tor svi' komihn goodness? Justine, ik i ashau heh vam u' t'nash-veh ko-kai, uf kupi she shitau fi' eifa abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' innocence goh tor svik-tor? Ish-veh bovik bezhun seemed incapable t' sovek severity il guile, heh wi she has committed wuh riyeht-staya.” ak po' etek puzhu-tor ik wuh ri donku-tor shi-kar-tor had sagluvau wuh aitlun tor gla-tor t'nash-veh krei. T'nash-veh sa-mekh istau ish-veh ri tor hal-tor tonk'peh leralmin-tor ik au losrak ish-veh tor ish-veh sha' judgment heh feelings tor klopau. “ha, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “i dungi hal-tor, hi she nam-tor guilty; heh du, skilsu, dungau sailau me; i fam yehat hal-tor sa'awek.” wuh idea t' nash yaret vesh' torture tor me, wi i kupi ri klee'fah. Etek svi-tor wuh gloomy prison tvi-shal heh beheld justine sitting fi' ein terp na' wuh weh-irak shaht; ish-veh el'ru vesh' manacled, heh ish-veh patam shom-tor fi' ish-veh mal-nef. She she-tor fi' seeing etek svi-tor, heh lu etek vesh' losrak sa'awek k' ish-veh, she threw herself na' wuh ash'ya t' elizabeth, weeping bitterly. T'nash-veh krei wept isha. “oh, justine!” leralmin-tor she. “po did du rob me t' t'nash-veh kim-shah consolation? I relied fi' ish-veh innocence, heh hi i vesh' yi maut wretched, i vesh' ri ni miserable u' i am i'.” “heh tor du isha dva-tor ik i am ni maut, maut wicked? Tor du isha hau k' t'nash-veh nemut tor plesh-tor me, tor condemn me u' wuh murderer?” ish-veh spes vesh' suffocated k' sobs. “shen, t'nash-veh ri donku-tor ko-kan, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth; “po tor du kneel, kuv du nam-tor innocent? I am ri veh t' ish-veh nemut, i pudva-tor du guiltless, notwithstanding kanok evidence, abi' i puzhu-tor ik du had yourself afsakau ish-veh guilt. Ik report, du leralmin, nam-tor riyeht; heh nam-tor assured, tal-kam justine, ik nothing mokuhlek hutau t'nash-veh guhl'es svi' du na' wuh moment, tonk'peh ish-veh sha' confession.” “i did confess, tonk'peh i confessed wuh ti. I confessed, ik i lau prah absolution; tonk'peh i' ik falsehood ti heavier na' t'nash-veh khaf-spol do ek' t'nash-veh vath sins. Wuh oekon t' sha-ka-ri forgive me! Ek'wak opi' i vesh' condemned, t'nash-veh confessor has besieged me; au threatened heh menaced, abi' i siyah began tor nah-tor ik i vesh' wuh stislak ik au leralmin-tor i vesh'. Au threatened excommunication heh bogozh yon svi' t'nash-veh kim-shah moments kuv i fator obdurate. Tal-kam t'sai, i had rim tor nenikaya me; ek' glazhau fi' me u' wuh wretch doomed tor ignominy heh perdition. Ra sos tor? Svi' wuh ek'rasah wadan i subscribed tor wuh ti; heh i' goh am i truly miserable.” she svizh-tor, weeping, heh yi fator, “i nahp k' horror, t'nash-veh slor t'sai, ik du dang dva-tor ish-veh justine, ik ish-veh blessed ezyet had ni highly pudor-tor, heh ik du ashau, vesh' wuh creature capable t' wuh tr'y'kak if rim tonk'peh wuh e'shua himself kupi ma perpetrated. Tal-kam william! Dearest blessed kan! I ak dungau gla-tor du va'ashiv svi' sha-ka-ri, wilat etek dungau ek' nam-tor kunli; heh ik consoles me, going u' i am tor dash ignominy heh tevakh.” “oh, justine! Forgive me na' having na' veh moment distrusted du. Po did du confess? Tonk'peh ri tor la'tusa, tal-kam ko-kan. Ri tor pthak. I dungi afsakau, i dungi skan-tor ish-veh innocence. I dungi klimtau wuh stony khaf-spol t' ish-veh nemut k' t'nash-veh bezhun-masu heh prayers. Du dungau ri tev-tor! Du, t'nash-veh playfellow, t'nash-veh besu, t'nash-veh ko-kai, perish fi' wuh scaffold! Rai! Rai! I worla kupi rish-tor ni horrible wuh misfortune.” justine hutau ish-veh patam mournfully. “i ri tor pthak tor tev-tor, ” she leralmin-tor; “ik pang nam-tor vesht. Oekon ashenau t'nash-veh kobat'es heh mazhiv-kur-tor me courage tor palesh-tor wuh rasahkos. I trasha wuh maf heh sfith(-) panu; heh kuv du vokau me heh nah-tor t' me u' t' veh unjustly condemned, i am resigned tor wuh buk awaiting me. Oren-tor s' me, tal-kam t'sai, tor nekhau svi' tranush tor wuh dungi t' sha-ka-ri!” du' nash conversation i had retired tor wuh teruk t' wuh prison tvi-shal, wilat i kupi ip-sut wuh horrid thonaya ik ma me.
