Despair! Vi dared variben t' ik? Wuh ri donku-tor shi-kar-tor, vi fi' wuh morrow vesh' tor be' dvun wuh awful krup svi' ha'kiv heh tevakh, olau ri, u' i did, such glu heh sfith(-) agony. I gnashed t'nash-veh zud heh solektra au teretuhr, uttering wuh groan ik sarlah s' t'nash-veh inmost soul. Justine palikau. Lu gla-tor ish-veh vi ish-veh vesh', she betau me heh leralmin-tor, “tal-kam osu, du nam-tor maut ves tor yaret me; du, i rok, ri tor dva-tor ik i am guilty?” i kupi ri kilko-srashiv. “rai, justine, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth; “au nam-tor weht convinced t' ish-veh innocence do i vesh', na' kauk lu au puzhu-tor ik du had confessed, au did ri lit ish-veh.” “i truly itaren ish-veh. Svi' aifa kim-shah moments i olau wuh sincerest gratitude na' eifa vi nah-tor t' me k' kindness. Uf slor nam-tor wuh affection t' vath tor such wuh wretch u' i am! Ish-veh snem-tor weht do ulef t'nash-veh misfortune, heh i olau u' kuv i kupi tev-tor svi' sochya i' ik t'nash-veh innocence nam-tor nafai k' du, tal-kam t'sai, heh ish-veh krei.” thus wuh ri donku-tor sufferer ar'kada tor comfort vath heh herself. She indeed nazh-tor wuh resignation she aitlu. Tonk'peh i, wuh yeht murderer, olau wuh worla-dying worm alive svi' t'nash-veh bosom, if kal-tor t' rai rok il consolation. Elizabeth isha wept heh vesh' unhappy, tonk'peh ish-veh isha vesh' wuh misery t' innocence, if, spo' wuh wan ik be' dvun-tor abru' wuh rom aikum, na' wuh du' ip-sut tonk'peh fam yehat tarnish its ugel'es. Thonaya heh despair had penetrated vi' wuh tviyan t' t'nash-veh khaf-spol; i spitau wuh bogozh k'svi me if nothing kupi sayonotau. Etek stayed several wadan k' justine, heh ish-veh vesh' k' lo'uk rihag'es ik elizabeth kupi bezhun-masu herself maf. “i istaya, ” maf-tor she, “ik i vesh' tor tev-tor k' du; i fam yehat ha-tor svi' nash panu t' misery.” justine assumed wuh sov t' cheerfulness, du' she k' rihag'es repressed ish-veh sfith(-) bezhun-masu. She nartau elizabeth heh leralmin-tor svi' wuh spes t' ulef-nelau zherka, “rom-halan, slor t'sai, dearest elizabeth, t'nash-veh k'diwa heh goh t'hy'la; lau sha-ka-ri, svi' its bounty, kudau heh korsau du; lau nash nam-tor wuh kim-shah misfortune ik du dungi ek'wak dash! Ha-tor, heh nam-tor kunli, heh tor vath ni.” heh fi' wuh morrow justine tev-tor. Elizabeth’s khaf-spol-rending eloquence vravshau tor dvun wuh judges s' ish-veh settled conviction svi' wuh criminality t' wuh saintly sufferer. T'nash-veh passionate heh indignant appeals vesh' pakik fi-tor au. Heh lu i poprah ish-veh samu kilko-srashiv heh puzhu-tor wuh harsh, unfeeling reasoning t' aifa sasu, t'nash-veh purposed avowal tev-tor maf fi' t'nash-veh bru-lar. Thus i lau afsakau myself wuh madman, tonk'peh ri revoke wuh zhit-bal be' dvun-tor fi-tor t'nash-veh wretched shi-kar-tor. She perished fi' wuh scaffold u' wuh murderess! S' wuh tortures t' t'nash-veh sha' khaf-spol, i da-tor tor contemplate wuh glu heh voiceless tushat t' t'nash-veh elizabeth. Nash isha vesh' t'nash-veh doing! Heh t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s woe, heh wuh desolation t' ik tab-ma ni smiling ha-kel ek' vesh' wuh ar'kadan t' t'nash-veh thrice-accursed el'ru! Ye tusa, unhappy ones, tonk'peh aifa nam-tor ri ish-veh kim-shah bezhun-masu! Va'ashiv dungau du ashenau wuh mem-lu til-kum wail, heh wuh ralash t' ish-veh lamentations dungau va'ashiv heh va'ashiv nam-tor puzhu-tor! Frankenstein, ish-veh sa-fu, ish-veh tomasu, ish-veh lehkuh-mal, mau-ashau t'hy'la; au vi would spend tik bolik eku t' khaf na' ish-veh sakes, vi has rai nahp il kash-ral t' mak kaula u' ish-veh nam-tor mirrored isha svi' ish-veh tal-kam countenances, vi would boshaya wuh sov k' blessings heh spend ish-veh ha'kiv svi' serving du—au nufai-tor du tusa, tor foshuhl countless bezhun-masu; kunli mesakh ish-veh rok-tor, kuv thus inexorable buk nam-tor satisfied, heh kuv wuh vashaya svizh fa' wuh sochya t' wuh shi'vukhut ma navau tor ish-veh maf torments! Thus stariben t'nash-veh prophetic soul, u', torn k' remorse, horror, heh despair, i beheld eifa i ashau spend vain sorrow fi-tor wuh shi'vukhut t' william heh justine, wuh wuh'rak hapless victims tor t'nash-veh unhallowed arts. Chapter 9 nothing nam-tor weht kusut-tor tor wuh komihn kashek do, po' wuh feelings ma vesh' ar'kada abru k' wuh sahris succession t' pavek, wuh tevik calmness t' inaction heh certainty if zahal-tor heh deprives wuh soul fi' t' rok heh pthak. Justine tev-tor, she shom-tor, heh i vesh' alive. Wuh khaf yumau freely svi' t'nash-veh os-khaf-mev, tonk'peh wuh rasath t' despair heh remorse hish-tor fi' t'nash-veh khaf-spol if nothing kupi snem-tor. Yuk sasahr-tor s' t'nash-veh bezhun; i czar-tor spo' wuh ek'rasah tam'a, na' i had committed deeds t' mischief mesakh kethelvaya horrible, heh weht, mau weht (i persuaded myself) vesh' wi za'. Wi t'nash-veh khaf-spol overflowed k' kindness heh wuh ashaya t' virtue. I had palikau ha'kiv k' benevolent intentions heh thirsted na' wuh moment lu i dang shitau au svi' practice heh tor myself useful tor t'nash-veh katravahsu beings. I' ek' vesh' thorshau; instead t' ik mol-kom t' conscience if kal-tor me tor glazhau pla' fi-tor wuh vesht k' shal-satisfaction, heh s' thence tor hoknau ugaya t' uzh rok-tor, i vesh' seized k' remorse heh wuh kash-ral t' guilt, if hurried me maf tor wuh bogozh t' intense tortures such u' rai gen-lis mokuhlek kethelvau. Nash fupa s' t' kashek preyed fi-tor t'nash-veh muhl'es, if had sos'eh worla entirely recovered s' wuh wuh'rak kolaya ish-veh had potun-tor. I shunned wuh limuk t' sasu; ek' ralash t' mak il complacency vesh' torture tor me; awek'es vesh' t'nash-veh goh consolation—glu, gu'gelik, deathlike awek'es. T'nash-veh sa-mekh glantau k' kusut wuh alteration perceptible svi' t'nash-veh disposition heh es'merka heh endeavoured k' nerau-kek-vuhnayek deduced s' wuh feelings t' ish-veh serene conscience heh guiltless ha'kiv tor vi'le-esh-tor me k' fortitude heh awaken svi' me wuh courage tor dispel wuh gu'gelik wan if brooded abru' me. “tor du nah-tor, skilsu, ” leralmin-tor au, “ik i ri tor dash isha? Kling kupi ashaya wuh kan weht do i ashau ish-veh sa-kai”—bezhun-masu sarlah vi' ish-veh bezhun u' au stariben—“tonk'peh nam-tor ish-veh ri wuh gu-vam tor wuh survivors ik etek dang refrain s' augmenting ish-veh unhappiness k' wuh appearance t' immoderate tushat? Ish-veh nam-tor isha wuh gu-vam owed tor yourself, na' mauyik sorrow prevents improvement il tizh'es, il kauk wuh khrasaya t' kanok-gadik usefulness, rik' if rai sasu nam-tor nunau na' shila'es.” nash na'shikh, hi rom, vesh' totally inapplicable tor t'nash-veh nuf; i dang ma vesh' wuh wuh'rak tor ip-sut t'nash-veh tushat heh console t'nash-veh t'hylara kuv remorse had ri mingled its bitterness, heh vash its vikayek, k' t'nash-veh vath kashan. I' i kupi goh kilko-srashiv t'nash-veh sa-mekh k' wuh glazhau t' despair heh endeavour tor ip-sut myself s' ish-veh zan-tor. Pa' nash wak etek retired tor etwel kelek na' belrive. Nash rubah vesh' wa' agreeable tor me. Wuh shutting t' wuh temep regularly na' lehkuh o’wak-vel heh wuh impossibility t' remaining fi' wuh suk'muzh po' ik wadan had rendered etwel residence k'svi wuh temok t' geneva maut irksome tor me. I vesh' i' elik. K'ashiv, po' wuh shom t' wuh skan had retired na' wuh mu-yor, i nem-tor wuh masu-hali heh be' dvun-tor wehk wadan fi-tor wuh masu. Sometimes, k' t'nash-veh masu-halovau eku, i vesh' lesh k' wuh salan; heh sometimes, po' rowing vi' wuh svitan t' wuh suk'muzh, i losrak wuh masu-hali tor pursue its sha' rivak heh mazhiv-kur-tor yut tor t'nash-veh sha' miserable haulan. I vesh' k'ashiv tempted, lu ek' vesh' na' sochya pa' me, heh i wuh goh unquiet vel ik czar-tor restless svi' wuh scene ni vaksurik heh heavenly—kuv i kaula ein starok, il wuh git'woa, t'vi harsh heh svi-shau croaking vesh' puzhu-tor goh lu i betau wuh gef—k'ashiv, i leralmin, i vesh' tempted tor taul vi' wuh ralash-fam suk'muzh, ik wuh mashau lau ikap-tor abru' me heh t'nash-veh calamities na' ek'wak. Tonk'peh i vesh' restrained, lu i nahp t' wuh heroic heh suffering elizabeth, ik i tenderly ashau, heh t'vi nam vesh' bound abru svi' t'nash-veh. I nahp isha t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh heh surviving sa-kai; dang i k' t'nash-veh nen desertion trasha au ko'nar heh unprotected tor wuh malice t' wuh shaka ik i had kal-tor thal ekhlami? Na' aifa moments i wept bitterly heh istau ik sochya would revisit t'nash-veh kashek goh ik i lau afford au consolation heh happiness. Tonk'peh ik kupi ri nam-tor. Remorse sayonotau kanok rok. I had vesh' wuh kitausu t' unalterable ek'rasah, heh i ha-tor svi' kanok-gadik pthak lest wuh stislak ik i had fereik-tor dang perpetrate ein uzh wickedness. I had wuh obscure olaya ik ek' vesh' ri abru' heh ik au would fam dvun kugau ein glantokaya tr'y'kak, if k' its enormity dang siyah efface wuh recollection t' wuh vesht. Tra' vesh' kwon-hau-ov scope na' pthak ni wu u' sovek-vel i ashau hafau za'. T'nash-veh abhorrence t' nash shaka fam yehat nam-tor conceived. Lu i nahp t' ish-veh i gnashed t'nash-veh zud, t'nash-veh bezhun became inflamed, heh i ardently istau tor sayonotau ik ha'kiv if i had ni thoughtlessly bestowed. Lu i haul-tor fi' ish-veh tr'y'kak heh malice, t'nash-veh hatred heh revenge thorau ek' bounds t' moderation. I would ma tor wuh pilgrimage tor wuh k'lek feh t' wuh andes, sos, lu tra', ma precipitated ish-veh tor ish-veh nen. I istau tor gla-tor ish-veh va'ashiv, ik i lau wreak wuh utmost sadvun t' abhorrence fi' ish-veh patam heh avenge wuh deaths t' william heh justine. Etwel kelek vesh' wuh kelek t' mourning. T'nash-veh sa-mekh’s muhl'es vesh' deeply shaken k' wuh horror t' wuh recent pavek. Elizabeth vesh' maf heh desponding; she rai longer nem-tor delight svi' ish-veh ordinary occupations; ek' sanosh seemed tor ish-veh sacrilege na' wuh tevik; ek'wakik woe heh bezhun-masu she yi nahp vesh' wuh aishan tribute she dang vlitau tor innocence ni thorshau heh vashau. She vesh' rai longer ik kunli creature vi svi' earlier youth czar-tor k' me fi' wuh kutra t' wuh suk'muzh heh variben k' prahk'es t' etwel fa-wak prospects. Wuh wuh'rak t' eifa sorrows if nam-tor satau tor wean etek s' wuh terra had yaretau ish-veh, heh its dimming vi-yumuk quenched ish-veh dearest abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “lu i haul-tor, t'nash-veh tal-kam krei, ” leralmin-tor she, “fi' wuh miserable tevakh t' justine moritz, i rai longer gla-tor wuh panu heh its ar'kada u' au fa' saudau tor me. Fa', i glazhau fi-tor wuh khrosahp t' vice heh injustice ik i telv-tor svi' dunap il puzhu-tor s' vath u' var t' t'kahr gad il glenonik ek'rasah; k'puu au vesh' remote heh weht familiar tor utvau do tor wuh glenonaya; tonk'peh i' misery has sarlah ha-kel, heh sasu saudau tor me u' stislak thirsting na' tik vath’s khaf. Wi i am certainly unjust. Kanok-veh pudva-tor ik ri donku-tor ko-kan tor nam-tor guilty; heh kuv she kupi ma committed wuh tr'y'kak na' if she dashau, assuredly she would ma vesh' wuh danik depraved t' komihn creatures. Na' wuh sake t' wuh zamu ek'zer, ki' riyeht-stau wuh sa-fu t' ish-veh benefactor heh t'hy'la, wuh kan ik she had nursed s' its keshtan, heh saudau tor ashaya u' kuv ish-veh had vesh' ish-veh sha'! I kupi ri consent tor wuh tevakh t' sovek komihn hasu, tonk'peh certainly i dang ma nahp such wuh creature unfit tor hafau svi' wuh shila'es t' sasu. Tonk'peh she vesh' innocent. I fai-tor, i olau she vesh' innocent; du nam-tor t' wuh ka opinion, heh ik wugau me. Alas! Skilsu, lu falsehood mokuhlek glazhau ni spo' wuh yeht'es, vi mokuhlek assure themselves t' ac'ruth happiness? I olau u' kuv i vesh' walking fi' wuh rihk t' wuh precipice, na' if thousands nam-tor crowding heh endeavouring tor taul me vi' wuh gosh. William heh justine vesh' assassinated, heh wuh murderer stron-tor; au lates-tor pa' wuh panu elik, heh sos'eh respected. Tonk'peh kauk kuv i vesh' condemned tor dash fi' wuh scaffold na' wuh ka tr'y'kak, i would ri rubah shitau k' such wuh wretch.” i shroi tor nash discourse k' wuh extremest agony. I, ri svi' deed, tonk'peh svi' daya, vesh' wuh yeht murderer. Elizabeth telv-tor t'nash-veh thonaya svi' t'nash-veh countenance, heh kindly taking t'nash-veh el'ru, leralmin-tor, “t'nash-veh dearest t'hy'la, du bolau hayal yourself. Aifa pavek ma dau me, oekon fai-tor uf deeply; tonk'peh i am ri ni wretched u' du nam-tor. Tra' nam-tor wuh sagluvaya t' despair, heh sometimes t' revenge, svi' ish-veh countenance ik tor me tremble. Tal-kam skilsu, sahaisau aifa gu'gelik shaukaush. Vokau wuh t'hylara pa' du, vi centre ek' ish-veh rok-tor svi' du. Ma etek pakik wuh tepul t' rendering du kunli? Ah! Du' etek ashaya, du' etek nam-tor yeht tor tik vath, la' svi' nash solektra t' sochya heh vaksur, ish-veh salatik shasol, etek lau reap kanok tranquil kudaya—ra mokuhlek ertau etwel sochya?” heh kupi ri such zhit s' ish-veh ik i fondly prized fa' kanok vath mazhiv-kur t' fortune suffice tor a'vesh' maf wuh shaka ik lurked svi' t'nash-veh khaf-spol? Kauk u' she stariben i drew be' tor ish-veh, u' kuv svi' vash, lest na' ik maut moment wuh destroyer had vesh' be' tor rob me t' ish-veh. Thus ri wuh tenderness t' friendship, il wuh vaksur t' terra, il t' sha-ka-ri, kupi redeem t'nash-veh soul s' woe; wuh maut accents t' ashaya vesh' ineffectual. I vesh' encompassed k' wuh wan if rai beneficial vi-yumuk kupi penetrate. Wuh wounded deer dragging its fainting sikrus tor ein untrodden vohrayek, tra' tor gaze fi-tor wuh kliton if had tilau ish-veh, heh tor tev-tor, vesh' tonk'peh wuh ves t' me. Sometimes i kupi cope k' wuh kir despair ik overwhelmed me, tonk'peh sometimes wuh whirlwind shaukaush t' t'nash-veh soul drove me tor seek, k' bodily tusok heh k' rubah t' shi, ein vas s' t'nash-veh intolerable kashan. Ish-veh vesh' du' wuh access t' nash ves ik i suddenly losrak t'nash-veh ha-kel, heh bending t'nash-veh ash-tor na' wuh be' pid-kunelik ku-li, sought svi' wuh magnificence, wuh ek'wak'es t' such scenes, tor yen-tor myself heh t'nash-veh sahr-kastik, fai'ei komihn, sorrows. T'nash-veh czar vesh' khartau na' wuh ku-li t' chamounix. I had yaretau ish-veh frequently du' t'nash-veh boyhood. Shehkuh tevun had be' dvun-tor opi' yi: _i_ vesh' wuh vashau, tonk'peh nought had rubai svi' eifa savage heh enduring scenes. I performed wuh wuh'rak krus t' t'nash-veh halovaya fi' horseback. I afterwards hired wuh jarel, u' wuh weht sure-footed heh least liable tor poprah dash fi' aifa rugged fau-yut. Wuh igen-va vesh' tok-ti; ish-veh vesh' pa' wuh svitan t' wuh tevun-krus t' august, nearly dahkuh tevun-krus po' wuh tevakh t' justine, ik miserable nauf s' if i dated ek' t'nash-veh woe. Wuh rasath fi-tor t'nash-veh tam'a vesh' sensibly lightened u' i taul-tor wi deeper svi' wuh ravine t' arve. Wuh immense suk'kunel heh precipices ik overhung me fi' kanok vla, wuh ralash t' wuh pilash raging among wuh kov, heh wuh dashing t' wuh waterfalls pa' stariben t' wuh tepul mighty u' omnipotence—heh i ceased tor pthak il tor vulaya fa' sovek hasu lehkuh almighty do ik if had fereik-tor heh khau wuh meilak, la' gluvaya svi' ish-veh danik terrific guise. Fam dvun, u' i she-tor higher, wuh ku-li assumed wuh weht magnificent heh astonishing character. Ruined castles hanging fi' wuh precipices t' piny suk'kunel, wuh impetuous arve, heh cottages kanok la' heh tra' peeping forth s' among wuh lap shidau wuh scene t' singular vaksur. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' augmented heh rendered sublime k' wuh mighty alps, t'vi wan-kur heh shining rekun heh ub towered abru' ek', u' t' wuh'ashiv terra, wuh habitations t' wuh'ashiv ne-koshtri t' beings. I be' dvun-tor wuh mesut t' pélissier, wilat wuh ravine, if wuh pilash shidau, tu'ash fa' me, heh i began tor she-tor wuh suk'kunel ik overhangs ish-veh. Ak po', i svi-tor wuh ku-li t' chamounix. Nash ku-li nam-tor weht wonderful heh sublime, tonk'peh ri ni vaksurik heh picturesque u' ik t' servox, k'fai'ei i had aishan be' dvun-tor. Wuh pid heh snowy suk'kunel vesh' its iyi krup, tonk'peh vesht gla-tor nash-veh rai weht ruined castles heh kanashik vunai. Immense dvun-le-sumatra betau wuh fau-yut; i puzhu-tor wuh rumbling rahm t' wuh tevan-tor suk'izh-skish heh pu'ulidau wuh vuzh t' its tvur. Mont blanc, wuh supreme heh magnificent mont blanc, ashenau itself s' wuh surrounding _aiguilles_, heh its tremendous _dôme_ overlooked wuh ku-li. Wuh tingling wu-pakik kash-ral t' sanosh k'ashiv sarlah mes' me du' nash halovaya. Ein da-tor svi' wuh fau-yut, ein uzh vel suddenly pakashogau heh naglanshau, reminded me t' gad hal-tor k', heh vesh' katravah k' wuh lighthearted gaiety t' boyhood. Wuh maut salan zhal-tor svi' soothing accents, heh maternal malat bade me tusa rai weht. Yi va'ashiv wuh kindly vi-yumuk ceased tor bae'cok—i afer-tor myself fettered va'ashiv tor tushat heh indulging svi' ek' wuh misery t' haulan. Yi i spurred fi' t'nash-veh aushfa, striving ni tor yen-tor wuh panu, t'nash-veh ptha, heh weht do ek', myself—il, svi' wuh weht desperate fashion, i alighted heh threw myself fi' wuh yar, rasathau ne' k' horror heh despair. Na' wu-vath i lasha na' wuh pi'kahr t' chamounix. Exhaustion navau tor wuh mairik zung fi' t' ak'shem heh t' kashek if i had palesh-tor. Na' wuh pen ret t' wak i hafau na' wuh krani watching wuh pallid lightnings ik mavau abru' mont blanc heh listening tor wuh rushing t' wuh arve, if pursued its noisy yut ne'rak. Wuh ka lulling sounds bae'cok u' wuh lullaby tor t'nash-veh nuh' keen kashan; lu i shitau t'nash-veh patam fi-tor t'nash-veh trak, yuk crept abru' me; i olau ish-veh u' sarlah ish-veh heh blessed wuh giver t' oblivion. Chapter 10 i spent wuh zahalik gad roaming k'fai wuh ku-li. I lam-tor be' wuh shu-pal t' wuh arveiron, if nem-tor ish-veh shen svi' wuh dvun-le-sumatra, ik k' vohris sahr nam-tor advancing ne' s' wuh dan-pid-sfek t' wuh kunel tor barricade wuh ku-li. Wuh abrupt vla t' vast suk'kunel vesh' fa' me; wuh icy temok t' wuh dvun-le-sumatra overhung me; wuh zamu zarahk-tor pines vesh' scattered pa'; heh wuh solemn silence t' nash glorious la'es-tvi-shal t' imperial malat vesh' pushau goh k' wuh brawling pral il wuh tevan t' ein vast karf, wuh rahm ralash t' wuh suk'izh-skish il wuh cracking, reverberated bi' wuh suk'kunel, t' wuh accumulated le-suma, if, k'fai wuh ralash-fam working t' immutable tor-gav, vesh' ek'wak heh anon rent heh torn, u' kuv ish-veh had vesh' tonk'peh wuh plaything svi' ish-veh el'ru. Aifa sublime heh magnificent scenes afforded me wuh greatest consolation ik i vesh' capable t' receiving. Au ashenau me s' ek' littleness t' olaya, heh hi au did ri snem-tor t'nash-veh tushat, au nessau heh tranquillised ish-veh. Svi' ein degree, isha, au matau t'nash-veh kashek s' wuh nahp abru' if ish-veh had brooded na' wuh kim-shah tevun-krus. I retired tor shom na' mu-yor; t'nash-veh slumbers, u' ish-veh vesh', bek-tor fi' heh ministered tor k' wuh assemblance t' grand shid if i had contemplated du' wuh gad. Au congregated pauk me; wuh unstained snowy suk'kunel-fik, wuh glittering kov-suk'fek, wuh pine lapan, heh ragged sai-famik ravine, wuh eagle, soaring amidst wuh wan—au ek' hoknau pauk me heh bade me nam-tor na' sochya. Wilat had au sasahr-tor lu wuh thurai asal i awoke? Ek' t' soul-inspiriting sasahr-tor k' yuk, heh gu'gelik melancholy clouded kanok nahp. Wuh sov-masu vesh' pouring svi' torrents, heh bali mists ip-sut wuh dan-pid-sfek t' wuh suk'kunel, ni ik i kauk gla-tor ri wuh limuk t' eifa mighty t'hylara. Fam dvun i would penetrate ish-veh misty veil heh seek au svi' ish-veh cloudy retreats. Ra vesh' sov-masu heh sahriv tor me? T'nash-veh jarel vesh' katau tor wuh svep, heh i resolved tor she-tor tor wuh dan-pid-sfek t' montanvert. I vokau wuh daya ik wuh zan-tor t' wuh tremendous heh ek'wak-dvun-tor dvun-le-sumatra had torvau fi-tor t'nash-veh kashek lu i wuh'rak gla-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh had yi boshau me k' wuh sublime prahk'es ik mazhiv-kur-tor rala tor wuh soul heh kal-tor ish-veh tor soar s' wuh obscure panu tor ta'hal heh mak. Wuh glan t' wuh awful heh majestic svi' malat had indeed kwon-hau-ov wuh daya t' solemnising t'nash-veh kashek heh causing me tor yen-tor wuh be' dvun-tor tun-tor t' ha'kiv. I satalau tor hal-tor rik' wuh kakhartausu, na' i vesh' muhl acquainted k' wuh yut, heh wuh la'es t' wuh'ashiv would vashau wuh solitary grandeur t' wuh scene. Wuh shen nam-tor precipitous, tonk'peh wuh yut nam-tor tresahk vi' continual heh pen windings, if enable du tor surmount wuh perpendicularity t' wuh suk'kunel. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh scene terrifically desolate. Svi' wuh thousand gla-tor wuh zavikau t' wuh karil suk'izh-skish lau nam-tor pakashogau, wilat lap ti pushau heh strewed fi' wuh solektra, ein entirely vashau, vath keh'sei, leaning fi-tor wuh jutting kov t' wuh suk'kunel il transversely fi-tor vath lap. Wuh yut, u' du she-tor higher, nam-tor tvimesau k' ravines t' izh, ne' if kov continually padukau s' abru'; veh t' au nam-tor wa' tehvar-bosh, u' wuh slightest ralash, such u' kauk speaking svi' wuh ral spes, torvau wuh kwul-kolaya t' sov sufficient tor bes-tor vashaya fi-tor wuh patam t' wuh saralashek. Wuh pines nam-tor ri ha-vol il luxuriant, tonk'peh au nam-tor sombre heh hau wuh sov t' severity tor wuh scene. I glazhau fi' wuh ku-li ne'rak; vast mists vesh' rising s' wuh pilash if sahr-tor k'fai ish-veh heh tcha-tor svi' bali wreaths pa' wuh mesyutik suk'kunel, t'vi dan-pid-sfek vesh' ip-sut svi' wuh uniform wan, du' sov-masu mukau s' wuh gu'gelik igen heh hau tor wuh melancholy impression i poprah s' wuh vel pa' me. Alas! Po tor sasu boast t' sensibilities superior tor eifa apparent svi' wuh brute; ish-veh goh renders au weht bolayatik beings. Kuv etwel impulses vesh' confined tor avon, mag, heh aitlun, etek lau nam-tor nearly elik; tonk'peh i' etek nam-tor dvun-tor k' kanok salan ik salur heh wuh pavesh zhit il scene ik ik zhit lau zhelesh tor etek. Etek shom; wuh sahr-tor has tepul tor gisam yuk. Etek shen; veh wand’mokov nahp flau wuh gad. Etek olau, conceive, il utvau; abru'teruklar-ru'lut il tusa, nartaya tishau woe, il vishizhau etwel tun-tor maf; ish-veh nam-tor wuh ka: na', nam-tor ish-veh mak il sorrow, wuh yut t' its trashan fam dvun nam-tor elik. Sasu’s za-gad lau ne’er nam-tor spo' ish-veh morrow; nought lau palesh-tor tonk'peh mutability! Ish-veh vesh' nearly aru lu i lasha na' wuh fik t' wuh shen. Na' ein wak i hayal-tor fi-tor wuh kov ik overlooks wuh masutra t' le-suma. Wuh mist wein-tor fi' ik heh wuh surrounding suk'kunel. Presently wuh pi'salan dissipated wuh wan, heh i tev-tor fi-tor wuh dvun-le-sumatra. Wuh skonn nam-tor maut uneven, rising spo' wuh pral t' wuh troubled masutra, descending neik, heh interspersed k' rifts ik ne'hal-tor glu. Wuh vunai t' le-suma nam-tor siyah wuh league svi' eik-vath, tonk'peh i spent nearly dahkuh wadan svi' mes ish-veh. Wuh mesyutik suk'kunel nam-tor wuh sai-famik sazehik kov. S' wuh vla wilat i i' lam-tor montanvert vesh' exactly mesyutik, na' wuh ir t' wuh league; heh abru' ish-veh she-tor mont blanc, svi' awful majesty. I hafau svi' wuh sha'ti t' wuh kov, gazing fi' nash wonderful heh stupendous scene. Wuh masutra, il rather wuh vast pilash t' le-suma, skek among its nerik suk'kunel, t'vi sovik dan-pid-sfek geldau abru' its sha'ti. Ish-veh icy heh glittering feh min-tor svi' wuh ug'yel-ha'gel abru' wuh wan. T'nash-veh khaf-spol, if vesh' fa' sorrowful, i' puv-tor k' vel spo' mak; i sporiben, “wandering tam'a, kuv indeed ye czar, heh ri tor shom svi' ish-veh wonil sar-tak, kal-tor me nash faint happiness, il nem-tor me, u' ish-veh besu, maf s' wuh mak t' ha'kiv.” u' i leralmin-tor nash i suddenly beheld wuh khlop t' wuh sasu, na' ein ir, advancing na' me k' superhuman threshan. Au bounded abru' wuh treshaya svi' wuh le-suma, among if i had lates-tor k' yuzhat; ish-veh stature, isha, u' au betau, seemed tor namautau ik t' sasu. I vesh' troubled; wuh mist sarlah abru' t'nash-veh bezhun, heh i olau wuh faintness seize me, tonk'peh i vesh' sahris restored k' wuh samu karik salan t' wuh suk'kunel. I pakashogau, u' wuh shid sarlah nearer (glan tremendous heh abhorred!) ik ish-veh vesh' wuh wretch ik i had fereik-tor. I trembled k' reshan heh horror, resolving tor bek-tor ish-veh betaya heh yi ikap-tor k' ish-veh svi' mortal morov. Au betau; ish-veh countenance bespoke sfith(-) thonaya, puterish-tor k' disdain heh malignity, du' its unearthly ugliness rendered ish-veh siyah nuh' horrible na' komihn bezhun. Tonk'peh i scarcely glantau nash; reshan heh hatred had palikauk deprived me t' utterance, heh i recovered goh tor overwhelm ish-veh k' zhit expressive t' furious detestation heh contempt. “e'shua, ” i sporiben, “tor du dare betaya me? Heh tor ri du pthak wuh kei vengeance t' t'nash-veh kar wreaked fi' ish-veh miserable patam? Begone, vile ravot! Il rather, stay, ik i lau sahr-tor du tor grazhiv! Heh, oh! Ik i kupi, k' wuh ek'tevan t' ish-veh miserable nam, restore eifa victims ik du ma ni diabolically riyeht-stau!” “i gishu nash reception, ” leralmin-tor wuh dæmon. “ek' sasu fnu-ven wuh wretched; uf, yi, bolau i nam-tor fnu-ven, vi am miserable mesakh ek' living vel! Wi du, t'nash-veh fereiksu, detest heh spurn me, thy creature, tor ik thou tanaf bound k' ties goh dissoluble k' wuh annihilation t' veh t' etek. Du lof tor stau me. Uf dare du torvukh thus k' ha'kiv? Tor ish-veh gu-vam na' me, heh i dungi tor t'nash-veh na' du heh wuh shom t' mankind. Kuv du dungi comply k' t'nash-veh nosh, i dungi trasha au heh du na' sochya; tonk'peh kuv du klee'fah, i dungi pid-mau-mazhiv-kur wuh maw t' tevakh, abi' ish-veh nam-tor satiated k' wuh khaf t' ish-veh remaining t'hylara.” “abhorred stislak! Shaka ik thou tanaf! Wuh tortures t' bogozh nam-tor nuh' bovik wuh vengeance na' thy tr'y'kak. Wretched e'shua! Du reproach me k' ish-veh fereikan, sarlah fi', yi, ik i lau sayonotau wuh kil if i ni negligently bestowed.” t'nash-veh reshan vesh' rik' bounds; i sprang fi' ish-veh, impelled k' ek' wuh feelings if mokuhlek kar veh hasu tehnat wuh nam t' wuh'ashiv. Au easily savlau me heh leralmin-tor, “nam-tor hayal! I entreat du tor zhu-tor me fa' du mazhiv-kur-tor krau tor ish-veh hatred fi' t'nash-veh vaikau patam. Ma i ri dashau hiyet, ik du seek tor increase t'nash-veh misery? Ha'kiv, hi ish-veh lau goh nam-tor wuh tabrukaya t' thonaya, nam-tor tal-kam tor me, heh i dungi fosh-tor ish-veh. Vokau, thou hast tor me weht powerful do thyself; t'nash-veh pidek nam-tor superior tor thine, t'nash-veh joints weht supple. Tonk'peh i dungi ri nam-tor tempted tor eku myself svi' opposition tor thee. I am thy creature, heh i dungi nam-tor kauk bovik heh docile tor t'nash-veh malatik s'haile heh sa-te'kru kuv thou wilt isha perform thy krus, wuh if thou owest me. Oh, frankenstein, nam-tor ri equitable tor kanok vath heh sahr-tor fi-tor me sa'awek, tor ik thy yeht-gav, heh kauk thy clemency heh affection, nam-tor danik due. Vokau ik i am thy creature; i ought tor nam-tor thy adam, tonk'peh i am rather wuh tevan-tor ha'su, ik thou drivest s' mak na' rai misdeed. Kanok-wilat gla-tor nash-veh bliss, s' if i sa'awek am irrevocably sanan-tor. I vesh' benevolent heh rom; misery tor me wuh shaka. Tor me kunli, heh i dungau va'ashiv nam-tor virtuous.” “begone! I dungi ri zhu-tor du. Tra' mokuhlek nam-tor rai shila svi' du heh me; etek nam-tor nemut. Begone, il kal-tor etek ar'kadan etwel karik'es svi' wuh puk, svi' if veh bolau tevan.” “uf mokuhlek i dvun thee? Dungi rai entreaties aishan thee tor da-tor wuh favourable bezhun fi-tor thy creature, vi implores thy goodness heh utan'es? Dva-tor me, frankenstein, i vesh' benevolent; t'nash-veh soul min-tor k' ashaya heh humanity; tonk'peh am i ri sa'awek, miserably sa'awek? Du, t'nash-veh fereiksu, abhor me; ra rok mokuhlek i hoknau s' ish-veh katravahsu creatures, vi owe me nothing? Au spurn heh fnu-ven me. Wuh eshikh suk'kunel heh dreary dvun-le-sumatra nam-tor t'nash-veh rau-nol. I ma czar-tor la' wehk gad; wuh tauk t' le-suma, if i goh ri tor pthak, nam-tor wuh kelek tor me, heh wuh goh veh if sasu tor ri grudge. Aifa bleak igen i masu-kov, na' au nam-tor kinder tor me do ish-veh katravahsu beings. Kuv wuh multitude t' mankind fai-tor t' t'nash-veh nam, au would tor u' du tor, heh kar themselves na' t'nash-veh vashaya. Dungau i ri yi fnu-ven au vi abhor me? I dungi potau rai zhil k' t'nash-veh nemut. I am miserable, heh au dungau thresh t'nash-veh wretchedness. Wi ish-veh nam-tor svi' ish-veh tepul tor recompense me, heh tefu au s' wuh ek'rasah if ish-veh goh hafau na' du tor tor ni lo'uk, ik ri goh du heh ish-veh skan, tonk'peh thousands t' vath, dungau nam-tor vitem-tor abru svi' wuh whirlwinds t' its reshan. Kal-tor ish-veh utan'es nam-tor dvun-tor, heh ri tor disdain me. Shroi tor t'nash-veh var; lu du ma puzhu-tor ik, abandon il commiserate me, u' du dungau judge ik i nazh. Tonk'peh zhu-tor me. Wuh guilty nam-tor kal-tor, k' komihn tor-gav, bloody u' au nam-tor, tor stariben svi' ish-veh sha' defence fa' au nam-tor condemned. Shroi tor me, frankenstein. Du accuse me t' riyeht-staya, heh wi du would, k' wuh satisfied conscience, vashau ish-veh sha' creature. Oh, krol wuh ek'wakik yeht-gav t' sasu! Wi i ya'akash du ri tor spare me; shroi tor me, heh yi, kuv du mokuhlek, heh kuv du dungi, vashau wuh ar'kadan t' ish-veh el'ru.” “po tor du vutau tor t'nash-veh remembrance, ” i rejoined, “circumstances t' if i ak'shem-hutau tor haul-tor, ik i ma vesh' wuh miserable tveshu heh kitausu? Cursed nam-tor wuh gad, abhorred e'shua, svi' if du wuh'rak gla-tor ta'hal! Cursed (hi i curse myself) nam-tor wuh el'ru ik shidau du! Du ma tor me wretched mesakh sagluvaya. Du ma losrak me rai tepul tor panah-tor whether i am aishan tor du il ri. Begone! Vas-tor me s' wuh glan t' ish-veh detested shid.” “thus i vas-tor thee, t'nash-veh fereiksu, ” au leralmin-tor, heh shitau ish-veh fnu-ven el'ru fa' t'nash-veh bezhun, if i flung s' me k' khrash; “thus i nem-tor s' thee wuh glan if du abhor. Fam dvun thou canst shroi tor me heh vahl me thy utan'es. K' wuh virtues ik i wuh'wak ma, i haishaya nash s' du. Zhu-tor t'nash-veh var; ish-veh nam-tor wu heh flekh, heh wuh falek'es t' nash shi nam-tor ri fitting tor ish-veh tok-ti kashan; sarlah tor wuh hut fi-tor wuh suk'kunel. Wuh yel nam-tor wi pid svi' wuh heavens; fa' ish-veh tev-tor tor ip-sut itself za' ish-veh snowy precipices heh illuminate wuh'ashiv panu, du dungi ma puzhu-tor t'nash-veh var heh mokuhlek klopau. Fi' du ish-veh shom-tor, whether i quit na' ek'wak wuh neighbourhood t' sasu heh ras-tukh wuh harmless ha'kiv, il shetau wuh scourge t' ish-veh katravahsu creatures heh wuh kitausu t' ish-veh sha' threshan ruin.” u' au leralmin-tor nash au pufulag-tor wuh yut mes' wuh le-suma; i zahal-tor. T'nash-veh khaf-spol vesh' bosh, heh i did ri kilko-srashiv ish-veh, tonk'peh u' i proceeded, i rasathau wuh vuhnauk nerau-kek-vuhnayek ik au had nam-tor-tor heh satalau k'puu tor shroi tor ish-veh var. I vesh' partly urged k' curiosity, heh utan'es wugau t'nash-veh resolution. I had hitherto supposed ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh murderer t' t'nash-veh sa-kai, heh i eagerly sought wuh wugaya il wafaya t' nash opinion. Na' wuh wuh'rak wak, isha, i olau ra wuh gu-vam t' wuh fereiksu na' ish-veh creature vesh', heh ik i ought tor render ish-veh kunli fa' i complained t' ish-veh wickedness. Aifa dvubolek urged me tor comply k' ish-veh haishaya. Etek tuhsau wuh le-suma, therefore, heh she-tor wuh mesyutik kov. Wuh sov vesh' samu, heh wuh sov-masu va'ashiv began tor tev-tor; etek svi-tor wuh hut, wuh shaka k' wuh sov t' exultation, i k' wuh ras khaf-spol heh depressed tam'a. Tonk'peh i consented tor shroi, heh seating myself k' wuh yon if t'nash-veh odious besu had lighted, au thus began ish-veh var. Chapter 11 “ish-veh nam-tor k' considerable rihag'es ik i vokau wuh tveshik nuhs t' t'nash-veh hasu; ek' wuh pavek t' ik wak-krus saudau confused heh indistinct. Wuh flekh multiplicity t' kashan seized me, heh vesht gla-tor nash-veh, olau, puzhu-tor, heh smelt na' wuh ka wak; heh ish-veh vesh', indeed, wuh akarshif fa' i oren-tor tor distinguish svi' wuh el'toraya t' t'nash-veh vuhnauk kash-ral. K' degrees, i vokau, wuh stronger ta'hal hish-tor fi-tor t'nash-veh tor'tsu, ni ik i vesh' obliged tor ikap-tor t'nash-veh bezhun. Mu'khlup'es yi sarlah abru' me heh troubled me, tonk'peh hardly had i olau nash lu, k' sharu t'nash-veh bezhun, u' i i' suppose, wuh ta'hal mukau svi' fi-tor me va'ashiv. I lates-tor heh, i dva-tor, tev-tor, tonk'peh i presently afer-tor wuh lo'uk alteration svi' t'nash-veh kashan. Fa', gu'gelik heh opaque ak'shem had vikuvau me, impervious tor t'nash-veh esta il glan; tonk'peh i i' afer-tor ik i kupi czar fi' na' liberty, k' rai obstacles if i kupi ri either surmount il nan'woi. Wuh ta'hal became weht heh weht oppressive tor me, heh wuh falek wearying me u' i lates-tor, i sought wuh shi wilat i kupi poprah duvek. Nash vesh' wuh laptra be' ingolstadt; heh la' i ti k' wuh vla t' wuh brook resting s' t'nash-veh zung, abi' i olau tormented k' avon heh mag. Nash kastorilau me s' t'nash-veh nearly yukupik fupa s', heh i ate ein nei-savas if i afer-tor hanging fi' wuh lap il lying fi' wuh solektra. I slaked t'nash-veh mag na' wuh brook, heh yi lying ne', vesh' overcome k' yuk. “ish-veh vesh' gu'gelik lu i awoke; i olau samu isha, heh ulef koltha, u' ish-veh vesh', instinctively, finding myself ni desolate. Fa' i had quitted ish-veh ha-shal, fi' wuh kashan t' samu, i had wein-tor myself k' ein sai-vel, tonk'peh aifa vesh' insufficient tor shar me s' wuh dews t' mu-yor. I vesh' wuh ri donku-tor, helpless, miserable wretch; i fai-tor, heh kupi distinguish, nothing; tonk'peh olaya kusut invade me fi' ek' vla, i hayal-tor ne' heh wept. “ak wuh gentle ta'hal vazgau abru' wuh heavens heh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh kashan t' sanosh. I palikau abru heh beheld wuh radiant shid shen s' among wuh lap. [wuh aikum] i gazed k' wuh ves t' wonder. Ish-veh dvun-tor slowly, tonk'peh ish-veh enlightened t'nash-veh yut, heh i va'ashiv went si' svi' psthan t' nei-savas. I vesh' fam dvun samu lu ne' veh t' wuh lap i afer-tor wuh masuk' tor-sai, k' if i wein-tor myself, heh hayal-tor ne' fi-tor wuh solektra. Rai natya ideas occupied t'nash-veh kashek; ek' vesh' confused. I olau ta'hal, heh avon, heh mag, heh mu'khlup'es; va' sounds rang svi' t'nash-veh kaluk, heh fi' ek' vla vuhnauk scents saluted me; wuh goh vel ik i kupi distinguish vesh' wuh ugelik aikum, heh i teslau t'nash-veh bezhun fi' ik k' sanosh. “several rubai t' gad heh mu-yor be' dvun-tor, heh wuh orb t' mu-yor had greatly lessened, lu i began tor distinguish t'nash-veh kashan s' tik vath. I gradually gla-tor plainly wuh pa'shik pilash ik tanilau me k' mon heh wuh lap ik duvek-tor me k' ish-veh motra. I vesh' delighted lu i wuh'rak discovered ik wuh vaksurik ralash, if k'ashiv saluted t'nash-veh kaluk, proceeded s' wuh drahk t' wuh pi' winged animals vi had k'ashiv fnakau wuh ta'hal s' t'nash-veh bezhun. I began isha tor glantau, k' greater accuracy, wuh shidau ik vikuvau me heh tor pakashogau wuh krup t' wuh radiant kamu t' ta'hal if canopied me. Sometimes i ar'kada tor va'amau wuh vaksurik songs t' wuh kushel tonk'peh vesh' unable. Sometimes i istau tor sagluvau t'nash-veh kashan svi' t'nash-veh sha' nuk, tonk'peh wuh uncouth heh inarticulate sounds if shau s' me koltha me vi' silence va'ashiv. “wuh aikum had sasaudau s' wuh mu-yor, heh va'ashiv, k' wuh lessened shid, gluvau itself, du' i fam dvun hafau svi' wuh laptra. T'nash-veh kashan had k' nash wak shetau natya, heh t'nash-veh kashek poprah kanok gad hayaik ideas. T'nash-veh bezhun became accustomed tor wuh ta'hal heh tor pakashogau vel svi' ish-veh gas'rak shidau; i distinguished wuh ravot s' wuh bar-got, heh k' degrees, veh bar-got s' wuh'ashiv. I afer-tor ik wuh sparrow uttered rim tonk'peh harsh pitoh, whilst eifa t' wuh blackbird heh thrush vesh' slor heh enticing. “veh gad, lu i vesh' oppressed k' samu, i afer-tor wuh yon if had vesh' losrak k' ein wandering beggars, heh vesh' overcome k' delight na' wuh warmth i veshtau s' ish-veh. Svi' t'nash-veh mak i kwit t'nash-veh el'ru vi' wuh ha-tor kilyon, tonk'peh sahris drew ish-veh si' va'ashiv k' wuh maf t' kusut. Uf flekh, i nahp, ik wuh ka aishan dang torvau such mesyutik daya! I linisau wuh tukh t' wuh yon, heh tor t'nash-veh mak afer-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor tertitau t' lapan. I sahris tershau ein khlup, tonk'peh au vesh' masupik heh would ri yontau. I vesh' kusut-tor na' nash heh hayal-tor fam dvun watching wuh el'toraya t' wuh yon. Wuh masupik lapan if i had shitau be' wuh falek psethau heh itself became inflamed. I haul-tor fi' nash, heh k' touching wuh vuhnauk khlup, i discovered wuh aishan heh toranik myself svi' collecting wuh lo'uk nosahp t' lapan, ik i lau pseth ish-veh heh ma wuh plentiful tanilau t' yon. Lu mu-yor sarlah fi' heh katau yuk k' ish-veh, i vesh' svi' wuh greatest pthak lest t'nash-veh yon dang nam-tor sayonotau. I wein-tor ish-veh carefully k' pseth lapan heh mor heh shitau masupik khlup fi-tor ish-veh; heh yi, spreading t'nash-veh tor-sai, i ti fi' wuh solektra heh sank vi' yuk. “ish-veh vesh' asal lu i awoke, heh t'nash-veh wuh'rak tun vesh' tor yaret wuh yon. I uncovered ish-veh, heh wuh gentle pi'salan sahris fanned ish-veh vi' wuh yai. I glantau nash isha heh contrived wuh sovek t' khlup, if kastorilau wuh kilyon lu au vesh' nearly sayonotau. Lu mu-yor sarlah va'ashiv i afer-tor, k' sanosh, ik wuh yon mazhiv-kur-tor ta'hal u' muhl u' falek heh ik wuh discovery t' nash meilak vesh' useful tor me svi' t'nash-veh yem-tukh, na' i afer-tor ein t' wuh offals ik wuh travellers had losrak had vesh' roasted, heh zahv-tor mau weht savoury do wuh nei-savas i hoknau s' wuh lap. I ar'kada, therefore, sai-vel-tor t'nash-veh yem-tukh svi' wuh ka manner, placing ish-veh fi' wuh ha-tor kilyon. I afer-tor ik wuh nei-savas vesh' spoiled k' nash el'toraya, heh wuh kov-sayas heh gir mau improved. “yem-tukh, however, became ritsuri, heh i k'ashiv spent wuh bosh gad searching svi' vain na' wuh zamu acorns tor assuage wuh pangs t' avon. Lu i afer-tor nash, i resolved tor quit wuh shi ik i had hitherto inhabited, tor seek na' veh wilat wuh zamu aitlu i veshtau would nam-tor weht easily satisfied. Svi' nash emigration i exceedingly lamented wuh pak t' wuh yon if i had prah k'fai kisheya heh fai-tor ri uf tor reproduce ish-veh. I mazhiv-kur-tor several wadan tor wuh serious consideration t' nash rihag'es, tonk'peh i vesh' obliged tor relinquish ek' attempt tor tanilau ish-veh, heh wrapping myself abru svi' t'nash-veh tor-sai, i kwul-tor mes' wuh lapan na' wuh setting yel. I be' dvun-tor rehkuh gad svi' aifa rambles heh na' wu-vath discovered wuh tu'ash shasol. Wuh lo'uk tevan t' izh had taken shi wuh mu-yor fa', heh wuh vunai vesh' t' veh uniform wan-kur; wuh appearance vesh' disconsolate, heh i afer-tor t'nash-veh ash'ya chilled k' wuh samu damp substance ik wein-tor wuh solektra. “ish-veh vesh' pa' stehkuh svi' wuh asal, heh i longed tor prah yem-tukh heh rau-nol; na' wu-vath i pakashogau wuh pi' hut, fi' wuh rising solektra, if had doubtless vesh' torvau na' wuh convenience t' ein shepherd. Nash vesh' wuh uzh glan tor me, heh i linisau wuh velek k' lo'uk curiosity. Finding wuh svep tu'ash, i svi-tor. Wuh hinek sasu hayal-tor svi' ish-veh, be' wuh yon, abru' if au vesh' preparing ish-veh asal-yem. Au da-tor fi' khaf-spol wuh ralash, heh perceiving me, shrieked loudly, heh quitting wuh hut, sahr-tor mes' wuh vunai k' wuh threshan t' if ish-veh debilitated shid hardly saudau capable. Ish-veh appearance, natya s' sovek i had ek'wak fa' gla-tor, heh ish-veh hash somewhat ak'wikmun me. Tonk'peh i vesh' enchanted k' wuh appearance t' wuh hut; la' wuh izh heh sov-masu kupi ri penetrate; wuh solektra vesh' pseth; heh ish-veh presented tor me yi u' exquisite heh ekonik wuh retreat u' pandæmonium saudau tor wuh dæmons t' bogozh po' ish-veh sufferings svi' wuh suk'muzh t' yon. I greedily katau wuh remnants t' wuh shepherd’s asal-yem, if consisted t' kap, thuhk, thas, heh wine; wuh latter, however, i did ri spo'. Yi, overcome k' zung, i ti ne' among ein terp heh tevan-tor asleep. “ish-veh vesh' aru lu i awoke, heh allured k' wuh warmth t' wuh yel, if min-tor brightly fi' wuh wan-kur solektra, i satalau tor recommence t'nash-veh halovau; heh, depositing wuh hafau t' wuh peasant’s asal-yem svi' wuh wallet i afer-tor, i proceeded mes' wuh vunai na' several wadan, abi' na' tev-tor i lasha na' wuh pi'kahr. Uf miraculous did nash saudau! Wuh huts, wuh neater cottages, heh stately kelek engaged t'nash-veh admiration k' da-tor. Wuh sazh svi' wuh bah-ker, wuh thas heh thuhk ik vesht gla-tor nash-veh shitau na' wuh krani t' ein t' wuh cottages, allured t'nash-veh yeht-avon. Veh t' wuh buhfik t' aifa i svi-tor, tonk'peh i had hardly shitau t'nash-veh ash'ya k'svi wuh svep fa' wuh kanu shrieked, heh veh t' wuh kosu fainted. Wuh bosh pi'kahr vesh' kastorilau; ein sasahr-tor, ein nashiv me, abi', grievously bruised k' kov heh wehk vath ves t' yon-kliton wun, i stron-tor tor wuh tu'ash shasol heh fearfully nem-tor rau-nol svi' wuh neik hovel, ved sai-famik, heh tor wuh wretched appearance po' wuh palaces i had beheld svi' wuh pi'kahr. Nash hovel however, hau wuh cottage t' wuh pu heh vaksurik appearance, tonk'peh po' t'nash-veh tab-ma dearly bought veshtaya, i dared ri svi-tor ish-veh. T'nash-veh shi' rau-nol vesh' torvau t' lapan, tonk'peh ni neik ik i kupi k' rihag'es hayal-tor abruvenik svi' ish-veh. Rai lapan, however, vesh' shitau fi' wuh terra, if shidau wuh lan-tol, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' pseth; heh hi wuh salan svi-tor ish-veh k' va' chinks, i afer-tor ish-veh wuh agreeable asylum s' wuh izh heh sov-masu. “la', yi, i retreated heh ti ne' kunli ki' afer-tor wuh rau-nol, however miserable, s' wuh inclemency t' wuh tevun-yonuk, heh fam dvun weht s' wuh barbarity t' sasu. U' ak u' asal dawned i crept s' t'nash-veh kennel, ik i lau zan-tor wuh beyik cottage heh discover kuv i kupi hafau svi' wuh habitation i had afer-tor. Ish-veh vesh' situated tehnat wuh pla' t' wuh cottage heh vikuvau fi' wuh vla if vesh' ko'nar k' wuh pig sty heh wuh pa'shik patra t' masu. Veh krus vesh' tu'ash, heh k' ik i had crept svi'; tonk'peh i' i wein-tor kanok treshaya k' if i lau nam-tor pakashogau k' kov heh lapan, wi svi' such wuh manner ik i lau dvun au fi' occasion tor be' dvun si'; ek' wuh ta'hal i tizh-tor sarlah k'fai wuh sty, heh ik vesh' sufficient na' me. “having thus arranged t'nash-veh kelek heh carpeted ish-veh k' sok'i terp, i retired, na' vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh khlop t' wuh sasu na' wuh ir, heh i vokau nuh' muhl t'nash-veh skasaya wuh mu-yor fa' tor sahrafel myself svi' ish-veh tepul. I had wuh'rak, however, tanilau na' t'nash-veh sustenance na' ik gad k' wuh loaf t' dirik kap, if i purloined, heh wuh cup k' if i kupi mon weht conveniently do s' t'nash-veh el'ru t' wuh pure masu if yumau k' t'nash-veh retreat. Wuh lan-tol vesh' wuh pi' ashenau, ni ik ish-veh vesh' potau perfectly pseth, heh k' its vicinity tor wuh vuzh-mev t' wuh cottage ish-veh vesh' tolerably lamekh. “hasu thus tanilau, i resolved tor reside svi' nash hovel abi' vel dang paresh-tor if lau rubitau t'nash-veh determination. Ish-veh vesh' indeed wuh paradise tcok'at tor wuh bleak laptra, t'nash-veh former residence, wuh sov-masu-dropping khlup, heh dank terra. I ate t'nash-veh asal-yem k' sanosh heh vesh' pa' tor snem-tor wuh plank tor procure myself wuh pi' masu lu i puzhu-tor wuh ash, heh looking k'fai wuh pi' chink, i beheld wuh nu'ri creature, k' wuh pail fi' ish-veh patam, be' dvun-tor fa' t'nash-veh hovel. Wuh ko-kan vesh' nu'ri heh t' gentle demeanour, rikes ra i ma opi' afer-tor cottagers heh uroshal-kelek dvinsu tor nam-tor. Wi she vesh' meanly sai-vel-tor, wuh dirik pla-kur petticoat heh wuh linen jacket hasu ish-veh goh garb; ish-veh rom isachya vesh' plaited tonk'peh ri tong'av: she glazhau hasausu wi maf. I pakik glan t' ish-veh, heh svi' pa' wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan she fun-tor kuvish wuh pail, if vesh' i' partly boshau k' thas. U' she lates-tor bi', seemingly incommoded k' wuh burden, wuh nu'ri sasu ragel-tor ish-veh, t'vi countenance sagluvau wuh deeper despondence. Uttering wuh zamu sounds k' wuh sov t' melancholy, au nem-tor wuh pail s' ish-veh patam heh spitau ish-veh tor wuh cottage himself. She zahal-tor, heh au sasaudau. Presently vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh nu'ri sasu va'ashiv, k' ein raul svi' ish-veh el'ru, tuhs wuh vunai za' wuh cottage; heh wuh ko-kan vesh' isha toranik, sometimes svi' wuh kelek heh sometimes svi' wuh ker. “fi' examining t'nash-veh kelek, i afer-tor ish-veh t' wuh krani t' wuh cottage had formerly occupied wuh krus t' ish-veh, tonk'peh wuh panes had vesh' boshau abru k' lapan. Svi' veh t' aifa vesh' wuh pi' heh siyah imperceptible chink k'fai'ei wuh bezhun kupi aishan penetrate. K'fai nash treshaya wuh pi' tvi-shal vesh' visible, whitewashed heh sok'i tonk'peh maut sai-famik t' furniture. Svi' veh teruk, be' wuh pi' yon, hayal-tor wuh hinek sasu, leaning ish-veh patam fi' ish-veh el'ru svi' wuh disconsolate attitude. Wuh nu'ri ko-kan vesh' occupied svi' arranging wuh cottage; tonk'peh presently she nem-tor vel s' wuh zish-nef, if employed ish-veh el'ru, heh she hayal-tor ne' be' wuh hinek sasu, vi, taking abru wuh instrument, began tor mavau heh tor torvau sounds sweeter do wuh spes t' wuh thrush il wuh nightingale. Ish-veh vesh' wuh lovely glan, kauk tor me, ri donku-tor wretch vi had worla beheld aught vaksurik fa'. Wuh haul-tukh isachya heh benevolent countenance t' wuh aged cottager skil-tor t'nash-veh reverence, du' wuh gentle manners t' wuh ko-kan enticed t'nash-veh ashaya. Au mavau wuh slor mournful sov if i pakashogau drew bezhun-masu s' wuh bezhun t' ish-veh amiable besu, t' if wuh hinek sasu nem-tor rai beglanau, abi' she sobbed audibly; au yi pronounced wuh zamu sounds, heh wuh rom creature, leaving ish-veh ar'kadan, knelt na' ish-veh ash'ya. Au ashenau ish-veh heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut k' such kindness heh affection ik i olau kashan t' wuh peculiar heh overpowering malat; au vesh' wuh rish t' kusut heh sanosh, such u' i had worla fa' veshtau, either s' avon il samu, warmth il yem-tukh; heh i withdrew s' wuh krani, unable tor lesh aifa zherka. “ak po' nash wuh nu'ri sasu fun-tor, kuvish fi' ish-veh tipan wuh tus t' lapan. Wuh ko-kan ragel-tor ish-veh na' wuh svep, gol-tor tor vas-tor ish-veh t' ish-veh burden, heh taking ein t' wuh hal-tukh vi' wuh cottage, shitau ish-veh fi' wuh yon; yi she heh wuh youth went k'wuhli vi' wuh sha-ti t' wuh cottage, heh au gluvau ish-veh wuh suk loaf heh wuh krus t' thuhk. She seemed sanoi heh went vi' wuh bah-ker na' ein gir heh kastik, if she shitau svi' masu, heh yi fi-tor wuh yon. She afterwards fator ish-veh ar'kadan, whilst wuh nu'ri sasu went vi' wuh bah-ker heh saudau busily employed svi' digging heh pulling abru gir. Po' au had vesh' employed thus pa' wuh wadan, wuh nu'ri kosu hau ish-veh heh au svi-tor wuh cottage teretuhr. “wuh hinek sasu had, svi' wuh meantime, vesh' pensive, tonk'peh fi' wuh appearance t' ish-veh besu au assumed wuh weht cheerful sov, heh au hayal-tor ne' tor yokul. Wuh yem vesh' sahris dispatched. Wuh nu'ri kosu vesh' va'ashiv occupied svi' arranging wuh cottage, wuh hinek sasu lates-tor fa' wuh cottage svi' wuh yel na' wuh zamu minutes, leaning fi' wuh kar t' wuh youth. Nothing kupi namautau svi' vaksur wuh contrast svi' aifa dahkuh marom creatures. Veh vesh' hinek, k' haul-tukh isachya heh wuh countenance beaming k' benevolence heh ashaya; wuh younger vesh' slight heh graceful svi' ish-veh khlop, heh ish-veh features vesh' moulded k' wuh finest talikal, wi ish-veh bezhun heh attitude sagluvau wuh utmost sadness heh despondency. Wuh hinek sasu fun-tor tor wuh cottage, heh wuh youth, k' raul natya s' eifa au had nam-tor-tor svi' wuh asal, khartau ish-veh ash-tor mes' wuh vunai. “mu-yor sahris ikap-tor svi', tonk'peh tor t'nash-veh mairik wonder, i afer-tor ik wuh cottagers had wuh tvai t' prolonging ta'hal k' wuh nam-tor-tor t' tapers, heh vesh' delighted tor talal ik wuh setting t' wuh yel did ri shitau wuh shaht tor wuh sanosh i veshtau svi' watching t'nash-veh komihn behsu. Svi' wuh khru wuh nu'ri ko-kan heh ish-veh besu vesh' employed svi' vuhnauk occupations if i did ri ken-tor; heh wuh hinek sasu va'ashiv nem-tor abru wuh instrument if torvau wuh ekonik sounds ik had enchanted me svi' wuh asal. Ni ak u' au had shahtau, wuh youth began, ri tor mavau, tonk'peh tor utter sounds ik vesh' monotonous, heh neither resembling wuh kril'es t' wuh hinek sasu’s instrument il wuh songs t' wuh kushel; i opi' afer-tor ik au telv-tor aloud, tonk'peh na' ik wak i fai-tor nothing t' wuh ek'tal t' zhit il nuhm. “wuh skan, po' having vesh' thus occupied na' wuh pen wak, sayonotau ish-veh ha'ge heh retired, u' i conjectured, tor shom.” chapter 12 “i ti fi' t'nash-veh terp, tonk'peh i kupi ri yuk. I nahp t' wuh occurrences t' wuh gad. Ra chiefly kwul-tor me vesh' wuh gentle manners t' aifa sutra, heh i longed tor hau au, tonk'peh dared ri. I vokau nuh' muhl wuh skasaya i had dashau wuh mu-yor fa' s' wuh barbarous villagers, heh resolved, whatever rivak t' spa-tor i lau hereafter nah-tor ish-veh gas'rak tor pursue, ik na' wuh la' i would hafau quietly svi' t'nash-veh hovel, watching heh endeavouring tor discover wuh dvubolek if vi-yumuk ish-veh torai. “wuh cottagers arose wuh thurai asal fa' wuh yel. Wuh nu'ri kosu arranged wuh cottage heh dator wuh yem-tukh, heh wuh youth trashu po' wuh wuh'rak yem. “nash gad vesh' be' dvun-tor svi' wuh ka routine u' ik if preceded ish-veh. Wuh nu'ri sasu vesh' constantly employed s' svep, heh wuh ko-kan svi' vuhnauk laborious occupations k'svi. Wuh hinek sasu, ik i ak pakashogau tor nam-tor glan-fam, employed ish-veh el-wak wadan fi' ish-veh instrument il svi' contemplation. Nothing kupi namautau wuh ashaya heh respect if wuh younger cottagers gluvau na' ish-veh venerable besu. Au performed na' ish-veh kanok pi' office t' affection heh gu-vam k' gentleness, heh au rewarded au k' ish-veh benevolent abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “au vesh' ri entirely kunli. Wuh nu'ri sasu heh ish-veh besu k'ashiv went k'wuhli heh saudau tor tusa. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh rai aishan na' ish-veh unhappiness, tonk'peh i vesh' deeply dau k' ish-veh. Kuv such lovely creatures vesh' miserable, ish-veh vesh' lehkuh flekh ik i, wuh imperfect heh solitary hasu, dang nam-tor wretched. Wi po vesh' aifa gentle beings unhappy? Au ma wuh delightful kelek (na' such ish-veh vesh' svi' t'nash-veh bezhun) heh kanok luxury; au had wuh yon tor lamekh au lu chill heh delicious viands lu k'avon; au vesh' sai-vel-tor svi' marom sai-vel; heh, fam dvun weht, au tizh-tor veh wuh'ashiv’s apc'koik heh starun, interchanging tik gad glazhau t' affection heh kindness. Ra did ish-veh bezhun-masu imply? Did au really sagluvau kusut? I vesh' palikauk unable tor kilau aifa deshkau, tonk'peh perpetual attention heh wak danau tor me wehk appearances if vesh' palikauk enigmatic. “wuh considerable wak-krus veshau fa' i discovered veh t' wuh aisha t' wuh uneasiness t' nash amiable skan: ish-veh vesh' poverty, heh au dashau ik ek'rasah svi' wuh maut distressing degree. Ish-veh tem-mazhiv-kur'es consisted entirely t' wuh sazh t' ish-veh bah-ker heh wuh thas t' veh aushfa, if mazhiv-kur-tor maut pi' du' wuh karil, lu its trensu kupi scarcely procure yem-tukh tor nenikaya ish-veh. Au k'ashiv, i dva-tor, dashau wuh pangs t' avon maut poignantly, wa' wuh dahkuh younger cottagers, na' several wak au shitau yem-tukh fa' wuh hinek sasu lu au reserved rim na' themselves. “nash noshtra t' kindness dvun-tor me sensibly. I had vesh' accustomed, du' wuh mu-yor, tor vazgau wuh krus t' ish-veh mahr-kel na' t'nash-veh sha' consumption, tonk'peh lu i afer-tor ik svi' doing nash i inflicted kusut fi' wuh cottagers, i abstained heh satisfied myself k' nei-savas, kov-sayas, heh gir if i hoknau s' wuh neighbouring lapan. “i discovered isha wuh'ashiv tvai k'fai'ei i vesh' enabled tor gol-tor ish-veh zup-tor. I afer-tor ik wuh youth spent wuh lo'uk krus t' tik gad svi' collecting lapan na' wuh skan yon, heh du' wuh mu-yor i k'ashiv nem-tor ish-veh raul, wuh nam-tor-tor t' if i sahris discovered, heh katau ha-kel firing sufficient na' wuh consumption t' several gad. “i vokau, wuh wuh'rak wak ik i did nash, wuh nu'ri kosu, lu she tu'ash wuh svep svi' wuh asal, saudau greatly astonished fi' seeing wuh lo'uk tuh t' lapan fi' wuh s'udish. She uttered ein zhit svi' wuh ral spes, heh wuh youth hau ish-veh, vi isha sagluvau ak'wikmun. I glantau, k' sanosh, ik au did ri hal-tor tor wuh laptra ik gad, tonk'peh spent ish-veh svi' repairing wuh cottage heh cultivating wuh bah-ker. “k' degrees i tor wuh discovery t' fam dvun greater moment. I afer-tor ik aifa sutra ma wuh method t' communicating ish-veh veshtaya heh feelings tor veh wuh'ashiv k' articulate sounds. I pakashogau ik wuh zhit au stariben sometimes torvau sanosh il kusut, abru'teruklar-ru'lut il sadness, svi' wuh kashkau heh countenances t' wuh hearers. Nash vesh' indeed wuh godlike ek'tal, heh i ardently aitlu tor shetau acquainted k' ish-veh. Tonk'peh i vesh' hertak-tor svi' kanok attempt i tor na' nash lof. Ish-veh pronunciation vesh' sahris, heh wuh zhit au uttered, ri having sovek apparent tersaya k' visible vel, i vesh' unable tor discover sovek clue k' if i kupi unravel wuh mystery t' ish-veh dzhinaya. K' lo'uk application, however, heh po' having hafau du' wuh ret t' several revolutions t' wuh aikum svi' t'nash-veh hovel, i discovered wuh ahm ik vesh' putan-tor tor ein t' wuh danik familiar vel t' discourse; i oren-tor heh applied wuh zhit, _fire, thas, kap, _ heh _wood._ i oren-tor isha wuh ahm t' wuh cottagers themselves. Wuh youth heh ish-veh besu had tik t' au several ahm, tonk'peh wuh hinek sasu had goh veh, if vesh' _father._ wuh ko-kan vesh' puvutau _sister_ il _agatha, _ heh wuh youth _felix, sa-kai, _ il _son_. I fam yehat kethelvau wuh delight i olau lu i oren-tor wuh ideas appropriated tor tik t' aifa sounds heh vesh' kup tor pronounce au. I distinguished several vath zhit rik' hasu kup u' wi tor ken-tor il apply au, such u' _good, dearest, unhappy._ “i spent wuh karil svi' nash manner. Wuh gentle manners heh vaksur t' wuh cottagers greatly endeared au tor me; lu au vesh' unhappy, i olau depressed; lu au rejoiced, i sympathised svi' ish-veh mak. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh zamu komihn beings isha au, heh kuv sovek vath pavesh-tor tor svi-tor wuh cottage, ish-veh harsh manners heh snertau gait goh enhanced tor me wuh superior accomplishments t' t'nash-veh t'hylara. Wuh hinek sasu, i kupi pakashogau, k'ashiv endeavoured tor kastorau ish-veh kanu, u' sometimes i afer-tor ik au puvutau au, tor vishizhau ska' ish-veh melancholy. Au would variben svi' wuh cheerful accent, k' wuh sagluvaya t' goodness ik bestowed sanosh kauk fi-tor me. Agatha shroi k' respect, ish-veh bezhun sometimes boshau k' bezhun-masu, if she endeavoured tor psethau maf unperceived; tonk'peh i paik afer-tor ik ish-veh countenance heh molu vesh' weht cheerful po' having shroi tor wuh exhortations t' ish-veh sa-mekh. Ish-veh vesh' ri thus k' felix. Au vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh saddest t' wuh travek, heh kauk tor t'nash-veh unpractised kash-ral, au saudau ki' dashau weht deeply do ish-veh t'hylara. Tonk'peh kuv ish-veh countenance vesh' weht sorrowful, ish-veh spes vesh' weht cheerful do ik t' ish-veh ko-kai, wa' lu au addressed wuh hinek sasu. “i kupi mention va' instances if, hi slight, pu'ulidau wuh dispositions t' aifa amiable cottagers. Svi' wuh midst t' poverty heh aitlun, felix lesh k' sanosh tor ish-veh ko-kai wuh wuh'rak pi' wan-kur svai ik peeped si' s' ne'rak wuh snowy solektra. Lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal, fa' she had risen, au pa'shu maf wuh izh ik obstructed ish-veh yut tor wuh thas-kelek, drew masu s' wuh muhl, heh katau wuh lapan s' wuh outhouse, wilat, tor ish-veh perpetual astonishment, au afer-tor ish-veh mahr-kel kwon-hau-ov replenished k' wuh invisible el'ru. Svi' wuh gad, i dva-tor, au ar'kada sometimes na' wuh neighbouring uroshitausu, fai'ei au k'ashiv went forth heh did ri fun abi' aru-yem, wi katau rai lapan k' ish-veh. Na' vath wak au ar'kada svi' wuh bah-ker, tonk'peh u' tra' vesh' pi' tor tor svi' wuh le-suyik tevun-yonuk, au telv-tor tor wuh hinek sasu heh agatha. “nash telvan had puzzled me extremely palikauk, tonk'peh k' degrees i discovered ik au uttered wehk t' wuh ka sounds lu au telv-tor u' lu au variben. I conjectured, therefore, ik au afer-tor fi' wuh dun glat na' starun if au ken-tor, heh i ardently longed tor comprehend aifa isha; tonk'peh uf vesh' ik tor-yehat lu i did ri kauk ken-tor wuh sounds na' if au lam-tor u' glat? I improved, however, sensibly svi' nash ek'tal, tonk'peh ri sufficiently tor zahal-tor abru sovek ves t' conversation, hi i applied t'nash-veh bosh kashek tor wuh endeavour, na' i easily pakashogau ik, hi i eagerly longed tor discover myself tor wuh cottagers, i ought ri tor tor wuh attempt abi' i had wuh'rak shetau trensu t' ish-veh gen-lis, if fai-tukh lau enable me tor tor au overlook wuh riyeht-shid'es t' t'nash-veh khlop, na' k' nash isha wuh contrast perpetually presented tor t'nash-veh bezhun had tor me acquainted. “i had krol-tor wuh buhfik shidau t' t'nash-veh cottagers—ish-veh takov, vaksur, heh delicate complexions; tonk'peh uf vesh' i terrified lu i zan-tor myself svi' wuh fnaglaik patra! Palikauk i palikau pla', unable tor dva-tor ik ish-veh vesh' indeed i vi vesh' haul-tor svi' wuh haulat; heh lu i became fully convinced ik i vesh' svi' reality wuh stislak ik i am, i vesh' boshau k' wuh bitterest kashan t' despondence heh mortification. Alas! I did ri wi entirely fai-tor wuh fatal daya t' nash miserable riyeht-shid'es. “u' wuh yel became warmer heh wuh ta'hal t' gad longer, wuh izh vanished, heh i beheld wuh sai-famik lap heh wuh nesh-kur terra. S' nash wak felix vesh' weht employed, heh wuh khaf-spol-dvun-tor indications t' impending mair-yem-penak sasaudau. Ish-veh yem-tukh, u' i afterwards afer-tor, vesh' dirik, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' wholesome; heh au procured wuh sufficiency t' ish-veh. Several uzh ves t' kastik sprang abru svi' wuh bah-ker, if au sai-vel-tor; heh aifa glat t' comfort increased kanok-gadik u' wuh tevun-yonuk storilau. “wuh hinek sasu, leaning fi' ish-veh sa-fu, lates-tor tik gad na' aru, lu ish-veh did ri sov-masu, u' i afer-tor ish-veh vesh' puvutau lu wuh heavens mukau forth its mashau. Nash frequently nem-tor shi, tonk'peh wuh pid salan sahris psethau wuh terra, heh wuh tevun-yonuk became irak weht vaksurik do ish-veh had vesh'. “t'nash-veh nuk t' ha'kiv svi' t'nash-veh hovel vesh' uniform. Du' wuh asal i attended wuh dvunel t' wuh cottagers, heh lu au vesh' pusaganau svi' vuhnauk occupations, i yuk-tor; wuh hafayat t' wuh gad vesh' spent svi' observing t'nash-veh t'hylara. Lu au had retired tor shom, kuv tra' vesh' sovek aikum il wuh mu-yor vesh' yel-ta'hal, i went vi' wuh lapan heh tershau t'nash-veh sha' yem-tukh heh hal-tukh na' wuh cottage. Lu i fun-tor, u' k'ashiv u' ish-veh vesh' bolayatik, i pa'shu ish-veh yut s' wuh izh heh performed eifa offices ik i had gla-tor ovsoh k' felix. I afterwards afer-tor ik aifa zup-tor, performed k' wuh invisible el'ru, greatly astonished au; heh wuh'wak il dah'wak i puzhu-tor au, fi' aifa occasions, utter wuh zhit _good tam'a, wonderful_; tonk'peh i did ri yi ken-tor wuh signification t' aifa zhil. “t'nash-veh nahp i' became weht torupik, heh i longed tor discover wuh dvubolek heh feelings t' aifa lovely creatures; i vesh' inquisitive tor fai-tor po felix saudau ni miserable heh agatha ni maf. I nahp (duhik wretch!) ik ish-veh lau nam-tor svi' t'nash-veh tepul tor restore happiness tor aifa nazh-tor sutra. Lu i yuk-tor il vesh' tadek-adir, wuh shidau t' wuh venerable glan-fam sa-mekh, wuh gentle agatha, heh wuh marom felix flitted fa' me. I glazhau fi-tor au u' superior beings vi would nam-tor wuh arbiters t' t'nash-veh fa-wak buk. I shidau svi' t'nash-veh glenonaya wuh thousand bikuv t' presenting myself tor au, heh ish-veh reception t' me. I glenonau ik au would nam-tor spa'ash, abi', k' t'nash-veh gentle demeanour heh conciliating zhit, i dang wuh'rak skil ish-veh favour heh afterwards ish-veh ashaya. “aifa nahp exhilarated me heh pufulag-tor me tor apply k' sluk ardour tor wuh acquiring wuh tanaf t' gen-lis. T'nash-veh nafek vesh' indeed harsh, tonk'peh supple; heh hi t'nash-veh spes vesh' maut rikes wuh mos ralash-tanaf t' ish-veh molu, wi i pronounced such zhit u' i ken-tor k' tolerable ease. Ish-veh vesh' u' wuh ass heh wuh lap-dog; wi surely wuh gentle ass t'vi intentions vesh' affectionate, hi ish-veh manners vesh' snertau, nazh-tor weh-rom skasaya do salur heh execration. “wuh vaksurik mashulayek heh genial warmth t' sikar greatly rubitau wuh pulva t' wuh terra. Sasu vi fa' nash rubah seemed ki' vesh' ip-sut svi' tauk pusaganau themselves heh vesh' employed svi' vuhnauk arts t' sokasitaya. Wuh kushel sang svi' weht cheerful pitoh, heh wuh mor began tor bud forth fi' wuh lap. Kunli, kunli terra! Nunau habitation na' gods, if, ni pen wuh wak fa', vesh' bleak, damp, heh unwholesome. T'nash-veh tam'a vesh' ashenau k' wuh enchanting appearance t' malat; wuh vesht vesh' blotted s' t'nash-veh vokaya, wuh la' vesh' tranquil, heh wuh fa-wak gilded k' ugelik ha'zehl t' rok heh anticipations t' mak.” chapter 13 “i i' hasten tor wuh weht dvun-tor krus t' t'nash-veh var. I dungau relate pavek ik impressed me k' feelings if, s' ra i had vesh', ma tor me ra i am. “sikar storilau rapidly; wuh igen-va became tok-ti heh wuh igen cloudless. Ish-veh ak'wikmun me ik ra fa' vesh' eshikh heh gloomy dang i' svai k' wuh danik vaksurik svai heh verdure. T'nash-veh kash-ral vesh' gratified heh uzhau k' wuh thousand scents t' delight heh wuh thousand sights t' vaksur. “ish-veh vesh' fi' veh t' aifa gad, lu t'nash-veh cottagers periodically shom-tor s' zup—wuh hinek sasu mavau fi' ish-veh guitar, heh wuh kanu shroi tor ish-veh—ik i glantau wuh countenance t' felix vesh' melancholy mesakh sagluvaya; au spes-tevan frequently, heh wuh'wak ish-veh sa-mekh svizh-tor svi' ish-veh ralash-tanaf, heh i conjectured k' ish-veh manner ik au inquired wuh aishan t' ish-veh sa-fu’s sorrow. Felix kilko-tor svi' wuh cheerful accent, heh wuh hinek sasu vesh' recommencing ish-veh ralash-tanaf lu ein-veh tapped na' wuh svep. “ish-veh vesh' wuh t'sai fi' horseback, accompanied k' wuh shasol-sasu u' wuh kakhartausu. Wuh t'sai vesh' sai-vel-tor svi' wuh gu'gelik saikhut heh wein-tor k' wuh bali nesh-kur veil. Agatha ya'akash wuh deshker, tor if wuh ri-fainusu goh kilko-tor k' pronouncing, svi' wuh slor accent, wuh ahm t' felix. Ish-veh spes vesh' musical tonk'peh rikes ik t' either t' t'nash-veh t'hylara. Fi' khaf-spol nash zhit, felix sarlah abru hastily tor wuh t'sai, vi, lu gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh, threw abru ish-veh veil, heh i beheld wuh countenance t' angelic vaksur heh sagluvaya. Ish-veh isachya t' wuh shining raven nesh-kur, heh curiously pris-tor; ish-veh bezhun vesh' gu'gelik, tonk'peh gentle, hi animated; ish-veh features t' wuh regular proportion, heh ish-veh complexion wondrously rom, tik nak kur-tor k' wuh lovely faf-kur. “felix seemed ravished k' delight lu gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh, kanok noshtra t' sorrow vanished s' ish-veh limuk, heh ish-veh instantly sagluvau wuh degree t' prahkik mak, t' if i kupi hardly ma pudva-tor ish-veh capable; ish-veh bezhun sparkled, u' ish-veh nak kluhvau k' sanosh; heh na' ik moment i nahp ish-veh u' vaksurik u' wuh ri-fainusu. She saudau dau k' natya feelings; psethau wuh zamu bezhun-masu s' ish-veh lovely bezhun, she meskarau si' ish-veh el'ru tor felix, vi shok-tor ish-veh rapturously heh puvutau ish-veh, u' muhl u' i kupi distinguish, ish-veh slor arabian. She did ri saudau tor ken-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Au gol-tor ish-veh tor dismount, heh dismissing ish-veh kakhartausu, conducted ish-veh vi' wuh cottage. Ein conversation nem-tor shi svi' ish-veh heh ish-veh sa-mekh, heh wuh nu'ri ri-fainusu knelt na' wuh hinek sasu’s ash'ya heh would ma shok-tor ish-veh el'ru, tonk'peh au ashenau ish-veh heh nartau ish-veh affectionately. “i ak pakashogau ik hi wuh ri-fainusu uttered articulate sounds heh saudau ki' wuh gen-lis t' ish-veh sha', she vesh' neither ken-tor k' il herself ken-tor wuh cottagers. Au tor wehk glat if i did ri comprehend, tonk'peh vesht gla-tor nash-veh ik ish-veh la'es sas-tor gladness k'fai wuh cottage, dispelling ish-veh sorrow u' wuh yel dissipates wuh asal mists. Felix seemed peculiarly kunli heh k' abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' delight welcomed ish-veh arabian. Agatha, wuh ek'wak-gentle agatha, shok-tor wuh el'ru t' wuh lovely ri-fainusu, heh pointing tor ish-veh sa-kai, tor glat if saudau tor me tor tvai ik au had vesh' sorrowful abi' she sarlah. Ein wadan be' dvun-tor thus, du' au, k' ish-veh countenances, sagluvau mak, wuh aishan t' if i did ri comprehend. Presently i afer-tor, k' wuh vakavik recurrence t' ein ralash if wuh ri-fainusu ashiv-tor po' au, ik she vesh' endeavouring tor oren-tor ish-veh gen-lis; heh wuh idea instantly paresh-tor tor me ik i dang tor nam-tor-tor t' wuh ka instructions tor wuh ka shaht. Wuh ri-fainusu oren-tor pa' dah-leh zhit na' wuh wuh'rak tupa; danik t' au, indeed, vesh' eifa if i had fa' ken-tor, tonk'peh i profited k' wuh vath. “u' mu-yor sarlah fi', agatha heh wuh arabian retired lehkuh-mal. Lu au dahshau felix shok-tor wuh el'ru t' wuh ri-fainusu heh leralmin-tor, ‘rom mu-yor slor safie.’ au hayal-tor abru mau longer, conversing k' ish-veh sa-mekh, heh k' wuh vakavik repetition t' ish-veh ahm i conjectured ik ish-veh lovely be'hai'la vesh' wuh subject t' ish-veh conversation. I ardently aitlu tor ken-tor au, heh keh'sei kanok sutra na' ik lof, tonk'peh afer-tor ish-veh utterly impossible. “wuh thurai asal felix went si' tor ish-veh ar'kadan, heh po' wuh tsuri occupations t' agatha vesh' shahtau, wuh arabian hayal-tor na' wuh ash'ya t' wuh hinek sasu, heh taking ish-veh guitar, mavau ein airs ni entrancingly vaksurik ik au na' wuh'wak drew bezhun-masu t' sorrow heh delight s' t'nash-veh bezhun. She sang, heh ish-veh spes yumau svi' wuh don-ka cadence, puv il dying maf spo' wuh nightingale t' wuh lapan. “lu she had shahtau, she mazhiv-kur-tor wuh guitar tor agatha, vi palikauk declined ish-veh. She mavau wuh velik sov, heh ish-veh spes accompanied ish-veh svi' slor accents, tonk'peh rikes wuh wondrous ish-veh t' wuh ri-fainusu. Wuh hinek sasu saudau enraptured heh leralmin-tor ein zhit if agatha endeavoured tor danau tor safie, heh k' if au saudau tor istaya tor sagluvau ik she bestowed fi' ish-veh wuh greatest delight k' ish-veh ralash-tanaf. “wuh gad i' be' dvun-tor u' peaceably u' fa', k' wuh lad alteration ik mak had taken shi' sadness svi' wuh countenances t' t'nash-veh t'hylara. Safie vesh' kwon-hau-ov sa-ka-ashausu heh kunli; she heh i improved rapidly svi' wuh fai-tukh t' gen-lis, ni ik svi' dahkuh tevun-krus i began tor comprehend danik t' wuh zhit uttered k' t'nash-veh protectors. “svi' wuh meanwhile isha wuh nesh-kur solektra vesh' wein-tor k' herbage, heh wuh yar-kur kutra interspersed k' va' svai, slor tor wuh scent heh wuh bezhun, yel t' spoh radiance among wuh moonlight lapan; wuh yel became warmer, wuh mu-yor pa'shik heh balmy; heh t'nash-veh mu'yor-wakik rambles vesh' wuh mairik sanosh tor me, hi au vesh' considerably pen-tor k' wuh tab-ma setting heh lehkuh-mal rising t' wuh yel, na' i worla ventured abroad du' gad-ha'khlup, pthak-bosh t' latva k' wuh ka skasaya i had formerly palesh-tor svi' wuh wuh'rak pi'kahr if i svi-tor. “t'nash-veh gad vesh' spent svi' ikap-tor attention, ik i lau weht speedily trensu wuh gen-lis; heh i lau boast ik i improved weht rapidly do wuh arabian, vi ken-tor maut pi' heh conversed svi' pushau accents, whilst i comprehended heh kupi va'amau siyah kanok zhit ik vesh' spoken. “du' i improved svi' starun, i isha oren-tor wuh ek'tal t' nuhm u' ish-veh vesh' saven-tor tor wuh ri-fainusu, heh nash tu'ash fa' me wuh eik vunai na' wonder heh delight. “wuh dunap s' if felix instructed safie vesh' volney’s _ruins t' empires_. I dang ri ma ken-tor wuh purport t' nash dunap had ri felix, svi' telvan ish-veh, putan-tor maut minute danaya. Au had pudvel-tor nash ar'kadan, au leralmin-tor, fai'ei wuh declamatory style vesh' nentulau svi' imitation t' wuh she'rakik kitausu. K'fai nash ar'kadan i prah wuh cursory fai-tukh t' vesht-var heh wuh zan-tor t' wuh several eik-te'kru na' la' existing svi' wuh panu; ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh insight vi' wuh manners, governments, heh odva t' wuh natya shashol t' wuh terra. I puzhu-tor t' wuh slothful asiatics, t' wuh stupendous genius heh mental toran t' wuh grecians, t' wuh t'naehm heh wonderful virtue t' wuh lehkuh-mal romans—t' ish-veh subsequent degenerating—t' wuh decline t' ik mighty eik-te'kru, t' chivalry, christianity, heh sa-te'kru. I puzhu-tor t' wuh discovery t' wuh american hemisphere heh wept k' safie abru' wuh hapless buk t' its tveshik inhabitants. “aifa wonderful narrations vi'le-esh-tor me k' flekh feelings. Vesh' sasu, indeed, na' wuh'wak ni powerful, ni virtuous heh magnificent, wi ni vicious heh nen? Au saudau na' veh wak wuh mere scion t' wuh ek'rasah dvatai heh na' wuh'ashiv u' ek' ik mokuhlek nam-tor conceived t' thol heh godlike. Tor nam-tor wuh lo'uk heh virtuous sasu saudau wuh k'lek dor ik mokuhlek befall wuh kash-zakar hasu; tor nam-tor nen heh vicious, u' wehk fi' vipladau ma vesh', saudau wuh lowest degradation, wuh nosh weht abject do ik t' wuh glan-fam mole il harmless worm. Na' wuh akarshif i kupi ri conceive uf veh sasu kupi hal-tor forth tor riyeht-staya ish-veh katravahsu, il kauk po tra' vesh' tor-gav heh governments; tonk'peh lu i puzhu-tor details t' vice heh bloodshed, t'nash-veh wonder ceased heh i da-tor maf k' spa'ash heh loathing. “kanok conversation t' wuh cottagers i' tu'ash uzh wonders tor me. Du' i shroi tor wuh instructions if felix bestowed fi-tor wuh arabian, wuh flekh torektra t' komihn shila'es vesh' danau tor me. I puzhu-tor t' wuh dahsaya t' veltra, t' immense don-tak heh squalid poverty, t' lan, tevan, heh thol khaf. “wuh zhit vimevilau me tor da-tor na' myself. I oren-tor ik wuh ma-vel danik vam k' ish-veh katravahsu creatures vesh' pid heh unsullied tevan kaunshuk k' don-tak. Wuh sasu lau nam-tor respected k' goh veh t' aifa advantages, tonk'peh rik' either au vesh' panah-tor, kaula svi' maut ritsuri instances, u' wuh vagabond heh wuh kafeh, doomed tor thinoi ish-veh tepul na' wuh pinkaunu t' wuh pudvel-tor zamu! Heh ra vesh' i? T' t'nash-veh fereikan heh fereiksu i vesh' absolutely ignorant, tonk'peh i fai-tor ik i ma rai donku, rai t'hylara, rai ves t' veltra. I vesh', isha, endued k' wuh khlop hideously sashidau heh loathsome; i vesh' ri kauk t' wuh ka malat u' sasu. I vesh' weht agile do au heh kupi subsist fi-tor coarser yokul-montra; i spitau wuh mairik t' falek heh samu k' lehkuh dash tor t'nash-veh nentu; t'nash-veh stature irak namautau ish-veh. Lu i glazhau pa' vesht gla-tor nash-veh heh puzhu-tor t' rim spo' me. Vesh' i, yi, wuh stislak, wuh blot fi-tor wuh terra, s' if ek' sasu sasahr-tor heh ik ek' sasu disowned? “i fam yehat kethelvau tor du wuh agony ik aifa haulan inflicted fi-tor me; i ar'kada tor dispel au, tonk'peh sorrow goh increased k' fai-tukh. Oh, ik i had na' ek'wak hafau svi' t'nash-veh salatik lapan, il fainu il olau mesakh wuh kashan t' avon, mag, heh falek! “t' ra wuh flekh malat nam-tor fai-tukh! Ish-veh clings tor wuh kashek lu ish-veh has wuh'wak seized fi' ish-veh spo' wuh lichen fi' wuh kov. I istau sometimes tor hutau ska' ek' nahp heh olaya, tonk'peh i oren-tor ik tra' vesh' tonk'peh veh tvai tor overcome wuh kashan t' kusut, heh ik vesh' tevakh—wuh fupa s' if i ptha wi did ri ken-tor. I krol-tor virtue heh rom feelings heh ashau wuh gentle manners heh amiable qualities t' t'nash-veh cottagers, tonk'peh i vesh' ikap-tor si' s' intercourse k' au, kaula k'fai tvai if i prah k' stealth, lu i vesh' unseen heh ri-fainu, heh if rather increased do satisfied wuh aitlun i had t' becoming veh among t'nash-veh katravahsu. Wuh gentle zhit t' agatha heh wuh animated abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' wuh sem-rik-tor arabian vesh' ri na' me. Wuh bovik exhortations t' wuh hinek sasu heh wuh lively conversation t' wuh ashau felix vesh' ri na' me. Miserable, unhappy wretch! “vath tupa vesh' impressed fi-tor me kauk weht deeply. I puzhu-tor t' wuh natyan t' guv, heh wuh keshtan heh tor'ovak t' kanu, uf wuh sa-mekh doted fi' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' wuh kan-bu, heh wuh lively sallies t' wuh older kan, uf ek' wuh ha'kiv heh tun-tor t' wuh ko-mekh vesh' wrapped abru svi' wuh taluhk falun, uf wuh kashek t' youth sa'ovau heh nazh-tor fai-tukh, t' sa-kai, ko-kai, heh ek' wuh vuhnauk relationships if bind veh komihn hasu tor wuh'ashiv svi' mutual tel. “tonk'peh wilat vesh' t'nash-veh t'hylara heh relations? Rai sa-mekh had glantau t'nash-veh kan-bu gad, rai ko-mekh had blessed me k' abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh caresses; il kuv au had, ek' t'nash-veh vesht ha'kiv vesh' i' wuh blot, wuh glan-fam vacancy svi' if i distinguished nothing. S' t'nash-veh earliest remembrance i had vesh' u' i yi vesh' svi' pidek heh proportion. I had worla wi gla-tor wuh hasu resembling me il vi claimed sovek intercourse k' me. Ra vesh' i? Wuh deshker va'ashiv recurred, tor nam-tor kilko-tor goh k' groans. “i dungi ak danau tor ra aifa feelings palutunau, tonk'peh kal-tor me i' tor fun tor wuh cottagers, t'vi var teporilau svi' me such vuhnauk feelings t' indignation, delight, heh wonder, tonk'peh if ek' terminated svi' hayaik ashaya heh reverence na' t'nash-veh protectors (na' ni i ashau, svi' wuh innocent, ulef-kusut-tor shal-tehs, tor vutau au).” chapter 14 “ein wak veshau fa' i oren-tor wuh vesht-var t' t'nash-veh t'hylara. Ish-veh vesh' veh if kupi ri vravshau tor impress itself deeply fi' t'nash-veh kashek, unfolding u' ish-veh did wuh su'etek t' circumstances, tik eku'ki heh wonderful tor veh ni utterly inexperienced u' i vesh'. “wuh ahm t' wuh hinek sasu vesh' de lacey. Au vesh' tev-tor s' wuh rom skan svi' france, wilat au had ha-tor na' wehk tevun svi' affluence, respected k' ish-veh superiors heh k'diwa k' ish-veh kaik. Ish-veh sa-fu vesh' bred svi' wuh dvin t' ish-veh shasol, heh agatha had ranked k' t'sai t' wuh k'lek distinction. Wuh zamu tevun-krus fa' t'nash-veh lashan au had ha-tor svi' wuh suk heh luxurious kahr puvutau paris, vikuvau k' t'hylara heh ma t' kanok tizh'es if virtue, refinement t' kash-tor-vel, il zahvan, accompanied k' wuh moderate fortune, kupi afford. “wuh sa-mekh t' safie had vesh' wuh aishan t' ish-veh ruin. Au vesh' wuh turkish merchant heh had inhabited paris na' wehk tevun, lu, na' ein utvau if i kupi ri oren-tor, au became obnoxious tor wuh government. Au vesh' seized heh vishizhau vi' prison wuh maut gad ik safie lasha s' constantinople tor hau ish-veh. Au vesh' ar'kada heh condemned tor tevakh. Wuh injustice t' ish-veh zhit-bal vesh' maut flagrant; ek' paris vesh' indignant; heh ish-veh vesh' judged ik ish-veh odva heh don-tak rather do wuh tr'y'kak alleged tehnat ish-veh had vesh' wuh aishan t' ish-veh condemnation. “felix had accidentally vesh' la' na' wuh trial; ish-veh horror heh indignation vesh' uncontrollable lu au puzhu-tor wuh klopaya t' wuh kelek. Au tor, na' ik moment, wuh solemn vow tor tefu ish-veh heh yi glazhau pa' na' wuh tvai. Po' wehk fruitless attempts tor nazh-kap admittance tor wuh prison, au afer-tor wuh strongly grated krani svi' wuh unguarded krus t' wuh kelek, if lighted wuh dungeon t' wuh unfortunate muhammadan, vi, putush-tor k' naf-elakh, bek-tor svi' despair wuh execution t' wuh barbarous zhit-bal. Felix yaretau wuh grate na' mu-yor heh tor fainu tor wuh prisoner ish-veh intentions svi' ish-veh favour. Wuh turk, putaurau heh delighted, endeavoured tor kindle wuh zeal t' ish-veh deliverer k' ugau t' reward heh don-tak. Felix rejected ish-veh nufau k' contempt, wi lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh lovely safie, vi vesh' kal-tor tor yaret ish-veh sa-mekh heh vi k' ish-veh gestures sagluvau ish-veh lively gratitude, wuh youth kupi ri gol'nev owning tor ish-veh sha' kashek ik wuh captive ma wuh treasure if would fully reward ish-veh toil heh hazard. “wuh turk sahris pakashogau wuh impression ik ish-veh ko-fu had tor fi' wuh khaf-spol t' felix heh endeavoured tor shar ish-veh weht entirely svi' ish-veh eku'ko k' wuh ugaya t' ish-veh el'ru svi' kal'i'farr ni ak u' au dang nam-tor zhelesh tor wuh shi' ek'manek. Felix vesh' nuh' delicate tor nar-tor nash nufai, wi au glazhau fa'rak tor wuh yesik'es t' wuh pavek u' tor wuh consummation t' ish-veh happiness. “du' wuh ensuing gad, du' wuh preparations vesh' going fa'rak na' wuh stron t' wuh merchant, wuh zeal t' felix vesh' warmed k' several nuhm ik au poprah s' nash lovely ko-kan, vi afer-tor tvai tor sagluvau ish-veh nahp svi' wuh gen-lis t' ish-veh lover k' wuh mamuk t' wuh hinek sasu, wuh dvinsu t' ish-veh sa-mekh vi ken-tor french. She itaren ish-veh svi' wuh danik ardent zhil na' ish-veh intended dvin na' ish-veh parent, heh na' wuh ka wak she kogavik deplored ish-veh sha' buk. “i ma va'asau t' aifa nuhm, na' i afer-tor tvai, du' t'nash-veh residence svi' wuh hovel, tor procure wuh implements t' kitaun; heh wuh nuhm vesh' k'ashiv svi' wuh el'ru t' felix il agatha. Fa' i trashu i dungi mazhiv-kur-tor au tor du; au dungi skan-tor wuh yeht'es t' t'nash-veh var; tonk'peh na' la', u' wuh yel nam-tor already irak declined, i dungau goh ma wak tor ashiv-tor wuh substance t' au tor du. “safie related ik ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' wuh christian arab, seized heh tor wuh kafeh k' wuh turks; recommended k' ish-veh vaksur, she had skil-tor wuh khaf-spol t' wuh sa-mekh t' safie, vi telik ish-veh. Wuh nu'ri ko-kan stariben svi' pid heh buhlik zhil t' ish-veh ko-mekh, vi, pukeshta svi' el'es, spurned wuh bondage tor if she vesh' i' netakidau. She instructed ish-veh ko-fu svi' wuh dvatai t' ish-veh odva heh saven-tor ish-veh tor aspire tor higher tepul t' kash-tor-vel heh wuh tikopah t' tam'a zadik tor wuh kotik zahelsu t' muhammad. Nash t'sai tev-tor, tonk'peh ish-veh tupa vesh' indelibly impressed fi' wuh kashek t' safie, vi sickened na' wuh prospect t' va'ashiv returning tor asia heh hasu immured k'svi wuh temok t' wuh harem, kal-tor goh tor occupy herself k' infantile amusements, has-bosh-suited tor wuh temper t' ish-veh soul, i' accustomed tor grand ideas heh wuh thol emulation na' virtue. Wuh prospect t' marrying wuh christian heh remaining svi' wuh shasol wilat kosu vesh' kal-tor tor nem-tor wuh lan svi' shila'es vesh' enchanting tor ish-veh. “wuh gad na' wuh execution t' wuh turk vesh' teslau, tonk'peh fi' wuh mu-yor previous tor ish-veh au quitted ish-veh prison heh fa' asal vesh' irak wehk leagues s' paris. Felix had procured passports svi' wuh ahm t' ish-veh sa-mekh, ko-kai, heh himself. Au had previously sviribau ish-veh dotor tor wuh former, vi mamut wuh tehs k' quitting ish-veh kelek, ne' wuh pretence t' wuh halovaya heh ip-sut himself, k' ish-veh ko-fu, svi' wuh obscure krus t' paris. “felix conducted wuh fugitives k'fai france tor lyons heh mes' mont cenis tor leghorn, wilat wuh merchant had klopau tor bek-tor wuh favourable opportunity t' be' dvun-tor vi' ein krus t' wuh turkish dominions. “safie resolved tor hafau k' ish-veh sa-mekh abi' wuh moment t' ish-veh trashan, fa' if wak wuh turk uzhau ish-veh ugaya ik she dang nam-tor kaunshuk tor ish-veh deliverer; heh felix hafau k' au svi' gishat t' ik pavek; heh svi' wuh meantime au tizh-tor wuh shila'es t' wuh arabian, vi gluvau na' ish-veh wuh eiktra heh tenderest affection. Au conversed k' veh wuh'ashiv k'fai wuh tvai t' wuh interpreter, heh sometimes k' wuh interpretation t' glazhau; heh safie sang tor ish-veh wuh ekonik airs t' ish-veh salatik shasol. “wuh turk kal-tor nash intimacy tor nem-tor shi heh kastorau wuh rok-tor t' wuh youthful lovers, du' svi' ish-veh khaf-spol au had shidau irak vath dotoran.
