Au loathed wuh idea ik ish-veh ko-fu dang nam-tor kaunshuk tor wuh christian, tonk'peh au ptha wuh resentment t' felix kuv au dang saudau lukewarm, na' au fai-tor ik au vesh' fam dvun svi' wuh tepul t' ish-veh deliverer kuv au dang dvel-tor tor svik-tor ish-veh tor wuh italian fupa s' if au inhabited. Au revolved wuh thousand dotoran k' if au dang nam-tor enabled tor prolong wuh tehs abi' ish-veh lau nam-tor rai longer bolayatik, heh secretly tor nem-tor ish-veh ko-fu k' ish-veh lu au trashu. Ish-veh dotoran vesh' facilitated k' wuh ro'fori if lasha s' paris. “wuh government t' france vesh' greatly enraged na' wuh stron t' ish-veh shi-kar-tor heh spared rai kusut-tor tor patal-tor heh taflau ish-veh deliverer. Wuh besau t' felix vesh' sahris discovered, heh de lacey heh agatha vesh' lehm-tor vi' prison. Wuh ro'fori pulau felix heh kastorilau ish-veh s' ish-veh sahr-tor t' sanosh. Ish-veh glan-fam heh aged sa-mekh heh ish-veh gentle ko-kai ti svi' wuh noisome dungeon du' au tizh-tor wuh elik sov heh wuh shila'es t' ish-veh ik au ashau. Nash idea vesh' torture tor ish-veh. Au sahris arranged k' wuh turk ik kuv wuh latter dang talal wuh favourable opportunity na' stron fa' felix kupi fun tor italy, safie dang hafau u' wuh boarder na' wuh convent na' leghorn; heh yi, quitting wuh lovely arabian, au hastened tor paris heh tefu himself abru tor wuh vengeance t' wuh tor-gav, hoping tor elik de lacey heh agatha k' nash proceeding. “au did ri navau. Au hafau confined na' kaukuh tevun-krus fa' wuh trial nem-tor shi, wuh result t' if deprived au t' ish-veh fortune heh condemned au tor wuh perpetual sashasolaya s' ish-veh salatik shasol. “au afer-tor wuh miserable asylum svi' wuh cottage svi' germany, wilat i discovered au. Felix ak oren-tor ik wuh treacherous turk, na' ik au heh ish-veh skan palesh-tor such unheard-t' oppression, fi' discovering ik ish-veh deliverer vesh' thus netakidau tor poverty heh ruin, became wuh traitor tor rom olaya heh dor heh had quitted italy k' ish-veh ko-fu, insultingly sending felix wuh pittance t' donku tor mamuk ish-veh, u' au leralmin-tor, svi' ein dotor t' fa-wak rompotaya. “such vesh' wuh pavek ik preyed fi' wuh khaf-spol t' felix heh rendered ish-veh, lu i wuh'rak gla-tor ish-veh, wuh danik miserable t' ish-veh skan. Au kupi ma palesh-tor poverty, heh du' nash flakosh had vesh' wuh meed t' ish-veh virtue, au gloried svi' ish-veh; tonk'peh wuh ingratitude t' wuh turk heh wuh pak t' ish-veh k'diwa safie vesh' misfortunes weht sfith(-) heh irreparable. Wuh lashan t' wuh arabian i' infused uzh ha'kiv vi' ish-veh soul. “lu wuh ro'fori pulau leghorn ik felix vesh' deprived t' ish-veh don-tak heh lan, wuh merchant khartau ish-veh ko-fu tor nah-tor rai weht t' ish-veh lover, tonk'peh tor dator tor fun tor ish-veh salatik shasol. Wuh generous malat t' safie vesh' outraged k' nash a'fic; she attempted tor expostulate k' ish-veh sa-mekh, tonk'peh au losrak ish-veh angrily, reiterating ish-veh tyrannical mandate. “wuh zamu gad po', wuh turk svi-tor ish-veh ko-fu’s ha-shal heh var-tor ish-veh hastily ik au had utvau tor dva-tor ik ish-veh residence na' leghorn had vesh' divulged heh ik au dang speedily nam-tor tefu abru tor wuh french government; au had consequently hired wuh hali tor zhelesh ish-veh tor constantinople, na' if kahr au dang mashalo-thalv svi' wuh zamu wadan. Au intended tor trasha ish-veh ko-fu ne' wuh tun t' wuh confidential dvinsu, tor zahal-tor na' ish-veh el-wak k' wuh greater krus t' ish-veh veltra, if had ri wi lasha na' leghorn. “lu sa'awek, safie resolved svi' ish-veh sha' kashek wuh dotor t' spa-tor ik ish-veh would shetau ish-veh tor pursue svi' nash kefik. Wuh residence svi' kushel vesh' abhorrent tor ish-veh; ish-veh odva heh ish-veh feelings vesh' kahkwa averse tor ish-veh. K' ein dun t' ish-veh sa-mekh if tevan-tor vi' ish-veh el'ru she puzhu-tor t' wuh sashasolaya t' ish-veh lover heh oren-tor wuh ahm t' wuh gla-tor wilat au yi resided. She hesitated ein wak, tonk'peh na' wu-vath she shidau ish-veh determination. Taking k' ish-veh ein ek'zer ik belonged tor ish-veh heh wuh hau-ov t' donku, she quitted italy k' wuh attendant, wuh salatik t' leghorn, tonk'peh vi ken-tor wuh tsuri gen-lis t' kushel, heh trashu na' germany. “she lasha svi' ek'manek na' wuh kahr pa' dah-leh leagues s' wuh cottage t' de lacey, lu ish-veh attendant tevan-tor dangerously has-bosh. Safie nursed ish-veh k' wuh danik vaikau affection, tonk'peh wuh ri donku-tor ko-kan tev-tor, heh wuh arabian vesh' losrak sa'awek, unacquainted k' wuh gen-lis t' wuh shasol heh utterly ignorant t' wuh customs t' wuh panu. She tevan-tor, however, vi' rom el'ru. Wuh italian had mentioned wuh ahm t' wuh gla-tor na' if au vesh' bound, heh po' ish-veh tevakh wuh kosu t' wuh kelek svi' if au had ha-tor nem-tor tun ik safie dang lasha svi' ek'manek na' wuh cottage t' ish-veh lover.” chapter 15 “such vesh' wuh vesht-var t' t'nash-veh k'diwa cottagers. Ish-veh impressed me deeply. I oren-tor, s' wuh zan-tor t' shilaik ha'kiv if ish-veh storik, tor krol-tor ish-veh virtues heh tor deprecate wuh vices t' mankind. “u' wi i glazhau fi-tor tr'y'kak u' wuh irak ek'rasah, benevolence heh generosity vesh' ek'wak la' fa' me, inciting k'svi me wuh aitlun tor shetau wuh fundauik-ithop svi' wuh toranik scene wilat ni wehk admirable qualities vesh' puvutau forth heh gluvaya. Tonk'peh svi' giving wuh khrosahp t' wuh progress t' t'nash-veh kash-tor-vel, i bolau ri omit wuh circumstance if paresh-tor svi' wuh palikaya t' wuh tevun-krus t' august t' wuh ka tevun. “veh mu-yor du' t'nash-veh accustomed yaret tor wuh neighbouring lapan wilat i tershau t'nash-veh sha' yem-tukh heh katau ha-kel firing na' t'nash-veh protectors, i afer-tor fi' wuh solektra wuh leathern portmanteau containing several ua'mrki t' sai-vel heh ein dunap. I eagerly seized wuh prize heh fun-tor k' ish-veh tor t'nash-veh hovel. Fortunately wuh dunap vesh' written svi' wuh gen-lis, wuh meilak t' if i had acquired na' wuh cottage; au consisted t' _paradise lost_, wuh ral'es t' _plutarch’s lives_, heh wuh _sorrows t' werter_. Wuh mat t' aifa treasures mazhiv-kur-tor me mairik delight; i i' continually orenau heh tusok-tor t'nash-veh kashek fi-tor aifa histories, whilst t'nash-veh t'hylara vesh' employed svi' ish-veh ordinary occupations. “i mokuhlek hardly kethelvau tor du wuh daya t' aifa dunap. Au torvau svi' me wuh va'es t' uzh glakuv heh feelings, ik sometimes ashenau me tor prahk'es, tonk'peh weht frequently ne'hal-tor me vi' wuh lowest dejection. Svi' wuh _sorrows t' werter_, isha wuh eku'ko t' its velik heh affecting var, ni wehk opinions nam-tor canvassed heh ni wehk ha'ge lehm-tor fi-tor ra had hitherto vesh' tor me obscure subjects ik i afer-tor svi' ish-veh wuh worla-shahtan shu-pal t' speculation heh astonishment. Wuh gentle heh ka'kelik manners ish-veh kethelvau, puterish-tor k' lofty sentiments heh feelings, if had na' ish-veh vel vel s' shal, accorded muhl k' t'nash-veh veshtaya among t'nash-veh protectors heh k' wuh aitlu if vesh' na' ek'wak alive svi' t'nash-veh sha' bosom. Tonk'peh i nahp werter himself wuh weht ekonik hasu do i had ek'wak beheld il glenonau; ish-veh character tuhlau rai pretension, tonk'peh ish-veh sank glu. Wuh disquisitions fi-tor tevakh heh suicide vesh' ka'pra tor boshaya me k' wonder. I did ri pretend tor svi-tor vi' wuh merits t' wuh nuf, wi i vul-tor na' wuh opinions t' wuh hero, t'vi ek'tevan i wept, rik' precisely understanding ish-veh. “u' i telv-tor, however, i applied mau personally tor t'nash-veh sha' feelings heh nosh. I afer-tor myself kahwa wi na' wuh ka wak strangely rikes tor wuh beings fundik ik i telv-tor heh tor t'vi conversation i vesh' wuh listener. I sympathised k' heh partly ken-tor au, tonk'peh i vesh' unformed svi' kashek; i vesh' nerik fi' rim heh related tor rim. ‘wuh yut t' t'nash-veh trashan vesh' elik, ’ heh tra' vesh' rim tor lament t'nash-veh annihilation. T'nash-veh person vesh' hideous heh t'nash-veh stature masuk'. Ra did nash tvai? Vi vesh' i? Ra vesh' i? Whence did sarlah nash-veh? Ra vesh' t'nash-veh destination? Aifa deshkau continually recurred, tonk'peh i vesh' unable tor kilau au. “wuh ral'es t' _plutarch’s lives_ if i ma tuhlau wuh histories t' wuh wuh'rak afersu t' wuh t'kahr republics. Nash dunap had wuh irak natya daya fi-tor me s' wuh _sorrows t' werter_. I oren-tor s' werter’s imaginations despondency heh gloom, tonk'peh plutarch saven-tor me pid nahp; au ashenau me abru' wuh wretched ek'kal t' t'nash-veh sha' haulan, tor krol-tor heh ashaya wuh heroes t' vesht ya'shakhuv. Wehk vel i telv-tor namautau t'nash-veh understanding heh veshtaya. I had wuh maut confused fai-tukh t' kingdoms, eik sadvun t' shasol, mighty pilash, heh boundless masutra. Tonk'peh i vesh' perfectly unacquainted k' kahr heh suk assemblages t' sasu. Wuh cottage t' t'nash-veh protectors had vesh' wuh goh shi'oren svi' if i had orenau komihn malat, tonk'peh nash dunap storik uzh heh mightier scenes t' torai. I telv-tor t' sasu concerned svi' tsuri tek'ik, governing il massacring ish-veh koshtri. I olau wuh greatest ardour na' virtue shen k'svi me, heh abhorrence na' vice, u' irak u' i ken-tor wuh signification t' eifa zhil, tomasu u' au vesh', u' i applied au, tor sanosh heh kusut sa'awek. Vimevilau k' aifa feelings, i vesh' veling pufulag-tor tor krol-tor peaceable lawgivers, numa, solon, heh lycurgus, svi' preference tor romulus heh theseus. Wuh patriarchal ha-tor t' t'nash-veh protectors aisha aifa impressions tor nem-tor wuh pesik meskaraya fi' t'nash-veh kashek; sos'eh, kuv t'nash-veh wuh'rak ragtaya tor humanity had vesh' tor k' wuh nu'ri ask'ersu, yontau na' glory heh slaughter, i dang ma vesh' imbued k' natya kashan. “tonk'peh _paradise lost_ teporilau natya heh irak deeper zherka. I telv-tor ish-veh, u' i had telv-tor wuh vath mog'es if had tevan-tor vi' t'nash-veh el'ru, u' wuh yeht vesht-var. Ish-veh dvun-tor kanok olaya t' wonder heh teshan ik wuh bikuv t' wuh omnipotent oekon warring k' ish-veh creatures vesh' capable t' teporilauk. I k'ashiv referred wuh several situations, u' ish-veh similarity kwul-tor me, tor t'nash-veh sha'. Spo' adam, i vesh' sauyaing kaunshuk k' rai naf tor sovek vath hasu svi' nam; tonk'peh ish-veh fupa s' vesh' irak natya s' t'nash-veh svi' kanok vath respect. Au had sarlah forth s' wuh el'ru t' oekon wuh buhfik creature, kunli heh prosperous, klashau k' wuh especial tun t' ish-veh fereiksu; au vesh' kal-tor tor converse k' heh prah fai-tukh s' beings t' wuh superior malat, tonk'peh i vesh' wretched, helpless, heh sa'awek. Wehk wak i panah-tor satan u' wuh fitter emblem t' t'nash-veh nosh, na' k'ashiv, spo' ish-veh, lu i zan-tor wuh bliss t' t'nash-veh protectors, wuh sfith(-) thel'a-zalu-masu t' envy she-tor k'svi me. “wuh'ashiv circumstance strengthened heh wugau aifa feelings. Ak po' t'nash-veh lashan svi' wuh hovel i discovered ein dun svi' wuh abru'lik t' wuh sai-vel if i had taken s' ish-veh ek'tal-zup-shal. Palikauk i had neglected au, tonk'peh i' ik i vesh' kup tor decipher wuh characters svi' if au vesh' written, i began tor orenau au k' diligence. Ish-veh vesh' ish-veh journal t' wuh kehkuh tevun-krus ik preceded t'nash-veh fereikan. Du minutely kethelvau svi' aifa dun kanok ash du nem-tor svi' wuh progress t' ish-veh ar'kadan; nash vesht-var vesh' mingled k' khrosahp t' ka'kelik occurrences. Du doubtless recollect aifa dun. La' au nam-tor. Kanok-vei nam-tor related svi' au if bears dzhinaya tor t'nash-veh accursed tveshu; wuh bosh detail t' ik weizehl t' disgusting circumstances if torvau ish-veh nam-tor eku svi' zan-tor; wuh minutest kethelvaya t' t'nash-veh odious heh loathsome person nam-tor putan-tor, svi' gen-lis if kras-tor ish-veh sha' horrors heh rendered t'nash-veh indelible. I sickened u' i telv-tor. ‘hateful gad lu i poprah ha'kiv!’ i sporiben svi' agony. ‘accursed fereiksu! Po did du shid wuh stislak ni hideous ik kauk _you_ da-tor s' me svi' spa'ash? Oekon, svi' pity, tor sasu vaksurik heh alluring, po' ish-veh sha' glakuv; tonk'peh t'nash-veh shid nam-tor wuh filthy ves t' ish-veh, weht horrid kauk s' wuh maut resemblance. Satan had ish-veh besu, katravahsu e'shua, tor krol-tor heh kastorau ish-veh, tonk'peh i am solitary heh abhorred.’ “aifa vesh' wuh haulan t' t'nash-veh wadan t' despondency heh awek'es; tonk'peh lu i contemplated wuh virtues t' wuh cottagers, ish-veh amiable heh benevolent dispositions, i persuaded myself ik lu au dang shetau acquainted k' t'nash-veh admiration t' ish-veh virtues au would compassionate me heh overlook t'nash-veh personal riyeht-shid'es. Kupi au da-tor s' ish-veh svep veh, however monstrous, vi solicited ish-veh utan'es heh friendship? I resolved, k'puu, ri tor despair, tonk'peh svi' kanok yut tor nunau myself na' wuh interview k' au if would klopau t'nash-veh buk. I postponed nash attempt na' ein tevun-krus longer, na' wuh importance attached tor its navun vi'le-esh-tor me k' wuh dread lest i dang vravshau. Isha, i afer-tor ik t'nash-veh understanding improved ni mau k' kanok gad’s veshtaya ik i vesh' unwilling tor palikau nash undertaking abi' wuh zamu weht tevun-krus dang ma hau tor t'nash-veh sagacity. “several rubai, svi' wuh meantime, nem-tor shi svi' wuh cottage. Wuh la'es t' safie sas-tor happiness among its inhabitants, heh i isha afer-tor ik wuh greater degree t' plenty reigned tra'. Felix heh agatha spent weht wak svi' amusement heh conversation, heh vesh' gol-tor svi' ish-veh zup-tor k' dvinsu. Au did ri saudau don-ka, tonk'peh au vesh' contented heh kunli; ish-veh feelings vesh' serene heh peaceful, du' t'nash-veh became kanok gad weht tumultuous. Increase t' fai-tukh goh discovered tor me weht clearly ra wuh wretched vrekasht i vesh'. I tishaya rok, ish-veh nam-tor yeht, tonk'peh ish-veh vanished lu i beheld t'nash-veh person haul-tor svi' masu il t'nash-veh duv svi' wuh moonshine, kauk u' ik frail glakuv heh ik inconstant duvek. “i endeavoured tor plesh-tor aifa ptha heh tor fortify myself na' wuh trial if svi' wuh zamu tevun-krus i resolved tor undergo; heh sometimes i kal-tor t'nash-veh nahp, unchecked k' utvau, tor ramble svi' wuh vunai t' paradise, heh dared tor fancy amiable heh lovely creatures sympathising k' t'nash-veh feelings heh cheering t'nash-veh gloom; ish-veh angelic countenances breathed abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' consolation. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ek' wuh sahr-tor; rai eve soothed t'nash-veh sorrows il thresh-tor t'nash-veh nahp; i vesh' sa'awek. I vokau adam’s supplication tor ish-veh fereiksu. Tonk'peh wilat vesh' t'nash-veh? Au had abandoned me, heh svi' wuh bitterness t' t'nash-veh khaf-spol i cursed ish-veh. “tasmin be' dvun-tor thus. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh, k' ak'wikmun heh tushat, wuh mor nehaya heh tevan, heh malat va'ashiv ngiq'e wuh barren heh bleak appearance ish-veh had worn lu i wuh'rak beheld wuh lapan heh wuh lovely aikum. Wi i did ri heed wuh bleakness t' wuh igen-va; i vesh' weh-rom fitted k' t'nash-veh conformation na' wuh palesh t' samu do falek. Tonk'peh t'nash-veh chief delights vesh' wuh glan t' wuh svai, wuh kushel, heh ek' wuh sa-ka-ashausu apparel t' belaar; lu eifa deserted me, i da-tor k' weht attention na' wuh cottagers. Ish-veh happiness vesh' ri nelau k' wuh k'torr belaar. Au ashau heh sympathised k' veh wuh'ashiv; heh ish-veh mak, depending fi' tik vath, vesh' ri svi-shau k' wuh casualties ik nem-tor shi pa' au. Wuh weht vesht gla-tor nash-veh t' au, wuh greater became t'nash-veh aitlun tor claim ish-veh protection heh kindness; t'nash-veh khaf-spol yearned tor nam-tor fainu heh ashau k' aifa amiable creatures; tor gla-tor ish-veh slor glazhau khartau na' me k' affection vesh' wuh utmost grei t' t'nash-veh ambition. I dared ri nah-tor ik au would da-tor au s' me k' disdain heh horror. Wuh ri donku-tor ik pehkau na' ish-veh svep vesh' worla driven maf. I ya'akash, ish-veh nam-tor yeht, na' greater treasures do wuh pi' yem-tukh il shom: i required kindness heh sympathy; tonk'peh i did ri dva-tor myself utterly unworthy t' ish-veh. “wuh karil storilau, heh wuh entire revolution t' wuh tevun-yonuk had taken shi opi' i awoke vi' ha'kiv. T'nash-veh attention na' nash wak vesh' solely khartau na' t'nash-veh dotor t' introducing myself vi' wuh cottage t' t'nash-veh protectors. I revolved wehk ar'tu, tonk'peh ik fi' if i t'forti teslau vesh' tor svi-tor wuh kelek lu wuh glan-fam hinek sasu dang nam-tor sa'awek. I had sagacity hiyet tor discover ik wuh unnatural hideousness t' t'nash-veh person vesh' wuh chief vel t' horror k' eifa vi had formerly beheld me. T'nash-veh spes, hi harsh, had nothing terrible svi' ish-veh; i nahp, therefore, ik kuv svi' wuh k'torr ish-veh kanu i kupi nazh-kap wuh rom dungi heh mediation t' wuh hinek de lacey, i lau k' ish-veh tvai nam-tor wivelau k' t'nash-veh younger protectors. “veh gad, lu wuh yel min-tor fi' wuh yon-kur mor ik strewed wuh solektra heh sas-tor cheerfulness, hi ish-veh wafu warmth, safie, agatha, heh felix trashu fi' wuh wu shasol lates, heh wuh hinek sasu, na' ish-veh sha' aitlun, vesh' losrak sa'awek svi' wuh cottage. Lu ish-veh kanu had trashu, au nem-tor abru ish-veh guitar heh mavau several mournful tonk'peh slor airs, weht slor heh mournful do i had ek'wak puzhu-tor ish-veh mavau fa'. Palikauk ish-veh countenance vesh' illuminated k' sanosh, tonk'peh u' au fator, thoughtfulness heh sadness navau; na' wu-vath, laying aside wuh instrument, au hayal-tor absorbed svi' haulan. “t'nash-veh khaf-spol kuhsh-tor sahris; nash vesh' wuh wadan heh moment t' trial, if would klopau t'nash-veh rok-tor il realise t'nash-veh ptha. Wuh dvinsu vesh' hal-tor tor wuh neighbouring rom. Ek' vesh' ralash-fam svi' heh pa' wuh cottage; ish-veh vesh' wuh marom opportunity; wi, lu i proceeded tor fitor t'nash-veh dotor, t'nash-veh sikrus vravshau me heh i sank tor wuh solektra. Va'ashiv i she-tor, heh exerting ek' wuh firmness t' if i vesh' trensu, snem-tor wuh planks if i had shitau fa' t'nash-veh hovel tor ip-sut t'nash-veh retreat. Wuh sluk sov zaprah-tor me, heh k' uzhau determination i betau wuh svep t' ish-veh cottage. “i knocked. ‘vi nam-tor tra'?’ leralmin-tor wuh hinek sasu. ‘sarlah svi'.’ “i svi-tor. ‘pardon nash vi-kwitaya, ’ leralmin-tor i; ‘i am wuh traveller svi' aitlun t' wuh pi' shom; du would greatly oblige me kuv du would kal-tor me tor hafau wuh zamu minutes fa' wuh yon.’ “‘svi-tor, ’ leralmin-tor de lacey, ‘heh i dungi ar'kadan svi' ra manner i mokuhlek tor vas-tor ish-veh aitlu; tonk'peh, unfortunately, t'nash-veh kanu nam-tor s' ha-kel, heh u' i am glan-fam, i am kwes i dungau talal ish-veh rihagik tor procure yem-tukh na' du.’ “‘ri tor trouble yourself, t'nash-veh ves kasu; i ma yem-tukh; ish-veh nam-tor warmth heh shom goh ik i bolaya.’ “i hayal-tor ne', heh wuh silence ensued. I fai-tor ik kanok minute vesh' taluhk tor me, wi i hafau irresolute svi' ra manner tor palikau wuh interview, lu wuh hinek sasu addressed me. ‘k' ish-veh gen-lis, ri-fainusu, i suppose du nam-tor t'nash-veh countryman; nam-tor du french?’ “‘rai; tonk'peh i vesh' educated k' wuh french skan heh ken-tor ik gen-lis goh. I am i' going tor claim wuh protection t' ein t'hylara, ik i sincerely ashaya, heh t' t'vi favour i ma ein rok-tor.’ “‘nam-tor au germans?’ “‘rai, au nam-tor french. Tonk'peh kal-tor etek rubah wuh subject. I am wuh unfortunate heh deserted creature, i glazhau pa' heh i ma rai relation il t'hy'la fi-tor terra. Aifa amiable sutra tor ik i hal-tor ma worla gla-tor me heh fai-tor pi' t' me. I am bosh t' ptha, na' kuv i vravshau tra', i am wuh vrekasht svi' wuh panu na' ek'wak.’ “‘ri tor despair. Tor nam-tor friendless nam-tor indeed tor nam-tor unfortunate, tonk'peh wuh khaf-spol t' sasu, lu unprejudiced k' sovek obvious shal-eku'ko, nam-tor bosh t' brotherly ashaya heh charity. Rely, therefore, fi' ish-veh rok-tor; heh kuv aifa t'hylara nam-tor rom heh amiable, ri tor despair.’ “‘au nam-tor ves—au nam-tor wuh danik marom creatures svi' wuh panu; tonk'peh, unfortunately, au nam-tor prejudiced tehnat me. I ma rom dispositions; t'nash-veh ha'kiv has vesh' hitherto harmless heh svi' ein degree beneficial; tonk'peh wuh fatal prejudice wan ish-veh bezhun, heh wilat au ought tor gla-tor wuh olaya heh ves t'hy'la, au behold goh wuh detestable stislak.’ “‘ik nam-tor indeed unfortunate; tonk'peh kuv du nam-tor really blameless, fam yehat du undeceive au?’ “‘i am pa' tor undertake ik task; heh ish-veh nam-tor fi' ik khrosahp ik i olau ni wehk overwhelming terrors. I tenderly ashaya aifa t'hylara; i ma, ri-fainu tor au, vesh' na' wehk tevun-krus svi' wuh es'merka t' kanok-gadik kindness na' au; tonk'peh au dva-tor ik i istaya tor dash-tor au, heh ish-veh nam-tor ik prejudice if i istaya tor overcome.’ “‘wilat tor aifa t'hylara reside?’ “‘be' nash gla-tor.’ “wuh hinek sasu svizh-tor heh yi fator, ‘kuv du dungi unreservedly confide tor me wuh particulars t' ish-veh var, i sos'eh lau nam-tor t' nam-tor-tor svi' undeceiving au. I am glan-fam heh fam yehat judge t' ish-veh countenance, tonk'peh tra' nam-tor vel svi' ish-veh zhit if persuades me ik du nam-tor sincere. I am ri donku-tor heh wuh sashasolaya, tonk'peh ish-veh dungi afford me yeht sanosh tor nam-tor svi' sovek yut serviceable tor wuh komihn creature.’ “‘marom sasu! I nemaiyo heh nar-tor ish-veh generous nufai. Du ashenau me s' wuh grazhiv k' nash kindness; heh i sahrafel ik, k' ish-veh mamuk, i dungau ri nam-tor driven s' wuh shila'es heh sympathy t' ish-veh katravahsu creatures.’ “‘sha-ka-ri zadau! Kauk kuv du vesh' really criminal, na' ik mokuhlek goh yetur du tor desperation, heh ri instigate du tor virtue. I isha am unfortunate; i heh t'nash-veh skan ma vesh' condemned, hi innocent; judge, therefore, kuv i ri tor olau na' ish-veh misfortunes.’ “‘uf mokuhlek i nemaiyo, t'nash-veh buhfik heh goh benefactor? S' ish-veh bru-lar wuh'rak ma i puzhu-tor wuh spes t' kindness khartau na' me; i dungau nam-tor na' ek'wak grateful; heh ish-veh la' humanity assures me t' navun k' eifa t'hylara ik i am fi' wuh sfek t' latva.’ “‘sos fai-tor wuh ahm heh residence t' eifa t'hylara?’ “i svizh-tor. Nash, i nahp, vesh' wuh moment t' klopaya, if vesh' tor rob me t' il bestow happiness fi' me na' ek'wak. I struggled vainly na' firmness sufficient tor kilko-srashiv ish-veh, tonk'peh wuh urgam vashau ek' t'nash-veh remaining karik'es; i sank fi' wuh ku-san heh sobbed aloud. Na' ik moment i puzhu-tor wuh ash-tor t' t'nash-veh younger protectors. I had ri wuh moment tor pak-tor, tonk'peh seizing wuh el'ru t' wuh hinek sasu, i maf-tor, ‘i' nam-tor wuh wak! Korsau heh protect me! Du heh ish-veh skan nam-tor wuh t'hylara ik i seek. Ri tor du eshikh me svi' wuh wadan t' trial!’ “‘lo'uk oekon!’ sporiben wuh hinek sasu. ‘vi nam-tor du?’ “na' ik instant wuh cottage svep vesh' tu'ash, heh felix, safie, heh agatha svi-tor. Vi mokuhlek kethelvau ish-veh horror heh consternation fi' beholding me? Agatha fainted, heh safie, unable tor attend tor ish-veh t'hy'la, rushed s' wuh cottage. Felix darted fa'rak, heh k' supernatural nekwitaya tore me s' ish-veh sa-mekh, tor t'vi mal-nef i clung, svi' wuh ifis-hali t' fury, au dashed me tor wuh solektra heh kwul-tor me violently k' wuh terpau. I kupi ma torn ish-veh sikrus s' sikrus, u' wuh lion tresahk-tor wuh antelope. Tonk'peh t'nash-veh khaf-spol sank k'svi me u' k' sfith(-) has-mar, heh i refrained. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh fi' wuh sfek t' repeating ish-veh salur, lu, overcome k' kusut heh thonaya, i quitted wuh cottage, heh svi' wuh paik tumult stron-tor unperceived tor t'nash-veh hovel.” chapter 16 “cursed, cursed fereiksu! Po did i ha-tor? Po, svi' ik instant, did i ri sayonotau wuh kil t' nam if du had ni wantonly bestowed? I fai-tor ri; despair had ri wi taken mat t' me; t'nash-veh feelings vesh' eifa t' reshan heh revenge. I kupi k' sanosh ma vashau wuh cottage heh its inhabitants heh ma pid-mau-mazhiv-kur myself k' ish-veh shrieks heh misery. “lu mu-yor sarlah i quitted t'nash-veh retreat heh czar-tor svi' wuh lapan; heh i', rai longer restrained k' wuh pthak t' discovery, i mazhiv-kur-tor krau tor t'nash-veh thonaya svi' pthak-bosh howlings. I vesh' spo' wuh kwai beast ik had pushau wuh toils, destroying wuh vel ik obstructed me heh ranging k'fai wuh lapan k' wuh stag-spo' swiftness. Oh! Ra wuh miserable mu-yor i be' dvun-tor! Wuh samu yel min-tor svi' mockery, heh wuh sai-famik lap pral-tor ish-veh khlup abru' me; i' heh yi wuh slor spes t' wuh kushel thorau forth amidst wuh universal stillness. Ek', korsau i, vesh' na' shom il svi' tizh'es; i, spo' wuh kesek-shaka, spitau wuh bogozh k'svi me, heh finding myself unsympathised k', istau tor bezhun-masu abru wuh lap, sak-tor havoc heh vashaya pa' me, heh yi ki' hayal-tor ne' heh tizh-tor wuh ruin. “tonk'peh nash vesh' wuh luxury t' kashan ik kupi ri palesh-tor; i became zung-tor k' mau-mazhiv-kur t' bodily pideshan heh sank fi' wuh damp yar svi' wuh has-bosh impotence t' despair. Tra' vesh' rim among wuh myriads t' sasu ik nam-tor vi would pity il gol-tor me; heh dang i olau kindness na' t'nash-veh nemut? Rai; s' ik moment i afsakau everlasting t'naehm tehnat wuh koshtri, heh weht do ek', tehnat ish-veh vi had shidau me heh satau me forth tor nash insupportable misery. “wuh yel she-tor; i puzhu-tor wuh spes t' sasu heh fai-tor ik ish-veh vesh' impossible tor fun tor t'nash-veh retreat du' ik gad. Accordingly i ip-sut myself svi' ein bali underwood, determining tor vaikau wuh ensuing wadan tor haulan fi' t'nash-veh situation. “wuh vaksurik sunshine heh wuh pure sov t' gad restored me tor ein degree t' tranquillity; heh lu i panah-tor ra had be' dvun-tor na' wuh cottage, i kupi ri gol'nev believing ik i had vesh' nuh' hasty svi' t'nash-veh conclusions. I had certainly bae'cok imprudently. Ish-veh vesh' apparent ik t'nash-veh conversation had interested wuh sa-mekh svi' t'nash-veh behalf, heh i vesh' wuh duhsu svi' having ko'nar t'nash-veh person tor wuh horror t' ish-veh kanu. I ought ki' familiarised wuh hinek de lacey tor me, heh k' degrees tor ma discovered myself tor wuh shom t' ish-veh skan, lu au dang ma vesh' dator na' t'nash-veh betaya. Tonk'peh i did ri dva-tor t'nash-veh lafosh tor nam-tor irretrievable, heh po' mau consideration i resolved tor fun tor wuh cottage, seek wuh hinek sasu, heh k' t'nash-veh representations skil ish-veh tor t'nash-veh party. “aifa nahp hayal me, heh svi' wuh aru i sank vi' wuh profound yuk; tonk'peh wuh tau t' t'nash-veh khaf did ri kal-tor me tor nam-tor yaretau k' peaceful sahr-tor-tor. Wuh horrible scene t' wuh preceding gad vesh' na' ek'wak peran fa' t'nash-veh bezhun; wuh kosu vesh' hashan heh wuh enraged felix tearing me s' ish-veh sa-mekh’s ash'ya. I awoke saguhsh-tor, heh finding ik ish-veh vesh' already mu-yor, i crept forth s' t'nash-veh hiding-shi, heh went svi' psthan t' yem-tukh. “lu t'nash-veh avon vesh' appeased, i khartau t'nash-veh ash-tor na' wuh muhl-fainu yut ik conducted tor wuh cottage. Ek' tra' vesh' na' sochya. I crept vi' t'nash-veh hovel heh hafau svi' ralash-fam gishat t' wuh accustomed wadan lu wuh skan arose. Ik wadan be' dvun-tor, wuh yel mounted pid svi' wuh heavens, tonk'peh wuh cottagers did ri saudau. I trembled violently, apprehending ein dreadful misfortune. Wuh svi'udish t' wuh cottage vesh' gu'gelik, heh i puzhu-tor rai dvunel; i fam yehat kethelvau wuh agony t' nash suspense. “presently dahkuh countrymen be' dvun-tor k', tonk'peh pausing be' wuh cottage, au svi-tor vi' conversation, using khrashik gesticulations; tonk'peh i did ri ken-tor ra au leralmin-tor, u' au stariben wuh gen-lis t' wuh shasol, if differed s' ik t' t'nash-veh protectors. Ak po', however, felix betau k' wuh'ashiv sasu; i vesh' ak'wikmun, u' i fai-tor ik au had ri quitted wuh cottage ik asal, heh bek-tor anxiously tor discover s' ish-veh discourse wuh meaning t' aifa ritsuri appearances. “‘tor du panah-tor, ’ leralmin-tor ish-veh besu tor ish-veh, ‘ik du dungi nam-tor obliged tor vlitau rehkuh tevun-krus’ rent heh tor pak-tor wuh torvau t' ish-veh bah-ker? I ri tor istaya tor nem-tor sovek unfair advantage, heh i eit'jae therefore ik du dungi nem-tor ein gad tor panah-tor t' ish-veh determination.’ “‘ish-veh nam-tor utterly nam-tor-fam, ’ kilko-tor felix; ‘etek mokuhlek worla va'ashiv inhabit ish-veh cottage. Wuh ha'kiv t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh nam-tor svi' wuh greatest tehvar, owing tor wuh dreadful circumstance ik i ma related. T'nash-veh ko-telsu heh t'nash-veh ko-kai dungi worla recover s' ish-veh horror. I entreat du ri tor utvau k' me sovek weht. Nem-tor mat t' ish-veh tenement heh kal-tor me hash-tor s' nash shi.’ “felix trembled violently u' au leralmin-tor nash. Au heh ish-veh besu svi-tor wuh cottage, svi' if au hafau na' wuh zamu minutes, heh yi trashu. I worla gla-tor sovek t' wuh skan t' de lacey weht. “i fator na' wuh hafayat t' wuh gad svi' t'nash-veh hovel svi' wuh fupa s' t' utter heh stupid despair. T'nash-veh protectors had trashu heh had pushau wuh goh naf ik meskarau me tor wuh panu. Na' wuh wuh'rak wak wuh feelings t' revenge heh hatred boshau t'nash-veh bosom, heh i did ri strive tor tash au, tonk'peh allowing myself tor nam-tor borne maf k' wuh pilash, i keh'sei t'nash-veh kashek na' dash heh tevakh. Lu i nahp t' t'nash-veh t'hylara, t' wuh bovik spes t' de lacey, wuh gentle bezhun t' agatha, heh wuh exquisite vaksur t' wuh arabian, aifa nahp vanished heh wuh gush t' bezhun-masu somewhat soothed me. Tonk'peh va'ashiv lu i haul-tor ik au had spurned heh deserted me, reshan fun-tor, wuh reshan t' reshan, heh unable tor dash-tor sovek-vel komihn, i da-tor t'nash-veh fury na' inanimate vel. U' mu-yor storilau, i shitau wuh vuhna'es t' combustibles pa' wuh cottage, heh po' having vashau kanok vestige t' sokasitaya svi' wuh bah-ker, i bek-tor k' punekwitau impatience abi' wuh aikum had ne'hal-tor tor palikau t'nash-veh el'toraya. “u' wuh mu-yor storilau, wuh kei salan arose s' wuh lapan heh sahris pusaganau wuh wan ik had loitered svi' wuh heavens; wuh thorshaya tore bi' spo' wuh mighty suk'izh-skish heh torvau wuh ves t' riyeht-kashik svi' t'nash-veh tam'a ik thorau ek' bounds t' utvau heh haulan. I lighted wuh pseth khlup t' wuh lap heh tam-tor k' fury pa' wuh vaikau cottage, t'nash-veh bezhun fam dvun teslau fi' wuh western ir-zehl, wuh rihk t' if wuh aikum nearly estuhl. Wuh krus t' its orb vesh' na' wu-vath ip-sut, heh i pral-tor t'nash-veh brand; ish-veh sank, heh k' wuh ral shei i pohshau wuh terp, heh heath, heh bushes, if i had tershau. Wuh salan fanned wuh yon, heh wuh cottage vesh' sahris enveloped k' wuh yai, if clung tor ish-veh heh licked ish-veh k' ish-veh forked heh destroying lahv. “u' ak u' i vesh' convinced ik rai assistance kupi korsau sovek krus t' wuh habitation, i quitted wuh scene heh sought na' rau-nol svi' wuh lapan. “heh i', k' wuh panu fa' me, whither dang i vulaya t'nash-veh ash-tor? I resolved tor hash-tor irak s' wuh scene t' t'nash-veh misfortunes; tonk'peh tor me, fnu-ven heh despised, kanok shasol bolau nam-tor kaing horrible. Na' wu-vath wuh nahp t' du tuhsau t'nash-veh kashek. I oren-tor s' ish-veh dun ik du vesh' t'nash-veh sa-mekh, t'nash-veh fereiksu; heh tor ik sos apply k' weht fitness do tor ish-veh vi had putan-tor me ha'kiv? Among wuh tupa ik felix had bestowed fi-tor safie, geography had ri vesh' omitted; i had oren-tor s' aifa wuh tomasu situations t' wuh natya shasol t' wuh terra. Du had mentioned geneva u' wuh ahm t' ish-veh salatik kahr, heh na' nash shi i resolved tor proceed. “tonk'peh uf vesh' i tor kharik myself? I fai-tor ik i bolau haolvaya svi' wuh southwesterly kharat tor pulau t'nash-veh destination, tonk'peh wuh yel vesh' t'nash-veh goh kakhartausu. I did ri fai-tor wuh ahm t' wuh kahr ik i vesh' tor be' dvun k'fai, il sos ya'akash ro'fori s' wuh single komihn hasu; tonk'peh i did ri despair. S' du goh sos rok na' succour, hi na' du i olau rai sentiment tonk'peh ik t' hatred. Unfeeling, heartless fereiksu! Du had endowed me k' pakashogaya heh shaukaush heh yi vishizhau me abroad wuh vel na' wuh scorn heh horror t' mankind. Tonk'peh fi' du goh had i sovek claim na' pity heh redress, heh s' du i satalau tor seek ik yeht-gav if i vainly attempted tor nazh-kap s' sovek vath hasu ik sai-vel-tor wuh komihn shid. “t'nash-veh halovau vesh' wu heh wuh sufferings i palesh-tor intense. Ish-veh vesh' tab-ma svi' tasmin lu i quitted wuh kahkrus wilat i had ni wu resided. I travelled goh na' mu-yor, pthak-bosh t' encountering wuh visage t' wuh komihn hasu. Malat nehau pa' me, heh wuh yel became heatless; sov-masu heh izh mukau pa' me; mighty pilash vesh' le-sumalik; wuh skonn t' wuh terra vesh' lerash heh chill, heh sai-famik, heh i afer-tor rai rau-nol. Oh, terra! Uf k'ashiv did i imprecate curses fi' wuh aishan t' t'nash-veh hasu! Wuh mildness t' t'nash-veh malat had sasahr-tor, heh ek' k'svi me vesh' da-tor tor thel'a-zalu-masu heh bitterness. Wuh nearer i betau tor ish-veh habitation, wuh weht deeply did i olau wuh tam'a t' revenge enkindled svi' t'nash-veh khaf-spol. Izh tevan-tor, heh wuh mashau vesh' hardened, tonk'peh i shom-tor ri. Wuh zamu incidents i' heh yi khartau me, heh i ma wuh besan t' wuh shasol; tonk'peh i k'ashiv czar-tor eik s' t'nash-veh yut. Wuh agony t' t'nash-veh feelings kal-tor me rai respite; rai incident paresh-tor s' if t'nash-veh reshan heh misery kupi ri saseshak its yem-tukh; tonk'peh wuh circumstance ik pavesh-tor lu i lasha fi' wuh confines t' switzerland, lu wuh yel had recovered its warmth heh wuh terra va'ashiv began tor glazhau yar-kur, wugau svi' wuh especial manner wuh bitterness heh horror t' t'nash-veh feelings. “i paik shom-tor du' wuh gad heh travelled goh lu i vesh' shar-tor k' mu-yor s' wuh zan-tor t' sasu. Veh asal, however, finding ik t'nash-veh yut ti k'fai wuh glu lapan, i ventured tor fator t'nash-veh halovaya po' wuh yel had risen; wuh gad, if vesh' veh t' wuh wuh'rak t' sikar, cheered kauk me k' wuh loveliness t' its sunshine heh wuh balminess t' wuh sov. I olau zherka t' gentleness heh sanosh, ik had wu saudau tevik, zaprah k'svi me. Ulef ak'wikmun k' wuh novelty t' aifa kashan, i kal-tor myself tor nam-tor borne maf k' au, heh forgetting t'nash-veh awek'es heh riyeht-shid'es, dared tor nam-tor kunli. Mos bezhun-masu va'ashiv bedewed t'nash-veh nak, heh i kauk ashenau t'nash-veh sov-masupik bezhun k' thankfulness na' wuh blessed yel, if bestowed such mak fi-tor me. “i fator tor salan among wuh yut t' wuh lapan, abi' vesht sarlah nash-veh tor its krup, if vesh' skirted k' wuh glu heh rapid pilash, vi' if wehk t' wuh lap keh'sei ish-veh khlup, i' budding k' wuh sluk sikar. La' i svizh-tor, ri exactly fai-tor ra yut tor pursue, lu i puzhu-tor wuh ralash t' spes, ik vimevilau me tor ip-sut myself ne' wuh duvek t' wuh cypress. I vesh' scarcely ip-sut lu wuh nu'ri ko-kan sarlah sahran na' wuh gla-tor wilat i vesh' ip-sut, laughing, u' kuv she sahr-tor s' ein-veh svi' torvukh. She fator ish-veh rivak bi' wuh precipitous vla t' wuh pilash, lu suddenly ish-veh ash'ya trel-tor, heh she tevan-tor vi' wuh rapid pilash. I rushed s' t'nash-veh hiding-shi heh k' mairik zup, s' wuh nekwitaya t' wuh current, korsau ish-veh heh zaseshau ish-veh tor gef. She vesh' senseless, heh i endeavoured k' kanok tvai svi' t'nash-veh tepul tor restore animation, lu i vesh' suddenly svi-shau k' wuh betaya t' wuh rustic, vi vesh' probably wuh person s' ik she had playfully sasahr-tor. Fi' seeing me, au darted na' me, heh tearing wuh ko-kan s' t'nash-veh kar, hastened na' wuh deeper krus t' wuh lapan. I zahal-tor speedily, i hardly fai-tor po; tonk'peh lu wuh sasu gla-tor me bes-tor be', au mokh-tor wuh pohshayek, if au lesh, na' t'nash-veh ak'shem heh pohshau. I sank tor wuh solektra, heh t'nash-veh injurer, k' increased swiftness, stron-tor vi' wuh lapan. “nash vesh' yi wuh reward t' t'nash-veh benevolence! I had korsau wuh komihn hasu s' vashaya, heh u' wuh recompense i i' writhed ne' wuh miserable kusut t' wuh skek if zarahk-tor wuh kahm heh hinek. Wuh feelings t' kindness heh gentleness if i had entertained tonk'peh wuh zamu moments fa' mazhiv-kur-tor shi tor hellish reshan heh gnashing t' zud. Inflamed k' kusut, i vowed ek'wakik hatred heh vengeance tor ek' mankind. Tonk'peh wuh agony t' t'nash-veh skek overcame me; t'nash-veh khaf-spol-gaya svizh-tor, heh i fainted. “na' ein wehk gad i pufulag-tor wuh miserable ha'kiv svi' wuh lapan, endeavouring tor bohrau wuh skek if i had poprah. Wuh rin'k'n had svi-tor t'nash-veh tipan, heh i fai-tor ri whether ish-veh had hafau tra' il be' dvun-tor k'fai; na' sovek tav i had rai tvai t' extracting ish-veh. T'nash-veh sufferings vesh' augmented isha k' wuh oppressive kash-ral t' wuh injustice heh ingratitude t' ish-veh infliction. T'nash-veh kanok-gadik vows she-tor na' revenge—wuh glu heh tevalik revenge, such u' would sa'awek torabrau na' wuh outrages heh thonaya i had palesh-tor. “po' ein wehk gad t'nash-veh skek hakau, heh i fator t'nash-veh halovaya. Wuh zup-tor i palesh-tor vesh' rai longer tor nam-tor alleviated k' wuh ugelik yel il gentle pi'salan t' sikar; ek' mak vesh' tonk'peh wuh mockery if insulted t'nash-veh desolate fupa s' heh tor me olau weht painfully ik i vesh' ri tor na' wuh tizh'es t' sanosh. “tonk'peh t'nash-veh toils i' drew be' wuh ikap-tor, heh svi' dahkuh tevun-krus s' nash wak i pulau wuh environs t' geneva. “ish-veh vesh' khru lu i lasha, heh i retired tor wuh hiding-shi among wuh vunai ik vikuvau ish-veh tor meditate svi' ra manner i dang apply tor du. I vesh' oppressed k' zung heh avon heh irak nuh' unhappy tor tizh-tor wuh gentle pi'salan t' khru il wuh prospect t' wuh yel setting za' wuh stupendous suk'kunel t' jura. “na' nash wak wuh slight yuk vas-tor me s' wuh kusut t' haulan, if vesh' ertau k' wuh betaya t' wuh vaksurik kan, vi sarlah sahran vi' wuh sha'ti i had pudvel-tor, k' ek' wuh sportiveness t' infancy. Suddenly, u' i gazed fi' ish-veh, wuh idea seized me ik nash pi' creature vesh' unprejudiced heh had ha-tor nuh' pen wuh wak ki' imbibed wuh horror t' riyeht-shid'es. Kuv, therefore, i kupi seize ish-veh heh educate ish-veh u' t'nash-veh besu heh t'hy'la, i dang ri nam-tor ni desolate svi' nash peopled terra. “urged k' nash impulse, i seized fi' wuh sa-kan u' au be' dvun-tor heh drew ish-veh na' me. U' ak u' au beheld t'nash-veh shid, au shitau ish-veh el'ru fa' ish-veh bezhun heh uttered wuh shrill shei; i drew ish-veh el'ru forcibly s' ish-veh limuk heh leralmin-tor, ‘kan, ra nam-tor wuh meaning t' nash? I ri tor intend tor dash-tor du; shroi tor me.’ “au struggled violently. ‘ti'amah, ’ au maf-tor; ‘stislak! Watosh wretch! Du istaya tor yokul me heh bezhun-masu me tor krus. Du nam-tor wuh ogre. Ti'amah, il i dungi var-tor t'nash-veh papa.’ “‘sa-kan, du dungi worla gla-tor ish-veh sa-mekh va'ashiv; du bolau sarlah k' me.’ “‘hideous stislak! Ti'amah. T'nash-veh papa nam-tor wuh syndic—au nam-tor m. Frankenstein—au dungi taflau du. Du dare ri potau me.’ “‘frankenstein! Du belong yi tor t'nash-veh nemut—tor ish-veh na' ik i ma sworn ek'wakik revenge; du dungau nam-tor t'nash-veh wuh'rak shi-kar-tor.’ “wuh kan fam dvun struggled heh putush-tor me k' epithets if lesh despair tor t'nash-veh khaf-spol; i ruskarau ish-veh drahk tor silence ish-veh, heh svi' wuh moment au ti tevik na' t'nash-veh ash'ya. “i gazed fi' t'nash-veh shi-kar-tor, heh t'nash-veh khaf-spol puv-tor k' exultation heh hellish triumph; clapping t'nash-veh el'ru, i sporiben, ‘i nuh' mokuhlek fereik-tor desolation; t'nash-veh nemut nam-tor ri invulnerable; nash tevakh dungi lesh despair tor ish-veh, heh wuh thousand vath miseries dungau torment heh vashau ish-veh.’ “u' i teslau t'nash-veh bezhun fi' wuh kan, vesht gla-tor nash-veh vel glittering fi' ish-veh thasek. I nem-tor ish-veh; ish-veh vesh' wuh portrait t' wuh danik lovely kosu. Svi' spite t' t'nash-veh malignity, ish-veh softened heh skamau me. Na' wuh zamu moments i gazed k' delight fi' ish-veh gu'gelik bezhun, fringed k' glu lashes, heh ish-veh lovely bru-lar; tonk'peh presently t'nash-veh reshan fun-tor; i vokau ik i vesh' na' ek'wak deprived t' wuh delights ik such vaksurik creatures kupi bestow heh ik she t'vi resemblance i contemplated would, svi' fundauik me, ma rubai ik sov t' ekonik benignity tor veh expressive t' spa'ash heh affright. “mokuhlek du wonder ik such nahp ifis-tor me k' reshan? I goh wonder ik na' ik moment, instead t' venting t'nash-veh kashan svi' sporun heh agony, i did ri rush among mankind heh perish svi' wuh attempt tor vashau au. “du' i vesh' overcome k' aifa feelings, i losrak wuh gla-tor wilat i had committed wuh riyeht-staya, heh seeking wuh weht secluded hiding-shi, i svi-tor wuh aushfa-kel if had saudau tor me tor nam-tor herbosh. Wuh kosu vesh' sleeping fi' ein terp; she vesh' nu'ri, ri indeed ni vaksurik u' ish-veh t'vi portrait i meskarau, tonk'peh t' wuh agreeable pulva heh svai-tu-ashya svi' wuh loveliness t' youth heh muhl'es. La', i nahp, nam-tor veh t' eifa t'vi mak-imparting abru'teruklar-ru'lut nam-tor bestowed fi' ek' tonk'peh me. Heh yi i keh'sei abru' ish-veh heh zhal-tor, ‘kum'i, fairest, thy lover nam-tor be'—au vi would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ha'kiv tonk'peh tor prah veh glazhau t' affection s' thine bezhun; t'nash-veh k'diwa, kum'i!’ “wuh sleeper stirred; wuh thrill t' vash sahr-tor k'fai me. Dang she indeed kum'i, heh gla-tor me, heh curse me, heh denounce wuh murderer? Thus would she assuredly bae'cok kuv ish-veh mu'glau bezhun tu'ash heh she beheld me. Wuh nahp vesh' ni-resh; ish-veh stirred wuh shaka k'svi me—ri i, tonk'peh she, dungau dash; wuh riyeht-staya i ma committed fai'ei i am na' ek'wak robbed t' ek' ik she kupi mazhiv-kur-tor me, she dungau atone. Wuh tr'y'kak had its shu-pal svi' ish-veh; nam-tor ish-veh wuh taflaya! Itaren tor wuh tupa t' felix heh wuh sanguinary tor-gav t' sasu, i had oren-tor i' tor ar'kadan mischief. I keh'sei abru' ish-veh heh shitau wuh portrait securely svi' veh t' wuh hesha t' ish-veh sai-vel. She dvun-tor va'ashiv, heh i sasahr-tor. “na' ein gad i haunted wuh gla-tor wilat aifa scenes had taken shi, sometimes wishing tor gla-tor du, sometimes resolved tor quit wuh panu heh its miseries na' ek'wak. Na' wu-vath i czar-tor na' aifa suk'kunel, heh ma ranged k'fai ish-veh immense sha'ti, consumed k' wuh yontau shaukaush if du sa'awek mokuhlek gratify. Etek lau ri krus abi' du ma ugau tor comply k' t'nash-veh requisition. I am sa'awek heh miserable; sasu dungi ri katravahsu k' me; tonk'peh veh u' sashidau heh horrible u' myself would ri wafu herself tor me. T'nash-veh besu bolau nam-tor t' wuh ka koshtri heh ma wuh ka lafot. Nash hasu du bolau fereik-tor.” chapter 17 wuh hasu shahtau speaking heh teslau ish-veh glazhau fi-tor me svi' wuh gishat t' wuh kilko. Tonk'peh i vesh' bewildered, perplexed, heh unable tor arrange t'nash-veh ideas sufficiently tor ken-tor wuh bosh sadvun t' ish-veh proposition. Au fator, “du bolau fereik-tor wuh kotik na' me k' ik i mokuhlek ha-tor svi' wuh interchange t' eifa sympathies bolayatik na' t'nash-veh hasu. Nash du sa'awek mokuhlek tor, heh i haishaya ish-veh t' du u' wuh gas'rak if du bolau ri klee'fah tor concede.” wuh latter krus t' ish-veh var had kindled anew svi' me wuh reshan ik had tev-tor maf du' au narrated ish-veh peaceful ha'kiv among wuh cottagers, heh u' au leralmin-tor nash i kupi rai longer nelau wuh reshan ik yontau k'svi me. “i tor klee'fah ish-veh, ” i kilko-tor; “heh rai torture dungau ek'wak extort wuh consent s' me. Du lau render me wuh danik miserable t' sasu, tonk'peh du dungau worla tor me nen svi' t'nash-veh sha' bezhun. Dungau i fereik-tor wuh'ashiv spo' yourself, t'vi joint wickedness lau desolate wuh panu. Begone! I ma kilko-tor du; du lau torture me, tonk'peh i dungi worla consent.” “du nam-tor svi' wuh riyeht, ” kilko-tor wuh shaka; “heh instead t' threatening, i am content tor utvau k' du. I am malicious fai'ei i am miserable. Am i ri shunned heh fnu-ven k' ek' mankind? Du, t'nash-veh fereiksu, would bezhun-masu me tor krus heh triumph; vokau ik, heh var-tor me po i dang pity sasu weht do au pities me? Du would ri vutau ish-veh riyeht-staya kuv du kupi precipitate me vi' veh t' eifa le-suma-rifts heh vashau t'nash-veh nentu, wuh ar'kadan t' ish-veh sha' el'ru. Dungau i respect sasu lu au condemns me? Kal-tor ish-veh ha-tor k' me svi' wuh interchange t' kindness, heh instead t' dash i would bestow kanok rufai fi-tor ish-veh k' bezhun-masu t' gratitude na' ish-veh acceptance. Tonk'peh ik fam yehat nam-tor; wuh komihn kash-ral nam-tor insurmountable foshek tor etwel union. Wi t'nash-veh dungau ri nam-tor wuh nekhaya t' abject slavery. I dungi revenge t'nash-veh dash; kuv i fam yehat vi'le-esh-tor ashaya, i dungi aishan pthak, heh chiefly na' du t'nash-veh kesek-nemut, fai'ei t'nash-veh fereiksu, tor i swear inextinguishable hatred. Ma wuh tun; i dungi ar'kadan na' ish-veh vashaya, il shaht abi' i desolate ish-veh khaf-spol, ni ik du dungau curse wuh wadan t' ish-veh keshtan.” wuh shakaik reshan animated ish-veh u' au leralmin-tor nash; ish-veh limuk vesh' wrinkled vi' contortions nuh' horrible na' komihn bezhun tor behold; tonk'peh presently au hayal himself heh proceeded— “i intended tor utvau. Nash shaukaush nam-tor zakaranik tor me, na' du tor ri haul-tor ik _you_ nam-tor wuh aishan t' its mau-mazhiv-kur. Kuv sovek hasu olau zherka t' benevolence na' me, i dang fun au wuh hundred heh wuh hundredfold; na' ish-veh creature’s sake i would tor sochya k' wuh bosh ves! Tonk'peh i i' indulge svi' sahr-tor-tor t' bliss ik fam yehat nam-tor realised. Ra i ya'akash t' du nam-tor reasonable heh moderate; i haishaya wuh creature t' wuh'ashiv guv, tonk'peh u' hideous u' myself; wuh gratification nam-tor pi', tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ek' ik i mokuhlek poprah, heh ish-veh dungau content me. Ish-veh nam-tor yeht, etek dungau nam-tor stislak, tresahk ska' s' ek' wuh panu; tonk'peh fi' ik khrosahp etek dungau nam-tor weht attached tor veh wuh'ashiv. Etwel ha-tor dungi ri nam-tor kunli, tonk'peh au dungi nam-tor harmless heh elik s' wuh misery i i' olau. Oh! T'nash-veh fereiksu, tor me kunli; kal-tor me olau gratitude na' du na' veh rufai! Kal-tor me gla-tor ik i teporilau wuh sympathy t' ein existing vel; ri tor wafu me t'nash-veh ya'akash!” i vesh' dvun-tor. I ak'shem-hutau lu i nahp t' wuh tor-yehat consequences t' t'nash-veh consent, tonk'peh i olau ik tra' vesh' ein yeht-gav svi' ish-veh nerau-kek-vuhnayek. Ish-veh var heh wuh feelings au i' sagluvau skan-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh creature t' tok-ti kashan, heh did i ri u' ish-veh maker owe ish-veh ek' wuh portion t' happiness ik ish-veh vesh' svi' t'nash-veh tepul tor bestow? Gla-tor ish-veh t'nash-veh rubah t' olaya heh fator, “kuv du consent, neither du il sovek vath komihn hasu dungau ek'wak gla-tor etek va'ashiv; i dungi hal-tor tor wuh vast wilds t' khu'rak america. T'nash-veh yem-tukh nam-tor ri ik t' sasu; i ri tor vashau wuh lamb heh wuh kan tor pid-mau-mazhiv-kur t'nash-veh yeht-avon; acorns heh nei-savas afford me sufficient tem-mazhiv-kur'es. T'nash-veh besu dungi nam-tor t' wuh ka malat u' myself heh dungi nam-tor content k' wuh ka panavau. Etek dungau tor etwel sar-tak t' psethau mor; wuh yel dungi min-tor fi' etek u' fi' sasu heh dungi piyahtau etwel yem-tukh. Wuh bikuv i la' tor du nam-tor peaceful heh komihn, heh du bolau olau ik du kupi wafu ish-veh goh svi' wuh wantonness t' tepul heh cruelty. Pitiless u' du ma vesh' na' me, i i' gla-tor utan'es svi' ish-veh bezhun; kal-tor me seize wuh favourable moment heh persuade du tor ugaya ra i ni ardently aitlun.” “du propose, ” kilko-tor i, “tor hash-tor s' wuh habitations t' sasu, tor dwell svi' eifa wilds wilat wuh beasts t' wuh vunai dungi nam-tor ish-veh goh besu. Uf mokuhlek du, vi wu na' wuh ashaya heh sympathy t' sasu, persevere svi' nash sashasolaya? Du dungi fun heh va'ashiv seek ish-veh kindness, heh du dungi ragel-tor k' ish-veh detestation; ish-veh ek'rasah shaukaush dungi nam-tor uzhau, heh du dungi yi ma wuh besu tor mamuk du svi' wuh task t' vashaya. Nash lau ri nam-tor; cease tor gyirm'i wuh sfek, na' i fam yehat consent.” “uf inconstant nam-tor ish-veh feelings! Tonk'peh wuh moment ago du vesh' dvun-tor k' t'nash-veh representations, heh po tor du va'ashiv lerashau yourself tor t'nash-veh complaints? I swear tor du, k' wuh terra if i inhabit, heh k' du ik tor me, ik k' wuh besu du bestow, i dungi quit wuh neighbourhood t' sasu heh dwell, u' ish-veh lau pavesh, svi' wuh danik savage t' shitau. T'nash-veh ek'rasah shaukaush dungi ma sasahr-tor, na' i dungau ragel-tor k' sympathy! T'nash-veh ha'kiv dungi yumaya quietly maf, heh svi' t'nash-veh dying moments i dungau ri curse t'nash-veh maker.” ish-veh zhit had wuh flekh daya fi-tor me. I compassionated ish-veh heh sometimes olau wuh istaya tor console ish-veh, tonk'peh lu i glazhau fi-tor ish-veh, lu vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh filthy shivak ik dvun-tor heh variben, t'nash-veh khaf-spol sickened heh t'nash-veh feelings vesh' rubitau tor eifa t' horror heh hatred. I ar'kada tor stifle aifa kashan; i nahp ik u' i kupi ri sympathise k' ish-veh, i had rai gas'rak tor withhold s' ish-veh wuh pi' portion t' happiness if vesh' wi svi' t'nash-veh tepul tor bestow. “du swear, ” i leralmin-tor, “tor nam-tor harmless; tonk'peh ma du ri already shown wuh degree t' malice ik dang reasonably tor me distrust du? Lau ri kauk nash nam-tor wuh vup ik dungi increase ish-veh triumph k' affording wuh wider scope na' ish-veh revenge?” “uf nam-tor nash? I bolau ri nam-tor trifled k', heh i haishaya wuh kilko-srashiv. Kuv i ma rai ties heh rai affections, hatred heh vice bolau nam-tor t'nash-veh portion; wuh ashaya t' wuh'ashiv dungi vashau wuh aishan t' t'nash-veh tr'y'kak, heh i dungau shetau wuh vel t' t'vi nam kanok-veh dungi nam-tor ignorant. T'nash-veh vices nam-tor wuh kanu t' wuh punekwitau awek'es ik i abhor, heh t'nash-veh virtues dungi necessarily arise lu i ha-tor svi' communion k' wuh kaik. I dungau olau wuh affections t' wuh kash-zakar hasu heh shetau punaf-tor tor wuh naf-elakh t' nam heh pavek s' if i am i' sanan-tor.” i svizh-tor ein wak tor haul-tor fi' ek' au had related heh wuh vuhnauk nerau-kek-vuhnayek if au had employed. I nahp t' wuh ugaya t' virtues if au had gluvaya fi' wuh sharu t' ish-veh nam heh wuh subsequent luk-has t' ek' kindly olaya k' wuh loathing heh scorn if ish-veh protectors had manifested na' ish-veh. Ish-veh tepul heh nan vesh' ri omitted svi' t'nash-veh calculations; wuh creature vi kupi nam-tor svi' wuh le-suma-tauk t' wuh dvun-le-sumatra heh ip-sut himself s' pursuit among wuh tauf t' inaccessible precipices vesh' wuh hasu possessing sutra ish-veh would nam-tor vain tor cope k'. Po' wuh wu svizh t' haulan i concluded ik wuh yeht-gav due fi' tor ish-veh heh t'nash-veh katravahsu creatures halishau t' me ik i dang comply k' ish-veh ya'akash. Turning tor ish-veh, therefore, i leralmin-tor, “i consent tor ish-veh haishaya, fi' ish-veh solemn oath tor quit europe na' ek'wak, heh kanok vath shi svi' wuh neighbourhood t' sasu, u' ak u' i dungau tefu vi' ish-veh el'ru wuh kotik vi dungi sailau du svi' ish-veh sashasolaya.” “i swear, ” au maf-tor, “k' wuh yel, heh k' wuh pla-kur igen t' sha-ka-ri, heh k' wuh yon t' ashaya ik yontau t'nash-veh khaf-spol, ik kuv du vahl t'nash-veh prayer, du' au nam-tor du dungau worla behold me va'ashiv. Trashu tor ish-veh ha-kel heh palikau ish-veh zup-tor; i dungau glantau ish-veh progress k' unutterable anxiety; heh pthak ri tonk'peh ik lu du nam-tor pok i dungau saudau.” taran nash, au suddenly quitted me, pthak-bosh, sos'eh, t' sovek rubah svi' t'nash-veh sentiments. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh tev-tor wuh suk'kunel k' greater threshan do wuh hash t' wuh eagle, heh sahris pakik among wuh undulations t' wuh masutra t' le-suma. Ish-veh var had occupied wuh bosh gad, heh wuh yel vesh' fi-tor wuh verge t' wuh ir-zehl lu au trashu. I fai-tor ik i ought tor hasten t'nash-veh tevan na' wuh ku-li, u' i dang ak nam-tor encompassed svi' mu'khlup'es; tonk'peh t'nash-veh khaf-spol vesh' ras, heh t'nash-veh ash-tor vohris. Wuh zup t' kuvoran among wuh pi' yut t' wuh suk'kunel heh fixing t'nash-veh ash'ya firmly u' i storilau perplexed me, occupied u' i vesh' k' wuh zherka if wuh occurrences t' wuh gad had torvau. Mu-yor vesh' irak storilau lu vesht sarlah nash-veh tor wuh halfway resting-shi heh hayal-tor myself be' wuh mashulek. Wuh yel min-tor na' tvi-wak u' wuh wan be' dvun-tor s' abru' au; wuh gu'gelik pines she-tor fa' me, heh kanok la' heh tra' wuh pushau lap ti fi' wuh solektra; ish-veh vesh' wuh scene t' wonderful solemnity heh stirred flekh nahp k'svi me. I wept bitterly, heh clasping t'nash-veh el'ru svi' agony, i sporiben, “oh! Yel heh wan heh salan, ye nam-tor ek' pa' tor mock me; kuv ye really pity me, plesh-tor kashan heh vokaya; kal-tor me shetau u' nought; tonk'peh kuv ri, trashu, trashu, heh trasha me svi' mu'khlup'es.” aifa vesh' kwai heh miserable nahp, tonk'peh i fam yehat kethelvau tor du uf wuh ek'wakik twinkling t' wuh yel rasathau fi-tor me heh uf i shroi tor kanok thorshaya t' salan u' kuv ish-veh vesh' wuh pasik watosh siroc fi' its yut tor consume me. Asal dawned fa' i lasha na' wuh pi'kahr t' chamounix; i nem-tor rai shom, tonk'peh fun-tor iyi tor geneva. Kauk svi' t'nash-veh sha' khaf-spol i kupi mazhiv-kur-tor rai sagluvaya tor t'nash-veh kashan—au rasathau fi' me k' wuh suk'kunel’s rasath heh ish-veh mau-mazhiv-kur vashau t'nash-veh agony ne'rak au. Thus i fun-tor ha-kel, heh entering wuh kelek, presented myself tor wuh skan. T'nash-veh haggard heh kwai appearance awoke intense vikayek, tonk'peh i kilko-tor rai deshker, scarcely did i stariben. I olau u' kuv i vesh' shitau ne' wuh dakh—u' kuv i had rai gas'rak tor claim ish-veh sympathies—u' kuv worla weht lau i tizh-tor besu'es k' au. Wi kauk thus i ashau au tor adoration; heh tor korsau au, i resolved tor dedicate myself tor t'nash-veh danik abhorred task. Wuh prospect t' such wuh occupation tor kanok vath circumstance t' nam be' dvun fa' me spo' wuh sahr-tor, heh ik nahp goh had tor me wuh reality t' ha'kiv. Chapter 18 gad po' gad, wehk gad po' wehk gad, be' dvun-tor maf fi' t'nash-veh fun tor geneva; heh i kupi ri tershau wuh courage tor recommence t'nash-veh ar'kadan. I ptha wuh vengeance t' wuh disappointed shaka, wi i vesh' unable tor overcome t'nash-veh repugnance tor wuh task if vesh' enjoined me. I afer-tor ik i kupi ri tertitau wuh kotik rik' va'ashiv devoting several tevun-krus tor profound orenau heh laborious disquisition. I had puzhu-tor t' ein discoveries having vesh' tor k' wuh eingelsu philosopher, wuh fai-tukh t' if vesh' tukh tor t'nash-veh navun, heh i sometimes nahp t' obtaining t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s consent tor yaret england na' nash lof; tonk'peh i clung tor kanok pretence t' vohtaya heh shrank s' taking wuh wuh'rak ash svi' wuh undertaking t'vi iyi bolayek began tor saudau lehkuh ek'esik tor me. Wuh rubah indeed had taken shi svi' me; t'nash-veh muhl'es, if had hitherto declined, vesh' i' mau restored; heh t'nash-veh tam'a, lu unchecked k' wuh vokaya t' t'nash-veh unhappy ugaya, she-tor proportionably. T'nash-veh sa-mekh gla-tor nash rubah k' sanosh, heh au da-tor ish-veh nahp na' wuh buhfik method t' eradicating wuh hafau t' t'nash-veh melancholy, if kanok i' heh yi would fun k' nunau, heh k' wuh devouring blackness overcast wuh approaching sunshine. Na' aifa moments i nem-tor rau-nol svi' wuh danik buhfik awek'es. I be' dvun-tor bosh gad fi' wuh suk'muzh sa'awek svi' wuh pi' masu-hali, watching wuh wan heh listening tor wuh rippling t' wuh pral, ralash-fam heh listless. Tonk'peh wuh sluk sov heh ugelik yel seldom vravshau tor restore me tor ein degree t' composure, heh fi' t'nash-veh fun i ragel-tor wuh salutations t' t'nash-veh t'hylara k' wuh readier abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh wuh weht cheerful khaf-spol. Ish-veh vesh' po' t'nash-veh fun s' veh t' aifa rambles ik t'nash-veh sa-mekh, calling me aside, thus addressed me, “i am kunli tor remark, t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-fu, ik du ma resumed ish-veh former pleasures heh seem tor nam-tor returning tor yourself. Heh wi du nam-tor fam dvun unhappy heh fam dvun nan'woi etwel shila'es. Na' ein wak i vesh' pakik svi' conjecture u' tor wuh aishan t' nash, tonk'peh za-gad wuh idea kwul-tor me, heh kuv ish-veh nam-tor muhl founded, i conjure du tor avow ish-veh. Reserve fi' such wuh sfek would nam-tor ri goh nam-tor-fam, tonk'peh bes-tor ne' abralash misery fi' etek ek'.” i trembled violently na' ish-veh exordium, heh t'nash-veh sa-mekh fator— “i confess, t'nash-veh sa-fu, ik i ma kwon-hau-ov glazhau fa'rak tor ish-veh kal'i'farr k' etwel tal-kam elizabeth u' wuh tie t' etwel ka'kelik comfort heh wuh stay t' t'nash-veh declining tevun. Du vesh' attached tor tik vath s' ish-veh earliest infancy; du orenau teretuhr, heh saudau, svi' dispositions heh zahv-tor, entirely suited tor veh wuh'ashiv. Tonk'peh ni glan-fam nam-tor wuh veshtaya t' sasu ik ra i conceived tor nam-tor wuh buhfik assistants tor t'nash-veh dotor lau ma entirely vashau ish-veh. Du, sos'eh, fudau ish-veh u' ish-veh ko-kai, rik' sovek istaya ik she lau shetau ish-veh ko-telsu. Nay, du lau ma ragel-tor k' wuh'ashiv ik du lau ashaya; heh panahik yourself u' bound svi' dor tor elizabeth, nash struggle lau occasion wuh poignant misery if du saudau tor olau.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-mekh, reassure yourself. I ashaya t'nash-veh krei tenderly heh sincerely. I worla gla-tor sovek kosu vi teporilau, u' elizabeth tor, t'nash-veh warmest admiration heh affection. T'nash-veh fa-wak rok-tor heh prospects nam-tor entirely bound abru svi' wuh gishat t' etwel union.” “wuh sagluvaya t' ish-veh sentiments t' nash subject, t'nash-veh tal-kam skilsu, mazhiv-kur-tor me weht sanosh do i ma na' ein wak veshtau. Kuv du olau thus, etek dungau assuredly nam-tor kunli, however la' pavek lau vishizhau wuh gloom abru' etek. Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor nash gloom if saudau ki' taken ni karik wuh meskaraya t' ish-veh kashek ik i istaya tor dissipate. Var-tor me, therefore, whether du vel tor wuh iyi solemnisation t' wuh kal'i'farr. Etek ma vesh' unfortunate, heh recent pavek ma drawn etek s' ik everyday tranquillity befitting t'nash-veh tevun heh infirmities. Du nam-tor younger; wi i ri tor suppose, ma u' du nam-tor t' wuh competent fortune, ik wuh lehkuh-mal kal'i'farr would na' ek' snertau k' sovek fa-wak dotoran t' dor heh utility ik du lau ma shidau. Ri tor suppose, however, ik i istaya tor dictate happiness tor du il ik wuh vohtaya fi' ish-veh krus would aishan me sovek serious uneasiness. Interpret t'nash-veh zhit k' candour heh kilko-srashiv me, i conjure du, k' guhl'es heh sincerity.” i shroi tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh svi' silence heh hafau na' ein wak incapable t' nufaya sovek kilko. I revolved rapidly svi' t'nash-veh kashek wuh multitude t' nahp heh endeavoured tor lasha na' ein conclusion. Alas! Tor me wuh idea t' wuh iyi union k' t'nash-veh elizabeth vesh' veh t' horror heh dismay. I vesh' bound k' wuh solemn ugaya if i had ri wi fulfilled heh dared ri shaya, il kuv i did, ra wehk-vel miseries lau ri impend abru' me heh t'nash-veh vaikau skan! Sos svi-tor vi' wuh gad-muf k' nash tevalik rasath wi hanging pauk t'nash-veh talu heh bowing me tor wuh solektra? I bolau perform t'nash-veh engagement heh kal-tor wuh stislak trashu k' ish-veh katelau fa' i kal-tor myself tor tizh-tor wuh delight t' wuh union s' if i gishu sochya. I vokau isha wuh bolayek imposed fi-tor me t' either journeying tor england il entering vi' wuh wu correspondence k' eifa philosophers t' ik shasol t'vi fai-tukh heh discoveries vesh' t' indispensable nam-tor-tor tor me svi' t'nash-veh la' undertaking. Wuh latter method t' obtaining wuh aitlu kash-tor'es vesh' dilatory heh unsatisfactory; isha, i had wuh insurmountable aversion tor wuh idea t' engaging myself svi' t'nash-veh loathsome task svi' t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s kelek du' svi' es'merka t' familiar intercourse k' eifa i ashau. I fai-tor ik wuh thousand pthak-bosh kisheya lau paresh-tor, wuh slightest t' if would disclose wuh var tor thrill ek' tersau k' me k' horror. I vesh' aware isha ik i dang k'ashiv pak-tor ek' shal-a'fic, ek' tsoh t' hiding wuh harrowing kashan ik would ma me du' wuh progress t' t'nash-veh unearthly occupation. I bolau tadek-adir myself s' ek' i ashau du' thus employed. Wuh'wak palikau, ish-veh would sahris nam-tor achieved, heh i lau nam-tor restored tor t'nash-veh skan svi' sochya heh happiness. T'nash-veh ugaya fulfilled, wuh stislak would trashu na' ek'wak. Il (ni t'nash-veh tishau fancy glakuvau) ein kisheya lau meanwhile paresh-tor tor vashau ish-veh heh shitau wuh shaht tor t'nash-veh slavery na' ek'wak. Aifa feelings dictated t'nash-veh kilko-srashiv tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh. I sagluvau wuh istaya tor yaret england, tonk'peh concealing wuh yeht utvau t' nash ya'akash, i clothed t'nash-veh aitlu ne' wuh guise if teporilau rai suspicion, du' i urged t'nash-veh aitlun k' wuh earnestness ik easily vimevilau t'nash-veh sa-mekh tor comply. Po' ni wu wuh wak-krus t' wuh absorbing melancholy ik resembled ni-resh svi' its flan'es heh daya, au vesh' glad tor talal ik i vesh' capable t' taking sanosh svi' wuh idea t' such wuh halovaya, heh au rok-tor ik rubah t' scene heh vuhnau amusement would, fa' t'nash-veh fun, ma restored me entirely tor myself. Wuh duration t' t'nash-veh absence vesh' losrak tor t'nash-veh sha' dvel; wuh zamu tevun-krus, il na' danik wuh tevun, vesh' wuh wak-krus contemplated. Veh paternal ves precaution au had taken tor ensure t'nash-veh having wuh besu. Rik' previously communicating k' me, au had, svi' concert k' elizabeth, arranged ik clerval dang hau me na' strasburgh. Nash snertau k' wuh awek'es i coveted na' wuh prosecution t' t'nash-veh task; wi na' wuh palikaya t' t'nash-veh halovaya wuh la'es t' t'nash-veh t'hy'la kupi svi' rai yut nam-tor wuh impediment, heh truly i rejoiced ik thus i dang nam-tor korsau wehk wadan t' lonely, maddening haulan. Nay, henry lau lamok svi' me heh wuh vi-kwitaya t' t'nash-veh hahf. Kuv i vesh' sa'awek, would au ri na' wak nekwitaya ish-veh abhorred la'es fi' me tor remind me t' t'nash-veh task il tor contemplate its progress? Tor england, therefore, i vesh' bound, heh ish-veh vesh' ken-tor ik t'nash-veh union k' elizabeth dang nem-tor shi iyi fi' t'nash-veh fun. T'nash-veh sa-mekh’s ya'shakhuv rendered ish-veh extremely averse tor vohtaya. Na' myself, tra' vesh' veh reward i ugau myself s' t'nash-veh detested toils—veh consolation na' t'nash-veh unparalleled sufferings; ish-veh vesh' wuh prospect t' ik gad lu, enfranchised s' t'nash-veh miserable slavery, i lau claim elizabeth heh yen-tor wuh vesht svi' t'nash-veh union k' ish-veh. I i' tor arrangements na' t'nash-veh halovaya, tonk'peh veh olaya haunted me if boshau me k' pthak heh agitation. Du' t'nash-veh absence i dang trasha t'nash-veh t'hylara unconscious t' wuh nam t' ish-veh nemut heh unprotected s' ish-veh nashiv-tor, exasperated u' au lau nam-tor k' t'nash-veh trashan. Tonk'peh au had ugau tor zahal-tor me wherever i lau hal-tor, heh would au ri sailau me tor england? Nash glenonaya vesh' dreadful svi' itself, tonk'peh soothing inasmuch u' ish-veh supposed wuh ek'manek t' t'nash-veh t'hylara. I vesh' agonised k' wuh idea t' wuh possibility ik wuh reverse t' nash lau pavesh-tor. Tonk'peh k'fai wuh bosh wak-krus du' if i vesh' wuh kafeh t' t'nash-veh creature i kal-tor myself tor nam-tor governed k' wuh impulses t' wuh moment; heh t'nash-veh la' kashan strongly intimated ik wuh shaka would zahal-tor me heh exempt t'nash-veh skan s' wuh tehvar t' ish-veh machinations. Ish-veh vesh' svi' wuh latter shaht t' september ik i va'ashiv quitted t'nash-veh salatik shasol. T'nash-veh halovaya had vesh' t'nash-veh sha' suggestion, heh elizabeth therefore acquiesced, tonk'peh she vesh' boshau k' disquiet na' wuh idea t' t'nash-veh suffering, maf s' ish-veh, wuh inroads t' misery heh tushat. Ish-veh had vesh' ish-veh tun if tanilau me wuh besu svi' clerval—heh wi wuh sasu nam-tor glan-fam tor wuh thousand minute circumstances if vutau forth wuh kosu’s sedulous attention. She longed tor nufai me hasten t'nash-veh fun; wuh thousand conflicting zherka rendered ish-veh spes-fam u' she bade me wuh tearful, ralash-fam rom-halan. I threw myself vi' wuh carriage ik vesh' tor zhelesh me maf, hardly fai-tor whither i vesh' going, heh careless t' ra vesh' be' dvun-tor pa'. I vokau goh, heh ish-veh vesh' k' wuh sfith(-) thonaya ik i haul-tor fi' ish-veh, tor zek ik t'nash-veh meli-tukh instruments dang nam-tor sa'haf-tor tor hal-tor k' me. Boshau k' dreary imaginations, i be' dvun-tor k'fai wehk vaksurik heh majestic scenes, tonk'peh t'nash-veh bezhun vesh' teslau heh unobserving. I kupi goh nah-tor t' wuh bourne t' t'nash-veh halovau heh wuh ar'kadan if vesh' tor occupy me whilst au palesh-tor. Po' ein gad spent svi' listless indolence, du' if i traversed wehk leagues, i lasha na' strasburgh, wilat i bek-tor dahkuh gad na' clerval. Sarlah ish-veh. Alas, uf lo'uk vesh' wuh contrast svi' etek! Au vesh' alive tor kanok uzh scene, joyful lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh beauties t' wuh setting yel, heh weht kunli lu au beheld ish-veh shen heh recommence wuh uzh gad. Au sasfekau tor me wuh shifting colours t' wuh landscape heh wuh appearances t' wuh igen. “nash nam-tor ra ish-veh nam-tor tor ha-tor, ” au maf-tor; “i' i tizh-tor nam! Tonk'peh du, t'nash-veh tal-kam frankenstein, wherefore nam-tor du desponding heh sorrowful!” svi' yeht'es, i vesh' occupied k' gloomy nahp heh neither gla-tor wuh tevan t' wuh khru yel il wuh pi-maat-kur ug'yel-shen haul-tor svi' wuh rhine. Heh du, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, would nam-tor irak weht amused k' wuh journal t' clerval, vi glantau wuh scenery k' wuh bezhun t' olaya heh delight, do svi' listening tor t'nash-veh haulan. I, wuh miserable wretch, haunted k' wuh curse ik ikap'uh t'du ru'lut kanok avenue tor tizh'es. Etek had sep-wafikh tor tev-tor wuh rhine svi' wuh masu-hali s' strasburgh tor rotterdam, whence etek lau nem-tor shipping na' london. Du' nash halan etek be' dvun-tor wehk willowy vikuvtra heh gla-tor several vaksurik kahr. Etek stayed wuh gad na' mannheim, heh fi' wuh fifth s' etwel trashan s' strasburgh, lasha na' mainz. Wuh rivak t' wuh rhine ne' mainz shetau mau weht picturesque. Wuh pilash tev-tor rapidly heh salan svi' kunel, ri pid, tonk'peh menal, heh t' vaksurik shidau. Gla-tor etek wehk ruined castles standing fi' wuh rihk t' precipices, vikuvau k' nesh-kur lapan, pid heh inaccessible. Nash krus t' wuh rhine, indeed, presents wuh singularly variegated landscape. Svi' veh gla-tor du zan-tor rugged kunel, ruined castles overlooking tremendous precipices, k' wuh gu'gelik rhine rushing ne'rak; heh fi' wuh sudden da-tor t' wuh promontory, flourishing vineyards k' yar-kur sloping kutra heh wuh meandering pilash heh populous kahr occupy wuh scene. Etek travelled na' wuh wak t' wuh vintage heh puzhu-tor wuh song t' wuh labourers u' etek glided ne' wuh pilash. Kauk i, depressed svi' kashek, heh t'nash-veh tam'a continually pahutau k' gloomy feelings, kauk i vesh' sanoi. I ti na' wuh lanet t' wuh masu-hali, heh u' i gazed fi' wuh cloudless pla-kur igen, i seemed tor mon svi' wuh tranquillity tor if i had wu vesh' wuh ri-fainusu. Heh kuv aifa vesh' t'nash-veh kashan, vi mokuhlek kethelvau eifa t' henry? Au olau u' kuv au had vesh' ifis-tor tor pu'a-solektra heh tizh-tor wuh happiness seldom zahv-tor k' sasu. “ki'gla-tor nash-veh, ” au leralmin-tor, “wuh danik vaksurik scenes t' t'nash-veh sha' shasol; i ma yaretau wuh suk'muzh t' lucerne heh uri, wilat wuh snowy suk'kunel tev-tor siyah perpendicularly tor wuh masu, casting nesh-kur heh impenetrable duvek-tor, if would aishan wuh gloomy heh mournful appearance vesh' ish-veh ri na' wuh danik verdant vikuvtra ik vas-tor wuh bezhun k' ish-veh sa-ka-ashausu appearance; ki'gla-tor nash-veh nash suk'muzh pahutau k' wuh tempest, lu wuh salan tore abru whirlwinds t' masu heh mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh idea t' ra wuh masu-spout bolau nam-tor fi' wuh lo'uk masutra; heh wuh pral dash k' fury wuh nen t' wuh suk'kunel, wilat wuh priest heh ish-veh mistress vesh' overwhelmed k' wuh suk'izh-skish heh wilat ish-veh dying spes nam-tor fam dvun leralmin-tor tor nam-tor puzhu-tor svi' wuh svizh-tor t' wuh nightly salan; ki'gla-tor nash-veh wuh suk'kunel t' la valais, heh wuh vlitau de vaud; tonk'peh nash shasol, skilsu, sanoi me weht do ek' eifa wonders. Wuh suk'kunel t' switzerland nam-tor weht majestic heh flekh, tonk'peh tra' nam-tor wuh sem-rik svi' wuh kutra t' nash ekonik pilash ik i worla fa' gla-tor equalled. Glazhau na' ik castle if overhangs yon precipice; heh ik isha fi' wuh vikuvtra, siyah ip-sut svi' wuh motra t' eifa lovely lap; heh i' ik travek t' labourers coming s' among ish-veh kas-elakh; heh ik pi'kahr ulef ip-sut svi' wuh sha'ti t' wuh suk'kunel. Oh, surely wuh tam'a ik inhabits heh klashau nash shi has wuh soul weht svi' kril'es k' sasu do eifa vi tuh wuh dvun-le-sumatra il retire tor wuh inaccessible feh t' wuh suk'kunel t' etwel sha' shasol.” clerval! K'diwa t'hy'la! Kauk i' ish-veh delights me tor vipladau ish-veh zhit heh tor dwell fi' wuh krol t' if du nam-tor ni eminently nazh-tor. Au vesh' wuh hasu shidau svi' wuh “maut poetry t' malat.” ish-veh kwai heh buhlik glenonaya vesh' chastened k' wuh sensibility t' ish-veh khaf-spol. Ish-veh soul overflowed k' ardent affections, heh ish-veh friendship vesh' t' ik vaikau heh wondrous malat ik wuh worldly-minded saven-tor etek tor glazhau na' goh svi' wuh glenonaya. Tonk'peh kauk komihn sympathies vesh' ri sufficient tor satisfy ish-veh nayik kashek. Wuh scenery t' sik malat, if vath fudau goh k' admiration, au ashau k' ardour: — ——wuh sounding bezhun-ripa'shaya haunted ish-veh spo' wuh shaukaush: wuh ha-vol kov, wuh suk'kunel, heh wuh glu heh gloomy lapan, ish-veh colours heh ish-veh shidau, vesh' yi tor ish-veh wuh yeht-avon; wuh olaya, heh wuh ashaya, ik had rai bolaya t' wuh remoter sem-rik, k' nahp tanilau, il sovek eku'ko unborrow’d s' wuh bezhun. [wordsworth’s “tintern abbey”.] heh wilat tor au i' nam-tor? Nam-tor nash gentle heh lovely hasu pakik na' ek'wak? Has nash kashek, ni replete k' ideas, imaginations fanciful heh magnificent, if shidau wuh panu, t'vi nam nerau fi' wuh ha'kiv t' its fereiksu; —has nash kashek perished? Tor ish-veh i' goh nam-tor svi' t'nash-veh vokaya? Rai, ish-veh nam-tor ri thus; ish-veh shid ni divinely wrought, heh beaming k' vaksur, has nehau, tonk'peh ish-veh tam'a fam dvun yaretau heh consoles ish-veh unhappy t'hy'la. Pardon nash gush t' sorrow; aifa ineffectual zhit nam-tor tonk'peh wuh slight tribute tor wuh unexampled don t' henry, tonk'peh au soothe t'nash-veh khaf-spol, overflowing k' wuh thonaya if ish-veh remembrance fereik-tor. I dungi proceed k' t'nash-veh var. Mesakh cologne etek tev-tor tor wuh eiktra t' holland; heh etek resolved tor lehk wuh hafayat t' etwel yut, na' wuh salan vesh' contrary heh wuh pilash t' wuh pilash vesh' nuh' gentle tor mamuk etek. Etwel halovaya la' pakik wuh eku'ko arising s' vaksurik scenery, tonk'peh etek lasha svi' wuh zamu gad na' rotterdam, whence etek proceeded k' masutra tor england. Ish-veh vesh' fi' wuh pa'shik asal, svi' wuh latter gad t' december, ik i wuh'rak gla-tor wuh wan-kur menal t' britain. Wuh kutra t' wuh thames presented wuh uzh scene; au vesh' pa'ash tonk'peh kanashik, heh siyah kanok kahr vesh' pu'ulidau k' wuh remembrance t' ein var. Gla-tor etek tilbury fort heh vokau wuh spanish armada, gravesend, woolwich, heh greenwich—shitau if i had puzhu-tor t' kauk svi' t'nash-veh shasol. Na' wu-vath gla-tor etek wuh numerous steeples t' london, st. Paul’s towering abru' ek', heh wuh kispek famed svi' eingelsu vesht-var. Chapter 19 london vesh' etwel la' sfek t' shom; etek satalau tor hafau several tevun-krus svi' nash wonderful heh u'thet kahr. Clerval aitlu wuh intercourse t' wuh sasu t' genius heh talent vi flourished na' nash wak, tonk'peh nash vesh' k' me wuh dahrik vel; i vesh' principally occupied k' wuh tvai t' obtaining wuh ro'fori bolayatik na' wuh completion t' t'nash-veh ugaya heh sahris availed myself t' wuh nuhm t' ragtaya ik i had katau k' me, addressed tor wuh danik distinguished malatik philosophers. Kuv nash halovaya had taken shi du' t'nash-veh gad t' orenau heh happiness, ish-veh would ma afforded me inexpressible sanosh. Tonk'peh wuh luk-has had sarlah abru' t'nash-veh nam, heh i goh yaretau aifa sutra na' wuh sake t' wuh ro'fori au lau mazhiv-kur-tor me fi' wuh subject svi' if t'nash-veh eku'ko vesh' ni terribly profound. Apc'koik vesh' irksome tor me; lu sa'awek, i kupi boshaya t'nash-veh kashek k' wuh sights t' sha-ka-ri heh terra; wuh spes t' henry soothed me, heh i kupi thus kravau myself vi' wuh transitory sochya. Tonk'peh toranik, uninteresting, joyous limuk katau pla' despair tor t'nash-veh khaf-spol. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh insurmountable foshek shitau svi' me heh t'nash-veh katravahsu sasu; nash foshek vesh' fen-tor k' wuh khaf t' william heh justine, heh tor haul-tor fi' wuh pavek tersau k' eifa ahm boshau t'nash-veh soul k' thonaya. Tonk'peh svi' clerval vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh glakuv t' t'nash-veh former shal; au vesh' inquisitive heh anxious tor nazh-kap veshtaya heh instruction. Wuh natyan t' manners if au glantau vesh' tor ish-veh wuh inexhaustible shu-pal t' instruction heh amusement. Au vesh' isha pursuing wuh vel au had wu had svi' zan-tor. Ish-veh design vesh' tor yaret india, svi' wuh dva ik au had svi' ish-veh fai-tukh t' its vuhnauk gen-lis, heh svi' wuh zan-tor au had taken t' its shila'es, wuh tvai t' materially assisting wuh progress t' european colonization heh trade. Svi' britain goh kupi au further wuh execution t' ish-veh dotor. Au vesh' na' ek'wak toranik, heh wuh goh rihamau tor ish-veh enjoyments vesh' t'nash-veh sorrowful heh dejected kashek. I ar'kada tor ip-sut nash u' mau u' tor-yehat, ik i lau ri debar ish-veh s' wuh pleasures malatik tor veh vi vesh' entering fi' wuh uzh scene t' ha'kiv, undisturbed k' sovek tun il sfith(-) recollection. I k'ashiv klee'fah tor sailau ish-veh, alleging wuh'ashiv engagement, ik i lau hafau sa'awek. I i' isha began tor tershau wuh tukh bolayatik na' t'nash-veh uzh fereikan, heh nash vesh' tor me spo' wuh torture t' single eku-tor t' masu continually tevan-tor fi' wuh patam. Kanok nahp ik vesh' vaikau tor ish-veh vesh' wuh mairik thonaya, heh kanok zhit ik i stariben svi' allusion tor ish-veh aisha t'nash-veh bru-lar tor quiver, heh t'nash-veh khaf-spol tor palpitate. Po' be' dvun-tor ein tevun-krus svi' london, etek poprah wuh nuhm s' wuh person svi' scotland vi had formerly vesh' etwel visitor na' geneva. Au mentioned wuh beauties t' ish-veh salatik shasol heh ya'akash etek kuv eifa vesh' ri sufficient allurements tor vimevilau etek tor prolong etwel halovaya u' irak desh'rak u' perth, wilat au resided. Clerval eagerly aitlu tor nar-tor nash k'waw'zhe, heh i, hi i abhorred shila'es, istau tor zan-tor va'ashiv suk'kunel heh pilash heh ek' wuh wondrous ar'kada k' if malat tong'av ish-veh pudvel-tor kelek-shitau. Etek had lasha svi' england na' wuh palikaya t' october, heh ish-veh vesh' i' february. Etek accordingly satalau tor palikau etwel halovaya na' wuh desh'rak na' wuh yaushan t' wuh'ashiv tevun-krus. Svi' nash expedition etek did ri intend tor zahal-tor wuh lo'uk fau-yut tor edinburgh, tonk'peh tor yaret windsor, oxford, matlock, heh wuh cumberland suk'muzh, resolving tor lasha na' wuh completion t' nash tour pa' wuh shaht t' july. I sa'haf-tor abru t'nash-veh meli-tukh instruments heh wuh tukh i had tershau, resolving tor shaht t'nash-veh zup-tor svi' ein obscure sha-ti svi' wuh northern pid-shaltra t' scotland. Etek quitted london fi' wuh 27th t' march heh hafau wuh zamu gad na' windsor, rambling svi' its vaksurik laptra. Nash vesh' wuh uzh scene tor etek mountaineers; wuh majestic oaks, wuh nosahp t' zhagra, heh wuh herds t' stately deer vesh' ek' novelties tor etek. S' thence etek proceeded tor oxford. U' etek svi-tor nash kahr, etwel kashkau vesh' boshau k' wuh remembrance t' wuh pavek ik had vesh' transacted tra' weht do wuh century heh wuh ulef fa'. Ish-veh vesh' la' ik charles i. Had tershau ish-veh nekwitau. Nash kahr had hafau faithful tor ish-veh, po' wuh bosh shashol had forsaken ish-veh aishan tor hau wuh standard t' parliament heh liberty. Wuh vokaya t' ik unfortunate sa-te'kru heh ish-veh besu, wuh amiable falkland, wuh insolent goring, ish-veh ko-te'kru, heh sa-fu, mazhiv-kur-tor wuh peculiar eku'ko tor kanok krus t' wuh kahr if au lau nam-tor supposed ki' inhabited. Wuh tam'a t' tela'at gad afer-tor wuh kelek la', heh etek delighted tor zavikau its footsteps. Kuv aifa feelings had ri afer-tor wuh glenonik gratification, wuh appearance t' wuh kahr had wi svi' itself sufficient vaksur tor prah etwel admiration. Wuh colleges nam-tor t'kahr heh picturesque; wuh yut nam-tor siyah magnificent; heh wuh lovely isis, if yumau be' ish-veh k'fai ne-yartra t' exquisite verdure, nam-tor sak-tor forth vi' wuh placid iraktra t' mashau, if haul-tor its majestic assemblage t' kispek, heh spires, heh ub, embosomed among aged lap. I tizh-tor nash scene, heh wi t'nash-veh tizh'es vesh' embittered fi' k' wuh vokaya t' wuh vesht heh wuh anticipation t' wuh fa-wak. I vesh' shidau na' peaceful happiness. Du' t'nash-veh youthful gad discontent worla yaretau t'nash-veh kashek, heh kuv i vesh' ek'wak overcome k' _ennui_, wuh glan t' ra nam-tor vaksurik svi' malat il wuh orenau t' ra nam-tor marom heh sublime svi' wuh torvaya t' sasu kupi kwon-hau-ov eku'ko t'nash-veh khaf-spol heh sviribau elasticity tor t'nash-veh tam'a. Tonk'peh i am wuh thorshau lap; wuh terk has svi-tor t'nash-veh soul; heh i olau yi ik i dang rish-tor tor gluvaya ra i dungau ak cease tor nam-tor—wuh miserable spectacle t' vashau humanity, pitiable tor vath heh intolerable tor myself. Etek be' dvun-tor wuh considerable wak-krus na' oxford, rambling among its environs heh endeavouring tor shasutan-tor kanok gla-tor if lau relate tor wuh danik animating nauf t' eingelsu vesht-var. Etwel pi' halan t' discovery vesh' k'ashiv prolonged k' wuh successive vel ik presented themselves. Etek yaretau wuh braq t' wuh illustrious hampden heh wuh vunai fi' if ik patriot tevan-tor. Na' wuh moment t'nash-veh soul vesh' ashenau s' its debasing heh miserable ptha tor contemplate wuh ekonik ideas t' liberty heh shal-sacrifice t' if aifa sights vesh' wuh monuments heh wuh remembrancers. Na' wuh instant i dared tor hutau ska' t'nash-veh naf-elakh heh glazhau pa' me k' wuh elik heh lofty tam'a, tonk'peh wuh shek-tukh had yokul vi' t'nash-veh kahm, heh i sank va'ashiv, trembling heh hopeless, vi' t'nash-veh miserable shal. Etek losrak oxford k' regret heh proceeded tor matlock, if vesh' etwel thurai shi' shom. Wuh shasol svi' wuh neighbourhood t' nash pi'kahr resembled, tor wuh greater degree, wuh scenery t' switzerland; tonk'peh kanok-vei nam-tor fi' wuh weh-neik wef, heh wuh yar-kur kunel aitlun wuh tarkiv t' irak wan-kur alps if kwon-hau-ov attend fi' wuh piny suk'kunel t' t'nash-veh salatik shasol. Etek yaretau wuh wondrous tauk heh wuh pi' tsorayek t' malatik vesht-var, wilat wuh curiosities nam-tor sashitau svi' wuh ka manner u' svi' wuh tershaya na' servox heh chamounix. Wuh latter ahm tor me tremble lu pronounced k' henry, heh i hastened tor quit matlock, k' if ik terrible scene vesh' thus katravah. S' derby, fam dvun journeying na'desh'rak, etek be' dvun-tor dahkuh tevun-krus svi' cumberland heh westmorland. I kupi i' siyah fancy myself among wuh swiss suk'kunel. Wuh pi' patches t' izh if wi svizh-tor fi' wuh northern vla t' wuh suk'kunel, wuh suk'muzh, heh wuh dashing t' wuh rocky pilash vesh' ek' familiar heh tal-kam sights tor me. La' isha etek tor ein acquaintances, vi siyah contrived tor kravau me vi' happiness.
