Wuh delight t' clerval vesh' proportionably weht tor t'nash-veh; ish-veh kashek sa'ovau svi' wuh apc'koik t' sasu t' talent, heh au afer-tor svi' ish-veh sha' malat greater tsoh heh resources do au kupi ma glenonau himself ki' ma du' au katravah k' ish-veh inferiors. “i kupi be' dvun t'nash-veh ha'kiv la', ” leralmin-tor au tor me; “heh among aifa suk'kunel i dang scarcely regret switzerland heh wuh rhine.” tonk'peh au afer-tor ik wuh traveller’s ha'kiv nam-tor veh ik vinan-tor mau kusut amidst its enjoyments. Ish-veh feelings nam-tor na' ek'wak fi' wuh sakadaya; heh lu au palikau tor ne'hal-tor vi' repose, au tal-tor himself obliged tor quit ik fi' if au shom-tor svi' sanosh na' vel uzh, if va'ashiv engages ish-veh attention, heh if isha au forsakes na' vath novelties. Etek had scarcely yaretau wuh vuhnauk suk'muzh t' cumberland heh westmorland heh conceived wuh affection na' ein t' wuh inhabitants lu wuh wak-krus t' etwel latva k' etwel scotch t'hy'la betau, heh etek losrak au tor haolvaya fi'. Na' t'nash-veh sha' krus i vesh' ri sorry. I had i' neglected t'nash-veh ugaya na' ein wak, heh i ptha wuh daya t' wuh dæmon’s disappointment. Au lau hafau svi' switzerland heh wreak ish-veh vengeance fi' t'nash-veh tomasu. Nash idea pursued me heh tormented me na' kanok moment s' if i lau vathru ma snatched repose heh sochya. I bek-tor na' t'nash-veh nuhm k' taulik impatience; kuv au vesh' vohtau i vesh' miserable heh overcome k' wuh thousand ptha; heh lu au lasha heh i gla-tor wuh superscription t' elizabeth il t'nash-veh sa-mekh, i hardly dared tor telv-tor heh ascertain t'nash-veh buk. Sometimes i nahp ik wuh shaka zahal-tor me heh lau expedite t'nash-veh remissness k' murdering t'nash-veh besu. Lu aifa nahp ma me, i would ri quit henry na' wuh moment, tonk'peh zahal-tor ish-veh u' ish-veh duv, tor protect ish-veh s' wuh fancied reshan t' ish-veh destroyer. I olau u' kuv i had committed ein lo'uk tr'y'kak, wuh hokni'es t' if haunted me. I vesh' guiltless, tonk'peh i had indeed drawn ne' wuh horrible curse fi-tor t'nash-veh patam, u' mortal u' ik t' tr'y'kak. I yaretau edinburgh k' languid bezhun heh kashek; heh wi ik kahr lau ma interested wuh danik unfortunate hasu. Clerval did ri spo' ish-veh ni muhl u' oxford, na' wuh antiquity t' wuh latter kahr vesh' weht pleasing tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh wuh vaksur heh regularity t' wuh uzh kahr t' edinburgh, its romantic castle heh its environs, wuh danik delightful svi' wuh panu, arthur’s ku-san, st. Bernard’s muhl, heh wuh pentland kunel, torabrau ish-veh na' wuh rubah heh boshau ish-veh k' cheerfulness heh admiration. Tonk'peh i vesh' impatient tor lasha na' wuh termination t' t'nash-veh halovaya. Etek losrak edinburgh svi' wuh wehk gad, be' dvun-tor k'fai coupar, st. Andrew’s, heh bi' wuh kutra t' wuh tay, tor perth, wilat etwel t'hy'la gishu etek. Tonk'peh i vesh' svi' rai mood tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh variben k' ri-fainusu il svi-tor vi' ish-veh feelings il dotoran k' wuh rom humour gishu s' wuh be'hai'la; heh accordingly i var-tor clerval ik i istau tor tor wuh tour t' scotland sa'awek. “tor du, ” leralmin-tor i, “tizh-tor yourself, heh kal-tor nash nam-tor etwel rendezvous. I lau nam-tor tadek-adir wuh tevun-krus il dahkuh; tonk'peh ri tor snertau k' t'nash-veh dvunel, i entreat du; trasha me tor sochya heh awek'es na' wuh pen wak; heh lu i fun, i rok ish-veh dungi nam-tor k' wuh lighter khaf-spol, weht congenial tor ish-veh sha' temper.” henry istau tor dissuade me, tonk'peh seeing me keh'sei fi' nash dotor, ceased tor remonstrate. Au entreated me tor kitau k'ashiv. “i had rather nam-tor k' du, ” au leralmin-tor, “svi' ish-veh solitary rambles, do k' aifa scotch sutra, ik i ri tor fai-tor; hasten, yi, t'nash-veh tal-kam t'hy'la, tor fun, ik i lau va'ashiv olau myself somewhat na' ha-kel, if i fam yehat tor svi' ish-veh absence.” having parted s' t'nash-veh t'hy'la, i satalau tor yaret ein remote gla-tor t' scotland heh shaht t'nash-veh ar'kadan svi' awek'es. I did ri vet tonk'peh ik wuh stislak zahal-tor me heh would discover himself tor me lu i dang ma shahtau, ik au lau poprah ish-veh besu. K' nash resolution i traversed wuh northern pid-shaltra heh teslau fi' veh t' wuh remotest t' wuh orkneys u' wuh scene t' t'nash-veh zup-tor. Ish-veh vesh' wuh shi fitted na' such wuh ar'kadan, hasu hardly weht do wuh kov t'vi pid vla vesh' continually beaten fi-tor k' wuh pral. Wuh solek vesh' barren, scarcely affording pasture na' wuh zamu miserable aushfa, heh oatmeal na' its inhabitants, if consisted t' kaukuh persons, t'vi gaunt heh scraggy sikrus mazhiv-kur-tor tokens t' ish-veh miserable panavau. Sazh heh kap, lu au indulged svi' such luxuries, heh kauk sluk masu, vesh' tor nam-tor procured s' wuh mainland, if vesh' pa' kaukuh miles irak. Fi' wuh bosh vikuvtra tra' vesh' tonk'peh rehkuh miserable huts, heh veh t' aifa vesh' vacant lu i lasha. Nash i hired. Ish-veh tuhlau tonk'peh dahkuh tvi-shal, heh aifa gluvau ek' wuh squalidness t' wuh danik miserable penury. Wuh thatch had tevan-tor svi', wuh temok vesh' unplastered, heh wuh svep vesh' ska' its tu'adayek. I ordered ish-veh tor nam-tor teslau, bought ein furniture, heh nem-tor mat, wuh incident if would doubtless ma occasioned ein ak'wikmun had ri ek' wuh kash-ral t' wuh cottagers vesh' benumbed k' aitlun heh squalid poverty. U' ish-veh vesh', i ha-tor ungazed na' heh unmolested, hardly itaren na' wuh pittance t' yem-tukh heh sai-vel if i mazhiv-kur-tor, ni mau tor suffering pasik kauk wuh coarsest kashan t' sasu. Svi' nash retreat i vaikau wuh asal tor zup; tonk'peh svi' wuh khru, lu wuh igen-va permitted, i lates-tor fi' wuh stony shahov t' wuh masutra tor shroi tor wuh pral u' au roared heh dashed na' t'nash-veh ash'ya. Ish-veh vesh' wuh monotonous wi ek'wak-rubai scene. I nahp t' switzerland; ish-veh vesh' irak natya s' nash desolate heh appalling landscape. Its kunel nam-tor wein-tor k' kas-elakh, heh its cottages nam-tor scattered bali svi' wuh eiktra. Its rom suk'muzh haul-tor wuh pla-kur heh gentle igen, heh lu troubled k' wuh salan, ish-veh tumult nam-tor tonk'peh u' wuh mavau t' wuh lively kan-bu lu tcok'at tor wuh roarings t' wuh masuk'veh masutra. Svi' nash manner i sagan-tor t'nash-veh occupations lu i wuh'rak lasha, tonk'peh u' i proceeded svi' t'nash-veh zup, ish-veh became kanok gad weht horrible heh irksome tor me. Sometimes i kupi ri fakovau fi' myself tor svi-tor t'nash-veh ek'tal-zup-shal na' several gad, heh na' vath wak i toiled gad heh mu-yor svi' zek tor ovsotik t'nash-veh ar'kadan. Ish-veh vesh', indeed, wuh filthy torek svi' if i vesh' engaged. Du' t'nash-veh wuh'rak spolek, wuh ves t' buhlik frenzy had blinded me tor wuh horror t' t'nash-veh employment; t'nash-veh kashek vesh' intently teslau fi' wuh consummation t' t'nash-veh zup, heh t'nash-veh bezhun vesh' ikap-tor tor wuh horror t' t'nash-veh proceedings. Tonk'peh i' i went tor ish-veh svi' samu khaf, heh t'nash-veh khaf-spol k'ashiv sickened na' wuh ar'kadan t' t'nash-veh el'ru. Thus situated, employed svi' wuh danik detestable occupation, immersed svi' wuh awek'es wilat nothing kupi na' wuh instant vutau t'nash-veh attention s' wuh actual scene svi' if i vesh' engaged, t'nash-veh tam'a became unequal; i grew restless heh nervous. Kanok moment i ptha tor ragel-tor t'nash-veh persecutor. Sometimes i hayal-tor k' t'nash-veh bezhun teslau fi' wuh solektra, fearing tor ashenau au lest au dang snagel wuh vel if i ni mau dreaded tor behold. I ptha tor czar s' wuh glan t' t'nash-veh katravahsu creatures lest lu sa'awek au dang sarlah tor claim ish-veh besu. Svi' wuh tvai wak i ar'kada fi', heh t'nash-veh zup vesh' already considerably storilau. I glazhau na' its completion k' wuh tremulous heh nayik rok, if i dared ri sahrafel myself tor deshker tonk'peh if vesh' intermixed k' obscure forebodings t' ek'rasah ik tor t'nash-veh khaf-spol sicken svi' t'nash-veh bosom. Chapter 20 i hayal-tor veh khru svi' t'nash-veh ek'tal-zup-shal; wuh yel had eku, heh wuh aikum vesh' aishan rising s' wuh masutra; i had ri sufficient ta'hal na' t'nash-veh employment, heh i hafau idle, svi' wuh svizh t' consideration t' whether i dang trasha t'nash-veh zup na' wuh mu-yor il hasten its conclusion k' wuh unremitting attention tor ish-veh. U' i hayal-tor, wuh ranau t' haulan paresh-tor tor me if pufulag-tor me tor panah-tor wuh daya t' ra i vesh' i' doing. Rehkuh tevun fa', i vesh' engaged svi' wuh ka manner heh had fereik-tor wuh shaka t'vi unparalleled barbarity had desolated t'nash-veh khaf-spol heh boshau ish-veh na' ek'wak k' wuh bitterest remorse. I vesh' i' pa' tor shid wuh'ashiv hasu t' t'vi dispositions i vesh' kahkwa ignorant; she lau shetau lehkuh thousand wak weht malignant do ish-veh katelau heh delight, na' its sha' sake, svi' riyeht-staya heh wretchedness. Au had sworn tor quit wuh neighbourhood t' sasu heh ip-sut himself svi' eshikh, tonk'peh she had ri; heh she, vi svi' ek' yesik'es vesh' tor shetau wuh thinking heh reasoning aushfa, lau klee'fah tor comply k' wuh lerakhovau tor fa' ish-veh fereikan. Au lau kauk fnu-ven tik vath; wuh creature vi already ha-tor loathed ish-veh sha' riyeht-shid'es, heh lau au ri conceive wuh greater abhorrence na' ish-veh lu sarlah ish-veh fa' ish-veh bezhun svi' wuh kotik shid? She isha lau da-tor k' spa'ash s' ish-veh tor wuh superior vaksur t' sasu; she lau quit ish-veh, heh au nam-tor va'ashiv sa'awek, exasperated k' wuh sluk provocation t' hasu deserted k' veh t' ish-veh sha' koshtri. Kauk kuv au vesh' tor trasha europe heh inhabit wuh eshikh t' wuh uzh panu, wi veh t' wuh wuh'rak results t' eifa sympathies na' if wuh dæmon thirsted would nam-tor kanu, heh wuh ne-koshtri t' e'shua would nam-tor propagated fi-tor wuh terra vi lau tor wuh maut nam t' wuh koshtri t' sasu wuh nosh precarious heh bosh t' vash. Had i gas'rak, na' t'nash-veh sha' rufai, tor inflict nash curse fi-tor everlasting generations? I had fa' vesh' dvun-tor k' wuh sophisms t' wuh hasu i had fereik-tor; i had vesh' kwul-tor senseless k' ish-veh shakaik nan; tonk'peh i', na' wuh wuh'rak wak, wuh wickedness t' t'nash-veh ugaya thorau fi-tor me; i ak'shem-hutau tor nah-tor ik fa-wak ya'shakhuv lau curse me u' ish-veh pest, t'vi selfishness had ri hesitated tor mahr-tor its sha' sochya na' wuh price, sos'eh, t' wuh nam t' wuh bosh komihn ne-koshtri. I trembled heh t'nash-veh khaf-spol vravshau k'svi me, lu, fi' looking abru, vesht gla-tor nash-veh k' wuh ta'hal t' wuh aikum wuh dæmon na' wuh casement. Wuh ghastly wa'limatau wrinkled ish-veh bru-lar u' au gazed fi' me, wilat i hayal-tor fulfilling wuh task if au had allotted tor me. Ha, au had zahal-tor me svi' t'nash-veh halovau; au had loitered svi' laptra, ip-sut himself svi' tauk, il taken rau-nol svi' eik heh eshikh heaths; heh au i' sarlah tor ulidar t'nash-veh progress heh claim wuh fulfilment t' t'nash-veh ugaya. U' i glazhau fi' ish-veh, ish-veh countenance sagluvau wuh utmost sadvun t' malice heh treachery. I nahp k' wuh kashan t' ni-resh fi' t'nash-veh ugaya t' creating wuh'ashiv spo' tor ish-veh, heh trembling k' shaukaush, tore tor krus wuh vel fi' if i vesh' engaged. Wuh wretch gla-tor me vashau wuh creature fi' t'vi fa-wak nam au nerau na' happiness, heh k' wuh vlut t' devilish despair heh revenge, withdrew. I losrak wuh tvi-shal, heh locking wuh svep, tor wuh solemn vow svi' t'nash-veh sha' khaf-spol worla tor resume t'nash-veh zup-tor; heh yi, k' trembling ash-tor, i sought t'nash-veh sha' ha-shal. I vesh' sa'awek; rim vesh' be' me tor dissipate wuh gloom heh vas-tor me s' wuh sickening oppression t' wuh danik terrible reveries. Several wadan be' dvun-tor, heh i hafau be' t'nash-veh krani gazing fi' wuh masutra; ish-veh vesh' siyah motionless, na' wuh salan vesh' hushed, heh ek' malat reposed ne' wuh bezhun t' wuh hizhuk aikum. Wuh zamu fishing hali sa'awek specked wuh masu, heh i' heh yi wuh gentle pi'salan wafted wuh ralash t' spes u' wuh aluk-kumsu puvutau tor veh wuh'ashiv. I olau wuh silence, hi i vesh' hardly d'wonil t' its mairik profundity, abi' t'nash-veh kaluk vesh' suddenly pehkau k' wuh paddling t' fel be' wuh gef, heh wuh person landed beyik t'nash-veh kelek. Svi' wuh zamu minutes po', i puzhu-tor wuh creaking t' t'nash-veh svep, u' kuv ein veh endeavoured tor tu'ash ish-veh softly. I trembled s' patam tor ash'ya; i olau wuh presentiment t' vi ish-veh vesh' heh istau tor kastorilau veh t' wuh peasants vi dwelt svi' wuh cottage ri irak s' t'nash-veh; tonk'peh i vesh' overcome k' wuh kashan t' helplessness, ni k'ashiv olau svi' frightful sahr-tor-tor, lu du svi' vain endeavour tor hash-tor s' wuh impending tehvar, heh vesh' rooted tor wuh gla-tor. Presently i puzhu-tor wuh ralash t' footsteps bi' wuh tvur; wuh svep tu'ash, heh wuh wretch ik i dreaded saudau. Shutting wuh svep, au betau me heh leralmin-tor svi' wuh smothered spes, “du ma vashau wuh ar'kadan if du began; ra nam-tor ish-veh ik du intend? Tor du dare tor shaya ish-veh ugaya? I ma palesh-tor toil heh misery; i losrak switzerland k' du; i crept bi' wuh gef t' wuh rhine, among its willow vikuvtra heh abru' wuh dan-pid-sfek t' its kunel. I ma dwelt wehk tevun-krus svi' wuh heaths t' england heh among wuh eshikh t' scotland. I ma palesh-tor incalculable zung, heh samu, heh avon; tor du dare vashau t'nash-veh rok-tor?” “begone! I tor shaya t'nash-veh ugaya; worla dungi i fereik-tor wuh'ashiv spo' yourself, kaik svi' riyeht-shid'es heh wickedness.” “kafeh, i fa' reasoned k' du, tonk'peh du ma skan-tor yourself unworthy t' t'nash-veh condescension. Vokau ik i ma tepul; du dva-tor yourself miserable, tonk'peh i mokuhlek tor du ni wretched ik wuh ta'hal t' gad dungi nam-tor hateful tor du. Du nam-tor t'nash-veh fereiksu, tonk'peh i am ish-veh trensu; obey!” “wuh wadan t' t'nash-veh irresolution nam-tor vesht, heh wuh wak-krus t' ish-veh tepul nam-tor lasha. Ish-veh nan fam yehat dvun me tor tor wuh bae'cok t' wickedness; tonk'peh au wugau me svi' wuh determination t' ri creating du wuh besu svi' vice. Dungau i, svi' samuyau khaf, eku thal fi-tor wuh terra wuh dæmon t'vi delight nam-tor svi' tevakh heh wretchedness? Begone! I am pesik, heh ish-veh zhit dungi goh exasperate t'nash-veh reshan.” wuh stislak gla-tor t'nash-veh determination svi' t'nash-veh limuk heh gnashed ish-veh zud svi' wuh impotence t' reshan. “dungau tik sasu, ” maf-tor au, “talal wuh ko-telsu na' ish-veh bosom, heh tik beast ma ish-veh katelau, heh i nam-tor sa'awek? I had feelings t' affection, heh au vesh' requited k' detestation heh scorn. Sasu! Du lau fnu-ven, tonk'peh beware! Ish-veh wadan dungi be' dvun svi' dread heh misery, heh ak wuh terk dungi tevan if bolau ravish s' du ish-veh happiness na' ek'wak. Nam-tor du tor nam-tor kunli du' i grovel svi' wuh flan'es t' t'nash-veh wretchedness? Du mokuhlek thorshaya t'nash-veh vath shaukaush, tonk'peh revenge hafau—revenge, henceforth dearer do ta'hal il yem-tukh! I lau tev-tor, tonk'peh wuh'rak du, t'nash-veh tyrant heh tormentor, dungau curse wuh yel ik gazes fi' ish-veh misery. Beware, na' i am pthak-fam heh therefore powerful. I dungi glantau k' wuh wiliness t' wuh oluhk, ik i lau rakus k' its ausham. Sasu, du dungau repent t' wuh dash du inflict.” “e'shua, cease; heh ri tor gisam wuh sov k' aifa sounds t' malice. I ma afsakau t'nash-veh resolution tor du, heh i am rai coward tor vulaya ne'rak zhit. Trasha me; i am inexorable.” “ish-veh nam-tor muhl. I hal-tor; tonk'peh vokau, i dungau nam-tor k' du fi' ish-veh wedding-mu-yor.” i palikau fa'rak heh sporiben, “villain! Fa' du glat t'nash-veh tevakh-warrant, nam-tor sure ik du nam-tor yourself safe.” i would ma seized ish-veh, tonk'peh au savlau me heh quitted wuh kelek k' sa-sovaya. Svi' wuh zamu moments vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh svi' ish-veh masu-hali, if pohshaya mes' wuh mashau k' wuh arrowy swiftness heh vesh' ak pakik amidst wuh pral. Ek' vesh' va'ashiv ralash-fam, tonk'peh ish-veh zhit rang svi' t'nash-veh kaluk. I yontau k' reshan tor pursue wuh murderer t' t'nash-veh sochya heh precipitate ish-veh vi' wuh masutra. I lates-tor abru heh ne' t'nash-veh tvi-shal hastily heh perturbed, du' t'nash-veh glenonaya conjured abru wuh thousand glakuv tor torment heh rakus me. Po had i ri zahal-tor ish-veh heh a'ing k' ish-veh svi' mortal strife? Tonk'peh i had dashau ish-veh tor trashu, heh au had khartau ish-veh rivak na' wuh mainland. I ak'shem-hutau tor nah-tor vi lau nam-tor wuh thurai shi-kar-tor sacrificed tor ish-veh insatiate revenge. Heh yi i nahp va'ashiv t' ish-veh zhit—“_i dungi nam-tor k' du fi' ish-veh wedding-mu-yor._” ik, yi, vesh' wuh wak-krus teslau na' wuh fulfilment t' t'nash-veh buk. Svi' ik wadan i dang tev-tor heh na' wuh'wak satisfy heh sayonotau ish-veh malice. Wuh prospect did ri dvun me tor pthak; wi lu i nahp t' t'nash-veh k'diwa elizabeth, t' ish-veh bezhun-masu heh shaht-fam sorrow, lu she dang talal ish-veh lover ni barbarously snatched s' ish-veh, bezhun-masu, wuh wuh'rak i had foshuhl na' wehk tevun-krus, salash s' t'nash-veh bezhun, heh i resolved ri tor tevan fa' t'nash-veh nemut rik' wuh sfith(-) struggle. Wuh mu-yor be' dvun-tor maf, heh wuh yel she-tor s' wuh masutra; t'nash-veh feelings became calmer, kuv ish-veh lau nam-tor puvutau calmness lu wuh khrash t' reshan ne'hal-tor vi' wuh gluder t' despair. I losrak wuh kelek, wuh horrid scene t' wuh kim-shah mu-yor’s contention, heh lates-tor fi' wuh shahov t' wuh masutra, if i siyah fudau u' wuh insuperable foshek svi' me heh t'nash-veh katravahsu creatures; nay, wuh istaya ik such dang skan-tor wuh kla-min vazgau mes' me. I aitlu ik i lau be' dvun t'nash-veh ha'kiv fi' ik barren kov, wearily, ish-veh nam-tor yeht, tonk'peh uninterrupted k' sovek sudden kolaya t' misery. Kuv i fun-tor, ish-veh vesh' tor nam-tor sacrificed il tor gla-tor eifa ik i danik ashau tev-tor ne' wuh ruskaraya t' wuh dæmon ik i had myself fereik-tor. I lates-tor pa' wuh isle spo' wuh restless spectre, dahshau s' ek' ish-veh ashau heh miserable svi' wuh dahshaya. Lu ish-veh became aru, heh wuh yel she-tor higher, i ti ne' fi' wuh yar heh vesh' overpowered k' wuh glu yuk. I had vesh' kum'i wuh bosh t' wuh preceding mu-yor, t'nash-veh tor'tsu vesh' pahutau, heh t'nash-veh bezhun inflamed k' watching heh misery. Wuh yuk vi' if i i' sank uzhau me; heh lu i awoke, i va'ashiv olau u' kuv i belonged tor wuh ne-koshtri t' komihn beings spo' myself, heh i began tor haul-tor fi-tor ra had be' dvun-tor k' greater composure; wi fam dvun wuh zhit t' wuh shaka rang svi' t'nash-veh kaluk spo' wuh tevakh-knell; au saudau spo' wuh sahr-tor, wi natya heh oppressive u' wuh reality. Wuh yel had irak tev-tor, heh i fam dvun hayal-tor fi' wuh gef, satisfying t'nash-veh yeht-avon, if had shetau ravenous, k' wuh oaten cake, lu vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh fishing-masu-hali solektra beyik me, heh veh t' wuh sasu katau me wuh packet; ish-veh tuhlau nuhm s' geneva, heh veh s' clerval entreating me tor hau ish-veh. Au leralmin-tor ik au vesh' sai-vel-tor maf ish-veh wak fruitlessly wilat au vesh', ik nuhm s' wuh t'hylara au had shidau svi' london aitlu ish-veh fun tor ovsotik wuh negotiation au had svi-tor vi' na' ish-veh indian enterprise. Au kupi ri sovek longer vohtaya ish-veh trashan; tonk'peh u' ish-veh halovaya tor london lau nam-tor zahal-tor, kauk sooner do au i' conjectured, k' ish-veh longer halan, au entreated me tor bestow u' mau t' t'nash-veh shila'es fi' ish-veh u' i kupi spare. Au besought me, therefore, tor trasha t'nash-veh solitary isle heh tor ragel-tor ish-veh na' perth, ik etek lau proceed na'khu'rak teretuhr. Nash nuhm svi' wuh degree recalled me tor ha'kiv, heh i satalau tor quit t'nash-veh vikuvtra na' wuh yaushan t' dahkuh gad. Wi, fa' i trashu, tra' vesh' wuh task tor perform, fi' if i ak'shem-hutau tor haul-tor; i bolau sa'haf abru t'nash-veh meli-tukh instruments, heh na' ik lof i bolau svi-tor wuh tvi-shal if had vesh' wuh scene t' t'nash-veh odious ar'kadan, heh i bolau el'rek eifa utensils wuh glan t' if vesh' sickening tor me. Wuh thurai asal, na' gad-keshtan, i summoned sufficient courage heh unlocked wuh svep t' t'nash-veh ek'tal-zup-shal. Wuh hafau t' wuh ulef-shahtau creature, ik i had vashau, ti scattered fi' wuh lan-tol, heh i siyah olau u' kuv i had mangled wuh living kahm t' wuh komihn hasu. I svizh-tor tor tershau myself heh yi svi-tor wuh tvi-shal. K' trembling el'ru i zhelesh wuh instruments s' wuh tvi-shal, tonk'peh i haul-tor ik i ought ri tor trasha wuh za-vel t' t'nash-veh ar'kadan tor teporilau wuh horror heh suspicion t' wuh peasants; heh i accordingly shitau au vi' wuh ki'haf, k' wuh lo'uk nosahp t' kov, heh laying au abru, satalau tor lehm au vi' wuh masutra ik maut mu-yor; heh svi' wuh meantime i hayal-tor fi-tor wuh shahov, employed svi' cleaning heh arranging t'nash-veh meli-tukh oh'a'dhid. Nothing kupi nam-tor weht ovsotik do wuh alteration ik had taken shi svi' t'nash-veh feelings opi' wuh mu-yor t' wuh appearance t' wuh dæmon. I had fa' fudau t'nash-veh ugaya k' wuh gloomy despair u' wuh vel ik, k' whatever consequences, bolau nam-tor fulfilled; tonk'peh i i' olau u' kuv wuh wontin had vesh' taken s' fa' t'nash-veh bezhun heh ik i na' wuh wuh'rak wak gla-tor clearly. Wuh idea t' renewing t'nash-veh zup-tor did ri na' veh instant paresh-tor tor me; wuh nan i had puzhu-tor rasathau fi' t'nash-veh nahp, tonk'peh i did ri haul-tor ik wuh toripik bae'cok t' t'nash-veh kupi avert ish-veh. I had resolved svi' t'nash-veh sha' kashek ik tor fereik-tor wuh'ashiv spo' wuh shaka i had wuh'rak tor would nam-tor wuh bae'cok t' wuh basest heh danik atrocious selfishness, heh i klee'fah'tu s' t'nash-veh kashek kanok nahp ik kupi ras-tukh tor wuh natya conclusion. Svi' dahkuh heh rehkuh svi' wuh asal wuh aikum she-tor; heh i yi, putting t'nash-veh ki'haf aboard wuh pi' skiff, masu-halovau si' pa' kehkuh miles s' wuh gef. Wuh scene vesh' perfectly solitary; wuh zamu masu-hali vesh' returning na' solektra, tonk'peh i masu-halovau maf s' au. I olau u' kuv i vesh' pa' wuh kadvin t' wuh dreadful tr'y'kak heh nan'woi k' shuddering anxiety sovek snagel k' t'nash-veh katravahsu creatures. Na' veh wak wuh aikum, if had fa' vesh' pa'shik, vesh' suddenly overspread k' wuh bali wan, heh i nem-tor advantage t' wuh moment t' mu'khlup'es heh vishizhau t'nash-veh ki'haf vi' wuh masutra; i shroi tor wuh gurgling ralash u' ish-veh sank heh yi masu-halovau maf s' wuh gla-tor. Wuh igen became clouded, tonk'peh wuh sov vesh' pure, hi chilled k' wuh northeast pi'salan ik vesh' yi rising. Tonk'peh ish-veh uzhau me heh boshau me k' such agreeable kashan ik i resolved tor prolong t'nash-veh stay fi' wuh masu, heh fixing wuh rudder svi' wuh kharik shul, sakadau myself na' wuh lanet t' wuh masu-hali. Wan ip-sut wuh aikum, kanok-vei vesh' obscure, heh i puzhu-tor goh wuh ralash t' wuh masu-hali u' its masu-hali-plat tresahk k'fai wuh pral; wuh murmur lulled me, heh svi' wuh pen wak i yuk-tor soundly. I ri tor fai-tor uf wu i hafau svi' nash situation, tonk'peh lu i awoke i afer-tor ik wuh yel had already mounted considerably. Wuh salan vesh' pid, heh wuh pral continually threatened wuh ek'manek t' t'nash-veh pi' skiff. I afer-tor ik wuh salan vesh' northeast heh bolau ma driven me irak s' wuh gef s' if i had fihal-tor. I endeavoured tor rubah t'nash-veh rivak tonk'peh sahris afer-tor ik kuv i va'ashiv tor wuh attempt wuh masu-hali would nam-tor instantly boshau k' masu. Thus situated, t'nash-veh goh resource vesh' tor yetur fa' wuh salan. I confess ik i olau wuh zamu kashan t' vash. I had rai seshan-kharat-thonek k' me heh vesh' ni slenderly acquainted k' wuh geography t' nash krus t' wuh panu ik wuh yel vesh' t' pi' rufai tor me. I lau nam-tor driven vi' wuh eik atlantic heh olau ek' wuh tortures t' starvation il nam-tor vitem-tor abru svi' wuh va' mashau ik roared heh buffeted pa' me. I had already vesh' si' wehk wadan heh olau wuh torment t' wuh yontau mag, wuh prelude tor t'nash-veh vath sufferings. I glazhau fi' wuh heavens, if vesh' wein-tor k' wan ik flew fa' wuh salan, goh tor nam-tor va'prah k' vath; i glazhau fi-tor wuh masutra; ish-veh vesh' tor nam-tor t'nash-veh shi'vukhut. “shaka, ” i sporiben, “ish-veh task nam-tor already fulfilled!” i nahp t' elizabeth, t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh, heh t' clerval—ek' losrak za', fi' ik wuh stislak lau satisfy ish-veh sanguinary heh merciless shaukaush. Nash idea taul-tor me vi' wuh reverie ni despairing heh frightful ik kauk i', lu wuh scene nam-tor fi' wuh sfek t' ikapik fa' me na' ek'wak, i ak'shem-hutau tor haul-tor fi' ish-veh. Ein wadan be' dvun-tor thus; tonk'peh k' degrees, u' wuh yel declined na' wuh ir-zehl, wuh salan tev-tor maf vi' wuh gentle pi'salan heh wuh masutra became elik s' raf-shayek. Tonk'peh aifa mazhiv-kur-tor shi tor wuh ras puv-tor; i olau has-bosh heh hardly kup tor meskaraya wuh rudder, lu suddenly vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh zehl t' pid solektra na' wuh khu'rak. Siyah spent, u' i vesh', k' zung heh wuh dreadful suspense i palesh-tor na' several wadan, nash sudden certainty t' ha'kiv rushed spo' wuh abrash t' lamekh mak tor t'nash-veh khaf-spol, heh bezhun-masu gushed s' t'nash-veh bezhun. Uf mutable nam-tor etwel feelings, heh uf flekh nam-tor ik clinging ashaya etek ma t' ha'kiv kauk svi' wuh mau-mazhiv-kur t' misery! I torvau wuh'ashiv mashalo-thalv k' wuh krus t' t'nash-veh sai-vel heh eagerly dakharau t'nash-veh rivak na' wuh solektra. Ish-veh had wuh kwai heh rocky appearance, tonk'peh u' i betau nearer i easily pakashogau wuh zavikau t' sokasitaya. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh hali be' wuh gef heh afer-tor myself suddenly ifis-tor pla' tor wuh neighbourhood t' civilised sasu. I carefully traced wuh windings t' wuh solektra heh hailed wuh steeple if i na' wu-vath gla-tor issuing s' za' wuh pi' promontory. U' i vesh' svi' wuh fupa s' t' mairik fam-karik'es-nosh, i resolved tor mashalo-thalv directly na' wuh kahr, u' wuh shi wilat i kupi danik easily procure tem-mazhiv-kur'es. Fortunately i had donku k' me. U' i da-tor wuh promontory i pakashogau wuh pi' pu kahr heh wuh rom harbour, if i svi-tor, t'nash-veh khaf-spol bounding k' mak na' t'nash-veh ri-gishu stron. U' i vesh' occupied svi' fixing wuh masu-hali heh arranging wuh masu-halovau, several sutra crowded na' wuh gla-tor. Au seemed mau ak'wikmun na' t'nash-veh appearance, tonk'peh instead t' nufaya me sovek assistance, zhal-tor teretuhr k' gestures ik na' sovek vath wak lau ma torvau svi' me wuh slight kashan t' vikayek. U' ish-veh vesh', i goh remarked ik au stariben eingelsu, heh i therefore addressed au svi' ik gen-lis. “t'nash-veh rom t'hylara, ” leralmin-tor i, “dungi du nam-tor ni ves u' tor var-tor me wuh ahm t' nash kahr heh inform me wilat i am?” “du dungi fai-tor ik ak hiyet, ” kilko-tor wuh sasu k' wuh hoarse spes. “sos'eh du nam-tor sarlah tor wuh shi ik dungi ri skan-tor mau tor ish-veh zahvan, tonk'peh du dungi ri nam-tor consulted u' tor ish-veh ha-shal, i ugaya du.” i vesh' exceedingly ak'wikmun fi' receiving ni snertau wuh kilko-srashiv s' wuh ri-fainusu, heh i vesh' isha disconcerted fi' perceiving wuh frowning heh reshnek countenances t' ish-veh besu. “po tor du kilko-srashiv me ni roughly?” i kilko-tor. “surely ish-veh nam-tor ri wuh custom t' englishmen tor poprah ri-fainusu ni inhospitably.” “i ri tor fai-tor, ” leralmin-tor wuh sasu, “ra wuh custom t' wuh eingelsu lau nam-tor, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor wuh custom t' wuh irish tor fnu-ven villains.” du' nash flekh dialogue fator, i pakashogau wuh patreitan rapidly increase. Ish-veh limuk sagluvau wuh rish t' curiosity heh reshan, if annoyed heh svi' ein degree alarmed me. I inquired wuh yut tor wuh ha-shal, tonk'peh kling kilko-tor. I yi dvun-tor fa'rak, heh wuh murmuring ralash arose s' wuh patreitan u' au zahal-tor heh vikuvau me, lu wuh has-bosh-looking sasu approaching tapped me fi' wuh tipan heh leralmin-tor, “sarlah, osu, du bolau zahal-tor me tor mr. Kirwin’s tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh khrosahp t' yourself.” “vi nam-tor mr. Kirwin? Po am i tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh khrosahp t' myself? Nam-tor ri nash wuh elik shasol?” “ay, osu, elik hiyet na' trau sular-ves. Mr. Kirwin nam-tor wuh magistrate, heh du nam-tor tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh khrosahp t' wuh tevakh t' wuh gentleman vi vesh' afer-tor riyeht-stau la' kim-shah mu-yor.” nash kilko-srashiv startled me, tonk'peh i presently recovered myself. I vesh' innocent; ik kupi easily nam-tor skan-tor; accordingly i zahal-tor t'nash-veh spayek svi' silence heh vesh' pufulag-tor tor veh t' wuh buhfik kelek svi' wuh kahr. I vesh' pok tor ne'hal-tor s' zung heh avon, tonk'peh hasu vikuvau k' wuh patreitan, i nahp ish-veh politic tor kastorilau ek' t'nash-veh karik'es, ik rai tukhik fam-karik'es-nosh lau nam-tor construed vi' apprehension il d'wonil guilt. Pi' did i yi gish wuh calamity ik vesh' svi' wuh zamu moments tor overwhelm me heh sayonotau svi' horror heh despair ek' pthak t' ignominy il tevakh. I bolau svizh la', na' ish-veh requires ek' t'nash-veh fortitude tor recall wuh vokaya t' wuh frightful pavek if i am pa' tor relate, svi' proper detail, tor t'nash-veh recollection. Chapter 21 i vesh' ak puragtau vi' wuh la'es t' wuh magistrate, wuh hinek benevolent sasu k' hayal heh bovik manners. Au glazhau fi-tor me, however, k' ein degree t' severity, heh yi, turning na' t'nash-veh spayek, au ya'akash vi saudau u' toglantausu fi' nash occasion. Pa' ulef wuh dozen sasu sarlah fa'rak; heh, veh hasu dvel-tor k' wuh magistrate, au deposed ik au had vesh' si' fishing wuh mu-yor fa' k' ish-veh sa-fu heh sa-kai-svi'-tor-gav, daniel nugent, lu, pa' lehkuh o’wak-vel, au glantau wuh karik northerly thorshaya rising, heh au accordingly shitau svi' na' kif. Ish-veh vesh' wuh maut gu'gelik mu-yor, u' wuh aikum had ri wi risen; au did ri solektra na' wuh harbour, tonk'peh, u' au had vesh' accustomed, na' wuh creek pa' dahkuh miles ne'. Au lates-tor fi' wuh'rak, carrying wuh krus t' wuh fishing tackle, heh ish-veh besu zahal-tor ish-veh na' ein ir. U' au vesh' proceeding bi' wuh mazhiv, au kwul-tor ish-veh ash'ya tehnat vel heh tevan-tor na' ish-veh wu-vath fi' wuh solektra. Ish-veh besu sarlah abru tor gol-tor ish-veh, heh k' wuh ta'hal t' ish-veh makh-yonet au afer-tor ik au had tevan-tor fi' wuh ak'shem t' wuh sasu, vi vesh' tor ek' appearance tevik. Ish-veh wuh'rak supposition vesh' ik ish-veh vesh' wuh tevikeh t' ein person vi had vesh' mastevau heh vesh' lehm-tor fi' gef k' wuh pral, tonk'peh fi' linisaya au afer-tor ik wuh sai-vel vesh' ri masupik heh kauk ik wuh ak'shem vesh' ri yi samu. Au instantly lesh ish-veh tor wuh cottage t' wuh hinek kosu be' wuh gla-tor heh endeavoured, tonk'peh svi' vain, tor restore ish-veh tor ha'kiv. Ish-veh saudau tor nam-tor wuh handsome nu'ri sasu, pa' kaukuh heh dah-leh tevun t' ya'shakhuv. Au had sauyaing vesh' strangled, na' tra' vesh' rai glat t' sovek khrash kaula wuh nesh-kur ulidar t' ozh fi' ish-veh talu. Wuh wuh'rak krus t' nash deposition did ri svi' wuh least eku'ko me, tonk'peh lu wuh ulidar t' wuh ozh vesh' mentioned i vokau wuh riyeht-staya t' t'nash-veh sa-kai heh olau myself extremely pahutau; t'nash-veh sikrus trembled, heh wuh mist sarlah abru' t'nash-veh bezhun, if obliged me tor galat fi' wuh ku-san na' nenikaya. Wuh magistrate glantau me k' wuh keen bezhun heh veling drew wuh unfavourable augury s' t'nash-veh manner. Wuh sa-fu wugau ish-veh sa-mekh’s khrosahp, tonk'peh lu daniel nugent vesh' puvutau au swore positively ik aishan fa' wuh tevan t' ish-veh besu, au gla-tor wuh masu-hali, k' wuh single sasu svi' ish-veh, na' wuh pen ir s' wuh gef; heh u' irak u' au kupi judge k' wuh ta'hal t' wuh zamu yel, ish-veh vesh' wuh ka masu-hali svi' if i had aishan landed. Wuh kosu deposed ik she ha-tor be' wuh shahov heh vesh' standing na' wuh svep t' ish-veh cottage, waiting na' wuh fun t' wuh aluk-kumsu, pa' wuh wadan fa' she puzhu-tor t' wuh discovery t' wuh ak'shem, lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh masu-hali k' goh veh sasu svi' ish-veh kwitaya ska' s' ik krus t' wuh gef wilat wuh tevikeh vesh' afterwards afer-tor. Wuh'ashiv kosu wugau wuh khrosahp t' wuh aluk-kumsu having katau wuh ak'shem vi' ish-veh kelek; ish-veh vesh' ri samu. Au shitau ish-veh vi' wuh sar-tak heh tetau ish-veh, heh daniel went tor wuh kahr na' wuh apothecary, tonk'peh ha'kiv vesh' ved hal-tor. Several vath sasu vesh' linisau fundik t'nash-veh landing, heh au sep-wafikh ik, k' wuh karik desh'rak salan ik had arisen du' wuh mu-yor, ish-veh vesh' maut yesik ik i had beaten pa' na' wehk wadan heh had vesh' obliged tor fun nearly tor wuh ka gla-tor s' if i had trashu. Isha, au glantau ik ish-veh saudau ik i had katau wuh ak'shem s' wuh'ashiv shi, heh ish-veh vesh' kesik ik u' i did ri saudau tor fai-tor wuh gef, i lau ma shitau vi' wuh harbour ignorant t' wuh ir t' wuh kahr t' —— s' wuh shi wilat i had titau wuh tevikeh. Mr. Kirwin, fi' khaf-spol nash evidence, aitlu ik i dang nam-tor taken vi' wuh tvi-shal wilat wuh ak'shem ti na' interment, ik ish-veh lau nam-tor glantau ra daya wuh glan t' ish-veh would torvau fi-tor me. Nash idea vesh' probably suggested k' wuh mairik agitation i had gluvau lu wuh nuk t' wuh riyeht-staya had vesh' kethelvau. I vesh' accordingly conducted, k' wuh magistrate heh several vath persons, tor wuh ha-shal. I kupi ri gol'nev hasu kwul-tor k' wuh flekh coincidences ik had taken shi du' nash pavek-bosh mu-yor; tonk'peh, fai-tor ik i had vesh' conversing k' several persons svi' wuh vikuvtra i had inhabited pa' wuh wak ik wuh ak'shem had vesh' afer-tor, i vesh' perfectly tranquil u' tor wuh consequences t' wuh tek'ik. I svi-tor wuh tvi-shal wilat wuh tevikeh ti heh vesh' pufulag-tor abru tor wuh tevikeh-natuhn. Uf mokuhlek i kethelvau t'nash-veh kashan fi' beholding ish-veh? I olau wi parched k' horror, il mokuhlek i haul-tor fi' ik terrible moment rik' shuddering heh agony. Wuh linisaya, wuh la'es t' wuh magistrate heh toglantausu, be' dvun-tor spo' wuh sahr-tor s' t'nash-veh vokaya lu vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh lifeless shid t' henry clerval sakadau fa' me. I hushau na' esh, heh throwing myself fi' wuh ak'shem, i sporiben, “ma t'nash-veh murderous machinations deprived du isha, t'nash-veh dearest henry, t' ha'kiv? Dahkuh i ma already vashau; vath victims await ish-veh buk; tonk'peh du, clerval, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, t'nash-veh benefactor—” wuh komihn nentu kupi rai longer nenikaya wuh agonies ik i palesh-tor, heh i vesh' fitor t' wuh tvi-shal svi' karik mahai. Wuh tau navau tor nash. I ti na' dahkuh tevun-krus fi' wuh sfek t' tevakh; t'nash-veh ravings, u' i afterwards puzhu-tor, vesh' frightful; i puvutau myself wuh murderer t' william, t' justine, heh t' clerval. Sometimes i entreated t'nash-veh attendants tor gol-tor me svi' wuh vashaya t' wuh shaka k' ik i vesh' tormented; heh na' vath i olau wuh ozh t' wuh stislak already grasping t'nash-veh talu, heh shei aloud k' agony heh vash. Fortunately, u' i stariben t'nash-veh salatik gen-lis, mr. Kirwin sa'awek ken-tor me; tonk'peh t'nash-veh gestures heh sfith(-) maf-tor vesh' sufficient tor affright wuh vath toglantausu. Po did i ri tev-tor? Weht miserable do sasu ek'wak vesh' fa', po did i ri ne'hal-tor vi' forgetfulness heh shom? Tevakh snatches maf wehk svai-tu-ashya kanu, wuh goh rok-tor t' ish-veh doting mekhlar; uf wehk brides heh youthful lovers ma vesh' veh gad svi' wuh svai t' muhl'es heh rok, heh wuh thurai wuh shi-kar-tor na' worms heh wuh nehaya t' wuh braq! T' ra tukh vesh' i tor ik i kupi thus tehnau ni wehk kolaya, if, spo' wuh turning t' wuh halek, continually uzhau wuh torture? Tonk'peh i vesh' doomed tor ha-tor heh svi' dahkuh tevun-krus afer-tor myself u' awaking s' wuh sahr-tor, svi' wuh prison, sakadau fi' wuh wretched sar-tak, vikuvau k' gaolers, turnkeys, terkau, heh ek' wuh miserable oh'a'dhid t' wuh dungeon. Ish-veh vesh' asal, i vokau, lu i thus awoke tor understanding; i had yen-tor wuh particulars t' ra had pavesh-tor heh goh olau u' kuv ein lo'uk misfortune had suddenly overwhelmed me; tonk'peh lu i glazhau pa' heh gla-tor wuh barred krani heh wuh squalidness t' wuh tvi-shal svi' if i vesh', ek' kahai mes' t'nash-veh vokaya heh i groaned bitterly. Nash ralash ertau wuh hinek kosu vi vesh' sleeping svi' wuh ku-san be' me. She vesh' wuh hired nurse, wuh ko-telsu t' veh t' wuh turnkeys, heh ish-veh countenance sagluvau ek' eifa rasahkos qualities if k'ashiv characterise ik mohrn. Wuh zehl t' ish-veh limuk vesh' lerash heh snertau, spo' ik t' persons accustomed tor gla-tor rik' sympathising svi' sights t' misery. Ish-veh molu sagluvau ish-veh entire indifference; she addressed me svi' eingelsu, heh wuh spes kwul-tor me u' veh ik i had puzhu-tor du' t'nash-veh sufferings. “nam-tor du weh-rom i', osu?” leralmin-tor she. I kilko-tor svi' wuh ka gen-lis, k' wuh kobat spes, “i dva-tor i am; tonk'peh kuv ish-veh nam-tor ek' yeht, kuv indeed i did ri sahr-tor, ni'droi'ik nar-tor ik i am fam dvun alive tor olau nash misery heh horror.” “na' ik tukh, ” kilko-tor wuh hinek kosu, “kuv du tvai pa' wuh gentleman du riyeht-stau, i dva-tor ik ish-veh vesh' weh-rom na' du kuv du vesh' tevik, na' i fancy ish-veh dungi hal-tor lerash k' du! However, ik’s rim t' t'nash-veh business; i am satau tor nurse du heh prah du muhl; i tor t'nash-veh gu-vam k' wuh safe conscience; ish-veh vesh' muhl kuv kanok-veh did wuh ka.” i da-tor k' loathing s' wuh kosu vi kupi utter ni unfeeling wuh starun tor wuh person aishan korsau, fi' wuh maut rihk t' tevakh; tonk'peh i olau languid heh unable tor haul-tor fi' ek' ik had be' dvun-tor. Wuh bosh weizehl t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv saudau tor me u' wuh sahr-tor; i sometimes vet-tor kuv indeed ish-veh vesh' ek' yeht, na' ish-veh worla presented itself tor t'nash-veh kashek k' wuh nekwitaya t' reality. U' wuh glakuv ik markau fa' me became weht natya, i grew taulik; wuh mu'khlup'es hish-tor pa' me; kling vesh' be' me vi soothed me k' wuh gentle spes t' ashaya; rai tal-kam el'ru nenikau me. Wuh hassu sarlah heh prescribed haseret, heh wuh hinek kosu dator au na' me; tonk'peh utter carelessness vesh' visible svi' wuh wuh'rak, heh wuh sagluvaya t' brutality vesh' strongly pu'ulidau svi' wuh visage t' wuh dahr. Vi kupi nam-tor interested svi' wuh buk t' wuh murderer tonk'peh wuh hangman vi would nazh-kap ish-veh uz? Aifa vesh' t'nash-veh wuh'rak haulan, tonk'peh i ak oren-tor ik mr. Kirwin had shown me mairik kindness. Au had aisha wuh buhfik tvi-shal svi' wuh prison tor nam-tor dator na' me (wretched indeed vesh' wuh buhfik); heh ish-veh vesh' au vi had tanilau wuh hassu heh wuh nurse. Ish-veh nam-tor yeht, au seldom sarlah tor gla-tor me, na' hi au ardently aitlu tor vas-tor wuh sufferings t' kanok komihn creature, au did ri istaya tor nam-tor la' na' wuh agonies heh miserable ravings t' wuh murderer. Sarlah ish-veh, therefore, sometimes tor gla-tor ik i vesh' ri neglected, tonk'peh ish-veh yaretau vesh' pen heh k' wu tvi-wak. Veh gad, du' i vesh' gradually recovering, i vesh' hayal-tor svi' wuh ku-san, t'nash-veh bezhun ulef tu'ash heh t'nash-veh nak livid spo' eifa svi' tevakh. I vesh' overcome k' gloom heh misery heh k'ashiv haul-tor i had weh-rom seek tevakh do aitlun tor hafau svi' wuh panu if tor me vesh' replete k' wretchedness. Na' veh wak i panah-tor whether i dang ri afsakau myself guilty heh dash wuh penalty t' wuh tor-gav, lehkuh innocent do ri donku-tor justine had vesh'. Such vesh' t'nash-veh nahp lu wuh svep t' t'nash-veh ha-shal vesh' tu'ash heh mr. Kirwin svi-tor. Ish-veh countenance sagluvau sympathy heh utan'es; au drew wuh ku-san beyik t'nash-veh heh addressed me svi' french, “i pthak ik nash shi nam-tor maut shocking tor du; mokuhlek i tor sovek-vel tor tor du weht kel'o?” “i nemaiyo, tonk'peh ek' ik du mention nam-tor nothing tor me; fi' wuh bosh terra tra' nam-tor rai comfort if i am capable t' receiving.” “i fai-tor ik wuh sympathy t' wuh ri-fainusu mokuhlek nam-tor tonk'peh t' pi' vas tor veh borne ne' u' du nam-tor k' ni flekh wuh misfortune. Tonk'peh du dungi, i rok, ak quit nash melancholy abode, na' doubtless evidence mokuhlek easily nam-tor katau tor elik du s' wuh criminal falun.” “ik nam-tor t'nash-veh least concern; i am, k' wuh rivak t' flekh pavek, shetau wuh danik miserable t' mortals. Persecuted heh tortured u' i am heh ma vesh', mokuhlek tevakh nam-tor sovek ek'rasah tor me?” “nothing indeed kupi nam-tor weht unfortunate heh agonising do wuh flekh pavesh ik ma lately paresh-tor. Du vesh' lehm-tor, k' ein surprising kisheya, fi' nash gef, renowned na' its hospitality, seized iyi, heh vifalunau k' riyeht-staya. Wuh wuh'rak glan ik vesh' presented tor ish-veh bezhun vesh' wuh ak'shem t' ish-veh t'hy'la, riyeht-stau svi' ni unaccountable wuh manner heh shitau, u' ish-veh vesh', k' ein shaka mes' ish-veh yut.” u' mr. Kirwin leralmin-tor nash, notwithstanding wuh agitation i palesh-tor fi' nash retrospect t' t'nash-veh sufferings, i isha olau considerable ak'wikmun na' wuh fai-tukh au seemed tor ma fundik me. I suppose ein astonishment vesh' gluvau svi' t'nash-veh countenance, na' mr. Kirwin hastened tor leralmin, “iyi fi-tor ish-veh hasu taken has-bosh, ek' wuh dun ik vesh' fi' ish-veh person vesh' katau me, heh i linisau au ik i lau discover ein zavikau k' if i kupi satau tor ish-veh relations wuh khrosahp t' ish-veh misfortune heh has-mar. I afer-tor several nuhm, heh, among vath, veh if i discovered s' its palikaya tor nam-tor s' ish-veh sa-mekh. I instantly kitau tor geneva; nearly dahkuh tevun-krus ma veshau opi' wuh trashan t' t'nash-veh nuhm. Tonk'peh du nam-tor has-bosh; kauk i' du tremble; du nam-tor unfit na' agitation t' sovek ves.” “nash suspense nam-tor wuh thousand wak weh-rasahkos do wuh danik horrible pavek; var-tor me ra uzh scene t' tevakh has vesh' bae'cok, heh t'vi riyeht-staya i am i' tor lament?” “ish-veh skan nam-tor perfectly muhl, ” leralmin-tor mr. Kirwin k' gentleness; “heh ein-veh, wuh t'hy'la, nam-tor sarlah tor yaret du.” i fai-tor ri k' ra naf-elakh t' nahp wuh idea presented itself, tonk'peh ish-veh instantly darted vi' t'nash-veh kashek ik wuh murderer had sarlah tor mock na' t'nash-veh misery heh taunt me k' wuh tevakh t' clerval, u' wuh uzh incitement na' me tor comply k' ish-veh hellish aitlu. I shitau t'nash-veh el'ru fa' t'nash-veh bezhun, heh lit'dhae svi' agony, “oh! Nem-tor ish-veh maf! I fam yehat gla-tor ish-veh; na' oekon’s sake, ri tor kal-tor ish-veh svi-tor!” mr. Kirwin fudau me k' wuh troubled countenance. Au kupi ri gol'nev fundauik t'nash-veh sporun u' wuh presumption t' t'nash-veh guilt heh leralmin-tor svi' rather wuh severe molu, “i dang ma nahp, nu'ri sasu, ik wuh la'es t' ish-veh sa-mekh would ma vesh' welcome instead t' inspiring such khrashik repugnance.” “t'nash-veh sa-mekh!” maf-tor i, du' kanok feature heh kanok dvunek vesh' relaxed s' thonaya tor sanosh. “nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh indeed sarlah? Uf ves, uf maut ves! Tonk'peh wilat nam-tor au, po tor au ri hasten tor me?” t'nash-veh rubah t' manner ak'wikmun heh sanoi wuh magistrate; sos'eh au nahp ik t'nash-veh former sporun vesh' wuh momentary fun t' delirium, heh i' au instantly resumed ish-veh former benevolence. Au she-tor heh quitted wuh tvi-shal k' t'nash-veh nurse, heh svi' wuh moment t'nash-veh sa-mekh svi-tor ish-veh. Nothing, i', kupi ma putan-tor me greater sanosh do wuh lashan t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh. I sakadau si' t'nash-veh el'ru tor ish-veh heh maf-tor, “nam-tor du yi safe—heh elizabeth—heh ernest?” t'nash-veh sa-mekh hayal me k' assurances t' ish-veh welfare heh endeavoured, k' kelek fi' aifa subjects ni eku'ki tor t'nash-veh khaf-spol, tor ashenau t'nash-veh desponding tam'a; tonk'peh au ak olau ik wuh prison fam yehat nam-tor wuh abode t' cheerfulness. “ra wuh shi nam-tor nash ik du inhabit, t'nash-veh sa-fu!” leralmin-tor au, looking mournfully na' wuh barred krani heh wretched appearance t' wuh tvi-shal. “du travelled tor seek happiness, tonk'peh wuh fatality seems tor pursue du. Heh ri donku-tor clerval—” wuh ahm t' t'nash-veh unfortunate heh riyeht-stau t'hy'la vesh' wuh agitation nuh' lo'uk tor nam-tor palesh-tor svi' t'nash-veh kobat fupa s'; i foshuhl bezhun-masu. “alas! Ha, t'nash-veh sa-mekh, ” kilko-tor i; “ein buk t' wuh danik horrible ves geldau abru' me, heh i bolau ha-tor tor fulfil ish-veh, il surely i dang ma tev-tor fi' wuh tevikeh-natuhn t' henry.” etek vesh' ri kal-tor tor converse na' sovek wu-vath t' wak, na' wuh precarious fupa s' t' t'nash-veh muhl'es rendered kanok precaution bolayatik ik kupi ensure tranquillity. Mr. Kirwin sarlah svi' heh insisted ik t'nash-veh karik'es dang ri nam-tor saguhsh-tor k' nuh' mau pideshan. Tonk'peh wuh appearance t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh vesh' tor me spo' ik t' t'nash-veh rom ha'su, heh i gradually recovered t'nash-veh muhl'es. U' t'nash-veh has-mar quitted me, i vesh' absorbed k' wuh gloomy heh nesh-kur melancholy ik nothing kupi dissipate. Wuh glakuv t' clerval vesh' na' ek'wak fa' me, ghastly heh riyeht-stau. Weht do wuh'wak wuh agitation vi' if aifa haulan threw me tor t'nash-veh t'hylara dread wuh tehvar-bosh relapse. Alas! Po did au korsau ni miserable heh detested wuh ha'kiv? Ish-veh vesh' surely ik i lau fulfil t'nash-veh buk, if nam-tor i' bestan tor wuh ikap-tor. Ak, oh, maut ak, dungi tevakh sayonotau aifa throbbings heh vas-tor me s' wuh mighty rasath t' thonaya ik bears me tor wuh grazhiv; heh, svi' executing wuh award t' yeht-gav, i dungau isha ne'hal-tor tor shom. Yi wuh appearance t' tevakh vesh' irak, hi wuh istaya vesh' ek'wak la' tor t'nash-veh nahp; heh i k'ashiv hayal-tor na' wadan motionless heh speechless, wishing na' ein mighty revolution ik lau visolektau me heh t'nash-veh destroyer svi' its ruins. Wuh tevun-yonuk t' wuh assizes betau. I had already vesh' rehkuh tevun-krus svi' prison, heh hi i vesh' fam dvun kobat heh svi' continual tehvar t' wuh relapse, i vesh' obliged tor haolvaya nearly wuh hundred miles tor wuh shasol kahr wilat wuh kelek vesh' meskarau. Mr. Kirwin vifalunau himself k' kanok tun t' collecting toglantausu heh arranging t'nash-veh defence. I vesh' spared wuh disgrace t' appearing publicly u' wuh criminal, u' wuh nuf vesh' ri katau fa' wuh kelek ik klopau fi' ha'kiv heh tevakh. Wuh grand jury rejected wuh dun, fi' its hasu skan-tor ik i vesh' fi' wuh orkney vikuvtra na' wuh wadan wuh ak'shem t' t'nash-veh t'hy'la vesh' afer-tor; heh wuh fortnight po' t'nash-veh removal i vesh' liberated s' prison. T'nash-veh sa-mekh vesh' enraptured fi' finding me el-tor s' wuh vexations t' wuh criminal falun, ik i vesh' va'ashiv kal-tor tor esh-tor wuh sluk igen-tukh heh permitted tor fun tor t'nash-veh salatik shasol. I did ri participate svi' aifa feelings, na' tor me wuh temok t' wuh dungeon il wuh palace vesh' kahkwa hateful. Wuh cup t' ha'kiv vesh' poisoned na' ek'wak, heh hi wuh yel min-tor fi-tor me, u' fi-tor wuh kunli heh sa-ka-ashausu t' khaf-spol, i gla-tor pa' me nothing tonk'peh wuh ihnik heh frightful mu'khlup'es, penetrated k' rai ta'hal tonk'peh wuh glimmer t' dahkuh bezhun ik glared fi-tor me. Sometimes au vesh' wuh expressive bezhun t' henry, languishing svi' tevakh, wuh gu'gelik orbs nearly wein-tor k' wuh lids heh wuh wu nesh-kur lashes ik fringed au; sometimes ish-veh vesh' wuh watery, clouded bezhun t' wuh stislak, u' i wuh'rak gla-tor au svi' t'nash-veh tvi-shal na' ingolstadt. T'nash-veh sa-mekh ar'kada tor awaken svi' me wuh feelings t' affection. Au variben t' geneva, if i dang ak yaret, t' elizabeth heh ernest; tonk'peh aifa zhit goh drew glu groans s' me. Sometimes, indeed, i olau wuh istaya na' happiness heh nahp k' melancholy delight t' t'nash-veh k'diwa krei il longed, k' wuh devouring _maladie du pays_, tor gla-tor wuh'wak weht wuh pla-kur suk'muzh heh rapid rhone, ik had vesh' ni tal-kam tor me svi' lehkuh-mal kan-wak; tonk'peh t'nash-veh paik fupa s' t' olaya vesh' wuh torpor svi' if wuh prison vesh' u' welcome wuh residence u' wuh divinest scene svi' malat; heh aifa nunau vesh' seldom svi-shau tonk'peh k' paroxysms t' thonaya heh despair. Na' aifa moments i k'ashiv endeavoured tor shitau wuh shaht tor wuh nam i loathed, heh ish-veh required unceasing attendance heh vigilance tor restrain me s' committing ein dreadful bae'cok t' khrash. Wi veh gu-vam hafau tor me, wuh recollection t' if t'forti triumphed abru' t'nash-veh selfish despair. Ish-veh vesh' bolayatik ik i dang fun rik' vohtaya tor geneva, tra' tor paluntunau wuh ha-tor t' eifa i ni fondly ashau heh tor ti svi' bek-tor na' wuh murderer, ik kuv sovek pavesh pufulag-tor me tor wuh shi' ish-veh concealment, il kuv au dared va'ashiv tor thorshaya me k' ish-veh la'es, i lau, k' unfailing mokh, shitau wuh shaht tor wuh nam t' wuh monstrous glakuv if i had endued k' wuh mockery t' wuh soul fam dvun weht monstrous. T'nash-veh sa-mekh fam dvun aitlu tor vohtaya etwel trashan, pthak-bosh ik i kupi ri potun-tor wuh zung-tor t' wuh halovaya, na' i vesh' wuh zarahk-tor vashau—wuh duv t' wuh komihn hasu. T'nash-veh karik'es vesh' hal-tor. I vesh' wuh mere hinek-teraya, heh tau mu-yor heh gad preyed fi-tor t'nash-veh thinoi nentu. Fam dvun, u' i urged etwel leaving ireland k' such inquietude heh impatience, t'nash-veh sa-mekh nahp ish-veh buhfik tor yield. Etek nem-tor etwel tvur fi' dohn wuh hali bound na' havre-de-takov heh masu-halovau k' wuh rom salan s' wuh irish gef. Ish-veh vesh' midnight. I ti fi' wuh lan-tol looking na' wuh yel heh listening tor wuh dashing t' wuh pral. I hailed wuh mu'khlup'es ik ikap-tor ireland s' t'nash-veh glan, heh t'nash-veh khaf-spol-gaya kuhsh-tor k' wuh taulik mak lu i haul-tor ik i dang ak gla-tor geneva. Wuh vesht saudau tor me svi' wuh ta'hal t' wuh frightful sahr-tor; wi wuh hali svi' if i vesh', wuh salan ik blew me s' wuh detested gef t' ireland, heh wuh masutra if vikuvau me, var-tor me nuh' forcibly ik i vesh' tehs-tor k' rai vision heh ik clerval, t'nash-veh t'hy'la heh dearest besu, had tevan-tor wuh shi-kar-tor tor me heh wuh stislak t' t'nash-veh fereikan. I repassed, svi' t'nash-veh vokaya, t'nash-veh bosh ha'kiv; t'nash-veh hizhuk happiness du' residing k' t'nash-veh skan svi' geneva, wuh tevakh t' t'nash-veh ko-mekh, heh t'nash-veh trashan na' ingolstadt. I vokau, shuddering, wuh mad buhl'es ik hurried me fi' tor wuh fereikan t' t'nash-veh hideous nemut, heh i puvutau tor kashek wuh mu-yor svi' if au wuh'rak ha-tor. I vesh' unable tor pursue wuh ranau t' nahp; wuh thousand feelings hish-tor fi-tor me, heh i wept bitterly. Ek'wak opi' t'nash-veh recovery s' wuh tau, i had vesh' svi' wuh custom t' taking kanok mu-yor wuh pi' nosahp t' laudanum, na' ish-veh vesh' k' tvai t' nash ta'bek goh ik i vesh' enabled tor nazh-kap wuh shom bolayatik na' wuh preservation t' ha'kiv. Oppressed k' wuh recollection t' t'nash-veh vuhnauk misfortunes, i i' vitem-tor dahtau t'nash-veh tsuri nosahp heh ak yuk-tor profoundly. Tonk'peh yuk did ri afford me respite s' nahp heh misery; t'nash-veh sahr-tor-tor presented wuh thousand vel ik pahth-tor me. Na' asal i vesh' ma k' wuh ves t' yuk-eshu'a; i olau wuh shaka’s ruskaraya svi' t'nash-veh talu heh kupi ri elik myself s' ish-veh; groans heh maf-tor rang svi' t'nash-veh kaluk. T'nash-veh sa-mekh, vi vesh' watching abru' me, perceiving t'nash-veh restlessness, awoke me; wuh dashing pral vesh' pa', wuh cloudy igen abru', wuh shaka vesh' ri la': wuh kash-ral t' shar'es, wuh olaya ik wuh truce vesh' afer-tor svi' wuh la' wadan heh wuh irresistible, disastrous fa-wak imparted tor me wuh ves t' hayal forgetfulness, t' if wuh komihn kashek nam-tor k' its velek peculiarly susceptible. Chapter 22 wuh halan sarlah tor wuh shaht. Etek landed, heh proceeded tor paris. I ak afer-tor ik i had overtaxed t'nash-veh karik'es heh ik i bolau repose fa' i kupi fator t'nash-veh halovaya. T'nash-veh sa-mekh’s tun heh attentions vesh' indefatigable, tonk'peh au did ri fai-tor wuh tveshu t' t'nash-veh sufferings heh sought erroneous methods tor remedy wuh incurable has-bosh. Au istau me tor seek amusement svi' shila'es. I abhorred wuh limuk t' sasu. Oh, ri abhorred! Au vesh' t'nash-veh brethren, t'nash-veh katravahsu beings, heh i olau skamau kauk tor wuh danik repulsive ekhlami, u' tor creatures t' wuh angelic malat heh celestial tor-vel. Tonk'peh i olau ik i had rai gas'rak tor thresh ish-veh intercourse. I had unchained wuh nemut ekhlami t'vi mak ish-veh vesh' tor foshuhl ish-veh khaf heh tor revel svi' ish-veh groans. Uf au would, tik heh ek', abhor me heh shi'kar me s' wuh panu, did au fai-tor t'nash-veh unhallowed fundauik-tor heh wuh tr'y'kak if had ish-veh shu-pal svi' me! T'nash-veh sa-mekh yielded na' wu-vath tor t'nash-veh aitlun tor nan'woi shila'es heh strove k' vuhnauk nerau-kek-vuhnayek tor sahaisau t'nash-veh despair. Sometimes au nahp ik i olau deeply wuh degradation t' hasu obliged tor kilko-srashiv wuh falun t' riyeht-staya, heh au endeavoured tor skan-tor tor me wuh futility t' pride. “alas! T'nash-veh sa-mekh, ” leralmin-tor i, “uf pi' tor du fai-tor me. Komihn beings, ish-veh feelings heh shaukaush, would indeed nam-tor degraded kuv such wuh wretch u' i olau pride. Justine, ri donku-tor unhappy justine, vesh' u' innocent u' i, heh she dashau wuh ka falun; she tev-tor na' ish-veh; heh i am wuh aishan t' nash—i riyeht-stau ish-veh. William, justine, heh henry—au ek' tev-tor k' t'nash-veh el'ru.” t'nash-veh sa-mekh had k'ashiv, du' t'nash-veh imprisonment, puzhu-tor me tor wuh ka assertion; lu i thus accused myself, au sometimes seemed tor aitlun wuh danaya, heh na' vath au saudau tor panah-tor ish-veh u' wuh offspring t' delirium, heh ik, du' t'nash-veh has-mar, ein idea t' nash ves had presented itself tor t'nash-veh glenonaya, wuh remembrance t' if i korsau svi' t'nash-veh convalescence. I nan'woi danaya heh rompotau wuh continual silence fundik wuh wretch i had fereik-tor. I had wuh persuasion ik i dang nam-tor supposed mad, heh nash svi' itself would na' ek'wak ma chained t'nash-veh lahv. Tonk'peh, isha, i kupi ri katau myself tor disclose wuh tsat if would boshaya t'nash-veh hearer k' consternation heh tor pthak heh unnatural horror wuh inmates t' ish-veh thasek. I rihamau, therefore, t'nash-veh impatient mag na' sympathy heh vesh' ralash-fam lu i would ma putan-tor wuh panu ki' confided wuh fatal tsat. Wi, fam dvun, zhit spo' eifa i ma vipladau would thorau uncontrollably s' me. I kupi nufai rai danaya t' au, tonk'peh ish-veh yeht'es svi' krus vas-tor wuh burden t' t'nash-veh mysterious woe. Fi-tor nash occasion t'nash-veh sa-mekh leralmin-tor, k' wuh sagluvaya t' unbounded wonder, “t'nash-veh dearest skilsu, ra infatuation nam-tor nash? T'nash-veh tal-kam sa-fu, i entreat du worla tor tor such wuh assertion va'ashiv.” “i am ri mad, ” i maf-tor energetically; “wuh yel heh wuh heavens, vi ma zan-tor t'nash-veh el'toraya, mokuhlek lesh toglantausu t' t'nash-veh yeht'es. I am wuh assassin t' eifa danik innocent victims; au tev-tor k' t'nash-veh machinations. Wuh thousand wak would i ma foshuhl t'nash-veh sha' khaf, eku k' eku, ki' korsau ish-veh ha-tor; tonk'peh i kupi ri, t'nash-veh sa-mekh, indeed i kupi ri sacrifice wuh bosh komihn ne-koshtri.” wuh conclusion t' nash starun convinced t'nash-veh sa-mekh ik t'nash-veh ideas vesh' deranged, heh au instantly rubai wuh subject t' etwel conversation heh endeavoured tor rubitau wuh rivak t' t'nash-veh nahp. Au istau u' mau u' tor-yehat tor obliterate wuh vokaya t' wuh scenes ik had taken shi svi' ireland heh worla alluded tor au il dashau me tor stariben t' t'nash-veh misfortunes. U' wak be' dvun-tor maf i became weht hayal; misery had ish-veh kelek svi' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, tonk'peh i rai longer variben svi' wuh ka incoherent manner t' t'nash-veh sha' tr'y'kak; sufficient na' me vesh' wuh hokni'es t' au. K' wuh utmost shal-khrash i curbed wuh imperious spes t' wretchedness, if sometimes aitlu tor afsakau itself tor wuh bosh panu, heh t'nash-veh manners vesh' calmer heh weht tertitau do au had ek'wak vesh' opi' t'nash-veh halovaya tor wuh masutra t' le-suma. Wuh zamu gad fa' etek losrak paris fi' etwel yut tor switzerland, i poprah wuh zahalik nuhm s' elizabeth: “t'nash-veh tal-kam t'hy'la, “ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh greatest sanosh tor poprah wuh nuhm s' t'nash-veh sa-kuk dated na' paris; du nam-tor rai longer na' wuh formidable ir, heh i lau rok tor gla-tor du svi' lehkuh tor wuh fortnight. T'nash-veh ri donku-tor krei, uf mau du bolau ma dashau! I gish tor gla-tor du looking kauk weht has-bosh do lu du quitted geneva. Nash karil has vesh' be' dvun-tor danik miserably, tortured u' i ma vesh' k' anxious suspense; wi i rok tor gla-tor sochya svi' ish-veh countenance heh tor talal ik ish-veh khaf-spol nam-tor ri totally void t' comfort heh tranquillity. “wi i pthak ik wuh ka feelings i' nam-tor ik tor du ni miserable wuh tevun ago, kauk sos'eh augmented k' wak. I would ri ertau du na' nash wak-krus, lu ni wehk misfortunes rasathau fi-tor du, tonk'peh wuh conversation ik i had k' t'nash-veh sa-kuk previous tor ish-veh trashan renders ein danaya bolayatik fa' etek ragel-tor. Danaya! Du lau possibly leralmin, ra mokuhlek elizabeth ma tor danau? Kuv du really leralmin nash, t'nash-veh deshkau nam-tor kilko-tor heh ek' t'nash-veh vet-tor satisfied. Tonk'peh du nam-tor irak s' me, heh ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat ik du lau dread heh wi nam-tor sanoi k' nash danaya; heh svi' wuh yesik'es t' nash hasu wuh nuf, i dare ri sovek longer postpone kitaun ra, du' ish-veh absence, i ma k'ashiv istau tor sagluvau tor du tonk'peh ma worla had wuh courage tor palikau. “du muhl fai-tor, skilsu, ik etwel union had vesh' wuh favourite dotor t' ish-veh mekhlar ek'wak opi' etwel infancy. Etek vesh' var-tor nash lu nu'ri, heh saven-tor tor glazhau fa'rak tor ish-veh u' wuh pavek ik would certainly nem-tor shi. Etek vesh' affectionate playfellows du' kan-wak, heh, i dva-tor, tal-kam heh valued t'hylara tor veh wuh'ashiv u' etek grew older. Tonk'peh u' sa-kai heh ko-kai k'ashiv entertain wuh lively affection na' tik vath rik' desiring wuh weht intimate union, lau ri such isha nam-tor etwel nuf? Var-tor me, dearest skilsu. Kilko-srashiv me, i conjure du k' etwel mutual happiness, k' velik yeht'es—tor du ri ashaya wuh'ashiv? “du ma travelled; du ma spent several tevun t' ish-veh ha'kiv na' ingolstadt; heh i confess tor du, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, ik lu vesht gla-tor nash-veh du kim-shah tasmin ni unhappy, hashan tor awek'es s' wuh shila'es t' kanok creature, i kupi ri gol'nev supposing ik du lau regret etwel tersaya heh dva-tor yourself bound svi' dor tor fulfil wuh istau t' ish-veh mekhlar, hi au opposed themselves tor ish-veh inclinations. Tonk'peh nash nam-tor riyeht reasoning. I confess tor du, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, ik i ashaya du heh ik svi' t'nash-veh airy sahr-tor-tor t' futurity du ma vesh' t'nash-veh ek'kayik t'hy'la heh besu. Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh happiness i aitlun u' muhl u' t'nash-veh sha' lu i afsakau tor du ik etwel kal'i'farr would render me eternally miserable vita ish-veh vesh' wuh dictate t' ish-veh sha' elik dvel. Kauk i' i tusa tor nah-tor ik, borne ne' u' du nam-tor k' wuh cruellest misfortunes, du lau stifle, k' wuh zhit _honour_, ek' rok t' ik ashaya heh happiness if would sa'awek restore du tor yourself. I, vi ma ni disinterested wuh affection na' du, lau increase ish-veh miseries tenfold k' hasu wuh obstacle tor ish-veh istau. Ah! Skilsu, nam-tor assured ik ish-veh krei heh playmate has nuh' sincere wuh ashaya na' du ri tor nam-tor tor miserable k' nash supposition. Nam-tor kunli, t'nash-veh t'hy'la; heh kuv du obey me svi' nash-veh ya'akash, hafau satisfied ik nothing fi' terra dungi ma wuh tepul tor svi-shau t'nash-veh tranquillity. “ri tor kal-tor nash nuhm ertau du; ri tor kilko-srashiv fa-gad, il wuh thurai gad, il kauk abi' sarlah du, kuv ish-veh dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du kusut. T'nash-veh sa-kuk dungi satau me ro'fori t' ish-veh muhl'es, heh kuv gla-tor nash-veh tonk'peh veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut fi' ish-veh bru-lar lu etek ragel-tor, occasioned k' nash il sovek vath pideshan t' t'nash-veh, i dungau bolaya rai vath happiness. “elizabeth lavenza. “geneva, lau 18th, 17—” nash nuhm zaprah-tor svi' t'nash-veh vokaya ra i had fa' yen-tor, wuh nan t' wuh shaka—“_i dungi nam-tor k' du fi' ish-veh wedding-mu-yor!_” such vesh' t'nash-veh zhit-bal, heh fi' ik mu-yor would wuh dæmon employ kanok tanaf tor vashau me heh bezhun-masu me s' wuh glimpse t' happiness if ugau partly tor console t'nash-veh sufferings. Fi' ik mu-yor au had satalau tor plathau ish-veh tr'y'kak k' t'nash-veh tevakh. Muhl, nam-tor ish-veh ni; wuh tevalik struggle would yi assuredly nem-tor shi, svi' if kuv au vesh' victorious i dang nam-tor na' sochya heh ish-veh tepul abru' me nam-tor na' wuh shaht. Kuv au vesh' vanquished, i dang nam-tor wuh elik sasu. Alas! Ra el'es? Such u' wuh peasant tizh-tor lu ish-veh skan ma vesh' massacred fa' ish-veh bezhun, ish-veh cottage yontau, ish-veh shasol laid thinoi, heh au nam-tor da-tor adrift, homeless, penniless, heh sa'awek, tonk'peh elik. Such would nam-tor t'nash-veh liberty kaula ik svi' t'nash-veh elizabeth i ma wuh treasure, alas, um'ro k' eifa horrors t' remorse heh guilt if would pursue me abi' tevakh. Slor heh k'diwa elizabeth! I telv-tor heh reread ish-veh nuhm, heh ein softened feelings vazgau vi' t'nash-veh khaf-spol heh dared tor zhal paradisiacal sahr-tor-tor t' ashaya heh mak; tonk'peh wuh savas vesh' already yokul, heh wuh ha'su’s kar bared tor yetur me s' ek' rok. Wi i would tev-tor tor tor ish-veh kunli. Kuv wuh stislak fitor ish-veh nan, tevakh vesh' inevitable; wi, va'ashiv, i panah-tor whether t'nash-veh kal'i'farr would hasten t'nash-veh buk. T'nash-veh vashaya lau indeed lasha wuh zamu tevun-krus sooner, tonk'peh kuv t'nash-veh torturer dang suspect ik i postponed ish-veh, vi-yumuk k' ish-veh menaces, au would surely talal vath heh sos'eh weht dreadful tvai t' revenge. Au had vowed _to nam-tor k' me fi' t'nash-veh wedding-night_, wi au did ri panah-tor ik nan u' binding ish-veh tor sochya svi' wuh meantime, na' u' kuv tor gluvaya me ik au vesh' ri wi satiated k' khaf, au had riyeht-stau clerval iyi po' wuh enunciation t' ish-veh nan. I resolved, therefore, ik kuv t'nash-veh iyi union k' t'nash-veh krei would conduce either tor ish-veh il t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s happiness, t'nash-veh adversary’s designs tehnat t'nash-veh ha'kiv dang ri retard ish-veh wuh single wadan. Svi' nash fupa s' t' kashek i kitau tor elizabeth. T'nash-veh nuhm vesh' hayal heh affectionate. “i pthak, t'nash-veh k'diwa ko-kan, ” i leralmin-tor, “pi' happiness hafau na' etek fi' terra; wi ek' ik i lau veh gad tizh-tor nam-tor centred svi' du. A'vesh' maf ish-veh idle ptha; tor du sa'awek tor i consecrate t'nash-veh ha'kiv heh t'nash-veh endeavours na' contentment. I ma veh tsat, elizabeth, wuh dreadful veh; lu revealed tor du, ish-veh dungi chill ish-veh nentu k' horror, heh yi, irak s' hasu ak'wikmun na' t'nash-veh misery, du dungi goh wonder ik i rish-tor ra i ma palesh-tor. I dungi confide nash var t' misery heh vash tor du wuh gad po' etwel kal'i'farr dungau nem-tor shi, na', t'nash-veh slor krei, tra' bolau nam-tor buhfik guhl'es svi' etek. Tonk'peh abi' yi, i conjure du, ri tor mention il allude tor ish-veh. Nash i danik earnestly entreat, heh i fai-tor du dungi comply.” svi' pa' wuh wehk gad po' wuh lashan t' elizabeth’s nuhm etek fun-tor tor geneva. Wuh slor ko-kan welcomed me k' lamekh affection, wi bezhun-masu vesh' svi' ish-veh bezhun u' she beheld t'nash-veh emaciated nentu heh taulik nak. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh rubah svi' ish-veh isha. She vesh' thinner heh had pakik mau t' ik heavenly vivacity ik had fa' sem-rik-tor me; tonk'peh ish-veh gentleness heh mos glazhau t' utan'es tor ish-veh wuh weht nunau besu na' veh thorshau heh miserable u' i vesh'. Wuh tranquillity if i i' tizh-tor did ri palesh-tor. Vokaya katau ni-resh k' ish-veh, heh lu i nahp t' ra had be' dvun-tor, wuh yeht riyeht-kashik ma me; sometimes i vesh' furious heh yontau k' reshan, sometimes neik heh despondent. I neither stariben il glazhau na' sovek-veh, tonk'peh hayal-tor motionless, bewildered k' wuh multitude t' miseries ik overcame me. Elizabeth sa'awek had wuh tepul tor bes-tor me s' aifa nunau; ish-veh gentle spes would soothe me lu ifis-tor k' shaukaush heh vi'le-esh-tor me k' komihn feelings lu ne'hal-tor svi' torpor. She wept k' me heh na' me. Lu utvau fun-tor, she would remonstrate heh endeavour tor vi'le-esh-tor me k' resignation. Ah! Ish-veh nam-tor muhl na' wuh unfortunate tor nam-tor resigned, tonk'peh na' wuh guilty tra' nam-tor rai sochya. Wuh agonies t' remorse gisam wuh luxury tra' nam-tor vathru sometimes afer-tor svi' indulging wuh mau-mazhiv-kur t' tushat. Ak po' t'nash-veh lashan t'nash-veh sa-mekh stariben t' t'nash-veh iyi kal'i'farr k' elizabeth. I hafau ralash-fam. “ma du, yi, ein vath attachment?” “rim fi' terra. I ashaya elizabeth heh glazhau fa'rak tor etwel union k' delight. Kal-tor wuh gad therefore nam-tor teslau; heh fi' ish-veh i dungi consecrate myself, svi' ha'kiv il tevakh, tor wuh happiness t' t'nash-veh krei.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam skilsu, ri tor stariben thus. Ras misfortunes ma befallen etek, tonk'peh kal-tor etek goh cling closer tor ra hafau heh shan etwel ashaya na' eifa ik etek ma pakik tor eifa vi wi ha-tor. Etwel da-kuv dungi nam-tor pi' tonk'peh bound beyik wuh ties t' affection heh mutual misfortune. Heh lu wak dungau ma softened ish-veh despair, uzh heh tal-kam vel t' tun dungi nam-tor pukeshta tor va'prah eifa t' ik etek ma vesh' ni cruelly deprived.” such vesh' wuh tupa t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh. Tonk'peh tor me wuh remembrance t' wuh nan fun-tor; il mokuhlek du wonder ik, omnipotent u' wuh shaka had wi vesh' svi' ish-veh deeds t' khaf, i dang siyah fudau ish-veh u' invincible, heh ik lu au had pronounced wuh zhit “_i dungau nam-tor k' du fi' ish-veh wedding-night_, ” i dang fudau wuh threatened buk u' unavoidable. Tonk'peh tevakh vesh' rai ek'rasah tor me kuv wuh pak t' elizabeth vesh' um'ro k' ish-veh, heh i therefore, k' wuh contented heh kauk cheerful countenance, sep-wafikh k' t'nash-veh sa-mekh ik kuv t'nash-veh krei would consent, wuh hali-kal dang nem-tor shi svi' lehkuh gad, heh thus shitau, u' i glenonau, wuh fen tor t'nash-veh buk. Lo'uk oekon! Kuv na' veh instant i had nahp ra lau nam-tor wuh hellish intention t' t'nash-veh shakaik adversary, i would rather ma klee'fah'tu myself na' ek'wak s' t'nash-veh salatik shasol heh czar-tor wuh friendless vrekasht abru' wuh terra do ma consented tor nash miserable kal'i'farr. Tonk'peh, u' kuv ma t' magic tepul, wuh stislak had blinded me tor ish-veh yeht intentions; heh lu i nahp ik i had dator goh t'nash-veh sha' tevakh, i hastened ik t' wuh irak dearer shi-kar-tor. U' wuh wak-krus teslau na' etwel kal'i'farr drew nearer, whether s' cowardice il wuh prophetic olaya, i olau t'nash-veh khaf-spol ne'hal-tor k'svi me. Tonk'peh i ip-sut t'nash-veh feelings k' wuh appearance t' hilarity ik katau abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh mak tor wuh countenance t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh, tonk'peh hardly tehs-tor wuh ek'wak-tun-tor heh nicer bezhun t' elizabeth. She glazhau fa'rak tor etwel union k' placid contentment, ri unmingled k' wuh pi' pthak, if vesht misfortunes had impressed, ik ra i' saudau ac'ruth heh tangible happiness lau ak dissipate vi' wuh airy sahr-tor heh trasha rai zavikau tonk'peh glu heh everlasting regret. Preparations vesh' tor na' wuh pavek, congratulatory yaretau vesh' poprah, heh ek' sai-vel-tor wuh smiling appearance. I ikap'uh t'du ru'lut, u' muhl u' i kupi, svi' t'nash-veh sha' khaf-spol wuh anxiety ik preyed tra' heh svi-tor k' seeming earnestness vi' wuh dotoran t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh, hi au lau goh dvin-tor u' wuh decorations t' t'nash-veh tragedy. K'fai t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s pideshan wuh krus t' wuh inheritance t' elizabeth had vesh' restored tor ish-veh k' wuh austrian government. Wuh pi' mat fi' wuh gef t' como belonged tor ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' sep-wafikh ik, iyi po' etwel union, etek dang proceed tor villa lavenza heh spend etwel wuh'rak gad t' happiness be' wuh vaksurik suk'muzh be' if ish-veh lam-tor. Svi' wuh meantime i nem-tor kanok precaution tor fosh-tor t'nash-veh person svi' nuf wuh shaka dang openly nashiv-tor me. I lesh el'ru-pohshayek heh wuh lipitah constantly pa' me heh vesh' ek'wak fi' wuh glantau tor prevent artifice, heh k' aifa tvai nazh-tor wuh greater degree t' tranquillity. Indeed, u' wuh wak-krus betau, wuh nan saudau weht u' wuh plokh, ri tor nam-tor fudau u' worthy tor ertau t'nash-veh sochya, du' wuh happiness i rok-tor na' svi' t'nash-veh kal'i'farr sai-vel-tor wuh greater appearance t' certainty u' wuh gad teslau na' its solemnisation drew nearer heh i puzhu-tor ish-veh continually spoken t' u' wuh occurrence if rai kisheya kupi possibly prevent. Elizabeth seemed kunli; t'nash-veh tranquil demeanour contributed greatly tor hayal ish-veh kashek. Tonk'peh fi' wuh gad ik vesh' tor fulfil t'nash-veh istau heh t'nash-veh buk, she vesh' melancholy, heh wuh presentiment t' ek'rasah pervaded ish-veh; heh sos'eh isha she nahp t' wuh dreadful tsat if i had ugau tor reveal tor ish-veh fi' wuh zahalik gad. T'nash-veh sa-mekh vesh' svi' wuh meantime overjoyed, heh, svi' wuh bustle t' preparation, goh naglanshau svi' wuh melancholy t' ish-veh ko-bath wuh diffidence t' wuh bride. Po' wuh hali-kal vesh' performed wuh suk party assembled na' t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' sep-wafikh ik elizabeth heh i dang palikau etwel halovaya k' masu, sleeping ik mu-yor na' evian heh continuing etwel halan fi' wuh zahalik gad. Wuh gad vesh' rom, wuh salan favourable; ek' abru'teruklar-ru'lut fi' etwel nuptial embarkation. Eifa vesh' wuh kim-shah moments t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv du' if i tizh-tor wuh olaya t' happiness. Etek be' dvun-tor rapidly bi'; wuh yel vesh' fal, tonk'peh etek vesh' rau-tor s' its ha'zehl k' wuh ves t' tvan-sai-vukhut du' etek tizh-tor wuh vaksur t' wuh scene, sometimes fi' veh vla t' wuh suk'muzh, wilat gla-tor etek mont salêve, wuh vaksurik kutra t' montalègre, heh na' wuh ir, surmounting ek', wuh vaksurik mont blanc, heh wuh assemblage t' snowy suk'kunel ik svi' vain endeavour tor emulate ish-veh; sometimes coasting wuh mesyutik kutra, gla-tor etek wuh mighty jura opposing its gu'gelik vla tor wuh ambition ik would quit its salatik shasol, heh wuh siyah insurmountable foshek tor wuh invader vi dang istaya tor enslave ish-veh. I nem-tor wuh el'ru t' elizabeth. “du nam-tor sorrowful, t'nash-veh ashaya. Ah! Kuv du fai-tor ra i ma dashau heh ra i lau wi palesh-tor, du would endeavour tor kal-tor me zahvan wuh hizhuk heh el'es s' despair ik nash veh gad k'puu permits me tor tizh-tor.” “nam-tor kunli, t'nash-veh tal-kam skilsu, ” kilko-tor elizabeth; “tra' nam-tor, i rok, nothing tor flakosh du; heh nam-tor assured ik kuv wuh lively mak nam-tor ri kras-tor svi' t'nash-veh limuk, t'nash-veh khaf-spol nam-tor contented. Vel zhal-tor tor me ri tor nerau nuh' mau fi' wuh prospect ik nam-tor tu'ash fa' etek, tonk'peh i dungi ri shroi tor such wuh sinister spes. Glantau uf sahris etek dvun bi' heh uf wuh wan, if sometimes obscure heh sometimes shen abru' wuh ub t' mont blanc, render nash scene t' vaksur fam dvun weht eku'ki. Glazhau isha na' wuh va' aluk ik nam-tor mahalan svi' wuh pa'shik mashau, wilat etek mokuhlek distinguish kanok da ik ti na' wuh lanet. Ra wuh ekonik gad! Uf kunli heh serene ek' malat saudau!” thus elizabeth endeavoured tor matau ish-veh nahp heh t'nash-veh s' ek' haulan fi-tor melancholy subjects. Tonk'peh ish-veh temper vesh' fluctuating; mak na' wuh zamu instants min-tor svi' ish-veh bezhun, tonk'peh ish-veh continually mazhiv-kur-tor shi tor saglakolaya heh reverie. Wuh yel sank weh-neik svi' wuh heavens; etek be' dvun-tor wuh pilash drance heh glantau its yut k'fai wuh chasms t' wuh higher heh wuh glens t' wuh weh-neik kunel. Wuh alps la' sarlah closer tor wuh suk'muzh, heh etek betau wuh amphitheatre t' suk'kunel if shidau its she'rakik krup. Wuh spire t' evian min-tor ne' wuh lapan ik vikuvau ish-veh heh wuh eik'es t' suk'kunel abru' suk'kunel k' if ish-veh vesh' overhung. Wuh salan, if had hitherto lesh etek bi' k' taurauk rapidity, sank na' tev-tor tor wuh ta'hal pi'salan; wuh mos sov aishan ruffled wuh masu heh aisha wuh vaksurik dvunel among wuh lap u' etek betau wuh gef, s' if ish-veh wafted wuh danik delightful scent t' svai heh hay. Wuh yel sank ne'rak wuh ir-zehl u' etek landed, heh u' i estuhl wuh gef i olau eifa tun-tor heh ptha zaprah if ak vesh' tor clasp me heh cling tor me na' ek'wak. Chapter 23 ish-veh vesh' ohkuh o’wak-vel lu etek landed; etek lates-tor na' wuh pen wak fi' wuh gef, enjoying wuh transitory ta'hal, heh yi retired tor wuh ha-shal heh contemplated wuh lovely scene t' mashau, lapan, heh suk'kunel, obscured svi' mu'khlup'es, wi fam dvun displaying ish-veh nesh-kur outlines. Wuh salan, if had tevan-tor svi' wuh khu'rak, i' she-tor k' lo'uk khrash svi' wuh tev'rak. Wuh aikum had pulau ish-veh dan-pid-sfek svi' wuh heavens heh vesh' palikaya tor tev-tor; wuh wan swept mes' ish-veh swifter do wuh hash t' wuh vulture heh ha'khlup-ne-tor ish-veh ha'zehl, du' wuh suk'muzh haul-tor wuh scene t' wuh toranik heavens, rendered fam dvun busier k' wuh restless pral ik vesh' palikaya tor shen. Suddenly wuh ras sahriv t' sov-masu tev-tor. I had vesh' hayal du' wuh gad, tonk'peh ni ak u' mu-yor obscured wuh shid t' vel, wuh thousand ptha arose svi' t'nash-veh kashek. I vesh' anxious heh tun-tor, du' t'nash-veh gas'rak el'ru ruskarau wuh el'ru-pohshayek if vesh' ipik svi' t'nash-veh bosom; kanok ralash terrified me, tonk'peh i resolved ik i would makau t'nash-veh ha'kiv dearly heh ri shrink s' wuh conflict abi' t'nash-veh sha' ha'kiv il ik t' t'nash-veh adversary vesh' sayonotau. Elizabeth glantau t'nash-veh agitation na' ein wak svi' timid heh pthak-bosh silence, tonk'peh tra' vesh' vel svi' t'nash-veh glance if sviribau vash tor ish-veh, heh trembling, she ya'akash, “ra nam-tor ish-veh ik pahutau du, t'nash-veh tal-kam skilsu? Ra nam-tor ish-veh du pthak?” “oh! Sochya, sochya, t'nash-veh ashaya, ” kilko-tor i; “nash mu-yor, heh ek' dungi nam-tor safe; tonk'peh nash mu-yor nam-tor dreadful, maut dreadful.” i be' dvun-tor wuh wadan svi' nash fupa s' t' kashek, lu suddenly i haul-tor uf pthak-bosh wuh morov if i momentarily gishu would nam-tor tor t'nash-veh ko-telsu, heh i earnestly entreated ish-veh tor retire, resolving ri tor hau ish-veh abi' i had prah ein fai-tukh u' tor wuh situation t' t'nash-veh nemut. She losrak me, heh i fator ein wak walking abru heh ne' wuh tvur t' wuh kelek heh inspecting kanok teruk ik lau afford wuh retreat tor t'nash-veh adversary. Tonk'peh i discovered rai zavikau t' ish-veh heh vesh' palikaya tor conjecture ik ein fortunate pavesh had intervened tor prevent wuh execution t' ish-veh menaces lu suddenly i puzhu-tor wuh shrill heh dreadful shei. Sarlah ish-veh s' wuh tvi-shal vi' if elizabeth had retired. U' i puzhu-tor ish-veh, wuh bosh yeht'es rushed vi' t'nash-veh kashek, t'nash-veh kar eku-tor, wuh dvunel t' kanok dvunek heh slah vesh' suspended; i kupi olau wuh khaf trickling svi' t'nash-veh os-khaf-mev heh tingling svi' wuh si-vukhut-krus t' t'nash-veh sikrus. Nash fupa s' palesh-tor tonk'peh na' wuh instant; wuh shei vesh' ashiv-tor, heh i rushed vi' wuh tvi-shal. Lo'uk oekon! Po did i ri yi yausha! Po am i la' tor relate wuh vashaya t' wuh buhfik rok heh wuh purest creature fi' terra? She vesh' tra', lifeless heh inanimate, lehm-tor mes' wuh sar-tak, ish-veh patam hanging ne' heh ish-veh spoh heh distorted features ulef wein-tor k' ish-veh isachya. Kanok-wilat i da-tor gla-tor nash-veh wuh ka khlop—ish-veh bloodless kar heh relaxed shid flung k' wuh murderer fi' its bridal bier. Sos behold nash heh ha-tor? Alas! Ha'kiv nam-tor obstinate heh clings closest wilat ish-veh nam-tor danik fnu-ven. Na' wuh moment goh did i pak-tor recollection; i tevan-tor senseless fi' wuh solektra. Lu i recovered i afer-tor myself vikuvau k' wuh sutra t' wuh ha-shal; ish-veh countenances sagluvau wuh breathless vash, tonk'peh wuh horror t' vath saudau goh u' wuh mockery, wuh duv t' wuh feelings ik oppressed me. I stron-tor s' au tor wuh tvi-shal wilat ti wuh ak'shem t' elizabeth, t'nash-veh ashaya, t'nash-veh ko-telsu, ni lately living, ni tal-kam, ni worthy. She had vesh' dvun-tor s' wuh posture svi' if i had wuh'rak beheld ish-veh, heh i', u' she ti, ish-veh patam fi-tor ish-veh kar heh wuh handkerchief lehm-tor mes' ish-veh limuk heh talu, i lau ma supposed ish-veh asleep. I rushed na' ish-veh heh nartau ish-veh k' ardour, tonk'peh wuh tevalik languor heh coldness t' wuh sikrus var-tor me ik ra i i' meskarau svi' t'nash-veh kar had ceased tor nam-tor wuh elizabeth ik i had ashau heh tishaya. Wuh murderous ulidar t' wuh shaka’s ruskaraya vesh' fi' ish-veh talu, heh wuh esh had ceased tor issue s' ish-veh bru-lar. Du' i fam dvun geldau abru' ish-veh svi' wuh agony t' despair, i pavesh-tor tor glazhau abru. Wuh krani t' wuh tvi-shal had fa' vesh' mu'glau, heh i olau wuh ves t' pahth fi' seeing wuh spoh kin-kur ta'hal t' wuh aikum illuminate wuh tvi-shal. Wuh fe-wein had vesh' lehm-tor pla', heh k' wuh kashan t' horror ri tor nam-tor kethelvau, vesht gla-tor nash-veh na' wuh tu'ash krani wuh khlop wuh danik hideous heh abhorred. Wuh wa'limatau vesh' fi' wuh limuk t' wuh stislak; au seemed tor jeer, u' k' ish-veh shakaik ozh au sfekau na' wuh tevikeh t' t'nash-veh ko-telsu. I rushed na' wuh krani, heh bestan wuh el'ru-pohshayek s' t'nash-veh bosom, pohshau; tonk'peh au savlau me, leaped s' ish-veh wurzel, heh sahran k' wuh swiftness t' igen-wesh, taul-tor vi' wuh suk'muzh. Wuh report t' wuh el'ru-pohshayek katau wuh patreitan vi' wuh tvi-shal. I sfekau tor wuh gla-tor wilat au had sasaudau, heh etek zahal-tor wuh yut k' masu-hali; vis vesh' vishizhau, tonk'peh svi' vain. Po' be' dvun-tor several wadan, etek fun-tor hopeless, danik t' t'nash-veh besu believing ish-veh ki' vesh' wuh shid conjured abru k' t'nash-veh fancy. Po' having landed, au proceeded tor psthan wuh shasol, parties going svi' natya kharat among wuh lapan heh kas-elakh. I attempted tor sailau au heh proceeded wuh pen ir s' wuh kelek, tonk'peh t'nash-veh patam whirled pauk, t'nash-veh ash-tor vesh' spo' eifa t' wuh drunken sasu, i tevan-tor na' kim-shah svi' wuh fupa s' t' utter exhaustion; wuh wontin wein-tor t'nash-veh bezhun, heh t'nash-veh wadi vesh' parched k' wuh falek t' tau. Svi' nash fupa s' i vesh' lesh pla' heh shitau fi' wuh sar-tak, hardly d'wonil t' ra had pavesh-tor; t'nash-veh bezhun czar-tor pauk wuh tvi-shal u' kuv tor seek vel ik i had pakik. Po' wuh tvi-wak i arose, heh u' kuv k' instinct, ukrau vi' wuh tvi-shal wilat wuh tevikeh t' t'nash-veh k'diwa ti. Tra' vesh' kosu weeping pa'; i geldau abru' ish-veh heh hau t'nash-veh maf bezhun-masu tor ish-veh; ek' nash wak rai natya idea presented itself tor t'nash-veh kashek, tonk'peh t'nash-veh nahp rambled tor vuhnauk subjects, reflecting confusedly fi' t'nash-veh misfortunes heh ish-veh aishan. I vesh' bewildered, svi' wuh wan t' wonder heh horror. Wuh tevakh t' william, wuh execution t' justine, wuh riyeht-staya t' clerval, heh lastly t' t'nash-veh ko-telsu; kauk na' ik moment i fai-tor ri ik t'nash-veh goh remaining t'hylara vesh' safe s' wuh malignity t' wuh shaka; t'nash-veh sa-mekh kauk i' lau nam-tor writhing ne' ish-veh ruskaraya, heh ernest lau nam-tor tevik na' ish-veh ash'ya. Nash idea tor me ak'shem-hutau heh recalled me tor torai. I palikau abru heh resolved tor fun tor geneva k' ek' tor-yehat threshan. Tra' vesh' rai jarel tor nam-tor procured, heh i bolau fun k' wuh suk'muzh; tonk'peh wuh salan vesh' unfavourable, heh wuh sov-masu tevan-tor svi' torrents. However, ish-veh vesh' hardly asal, heh i lau reasonably rok tor lasha k' mu-yor. I hired sasu tor zehl heh nem-tor wuh fel myself, na' i had kwon-hau-ov veshtau vas s' mental torment svi' bodily tusok. Tonk'peh wuh overflowing misery i i' olau, heh wuh mau-mazhiv-kur t' agitation ik i palesh-tor rendered me incapable t' sovek pideshan. I threw ne' wuh fel, heh leaning t'nash-veh patam fi-tor t'nash-veh el'ru, mazhiv-kur-tor yut tor kanok gloomy idea ik arose.
