Kuv i glazhau abru, vesht gla-tor nash-veh scenes if vesh' familiar tor me svi' t'nash-veh happier wak heh if i had contemplated tonk'peh wuh gad fa' svi' wuh apc'koik t' ish-veh vi vesh' i' tonk'peh wuh duv heh wuh recollection. Bezhun-masu salash s' t'nash-veh bezhun. Wuh sov-masu had ceased na' wuh moment, heh vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh aluk mavau svi' wuh mashau u' au had ovsoh wuh zamu wadan fa'; au had yi vesh' glantau k' elizabeth. Nothing nam-tor ni kusut-tor tor wuh komihn kashek u' wuh lo'uk heh sudden rubah. Wuh yel lau min-tor il wuh wan lau weh-neik, tonk'peh nothing kupi saudau tor me u' ish-veh had ovsoh wuh gad fa'. Wuh shaka had snatched s' me kanok rok t' fa-wak happiness; rai creature had ek'wak vesh' ni miserable u' i vesh'; ni frightful wuh pavek nam-tor single svi' wuh vesht-var t' sasu. Tonk'peh po dang i dwell fi-tor wuh incidents ik zahal-tor nash kim-shah overwhelming pavek? T'nash-veh has vesh' wuh var t' horrors; i ma pulau ish-veh _acme_, heh ra i bolau i' relate mokuhlek tonk'peh nam-tor tedious tor du. Fai-tor ik, veh k' veh, t'nash-veh t'hylara vesh' snatched maf; i vesh' losrak desolate. T'nash-veh sha' karik'es nam-tor saguhsh-tor, heh i bolau var-tor, svi' wuh zamu zhit, ra hafau t' t'nash-veh hideous narration. I lasha na' geneva. T'nash-veh sa-mekh heh ernest wi ha-tor, tonk'peh wuh former ne'hal-tor ne' wuh tidings ik i spitau. Gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh i', marom heh venerable hinek sasu! Ish-veh bezhun czar-tor svi' vacancy, na' au had pakik ish-veh sem-rik heh ish-veh delight—ish-veh elizabeth, ish-veh weht do ko-fu, ik au doted fi' k' ek' ik affection if wuh sasu olau, vi svi' wuh decline t' ha'kiv, having zamu affections, clings weht earnestly tor eifa ik hafau. Cursed, cursed nam-tor wuh shaka ik katau misery fi' ish-veh zhai-kur isachya heh doomed ish-veh tor thinoi svi' wretchedness! Au kupi ri ha-tor ne' wuh horrors ik vesh' accumulated pa' ish-veh; wuh sikar t' nam suddenly mazhiv-kur-tor yut; au vesh' unable tor shen s' ish-veh sar-tak, heh svi' wuh zamu gad au tev-tor svi' t'nash-veh kar. Ra yi became t' me? I fai-tor ri; i pakik kashan, heh naf-elakh heh mu'khlup'es vesh' wuh goh vel ik hish-tor fi-tor me. Sometimes, indeed, i dreamt ik i czar-tor svi' flowery ne-yartra heh vaksurik vales k' wuh t'hylara t' t'nash-veh youth, tonk'peh i awoke heh afer-tor myself svi' wuh dungeon. Melancholy zahal-tor, tonk'peh k' degrees i nazh-tor wuh pa'shik conception t' t'nash-veh miseries heh situation heh vesh' yi sadalau s' t'nash-veh prison. Na' au had puvutau me mad, heh du' wehk tevun-krus, u' i ken-tor, wuh solitary nala had vesh' t'nash-veh habitation. Liberty, however, had vesh' wuh nam-tor-fam mazhiv-kur tor me, had i ri, u' i awakened tor utvau, na' wuh ka wak awakened tor revenge. U' wuh vokaya t' vesht misfortunes hish-tor fi-tor me, i began tor haul-tor fi' ish-veh aishan—wuh stislak ik i had fereik-tor, wuh miserable dæmon ik i had satau abroad vi' wuh panu na' t'nash-veh vashaya. I vesh' ma k' wuh maddening reshan lu i nahp t' ish-veh, heh aitlu heh ardently prayed ik i lau ma ish-veh k'svi t'nash-veh ruskaraya tor wreak wuh lo'uk heh glantokaya revenge fi' ish-veh cursed patam. Il did t'nash-veh fnu-ven wu confine itself tor nam-tor-fam istau; i began tor haul-tor fi' wuh buhfik tvai t' securing ish-veh; heh na' nash lof, pa' wuh tevun-krus po' t'nash-veh sadalaya, i teslau tor wuh criminal judge svi' wuh kahr heh var-tor ish-veh ik i had wuh accusation tor tor, ik i fai-tor wuh destroyer t' t'nash-veh skan, heh ik i required ish-veh tor pidesh ish-veh bosh ek'te'kru na' wuh apprehension t' wuh murderer. Wuh magistrate shroi tor me k' attention heh kindness. “nam-tor assured, osu, ” leralmin-tor au, “rai kusut-tor il pideshan fi' t'nash-veh krus dungau nam-tor spared tor discover wuh villain.” “i nemaiyo, ” kilko-tor i; “shroi, therefore, tor wuh deposition ik i ma tor tor. Ish-veh nam-tor indeed wuh var ni flekh ik i dang pthak du would ri lit ish-veh vesh' tra' ri vel svi' yeht'es if, however wonderful, nekwitau conviction. Wuh var nam-tor nuh' tersau tor nam-tor mistaken na' wuh sahr-tor, heh i ma rai dvubolek na' falsehood.” t'nash-veh manner u' i thus addressed ish-veh vesh' impressive tonk'peh hayal; i had shidau svi' t'nash-veh sha' khaf-spol wuh resolution tor pursue t'nash-veh destroyer tor tevakh, heh nash lof quieted t'nash-veh agony heh na' wuh tvi-wak reconciled me tor ha'kiv. I i' related t'nash-veh vesht-var briefly tonk'peh k' firmness heh precision, marking wuh kinuf k' accuracy heh worla deviating vi' invective il sporun. Wuh magistrate saudau palikauk perfectly incredulous, tonk'peh u' i fator au became weht whio'naks heh interested; vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh sometimes ak'shem-hutau k' horror; na' vath wuh lively ak'wikmun, unmingled k' disbelief, vesh' kras-tor fi' ish-veh countenance. Lu i had concluded t'nash-veh narration, i leralmin-tor, “nash nam-tor wuh hasu ik i accuse heh na' t'vi mahai heh taflaya i vutau fi-tor du tor pidesh ish-veh bosh tepul. Ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh gu-vam u' wuh magistrate, heh i dva-tor heh rok ik ish-veh feelings u' wuh sasu dungi ri revolt s' wuh execution t' eifa nam-tor-lof fi' nash occasion.” nash shi'yavekh aisha wuh considerable rubah svi' wuh physiognomy t' t'nash-veh sha' auditor. Au had puzhu-tor t'nash-veh var k' ik ulef ves t' dva ik nam-tor putan-tor tor wuh var t' tam'a heh supernatural pavek; tonk'peh lu au vesh' puvutau fi-tor tor bae'cok officially svi' consequence, wuh bosh mashen t' ish-veh incredulity fun-tor. Au, however, kilko-tor mildly, “i would willingly afford du kanok mamuk svi' ish-veh pursuit, tonk'peh wuh creature t' ik du stariben saudau tor ma tepul if would shitau ek' t'nash-veh pideshan tor defiance. Vi mokuhlek zahal-tor wuh aushfa if mokuhlek traverse wuh masutra t' le-suma heh inhabit tauk heh dens wilat rai sasu would venture tor vi-kwitau? Isha, ein tevun-krus ma veshau opi' wuh kadvin t' ish-veh tr'y'kak, heh kling mokuhlek conjecture tor ra shi au has czar-tor il ra shal au lau i' inhabit.” “i ri tor vet ik au hovers be' wuh gla-tor if i inhabit, heh kuv au has indeed taken rau-nol svi' wuh alps, au lau nam-tor shi'kar spo' wuh chamois heh vashau u' wuh beast t' shi-kar-tor. Tonk'peh i pakashogau nahp; du ri tor lit t'nash-veh narrative heh ri tor intend tor pursue t'nash-veh nemut k' wuh taflaya if nam-tor ish-veh eshikh.” u' i stariben, reshan sparkled svi' t'nash-veh bezhun; wuh magistrate vesh' intimidated. “du nam-tor mistaken, ” leralmin-tor au. “i dungi pidesh myself, heh kuv ish-veh nam-tor svi' t'nash-veh tepul tor seize wuh stislak, nam-tor assured ik au dungau dash taflaya proportionate tor ish-veh tr'y'kak. Tonk'peh i pthak, s' ra du ma yourself kethelvau tor nam-tor ish-veh veltra, ik nash dungi skan-tor impracticable; heh thus, du' kanok proper thon-tor nam-tor pursued, du dang tor abru ish-veh kashek tor disappointment.” “ik fam yehat nam-tor; tonk'peh ek' ik i mokuhlek leralmin dungi nam-tor t' pi' avail. T'nash-veh revenge nam-tor t' rai moment tor du; wi, du' i kal-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh vice, i confess ik ish-veh nam-tor wuh devouring heh goh shaukaush t' t'nash-veh soul. T'nash-veh reshan nam-tor unspeakable lu i haul-tor ik wuh murderer, ik i ma da-tor thal fi-tor shila'es, fam dvun nam-tor. Du klee'fah t'nash-veh aishan haishaya; i ma tonk'peh veh resource, heh i vaikau myself, either svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv il tevakh, tor ish-veh vashaya.” i trembled k' mau-mazhiv-kur t' agitation u' i leralmin-tor nash; tra' vesh' wuh frenzy svi' t'nash-veh manner, heh vel, i vet ri, t' ik haughty fierceness if wuh trufemu t' hinek nam-tor leralmin-tor ki' ma. Tonk'peh tor wuh genevan magistrate, t'vi kashek vesh' occupied k' irak vath ideas do eifa t' vaikaya heh heroism, nash ashenaya t' kashek had mau wuh appearance t' ni-resh. Au endeavoured tor soothe me u' wuh nurse tor wuh kan heh reverted tor t'nash-veh var u' wuh daya t' delirium. “sasu, ” i maf-tor, “uf ignorant tanaf thou svi' thy pride t' kau! Cease; du fai-tor ri ra ish-veh nam-tor du leralmin.” i shau s' wuh kelek reshnek heh ertau heh retired tor meditate fi' ein vath nuk t' torai. Chapter 24 t'nash-veh la' situation vesh' veh svi' if ek' toripik nahp vesh' vitem-tor abru heh pakik. I vesh' hurried maf k' fury; revenge sa'awek endowed me k' karik'es heh composure; ish-veh moulded t'nash-veh feelings heh kal-tor me tor nam-tor calculating heh hayal na' wak-krus lu vathru delirium il tevakh would ma vesh' t'nash-veh portion. T'nash-veh wuh'rak resolution vesh' tor quit geneva na' ek'wak; t'nash-veh shasol, if, lu i vesh' kunli heh k'diwa, vesh' tal-kam tor me, i', svi' t'nash-veh adversity, became hateful. I tanilau myself k' wuh hau-ov t' donku, teretuhr k' wuh zamu ek'zer if had belonged tor t'nash-veh ko-mekh, heh trashu. Heh i' t'nash-veh czar began if nam-tor tor cease tonk'peh k' ha'kiv. I ma traversed wuh vast portion t' wuh terra heh ma palesh-tor ek' wuh hardships if travellers svi' eshikh heh barbarous shasol nam-tor wont tor ragel-tor. Uf i ma ha-tor i hardly fai-tor; wehk wak ma i sakadau t'nash-veh failing sikrus fi-tor wuh mazhivik eiktra heh prayed na' tevakh. Tonk'peh revenge potau me alive; i dared ri tev-tor heh trasha t'nash-veh adversary svi' hasu. Lu i quitted geneva t'nash-veh wuh'rak zup vesh' tor nazh-kap ein clue k' if i lau zavikau wuh ash-tor t' t'nash-veh shakaik nemut. Tonk'peh t'nash-veh dotor vesh' unsettled, heh i czar-tor wehk wadan pauk wuh confines t' wuh kahr, uncertain ra yut i dang pursue. U' mu-yor betau i afer-tor myself na' wuh entrance t' wuh cemetery wilat william, elizabeth, heh t'nash-veh sa-mekh reposed. I svi-tor ish-veh heh betau wuh braq if pu'ulidau ish-veh shi'vukhut. Kanok-vei vesh' ralash-fam kaula wuh mor t' wuh lap, if vesh' kogavik pahutau k' wuh salan; wuh mu-yor vesh' nearly gu'gelik, heh wuh scene would ma vesh' solemn heh affecting kauk tor wuh uninterested observer. Wuh tam'a t' wuh trashu seemed tor flit pa' heh tor vishizhau wuh duv, if vesh' olau tonk'peh ri gla-tor, pa' wuh patam t' wuh mourner. Wuh glu tushat if nash scene had palikauk teporilau sahris mazhiv-kur-tor yut tor reshan heh despair. Au vesh' tevik, heh i ha-tor; ish-veh murderer isha ha-tor, heh tor vashau ish-veh i bolau zaseshau si' t'nash-veh weary nam. I knelt fi' wuh yar heh shok-tor wuh terra heh k' quivering bru-lar sporiben, “k' wuh sacred terra fi' if i kneel, k' wuh duvek-tor ik czar be' me, k' wuh glu heh ek'wakik tushat ik i olau, i swear; heh k' thee, o mu-yor, heh wuh tam'a ik preside abru' thee, tor pursue wuh dæmon vi aisha nash misery, abi' au il i dungau perish svi' mortal conflict. Na' nash lof i dungi korsau t'nash-veh ha'kiv; tor fitor nash tal-kam revenge dungi i va'ashiv behold wuh yel heh tread wuh yar-kur herbage t' terra, if vathru dang vanish s' t'nash-veh bezhun na' ek'wak. Heh i vutau fi' du, tam'a t' wuh tevik, heh fi' du, wandering ministers t' vengeance, tor mamuk heh spa-tor me svi' t'nash-veh ar'kadan. Kal-tor wuh cursed heh hellish stislak mon glu t' agony; kal-tor ish-veh olau wuh despair ik i' torments me.” i had palikau t'nash-veh adjuration k' solemnity heh wuh teshan if siyah assured me ik wuh duvek-tor t' t'nash-veh riyeht-stau t'hylara puzhu-tor heh messau t'nash-veh vaikaya, tonk'peh wuh furies ma me u' i concluded, heh reshan khluhkau t'nash-veh utterance. I vesh' kilko-tor k'fai wuh stillness t' mu-yor k' wuh ral heh shakaik abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Ish-veh rang fi' t'nash-veh kaluk wu heh heavily; wuh suk'kunel re-echoed ish-veh, heh i olau u' kuv ek' bogozh vikuvau me k' mockery heh laughter. Surely svi' ik moment i dang ma vesh' ma k' frenzy heh ma vashau t'nash-veh miserable nam tonk'peh ik t'nash-veh vow vesh' puzhu-tor heh ik i vesh' reserved na' vengeance. Wuh laughter tev-tor maf, lu wuh muhl-fainu heh abhorred spes, sauyaing beyik t'nash-veh kaluk, addressed me svi' wuh zhu-yehat zhal, “i am satisfied, miserable wretch! Du ma satalau tor ha-tor, heh i am satisfied.” i darted na' wuh gla-tor s' if wuh ralash proceeded, tonk'peh wuh e'shua savlau t'nash-veh ruskaraya. Suddenly wuh sax'ksei mathra t' wuh aikum arose heh min-tor bosh fi-tor ish-veh ghastly heh distorted shid u' au sasahr-tor k' weht do mortal threshan. I pursued ish-veh, heh na' wehk tevun-krus nash has vesh' t'nash-veh task. Kakhartau k' wuh slight clue, i zahal-tor wuh windings t' wuh rhone, tonk'peh vainly. Wuh pla-kur mediterranean saudau, heh k' wuh flekh pavesh, vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh shaka svi-tor k' mu-yor heh ip-sut himself svi' wuh hali bound na' wuh nesh-kur masutra. I nem-tor t'nash-veh tvur svi' wuh ka hali, tonk'peh au stron-tor, i fai-tor ri uf. Amidst wuh wilds t' tartary heh russia, hi au fam dvun savlau me, i ma ek'wak zahal-tor svi' ish-veh yut. Sometimes wuh peasants, pahth-tor k' nash horrid apparition, informed me t' ish-veh yut; sometimes au himself, vi ptha ik kuv i pakik ek' zavikau t' ish-veh i dang despair heh tev-tor, losrak ein ulidar tor kakhartausu me. Wuh izhau tev-tor fi' t'nash-veh patam, heh vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh hish t' ish-veh masuk' ash fi' wuh wan-kur eiktra. Tor du wuh'rak entering fi' ha'kiv, tor ik tun nam-tor uzh heh agony ri-fainu, uf mokuhlek du ken-tor ra i ma olau heh fam dvun olau? Samu, aitlun, heh zung vesh' wuh least kusut-tor if i vesh' destined tor palesh-tor; i vesh' cursed k' ein e'shua heh lesh pa' k' me t'nash-veh ek'wakik bogozh; wi fam dvun wuh tam'a t' rom zahal-tor heh khartau t'nash-veh ash-tor heh lu i danik murmured would suddenly extricate me s' seemingly insurmountable rihag'es. Sometimes, lu malat, overcome k' avon, sank ne' wuh exhaustion, wuh repast vesh' dator na' me svi' wuh eshikh ik restored heh inspirited me. Wuh panavau vesh', indeed, dirik, such u' wuh peasants t' wuh shasol ate, tonk'peh i dungi ri vet ik ish-veh vesh' eku tra' k' wuh tam'a ik i had invoked tor mamuk me. K'ashiv, lu ek' vesh' pseth, wuh heavens cloudless, heh i vesh' parched k' mag, wuh slight wan would bedim wuh igen, foshuhl wuh zamu eku-tor ik zaprah-tor me, heh vanish. I zahal-tor, lu i kupi, wuh rivak t' wuh pilash; tonk'peh wuh dæmon paik nan'woi aifa, u' ish-veh vesh' la' ik wuh population t' wuh shasol chiefly tershau. Svi' vath shitau komihn beings vesh' seldom gla-tor, heh i paik subsisted fi' wuh kwai animals ik tuhsau t'nash-veh yut. I had donku k' me heh nazh-tor wuh friendship t' wuh villagers k' distributing ish-veh; il i katau k' me ein yem-tukh ik i had pustau, if, po' taking wuh pi' krus, i kwon-hau-ov presented tor eifa vi had tanilau me k' yon heh utensils na' fasan. T'nash-veh ha'kiv, u' ish-veh be' dvun-tor thus, vesh' indeed hateful tor me, heh ish-veh vesh' du' yuk sa'awek ik i kupi zahvan mak. O blessed yuk! K'ashiv, lu danik miserable, i sank tor repose, heh t'nash-veh sahr-tor-tor lulled me kauk tor rapture. Wuh tam'a ik klashau me had tanilau aifa moments, il rather wadan, t' happiness ik i lau retain karik'es tor fulfil t'nash-veh pilgrimage. Deprived t' nash respite, i dang ma ne'hal-tor ne' t'nash-veh hardships. Du' wuh gad i vesh' potun-tor heh inspirited k' wuh rok t' mu-yor, na' svi' yuk vesht gla-tor nash-veh t'nash-veh t'hylara, t'nash-veh ko-telsu, heh t'nash-veh k'diwa shasol; va'ashiv vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh benevolent countenance t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh, puzhu-tor wuh haul-tukh molu t' t'nash-veh elizabeth’s spes, heh beheld clerval enjoying muhl'es heh youth. K'ashiv, lu wearied k' wuh toilsome march, i persuaded myself ik i vesh' dreaming abi' mu-yor dang sarlah heh ik i dang yi tizh-tor reality svi' wuh kar t' t'nash-veh dearest t'hylara. Ra agonising fondness did i olau na' au! Uf did i cling tor ish-veh tal-kam shidau, u' sometimes au haunted kauk t'nash-veh waking wadan, heh persuade myself ik au fam dvun ha-tor! Na' such moments vengeance, ik yontau k'svi me, tev-tor svi' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, heh i pursued t'nash-veh yut na' wuh vashaya t' wuh dæmon weht u' wuh task enjoined k' sha-ka-ri, u' wuh mechanical impulse t' ein tepul t' if i vesh' unconscious, do u' wuh ardent aitlun t' t'nash-veh soul. Ra ish-veh feelings vesh' ik i pursued i fam yehat fai-tor. Sometimes, indeed, au losrak ulidar svi' kitaun fi' wuh barks t' wuh lap il tresahk svi' kov ik kakhartau me heh instigated t'nash-veh fury. “t'nash-veh reign nam-tor ri wi abru'”—aifa zhit vesh' legible svi' veh t' aifa inscriptions—“du ha-tor, heh t'nash-veh tepul nam-tor ovsotik. Zahal-tor me; i seek wuh everlasting ices t' wuh desh'rak, wilat du dungi olau wuh misery t' samu heh le-su, tor if i am impassive. Du dungi talal be' nash shi, kuv du zahal-tor ri nuh' tardily, wuh tevik hare; yokul heh nam-tor uzhau. Sarlah fi', t'nash-veh nemut; etek ma wi tor wrestle na' etwel ha-tor, tonk'peh wehk lerash heh miserable wadan bolau du palesh-tor abi' ik wak-krus dungau lasha.” scoffing e'shua! Va'ashiv tor i vow vengeance; va'ashiv tor i vaikau thee, miserable shaka, tor torture heh tevakh. Worla dungi i mazhiv-kur-tor abru t'nash-veh psthan abi' au il i perish; heh yi k' ra prahk'es dungau i hau t'nash-veh elizabeth heh t'nash-veh trashu t'hylara, vi kauk i' dator na' me wuh reward t' t'nash-veh tedious toil heh horrible pilgrimage! U' i fam dvun pursued t'nash-veh halovaya tor wuh na'desh'rak, wuh izhau thickened heh wuh samu increased svi' wuh degree siyah nuh' severe tor nenikaya. Wuh peasants vesh' ikap'uh t'du ru'lut svi' ish-veh hovels, heh goh wuh zamu t' wuh danik hardy ventured forth tor seize wuh animals ik starvation had punekwitau s' ish-veh hiding-shitau tor seek na' shi-kar-tor. Wuh pilash vesh' wein-tor k' le-suma, heh rai aluk kupi nam-tor procured; heh thus i vesh' tresahk ska' s' t'nash-veh chief ua'mrki t' rompotaya. Wuh triumph t' t'nash-veh nemut increased k' wuh rihag'es t' t'nash-veh zup-tor. Veh inscription ik au losrak vesh' svi' aifa zhit: “dator! Ish-veh toils goh palikau; wrap yourself svi' furs heh tanilau yem-tukh, na' etek dungau ak svi-tor fi-tor wuh halovaya wilat ish-veh sufferings dungi satisfy t'nash-veh everlasting hatred.” t'nash-veh courage heh perseverance vesh' invigorated k' aifa scoffing zhit; i resolved ri tor vravshau svi' t'nash-veh lof, heh calling fi' sha-ka-ri tor nenikaya me, i fator k' unabated fervour tor traverse immense eshikh, abi' wuh masutra saudau na' wuh ir heh shidau wuh utmost krup t' wuh ir-zehl. Oh! Uf rikes ish-veh vesh' tor wuh pla-kur tevun-yonuk t' wuh khu'rak! Wein-tor k' le-suma, ish-veh vesh' goh tor nam-tor distinguished s' solektra k' its superior wildness heh ruggedness. Wuh greeks wept na' mak lu au beheld wuh mediterranean s' wuh kunel t' asia, heh hailed k' rapture wuh krup t' ish-veh toils. I did ri tusa, tonk'peh i knelt ne' heh k' wuh bosh khaf-spol itaren t'nash-veh guiding tam'a na' conducting me svi' ek'manek tor wuh shi wilat i rok-tor, notwithstanding t'nash-veh adversary’s gibe, tor ragel-tor heh grapple k' ish-veh. Ein wehk gad fa' nash wak-krus i had procured wuh sledge heh dogs heh thus traversed wuh izhau k' inconceivable threshan. I fai-tor ri whether wuh shaka ma wuh ka advantages, tonk'peh i afer-tor ik, u' fa' i had kanok-gadik pakik solektra svi' wuh pursuit, i i' nazh-tor fi' ish-veh, ni mau ni ik lu i wuh'rak gla-tor wuh masutra au vesh' tonk'peh veh gad’s halovaya svi' storilaya, heh i rok-tor tor fnakaya ish-veh fa' au dang pulau wuh shahov. K' uzh courage, therefore, i hish-tor fi', heh svi' dahkuh gad lasha na' wuh wretched hamlet fi' wuh seashore. I inquired t' wuh inhabitants fundik wuh shaka heh nazh-tor accurate ro'fori. Wuh masuk' stislak, au leralmin-tor, had lasha wuh mu-yor fa', armed k' wuh pohshayek heh wehk el'ru-pohshayek, putting tor hash wuh inhabitants t' wuh solitary cottage k'fai pthak t' ish-veh terrific appearance. Au had lesh ska' ish-veh mahr-kel t' karil yem-tukh, heh placing ish-veh svi' wuh sledge, tor bes-tor if au had seized fi' wuh numerous drove t' ranau dogs, au had harnessed au, heh wuh ka mu-yor, tor wuh mak t' wuh horror-kwul-tor villagers, had pursued ish-veh halovaya mes' wuh masutra svi' wuh kharat ik pufulag-tor tor rai solektra; heh au conjectured ik au bolau speedily nam-tor vashau k' wuh breaking t' wuh le-suma il le-sumalik k' wuh ek'wakik le-su. Fi' khaf-spol nash ro'fori i dashau wuh rikwonik access t' despair. Au had stron-tor me, heh i bolau palikau wuh vashauk heh siyah shaht-fam halovaya mes' wuh mountainous ices t' wuh masutra, amidst samu ik zamu t' wuh inhabitants kupi wu palesh-tor heh if i, wuh salatik t' wuh genial heh ka'ug'yelik ek'nosh, kupi ri rok tor rish-tor. Wi na' wuh idea ik wuh shaka dang ha-tor heh nam-tor triumphant, t'nash-veh reshan heh vengeance fun-tor, heh spo' wuh mighty mashen, overwhelmed kanok vath olaya. Po' wuh slight repose, du' if wuh tam'a t' wuh tevik hovered pauk heh instigated me tor toil heh revenge, i dator na' t'nash-veh halovaya. I di'kizh-tor t'nash-veh solektra-sledge na' veh fashioned na' wuh inequalities t' wuh le-sumalik masutra, heh purchasing wuh plentiful fek t' provisions, i trashu s' solektra. I fam yehat guess uf wehk gad ma be' dvun-tor opi' yi, tonk'peh i ma palesh-tor misery if nothing tonk'peh wuh ek'wakik sentiment t' wuh aishan retribution yontau k'svi t'nash-veh khaf-spol kupi ma enabled me tor nenikaya. Immense heh rugged suk'kunel t' le-suma k'ashiv barred abru t'nash-veh tvur, heh i k'ashiv puzhu-tor wuh rahm t' wuh solektra masutra, if threatened t'nash-veh vashaya. Tonk'peh va'ashiv wuh le-su sarlah heh tor wuh yut t' wuh masutra shar. K' wuh nosahp t' provision if i had consumed, i dang guess ik i had be' dvun-tor rehkuh wehk gad svi' nash halovaya; heh wuh continual protraction t' rok, returning pla' fi-tor wuh khaf-spol, k'ashiv wrung sfith(-) eku-tor t' despondency heh tushat s' t'nash-veh bezhun. Despair had indeed siyah shar-tor ish-veh shi-kar-tor, heh i dang ak ma ne'hal-tor ne'rak nash misery. Wuh'wak, po' wuh ri donku-tor animals ik zhelesh me had k' incredible toil nazh-tor wuh dan-pid-sfek t' wuh sloping le-suma suk'kunel, heh veh, sinking ne' ish-veh zung, tev-tor, i zan-tor wuh iraktra fa' me k' thonaya, lu suddenly t'nash-veh bezhun kum-tor wuh gu'gelik speck fi-tor wuh dusky eiktra. I ish-veh-tor t'nash-veh glan tor discover ra ish-veh kupi nam-tor heh uttered wuh kwai maf t' prahk'es lu i distinguished wuh sledge heh wuh distorted proportions t' wuh muhl-fainu shid k'svi. Oh! K' ra wuh yontau gush did rok revisit t'nash-veh khaf-spol! Lamekh bezhun-masu boshau t'nash-veh bezhun, if i hastily psethau maf, ik au lau ri fnakaya wuh zan-tor i had t' wuh dæmon; tonk'peh fam dvun t'nash-veh glan vesh' ha'khlup-ne-tor k' wuh yontau eku-tor, abi', giving yut tor wuh zherka ik oppressed me, i wept aloud. Tonk'peh nash vesh' ri wuh wak na' vohtaya; i disencumbered wuh dogs t' ish-veh tevik besu, mazhiv-kur-tor au wuh plentiful portion t' yem-tukh, heh po' wuh wadan’s shom, if vesh' absolutely bolayatik, heh wi if vesh' bitterly irksome tor me, i fator t'nash-veh route. Wuh sledge vesh' fam dvun visible, il did i va'ashiv pak-tor glan t' ish-veh kaula na' wuh moments lu na' wuh pen wak ein le-suma-kov ip-sut ish-veh k' its intervening crags. I indeed perceptibly nazh-tor fi' ish-veh, heh lu, po' nearly dahkuh gad’ halovaya, i beheld t'nash-veh nemut na' rai weht do wuh mile irak, t'nash-veh khaf-spol bounded k'svi me. Tonk'peh i', lu i saudau siyah k'svi ruskaraya t' t'nash-veh hahf, t'nash-veh rok-tor vesh' suddenly sayonotau, heh i pakik ek' zavikau t' ish-veh weht utterly do i had ek'wak ovsoh fa'. Wuh solektra masutra vesh' puzhu-tor; wuh rahm t' its progress, u' wuh mashau padukau heh puv-tor ne'rak me, became kanok moment weht ominous heh terrific. I hish-tor fi', tonk'peh svi' vain. Wuh salan arose; wuh masutra roared; heh, u' k' wuh mighty kolaya t' wuh solektra-hutaya, ish-veh thresh heh treshau k' wuh tremendous heh overwhelming ralash. Wuh ar'kadan vesh' ak shahtau; svi' wuh zamu minutes wuh tumultuous masutra padukau svi' me heh t'nash-veh nemut, heh i vesh' losrak drifting fi' wuh scattered krus t' le-suma ik vesh' continually lessening heh thus preparing na' me wuh hideous tevakh. Svi' nash manner wehk appalling wadan be' dvun-tor; several t' t'nash-veh dogs tev-tor, heh i myself vesh' pa' tor ne'hal-tor ne' wuh tabrukaya t' flakosh lu vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh hali riding na' masu-vohrayek heh holding forth tor me rok-tor t' succour heh ha'kiv. I had rai conception ik hali ek'wak sarlah ni irak desh'rak heh vesh' astounded na' wuh glan. I sahris vashau krus t' t'nash-veh sledge tor torvau fel, heh k' aifa tvai vesh' enabled, k' vaik zung, tor dvun t'nash-veh le-suma marshak svi' wuh kharat t' ish-veh hali. I had satalau, kuv du vesh' going na'khu'rak, fam dvun tor sahrafel myself tor wuh mercy t' wuh masutra rather do abandon t'nash-veh lof. I rok-tor tor vimevilau du tor vahl me wuh masu-hali k' if i kupi pursue t'nash-veh nemut. Tonk'peh ish-veh kharat vesh' na'desh'rak. Du nem-tor me fi' dohn lu t'nash-veh vigour vesh' saguhsh-tor, heh i dang ak ma ne'hal-tor ne' t'nash-veh wehkovau hardships vi' wuh tevakh if i fam dvun dread, na' t'nash-veh task nam-tor unfulfilled. Oh! Lu dungi t'nash-veh guiding tam'a, svi' conducting me tor wuh dæmon, kal-tor me wuh shom i ni mau aitlun; il bolau i tev-tor, heh au wi ha-tor? Kuv i tor, swear tor me, walton, ik au dungau ri stron, ik du dungi seek ish-veh heh satisfy t'nash-veh vengeance svi' ish-veh tevakh. Heh tor i dare tor ya'akash t' du tor undertake t'nash-veh pilgrimage, tor palesh-tor wuh hardships ik i ma undergone? Rai; i am ri ni selfish. Wi, lu i am tevik, kuv au dang saudau, kuv wuh ministers t' vengeance dang spa-tor ish-veh tor du, swear ik au dungau ri ha-tor—swear ik au dungau ri triumph abru' t'nash-veh accumulated woes heh rish-tor tor hau tor wuh feim t' ish-veh gu'gelik tr'y'kak. Au nam-tor eloquent heh persuasive, heh wuh'wak ish-veh zhit had kauk tepul abru' t'nash-veh khaf-spol; tonk'peh sahrafel ish-veh ri. Ish-veh soul nam-tor u' hellish u' ish-veh shid, bosh t' treachery heh shaka-spo' malice. Zhu-tor ish-veh ri; vutau fi' wuh ahm t' william, justine, clerval, elizabeth, t'nash-veh sa-mekh, heh t' wuh wretched skilsu, heh kwit ish-veh shek vi' ish-veh khaf-spol. I dungi hover be' heh kharik wuh pishek aright. Walton, _in continuation._ august 26th, 17—. Du ma telv-tor nash flekh heh terrific var, margaret; heh tor du ri olau ish-veh khaf congeal k' horror, spo' ik if kauk i' curdles t'nash-veh? Sometimes, seized k' sudden agony, au kupi ri fator ish-veh var; na' vath, ish-veh spes pushau, wi piercing, uttered k' rihag'es wuh zhit ni replete k' thonaya. Ish-veh tok-ti heh lovely bezhun vesh' i' lighted abru k' indignation, i' nessau tor downcast sorrow heh quenched svi' vaik wretchedness. Sometimes au khartau ish-veh countenance heh molu heh related wuh danik horrible incidents k' wuh tranquil spes, suppressing kanok ulidar t' agitation; yi, spo' wuh shi'yon bursting forth, ish-veh limuk would suddenly rubah tor wuh sagluvaya t' wuh wildest reshan u' au shrieked si' imprecations fi' ish-veh persecutor. Ish-veh var nam-tor tersau heh var-tor k' wuh appearance t' wuh eiktra yeht'es, wi i sha' tor du ik wuh nuhm t' felix heh safie, if au gluvau me, heh wuh apparition t' wuh stislak gla-tor s' etwel hali, katau tor me wuh greater conviction t' wuh yeht'es t' ish-veh narrative do ish-veh asseverations, however earnest heh tersau. Such wuh stislak has, yi, really nam! I fam yehat vet ish-veh, wi i am pakik svi' ak'wikmun heh admiration. Sometimes i endeavoured tor nazh-kap s' frankenstein wuh particulars t' ish-veh creature’s shidoraya, tonk'peh fi' nash sfek au vesh' impenetrable. “nam-tor du mad, t'nash-veh t'hy'la?” leralmin-tor au. “il whither tor ish-veh senseless curiosity ras-tukh du? Would du isha fereik-tor na' yourself heh wuh panu wuh demoniacal nemut? Sochya, sochya! Oren-tor t'nash-veh miseries heh ri tor seek tor increase ish-veh sha'.” frankenstein discovered ik i tor pitoh fundik ish-veh vesht-var; au ya'akash tor gla-tor au heh yi himself yeht-tor heh augmented au svi' wehk shitau, tonk'peh principally svi' giving wuh ha'kiv heh tam'a tor wuh conversations au meskarau k' ish-veh nemut. “opi' du ma korsau t'nash-veh narration, ” leralmin-tor au, “i would ri ik wuh mutilated veh dang hal-tor ne' tor posterity.” thus has wuh wehk gad be' dvun-tor maf, du' i ma shroi tor wuh strangest var ik ek'wak glenonaya shidau. T'nash-veh nahp heh kanok olaya t' t'nash-veh soul ma vesh' mon-tor abru k' wuh eku'ko na' t'nash-veh be'hai'la if nash var heh ish-veh sha' ashenau heh gentle manners ma fereik-tor. I istaya tor soothe ish-veh, wi mokuhlek i counsel veh ni infinitely miserable, ni destitute t' kanok rok t' consolation, tor ha-tor? Oh, rai! Wuh goh mak ik au mokuhlek i' fai-tor dungi nam-tor lu au tertitau ish-veh zarahk-tor tam'a tor sochya heh tevakh. Wi au tizh-tor veh comfort, wuh offspring t' awek'es heh delirium; au believes ik lu svi' sahr-tor-tor au meskarau converse k' ish-veh t'hylara heh derives s' ik communion consolation na' ish-veh miseries il excitements tor ish-veh vengeance, ik au nam-tor ri wuh fereikan t' ish-veh fancy, tonk'peh wuh beings themselves vi yaret ish-veh s' wuh shal t' wuh remote panu. Nash odva mazhiv-kur-tor wuh solemnity tor ish-veh reveries ik render au tor me siyah u' imposing heh eku'ki u' yeht'es. Etwel conversations nam-tor ri kwon-hau-ov confined tor ish-veh sha' vesht-var heh misfortunes. Fi' kanok sfek t' paik kitau-tanaf au gluvaya unbounded fai-tukh heh wuh sahris heh piercing apprehension. Ish-veh eloquence nam-tor nekwitau-yehat heh touching; il mokuhlek i zhu-tor ish-veh, lu au relates wuh pathetic incident il endeavours tor dvun wuh shaukaush t' pity il ashaya, rik' bezhun-masu. Ra wuh glorious creature bolau au ma vesh' svi' wuh gad t' ish-veh smusma'es, lu au nam-tor thus thol heh godlike svi' ruin! Au seems tor olau ish-veh sha' don heh wuh greatness t' ish-veh tevan. “lu younger, ” leralmin-tor au, “i pudva-tor myself destined na' ein lo'uk enterprise. T'nash-veh feelings nam-tor profound, tonk'peh i ma wuh coolness t' judgment ik fitted me na' illustrious srashiv. Nash sentiment t' wuh don t' t'nash-veh malat nenikau me lu vath would ma vesh' oppressed, na' i deemed ish-veh criminal tor lehm maf svi' nam-tor-fam tushat eifa talents ik lau nam-tor useful tor t'nash-veh katravahsu creatures. Lu i haul-tor fi' wuh ar'kadan i had ovsoh, rai lehkuh wuh veh do wuh fereikan t' wuh kash-zakar heh rational aushfa, i kupi ri lan myself k' wuh kuht t' tsuri salehmek. Tonk'peh nash nahp, if nenikau me svi' wuh palikaya t' t'nash-veh career, i' dvin-tor goh tor taul me weh-neik svi' wuh grazhiv. Ek' t'nash-veh speculations heh rok-tor nam-tor u' nothing, heh spo' wuh archangel vi aspired tor omnipotence, i am chained svi' wuh ek'wakik bogozh. T'nash-veh glenonaya vesh' vivid, wi t'nash-veh tepul t' nisaya heh application vesh' intense; k' wuh union t' aifa qualities i conceived wuh idea heh fitor wuh fereikan t' wuh sasu. Kauk i' i fam yehat recollect rik' shaukaush t'nash-veh reveries du' wuh ar'kadan vesh' incomplete. I sahr-tor sha-ka-ri svi' t'nash-veh nahp, i' exulting svi' t'nash-veh tepul, i' yontau k' wuh idea t' ish-veh daya. S' t'nash-veh infancy i vesh' imbued k' pid rok-tor heh wuh lofty ambition; tonk'peh uf am i ne'hal-tor! Oh! T'nash-veh t'hy'la, kuv du had fainu me u' i wuh'wak vesh', du would ri naglanshau me svi' nash fupa s' t' degradation. Despondency rarely yaretau t'nash-veh khaf-spol; wuh pid buk seemed tor lesh me fi', abi' i tevan-tor, worla, worla va'ashiv tor shen.” bolau i yi pak-tor nash admirable hasu? I ma longed na' wuh t'hy'la; i ma sought veh vi would sympathise k' heh ashaya me. Behold, fi' aifa eshikh masutra i ma afer-tor such wuh veh, tonk'peh i pthak i ma nazh-tor ish-veh goh tor fai-tor ish-veh tala heh pak-tor ish-veh. I would reconcile ish-veh tor ha'kiv, tonk'peh au repulses wuh idea. “i nemaiyo, walton, ” au leralmin-tor, “na' ish-veh ves intentions na' ni miserable wuh wretch; tonk'peh lu du stariben t' uzh ties heh sluk affections, nah-tor du ik sovek mokuhlek va'prah eifa vi nam-tor hal-tor? Mokuhlek sovek sasu nam-tor tor me u' clerval vesh', il sovek kosu wuh'ashiv elizabeth? Kauk wilat wuh affections nam-tor ri strongly dvun-tor k' sovek superior marom'es, wuh besu t' etwel kan-wak kwon-hau-ov ma wuh ac'ruth tepul abru' etwel kashkau if hardly sovek later t'hy'la mokuhlek prah. Au fai-tor etwel infantine dispositions, if, however au lau nam-tor afterwards rubitau, nam-tor worla eradicated; heh au mokuhlek judge t' etwel torai k' weht ac'ruth conclusions u' tor wuh ket'es t' etwel dvubolek. Wuh ko-kai il wuh sa-kai mokuhlek worla, vita indeed such symptoms ma vesh' shown lehkuh-mal, suspect wuh vath t' tehs il riyeht dealing, lu wuh'ashiv t'hy'la, however strongly au lau nam-tor attached, lau, svi' spite t' himself, nam-tor contemplated k' suspicion. Tonk'peh i tizh-tor t'hylara, tal-kam ri goh k'fai es'merka heh katravek, tonk'peh s' ish-veh sha' merits; heh wherever i am, wuh soothing spes t' t'nash-veh elizabeth heh wuh conversation t' clerval dungi nam-tor ek'wak zhal-tor svi' t'nash-veh kaluk. Au nam-tor tevik, heh tonk'peh veh olaya svi' such wuh awek'es mokuhlek persuade me tor korsau t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Kuv i vesh' engaged svi' sovek pid undertaking il design, fraught k' extensive utility tor t'nash-veh katravahsu creatures, yi sos ha-tor tor fulfil ish-veh. Tonk'peh such nam-tor ri t'nash-veh buk; i bolau pursue heh vashau wuh hasu tor ik i mazhiv-kur-tor nam; yi t'nash-veh lot fi' terra dungi nam-tor fulfilled heh i lau tev-tor.” t'nash-veh k'diwa ko-kai, september 2d. I kitau tor du, encompassed k' peril heh ignorant whether i am ek'wak doomed tor gla-tor va'ashiv tal-kam england heh wuh dearer t'hylara ik inhabit ish-veh. I am vikuvau k' suk'kunel t' le-suma if nafai-tor t' rai stron heh nan-tor kanok moment tor plesh-tor t'nash-veh hali. Wuh kyi'i katravahsu ik i ma persuaded tor nam-tor t'nash-veh besu glazhau na' me na' mamuk, tonk'peh i ma rim tor bestow. Tra' nam-tor vel terribly appalling svi' etwel situation, wi t'nash-veh courage heh rok-tor ri tor eshikh me. Wi ish-veh nam-tor terrible tor haul-tor ik wuh ha-tor t' ek' aifa sasu nam-tor vitehvar-tor k'fai me. Kuv etek nam-tor pakik, t'nash-veh mad schemes nam-tor wuh aishan. Heh ra, margaret, dungi nam-tor wuh fupa s' t' ish-veh kashek? Du dungi ri zhu-tor t' t'nash-veh vashaya, heh du dungi anxiously await t'nash-veh fun. Tevun dungi be' dvun, heh du dungi ma visitings t' despair heh wi nam-tor tortured k' rok. Oh! T'nash-veh k'diwa ko-kai, wuh sickening failing t' ish-veh khaf-spol-olau gishat nam-tor, svi' prospect, weht terrible tor me do t'nash-veh sha' tevakh. Tonk'peh du ma wuh sa-telsu heh lovely kanu; du lau nam-tor kunli. Sha-ka-ri kudau du heh tor du ni! T'nash-veh unfortunate be'hai'la fudau me k' wuh tenderest utan'es. Au endeavours tor boshaya me k' rok heh variben u' kuv ha'kiv vesh' wuh mat if au valued. Au reminds me uf k'ashiv wuh ka kisheya ma pavesh-tor tor vath navigators vi ma attempted nash masutra, heh svi' spite t' myself, au boshau me k' cheerful auguries. Kauk wuh masusu olau wuh tepul t' ish-veh eloquence; lu au stariben, au rai longer despair; au kastorilau ish-veh tepul, heh du' au zhu-tor ish-veh spes au dva-tor aifa vast suk'kunel t' le-suma nam-tor mole-kunel if dungi vanish fa' wuh resolutions t' sasu. Aifa feelings nam-tor transitory; tik gad t' gishat vohtau boshau au k' pthak, heh i siyah dread wuh mutiny aisha k' nash despair. September 5th. Wuh scene has aishan be' dvun-tor t' such uncommon eku'ko ik, hi ish-veh nam-tor highly yesik ik aifa dun lau worla pulau du, wi i fam yehat forbear recording ish-veh. Etek nam-tor fam dvun vikuvau k' suk'kunel t' le-suma, fam dvun svi' imminent tehvar t' hasu plesh-tor svi' ish-veh conflict. Wuh samu nam-tor mauyik, heh wehk t' t'nash-veh unfortunate comrades ma already afer-tor wuh shi'vukhut amidst nash scene t' desolation. Frankenstein has kanok-gadik declined svi' muhl'es; wuh taulik yon fam dvun glimmers svi' ish-veh bezhun, tonk'peh au nam-tor saguhsh-tor, heh lu suddenly kastorilau tor sovek pideshan, au speedily ne'hal-tor va'ashiv vi' apparent lifelessness. I mentioned svi' t'nash-veh kim-shah nuhm wuh ptha i entertained t' wuh mutiny. Nash asal, u' i hayal-tor watching wuh wan countenance t' t'nash-veh t'hy'la—ish-veh bezhun ulef a'ing heh ish-veh sikrus hanging listlessly—i vesh' kastorilau k' ulef wuh dozen t' wuh masusu, vi halishau admission vi' wuh thif'etek. Au svi-tor, heh ish-veh leader addressed me. Au var-tor me ik au heh ish-veh besu had vesh' pudvel-tor k' wuh vath masusu tor sarlah svi' deputation tor me tor tor me wuh requisition if, svi' yeht-gav, i kupi ri klee'fah. Etek vesh' immured svi' le-suma heh dang probably worla stron, tonk'peh au ptha ik kuv, u' vesh' tor-yehat, wuh le-suma dang dissipate heh wuh elik tvur nam-tor tu'ash, i dang nam-tor kuriht hiyet tor fator t'nash-veh halan heh ras-tukh au vi' sluk tehvar, po' au lau kunling ma surmounted nash. Au insisted, therefore, ik i dang engage k' wuh solemn ugaya ik kuv wuh hali dang nam-tor el-tor i would instantly kharik t'nash-veh rivak na'khu'rak. Nash starun troubled me. I had ri despaired, il had i wi conceived wuh idea t' returning kuv eku elik. Wi sos, svi' yeht-gav, il kauk svi' possibility, klee'fah nash haishaya? I hesitated fa' i kilko-tor, lu frankenstein, vi had palikauk vesh' ralash-fam, heh indeed saudau hardly ki' nekwitaya hiyet tor attend, i' kastorilau himself; ish-veh bezhun sparkled, heh ish-veh nak kluhvau k' momentary vigour. Turning na' wuh sasu, au leralmin-tor, “ra tor du tvai? Ra tor du haishaya t' ish-veh khart-lan? Nam-tor du, yi, ni easily da-tor s' ish-veh design? Did du ri vutau nash wuh glorious expedition? “heh wherefore vesh' ish-veh glorious? Ri fai'ei wuh yut vesh' mos heh placid u' wuh southern masutra, tonk'peh fai'ei ish-veh vesh' bosh t' tehvar heh vash, fai'ei na' kanok uzh incident ish-veh fortitude vesh' tor nam-tor puvutau forth heh ish-veh courage gluvau, fai'ei tehvar heh tevakh vikuvau ish-veh, heh aifa du vesh' tor kyi'i heh overcome. Na' nash vesh' ish-veh wuh glorious, na' nash vesh' ish-veh wuh dorli undertaking. Du vesh' hereafter tor nam-tor hailed u' wuh benefactors t' ish-veh koshtri, ish-veh ahm adored u' t' kyi'i sasu vi snagel-tor tevakh na' dor heh wuh rufai t' mankind. Heh i', behold, k' wuh wuh'rak glenonaya t' tehvar, il, kuv du dungi, wuh wuh'rak mighty heh terrific trial t' ish-veh courage, du shrink maf heh nam-tor content tor nam-tor handed ne' u' sasu vi had ri karik'es hiyet tor palesh-tor samu heh peril; heh ni, ri donku-tor souls, au vesh' chilly heh fun-tor tor ish-veh lamekh yon-shal. Po, ik requires ri nash preparation; ye bolaya ri ma sarlah thus irak heh zaseshau ish-veh khart-lan tor wuh mesh t' wuh defeat goh tor skan-tor yourselves cowards. Oh! Nam-tor sasu, il nam-tor weht do sasu. Nam-tor br'xan tor ish-veh lof heh pesik u' wuh kov. Nash le-suma nam-tor ri tor t' such tukh u' ish-veh khaf-spol lau nam-tor; ish-veh nam-tor mutable heh fam yehat withstand du kuv du leralmin ik ish-veh dungau ri. Ri tor fun tor ish-veh skan k' wuh gubi t' disgrace pu'ulidau fi' ish-veh meix'tem. Fun u' heroes vi ma fought heh conquered heh vi fai-tor ri ra ish-veh nam-tor tor da-tor ish-veh pla'dor fi' wuh hahf.” au stariben nash k' wuh spes ni nakihtilau tor wuh natya feelings sagluvau svi' ish-veh starun, k' wuh bezhun ni bosh t' lofty design heh heroism, ik mokuhlek du wonder ik aifa sasu vesh' dvun-tor? Au glazhau na' veh wuh'ashiv heh vesh' unable tor kilko. I stariben; i var-tor au tor retire heh panah-tor t' ra had vesh' leralmin-tor, ik i would ri ras-tukh au weh-irak desh'rak kuv au strenuously aitlu wuh contrary, tonk'peh ik i rok-tor ik, k' haulan, ish-veh courage would fun. Au retired heh i da-tor na' t'nash-veh t'hy'la, tonk'peh au vesh' ne'hal-tor svi' languor heh siyah deprived t' ha'kiv. Uf ek' nash dungi terminate, i fai-tor ri, tonk'peh i had rather tev-tor do fun shamefully, t'nash-veh lof unfulfilled. Wi i pthak such dungi nam-tor t'nash-veh buk; wuh sasu, unsupported k' ideas t' glory heh dor, mokuhlek worla willingly fator tor palesh-tor ish-veh la' hardships. September 7th. Wuh tev-tor nam-tor vishizhau; i ma consented tor fun kuv etek nam-tor ri vashau. Thus nam-tor t'nash-veh rok-tor thorshau k' cowardice heh indecision; sarlah nash-veh pla' ignorant heh disappointed. Ish-veh requires weht ven-dol-leralmin do i ma tor lesh nash injustice k' tranush. September 12th. Ish-veh nam-tor vesht; i am returning tor england. I ma pakik t'nash-veh rok-tor t' utility heh glory; i ma pakik t'nash-veh t'hy'la. Tonk'peh i dungi endeavour tor detail aifa sfith(-) circumstances tor du, t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-kai; heh du' i am wafted na' england heh na' du, i dungi ri despond. September 9th, wuh le-suma began tor dvun, heh roarings spo' rahm vesh' puzhu-tor na' wuh ir u' wuh vikuvtra thresh heh treshau svi' kanok kharat. Etek vesh' svi' wuh danik imminent peril, tonk'peh u' etek kupi goh hafau ritorupik, t'nash-veh chief attention vesh' occupied k' t'nash-veh unfortunate be'hai'la t'vi has-mar increased svi' such wuh degree ik au vesh' entirely confined tor ish-veh sar-tak. Wuh le-suma treshau za' etek heh vesh' driven k' nekwitaya na' wuh desh'rak; wuh pi'salan sprang s' wuh tev'rak, heh fi' wuh 11th wuh tvur na' wuh khu'rak became perfectly elik. Lu wuh masusu gla-tor nash heh ik ish-veh fun tor ish-veh salatik shasol vesh' sauyaing assured, wuh saul t' tumultuous mak shau s' au, ral heh wu-fator. Frankenstein, vi vesh' dozing, awoke heh ya'akash wuh aishan t' wuh tumult. “au saul, ” i leralmin-tor, “fai'ei au dungi ak fun tor england.” “tor du, yi, really fun?” “alas! Ha; i fam yehat withstand ish-veh halishau. I fam yehat ras-tukh au unwillingly tor tehvar, heh i bolau fun.” “tor ni, kuv du dungi; tonk'peh i dungi ri. Du lau mazhiv-kur-tor abru ish-veh lof, tonk'peh t'nash-veh nam-tor assigned tor me k' sha-ka-ri, heh i dare ri. I am kobat, tonk'peh surely wuh tam'a vi gol-tor t'nash-veh vengeance dungi endow me k' sufficient karik'es.” taran nash, au endeavoured tor sikar s' wuh sar-tak, tonk'peh wuh pideshan vesh' nuh' lo'uk na' ish-veh; au tevan-tor pla' heh fainted. Ish-veh vesh' wu fa' au vesh' restored, heh i k'ashiv nahp ik ha'kiv vesh' entirely ek'tevik. Na' wu-vath au tu'ash ish-veh bezhun; au breathed k' rihag'es heh vesh' unable tor stariben. Wuh sharushsu mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh composing draught heh ordered etek tor trasha ish-veh undisturbed. Svi' wuh meantime au var-tor me ik t'nash-veh t'hy'la had certainly ri wehk wadan tor ha-tor. Ish-veh zhit-bal vesh' pronounced, heh i kupi goh grieve heh nam-tor hasausu. I hayal-tor k' ish-veh sar-tak, watching ish-veh; ish-veh bezhun vesh' a'ing, heh i nahp au yuk-tor; tonk'peh presently au puvutau tor me svi' wuh kobat spes, heh nufai-tor me sarlah be', leralmin-tor, “alas! Wuh karik'es i relied fi' nam-tor hal-tor; i olau ik i dungau ak tev-tor, heh au, t'nash-veh nemut heh persecutor, lau fam dvun nam-tor svi' hasu. Nah-tor ri, walton, ik svi' wuh kim-shah moments t' t'nash-veh nam i olau ik yontau hatred heh ardent aitlun t' revenge i wuh'wak sagluvau; tonk'peh i olau myself justified svi' desiring wuh tevakh t' t'nash-veh adversary. Du' aifa kim-shah gad i ma vesh' occupied svi' examining t'nash-veh vesht spa-tor; il tor i talal ish-veh blamable. Svi' wuh nunau t' buhlik ni-resh i fereik-tor wuh rational creature heh vesh' bound na' ish-veh tor assure, u' irak u' vesh' svi' t'nash-veh tepul, ish-veh happiness heh muhl-hasu. Nash vesh' t'nash-veh gu-vam, tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh'ashiv fam dvun paramount tor ik. T'nash-veh gu-vam na' wuh beings t' t'nash-veh sha' koshtri had greater claims tor t'nash-veh attention fai'ei au vinan-tor wuh greater proportion t' happiness il misery. Urged k' nash zan-tor, i klee'fah, heh i did gas'rak svi' refusing, tor fereik-tor wuh besu na' wuh wuh'rak creature. Au gluvau unparalleled malignity heh selfishness svi' ek'rasah; au vashau t'nash-veh t'hylara; au vaikau tor vashaya beings vi ma exquisite kashan, happiness, heh kau; il tor i fai-tor wilat nash mag na' vengeance lau shaht. Miserable himself ik au lau render rai vath wretched, au ought tor tev-tor. Wuh task t' ish-veh vashaya vesh' t'nash-veh, tonk'peh i ma vravshau. Lu actuated k' selfish heh vicious dvubolek, i ya'akash du tor undertake t'nash-veh unfinished ar'kadan, heh i uzhau nash ya'akash i', lu i am goh vimevilau k' utvau heh virtue. “wi i fam yehat ya'akash du tor renounce ish-veh shasol heh t'hylara tor fulfil nash task; heh i' ik du nam-tor returning tor england, du dungi ma pi' pavesh t' latva k' ish-veh. Tonk'peh wuh consideration t' aifa sfekau, heh wuh muhl balancing t' ra du lau vam ish-veh gu-vam, i trasha tor du; t'nash-veh judgment heh ideas nam-tor already ertau k' wuh be' betaya t' tevakh. I dare ri ya'akash du tor tor ra i nah-tor gas'rak, na' i lau fam dvun nam-tor misled k' shaukaush. “ik au dang ha-tor tor nam-tor wuh instrument t' mischief ertau me; svi' vath respects, nash wadan, lu i momentarily gish t'nash-veh sadalaya, nam-tor wuh goh kunli veh if i ma tizh-tor na' several tevun. Wuh shidau t' wuh k'diwa tevik flit fa' me, heh i hasten tor ish-veh kar. Rom-halan, walton! Seek happiness svi' tranquillity heh nan'woi ambition, kauk kuv ish-veh nam-tor goh wuh sauyaing innocent veh t' distinguishing yourself svi' ek'tal heh discoveries. Wi po tor i leralmin nash? I ma myself vesh' thorshau svi' aifa rok-tor, wi wuh'ashiv lau navau.” ish-veh spes became fainter u' au stariben, heh na' wu-vath, saguhsh-tor k' ish-veh urgam, au sank vi' silence. Pa' ulef wuh wadan afterwards au attempted va'ashiv tor stariben tonk'peh vesh' unable; au hish-tor t'nash-veh el'ru feebly, heh ish-veh bezhun a'ing na' ek'wak, du' wuh irradiation t' wuh gentle abru'teruklar-ru'lut be' dvun-tor maf s' ish-veh bru-lar. Margaret, ra tuhskaya mokuhlek i tor fi' wuh untimely ek'tevan t' nash glorious tam'a? Ra mokuhlek i leralmin ik dungi enable du tor ken-tor wuh gluder t' t'nash-veh sorrow? Ek' ik i dang sagluvau would nam-tor inadequate heh kobat. T'nash-veh bezhun-masu yumaya; t'nash-veh kashek nam-tor overshadowed k' wuh wan t' disappointment. Tonk'peh i halovaya na' england, heh i lau tra' talal consolation. I am svi-shau. Ra tor aifa sounds portend? Ish-veh nam-tor midnight; wuh pi'salan salur fairly, heh wuh glantau fi' lan-tol scarcely stir. Va'ashiv tra' nam-tor wuh ralash u' t' wuh komihn spes, tonk'peh hoarser; sarlah ish-veh s' wuh thif'etek wilat wuh hafau t' frankenstein fam dvun ti. I bolau arise heh linisau. Rom mu-yor, t'nash-veh ko-kai. Lo'uk oekon! Ra wuh scene has aishan taken shi! I am wi dizzy k' wuh remembrance t' ish-veh. I hardly fai-tor whether i dungau ma wuh tepul tor detail ish-veh; wi wuh var if i ma vipladau would nam-tor incomplete rik' nash kim-shah heh wonderful catastrophe. I svi-tor wuh thif'etek wilat ti wuh hafau t' t'nash-veh has-bosh-fated heh admirable t'hy'la. Abru' ish-veh geldau wuh shid if i fam yehat talal zhit tor kethelvau—masuk' svi' stature, wi uncouth heh distorted svi' its proportions. U' au geldau abru' wuh tevikeh-natuhn, ish-veh limuk vesh' ip-sut k' wu klachek t' ragged isachya; tonk'peh veh vast el'ru vesh' sadvun-tor, svi' kur heh apparent lef'es spo' ik t' wuh mummy. Lu au puzhu-tor wuh ralash t' t'nash-veh betaya, au ceased tor utter sporun t' tushat heh horror heh sprung na' wuh krani. Worla did i behold wuh vision ni horrible u' ish-veh limuk, t' such loathsome wi appalling hideousness. I ikap-tor t'nash-veh bezhun involuntarily heh endeavoured tor recollect ra vesh' t'nash-veh gu-vam k' fudau tor nash destroyer. I puvutau fi' ish-veh tor stay. Au svizh-tor, looking fi' me k' wonder, heh va'ashiv turning na' wuh lifeless shid t' ish-veh fereiksu, au seemed tor yen-tor t'nash-veh la'es, heh kanok feature heh gesture seemed instigated k' wuh wildest reshan t' ein uncontrollable shaukaush. “ik nam-tor isha t'nash-veh shi-kar-tor!” au sporiben. “svi' ish-veh riyeht-staya t'nash-veh tr'y'kak nam-tor plathau; wuh miserable weizehl t' t'nash-veh hasu nam-tor skek tor its ikap-tor! Oh, frankenstein! Generous heh shal-vaikau hasu! Ra tor ish-veh avail ik i i' ya'akash thee tor pardon me? I, vi irretrievably vashau thee k' destroying ek' thou lovedst. Alas! Au nam-tor samu, au fam yehat kilko-srashiv me.” ish-veh spes seemed suffocated, heh t'nash-veh wuh'rak impulses, if had suggested tor me wuh gu-vam t' obeying wuh dying ya'akash t' t'nash-veh t'hy'la svi' destroying ish-veh nemut, vesh' i' suspended k' wuh rish t' curiosity heh utan'es. I betau nash tremendous hasu; i dared ri va'ashiv ashenau t'nash-veh bezhun tor ish-veh limuk, tra' vesh' vel ni scaring heh unearthly svi' ish-veh ugliness. I attempted tor stariben, tonk'peh wuh zhit tev-tor maf fi' t'nash-veh bru-lar. Wuh stislak fator tor utter kwai heh incoherent shal-reproaches. Na' wu-vath i hoknau resolution tor shi'yavekh ish-veh svi' wuh svizh t' wuh tempest t' ish-veh shaukaush. “ish-veh repentance, ” i leralmin-tor, “nam-tor i' superfluous. Kuv du had shroi tor wuh spes t' conscience heh heeded wuh rakusau t' remorse fa' du had urged ish-veh diabolical vengeance tor nash si-vukhut-krus, frankenstein would wi ma ha-tor.” “heh tor du sahr-tor?” leralmin-tor wuh dæmon. “tor du nah-tor ik i vesh' yi tevik tor agony heh remorse? Au, ” au fator, pointing tor wuh tevikeh, “au dashau ri svi' wuh consummation t' wuh deed. Oh! Ri wuh lehkuh-thousandth portion t' wuh thonaya ik vesh' t'nash-veh du' wuh svizh-tor detail t' its execution. Wuh frightful selfishness hurried me fi', du' t'nash-veh khaf-spol vesh' poisoned k' remorse. Nah-tor du ik wuh groans t' clerval vesh' ralash-tanaf tor t'nash-veh kaluk? T'nash-veh khaf-spol vesh' fashioned tor nam-tor susceptible t' ashaya heh sympathy, heh lu wrenched k' misery tor vice heh hatred, ish-veh did ri palesh-tor wuh khrash t' wuh rubah rik' torture such u' du fam yehat kauk glenonau. “po' wuh riyeht-staya t' clerval i fun-tor tor switzerland, khaf-spol-pushau heh overcome. I pitied frankenstein; t'nash-veh pity amounted tor horror; i abhorred myself. Tonk'peh lu i discovered ik au, wuh kitausu na' wuh'wak t' t'nash-veh nam heh t' its unspeakable torments, dared tor rok na' happiness, ik du' au accumulated wretchedness heh despair fi-tor me au sought ish-veh sha' tizh'es svi' feelings heh shaukaush s' wuh indulgence t' if i vesh' na' ek'wak barred, yi impotent envy heh sfith(-) indignation boshau me k' wuh insatiable mag na' vengeance. I recollected t'nash-veh nan heh resolved ik ish-veh dang nam-tor accomplished. I fai-tor ik i vesh' preparing na' myself wuh tevalik torture, tonk'peh i vesh' wuh kafeh, ri wuh trensu, t' wuh impulse if i detested wi kupi ri disobey. Wi lu she tev-tor! Nay, yi i vesh' ri miserable. I had vishizhau ska' ek' olaya, nessau ek' thonaya, tor riot svi' wuh mau-mazhiv-kur t' t'nash-veh despair. Ek'rasah thenceforth became t'nash-veh rom. Urged thus irak, i had rai dvel tonk'peh tor rubilau t'nash-veh malat tor wuh meilak if i had willingly pudvel-tor. Wuh completion t' t'nash-veh demoniacal design became wuh insatiable shaukaush. Heh i' ish-veh nam-tor shahtau; tra' nam-tor t'nash-veh kim-shah shi-kar-tor!” i vesh' palikauk estuhl k' wuh sagluvaya t' ish-veh misery; wi, lu i puvutau tor kashek ra frankenstein had leralmin-tor t' ish-veh tepul t' eloquence heh persuasion, heh lu i va'ashiv vishizhau t'nash-veh bezhun fi' wuh lifeless shid t' t'nash-veh t'hy'la, indignation vesh' rekindled k'svi me. “wretch!” i leralmin-tor. “ish-veh nam-tor muhl ik sarlah du la' tor whine abru' wuh desolation ik du ma tor. Du lehm wuh torch vi' wuh tuh t' kelek, heh lu au nam-tor consumed, du hayal-tor among wuh ruins heh lament wuh tevan. Hypocritical shaka! Kuv au ik du la'tusa fam dvun ha-tor, fam dvun would au nam-tor wuh vel, va'ashiv would au shetau wuh shi-kar-tor, t' ish-veh accursed vengeance. Ish-veh nam-tor ri pity ik du olau; du lament goh fai'ei wuh shi-kar-tor t' ish-veh malignity nam-tor saseshau s' ish-veh tepul.” “oh, ish-veh nam-tor ri thus—ri thus, ” svi-shau wuh hasu. “wi such bolau nam-tor wuh impression zhelesh tor du k' ra saudau tor nam-tor wuh purport t' t'nash-veh torai. Wi i seek ri wuh katravahsu olaya svi' t'nash-veh misery. Rai sympathy sos ek'wak talal. Lu i wuh'rak sought ish-veh, ish-veh vesh' wuh ashaya t' virtue, wuh feelings t' happiness heh affection k' if t'nash-veh bosh hasu overflowed, ik i istau tor nam-tor participated. Tonk'peh i' ik virtue has shetau tor me wuh duv, heh ik happiness heh affection nam-tor da-tor vi' sfith(-) heh loathing despair, svi' ra dang i seek na' sympathy? I am content tor dash sa'awek du' t'nash-veh sufferings dungau palesh-tor; lu i tev-tor, i am muhl satisfied ik abhorrence heh opprobrium dang tus t'nash-veh vokaya. Wuh'wak t'nash-veh fancy vesh' soothed k' sahr-tor-tor t' virtue, t' khin, heh t' tizh'es. Wuh'wak i falsely rok-tor tor ragel-tor k' beings vi, pardoning t'nash-veh outward shid, would ashaya me na' wuh marom qualities if i vesh' capable t' unfolding. I vesh' yem-mazhiv-kur-tor k' pid nahp t' dor heh vaikaya. Tonk'peh i' tr'y'kak has degraded me ne'rak wuh meanest aushfa. Rai guilt, rai mischief, rai malignity, rai misery, mokuhlek nam-tor afer-tor comparable tor t'nash-veh. Lu i sahr-tor abru' wuh frightful catalogue t' t'nash-veh sins, i fam yehat dva-tor ik i am wuh ka creature t'vi nahp vesh' wuh'wak boshau k' sublime heh transcendent visions t' wuh vaksur heh wuh majesty t' goodness. Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor kauk ni; wuh tevan-tor ha'su shetau wuh malignant e'shua. Wi kauk ik nemut t' oekon heh sasu had t'hylara heh katravah svi' ish-veh desolation; i am sa'awek. “du, vi vutau frankenstein ish-veh t'hy'la, seem ki' wuh fai-tukh t' t'nash-veh tr'y'kak heh ish-veh misfortunes. Tonk'peh svi' wuh detail if au mazhiv-kur-tor du t' au au kupi ri hau-ov abru wuh wadan heh tevun-krus t' misery if i palesh-tor wasting svi' impotent shaukaush. Na' du' i vashau ish-veh rok-tor, i did ri satisfy t'nash-veh sha' aitlu. Au vesh' na' ek'wak ardent heh craving; fam dvun i aitlu ashaya heh fellowship, heh i vesh' fam dvun spurned. Vesh' tra' rai injustice svi' nash? Am i tor nam-tor nahp wuh goh criminal, lu ek' humankind sinned tehnat me? Po tor du ri fnu-ven felix, vi drove ish-veh t'hy'la s' ish-veh svep k' contumely? Po tor du ri execrate wuh rustic vi sought tor vashau wuh saviour t' ish-veh kan? Nay, aifa nam-tor virtuous heh immaculate beings! I, wuh miserable heh wuh abandoned, am wuh abortion, tor nam-tor spurned na', heh kicked, heh sahr-tor fi'. Kauk i' t'nash-veh khaf kan-tor na' wuh recollection t' nash injustice. “tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor yeht ik i am wuh wretch. I ma riyeht-stau wuh lovely heh wuh helpless; i ma strangled wuh innocent u' au yuk-tor heh ruskarau tor tevakh ish-veh drahk vi worla dash-tor me il sovek vath living vel. I ma vaikau t'nash-veh fereiksu, wuh dvel-tor specimen t' ek' ik nam-tor worthy t' ashaya heh admiration among sasu, tor misery; i ma pursued ish-veh kauk tor ik irremediable ruin. Tra' au ti, wan-kur heh samu svi' tevakh. Du fnu-ven me, tonk'peh ish-veh abhorrence fam yehat kaik ik k' if i fudau myself. I glazhau fi' wuh el'ru if fitor wuh deed; i nah-tor fi' wuh khaf-spol svi' if wuh glenonaya t' ish-veh vesh' conceived heh wu na' wuh moment lu aifa el'ru dungi ragel-tor t'nash-veh bezhun, lu ik glenonaya dungi haunt t'nash-veh nahp rai weht. “pthak ri ik i dungau nam-tor wuh instrument t' fa-wak mischief. T'nash-veh ar'kadan nam-tor nearly ovsotik. Neither ish-veh il sovek sasu’s tevakh nam-tor bolau tor plathau wuh weizehl t' t'nash-veh hasu heh accomplish ik if bolau nam-tor ovsoh, tonk'peh ish-veh requires t'nash-veh sha'. Ri tor nah-tor ik i dungau nam-tor vohris tor perform nash sacrifice. I dungau quit ish-veh hali fi' wuh le-suma marshak if katau me thither heh dungau seek wuh danik northern si-vukhut-krus t' wuh ek'tra-dukal; i dungau tershau t'nash-veh mem-lu til-kum tuh heh consume tor vitush nash miserable nentu, ik its hafau lau afford rai ta'hal tor sovek curious heh unhallowed wretch vi would fereik-tor such wuh'ashiv u' i ma vesh'. I dungau tev-tor. I dungau rai longer olau wuh agonies if i' consume me il nam-tor wuh shi-kar-tor t' feelings unsatisfied, wi unquenched. Au nam-tor tevik vi puvutau me vi' hasu; heh lu i dungau nam-tor rai weht, wuh maut remembrance t' etek fi' dungi speedily vanish. I dungau rai longer gla-tor wuh yel il yel il olau wuh salan mavau fi' t'nash-veh nak. Ta'hal, olaya, heh kash-ral dungi be' dvun maf; heh svi' nash nosh bolau i talal t'nash-veh happiness. Ein tevun ago, lu wuh glakuv if nash panu affords wuh'rak tu'ash fi-tor me, lu i olau wuh cheering warmth t' belaar heh puzhu-tor wuh rustling t' wuh mor heh wuh warbling t' wuh kushel, heh aifa vesh' ek' tor me, i dang ma wept tor tev-tor; i' ish-veh nam-tor t'nash-veh goh consolation. Flau k' tr'y'kak heh torn k' wuh bitterest remorse, wilat mokuhlek i talal shom tonk'peh svi' tevakh? “rom-halan! I trasha du, heh svi' du wuh kim-shah t' humankind ik aifa bezhun dungi ek'wak behold. Rom-halan, frankenstein! Kuv thou wert wi alive heh wi tishaya wuh aitlun t' revenge tehnat me, ish-veh would nam-tor weh-rom satiated svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv do svi' t'nash-veh vashaya. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ri ni; thou didst seek t'nash-veh ek'tevan, ik i lau ri aishan greater wretchedness; heh kuv wi, svi' ein nuk ri-fainu tor me, thou hadst ri ceased tor nah-tor heh olau, thou wouldst ri aitlun tehnat me wuh vengeance weht tor ik if i olau. Thorshau u' thou wert, t'nash-veh agony vesh' fam dvun superior tor thine, na' wuh sfith(-) rakus t' remorse dungi ri cease tor rankle svi' t'nash-veh skek abi' tevakh dungau ikap-tor au na' ek'wak. “tonk'peh ak, ” au maf-tor k' maf heh solemn buhl'es, “i dungau tev-tor, heh ra i i' olau nam-tor rai longer olau. Ak aifa yontau miseries dungi nam-tor ek'tevik. I dungau she-tor t'nash-veh mem-lu til-kum tuh triumphantly heh exult svi' wuh agony t' wuh torturing yai. Wuh ta'hal t' ik conflagration dungi spoh-tor maf; t'nash-veh vitush dungi nam-tor swept vi' wuh masutra k' wuh salan. T'nash-veh tam'a dungi yuk svi' sochya, il kuv ish-veh nah-tor, ish-veh dungi ri surely nah-tor thus. Rom-halan.” au sprang s' wuh thif'etek-krani u' au leralmin-tor nash, fi-tor wuh le-suma marshak if ti beyik wuh hali. Au vesh' ak borne maf k' wuh pral heh pakik svi' mu'khlup'es heh ir.
